### [1] [Complex Effects of Salt on Small-Angle X-ray Scattering of BSA Originate From the Interplay of Ions and Hydration Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27913)
*Anshika Dhiman,Sanbo Qin,Huan-Xiang Zhou*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合新开发的FMAPIq方法与全原子显式溶剂分子动力学模拟，揭示了盐对牛血清白蛋白（BSA）小角X射线散射（SAXS）数据复杂影响的物理起源，表明这些效应源于离子与结合水的相互作用，从而建立了蛋白质-离子-水相互作用的普适图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盐是生物系统环境的必要组成部分，理解其对蛋白质等生物分子的效应具有基础性意义。然而，从蛋白质溶液的小角X射线散射（small-angle X-ray scattering, SAXS）数据中提取盐效应信息一直是一个重大挑战。

Method: 将新开发的FMAPIq方法与全原子显式溶剂分子动力学模拟（explicit-solvent all-atom molecular dynamics simulations）相结合，对不同盐浓度下牛血清白蛋白（bovine serum albumin, BSA）的SAXS数据进行分析。

Result: 盐水牛血清白蛋白SAXS数据的复杂效应源于离子与结合水（hydration water）之间的相互协同作用，修正了以往仅使用三种不同球形模型拟合数据的局限性。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了蛋白质-离子-水相互作用的一般性物理图像（general picture of protein-ion-water interactions），为从SAXS数据中提取盐效应信息提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Salts are an integral part of the environment for living systems and, therefore, understanding their effects on proteins and other biomolecules is of fundamental interest. Small-angle X-ray scattering (SAXS) of protein solutions can provide valuable information on salt effects, but extracting this information has been a significant challenge. For example, SAXS data of bovine serum albumin (BSA) at various salt concentrations were fit to three different spherical models. Here we combined the newly developed FMAPIq approach with explicit-solvent all-atom molecular dynamics simulations to show that the complex effects of salt on the SAXS of BSA originate from the interplay of ions and hydration water, leading to a general picture of protein-ion-water interactions.

</details>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Emergence of prethermal time quasicrystalline order in a quasiperiodically driven non-interacting spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27250)
*Davood Marripour,Jahanfar Abouie*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究准周期驱动非相互作用自旋-1/2链中的预热时间准晶序（prethermal time quasicrystalline order），通过精确对角化分析了时间自关联函数、动力学结构因子和纠缠熵。在高频区观察到不可公度频率处的稳健谱峰，标志着准周期时间平移对称性破缺（QTTSB）。系统显示出亚线性幂律增长的纠缠熵和预热平台，且非平衡寿命随驱动频率增加而快速延长。非对称伊辛耦合分布引入集体自旋刚性，增强了系统抗加热能力。TQC相在近邻交换扰动和旋转不完美性下保持稳健，表明该准周期驱动系统可作为长寿命非平衡时间序的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究准周期驱动（quasiperiodic driving）下非相互作用自旋系统中预热时间准晶序的存在性与稳定性，特别是超越Floquet理论的不可公度频率动力学行为。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法分析准周期驱动自旋-1/2链的时间自关联函数、动力学结构因子和纠缠熵；驱动由周期性开关的随机伊辛相互作用和旋转横向磁场组成，频率比设定为无理数。

Result: 高频区出现不可公度频率处的稳健谱峰，证实准周期时间平移对称性破缺；纠缠熵呈亚线性幂律增长后进入预热平台；非平衡寿命随驱动频率增加而快速延长；非对称伊辛耦合分布诱导集体自旋刚性，增强系统抗加热能力；TQC相对近邻交换扰动和旋转不完美性具有稳健性。

Conclusion: 准周期驱动系统可作为实现长寿命非平衡时间序的可行平台，揭示了无序、集体刚性（collective rigidity）与准周期驱动之间的协同机制。

Abstract: We study prethermal time quasicrystalline (TQC) order in a quasiperiodically driven chain of non-interacting spin-1/2 particles. The drive consists of two parts, switched on and off periodically with frequency $ω_d$: (i) disordered Ising interactions, with exchange couplings chosen from a symmetric interval $[-J/2, J/2]$, allowing random antiferromagnetic or ferromagnetic nearest-neighbor couplings, together with a random transverse field; and (ii) a rotating transverse magnetic field with frequency $Ω$.
  The ratio $ω_d/Ω$ is chosen to be irrational, producing multiple incommensurate frequencies and yielding quasiperiodic dynamics beyond Floquet theory. Using exact diagonalization, we analyze the time autocorrelation function, dynamical structure factor, and entanglement entropy (EE). In the high-frequency regime, robust spectral peaks at incommensurate frequencies (not integer multiples of the fundamental drives) signal quasiperiodic time-translation symmetry breaking (QTTSB). The EE exhibits sublinear power-law growth followed by a prethermal plateau, indicating suppressed resonant heating due to an energy scale mismatch. The nonequilibrium lifetime increases rapidly with driving frequency. Unlike symmetric disorder sampling, an asymmetric distribution of the Ising exchange couplings induces collective spin rigidity, enhancing the system's resistance to heating. The TQC phase remains stable against next-nearest-neighbor (NNN) exchange perturbations and rotational imperfections, with robustness comparable to discrete time crystals (TCs) under periodic driving. Our results establish this quasiperiodically driven system as a platform for long-lived nonequilibrium temporal order, revealing the interplay of disorder, collective rigidity, and quasiperiodic driving.

</details>


### [3] [Sampling two-dimensional spin systems with transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27738)
*Piotr Białas,Piotr Korcyl,Tomasz Stebel,Adam Stefański,Dawid Zapolski*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Transformer的分组自回归神经采样器，通过每次生成一组自旋（spin）而非单个自旋，并采用近似概率模型来提升计算效率。在Ising模型（Ising model）上实现了最高180×180自旋系统的采样，有效样本量（Effective Sample Size）相比先前最先进的神经采样器提升了约20倍，并在二维Edwards-Anderson模型（Edwards-Anderson model）上验证了64×64系统的可训练性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于稠密或卷积层的自回归神经网络（Autoregressive Neural Networks）虽已被证明可有效生成经典自旋系统（classical spin systems），但基于Transformer的采样方法通常被认为计算效率低下。本文旨在克服Transformer在神经采样中的效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出一种分组生成（group-wise generation）策略：Transformer每步生成一组自旋而非单个自旋；同时构建近似概率模型（model of approximated probabilities）以进一步优化算法效率。

Result: 在Ising模型上实现最高180×180自旋系统的采样；对于临界温度下128×128的Ising模型，有效样本量（Effective Sample Size）比先前最先进的神经采样器大~20倍；在二维Edwards-Anderson模型上成功训练64×64自旋系统。

Conclusion: 尽管所提方法在计算量上重于稠密网络或卷积神经网络（CNN）方法，但其在系统规模和采样效率上均取得了显著提升，验证了Transformer架构在经典自旋系统采样中的可行性与优势。

Abstract: Autoregressive Neural Networks based on dense or convolutional layers have recently been shown to be a viable strategy for generating classical spin systems. Unlike these methods, sampling with transformers is commonly considered to be computationally inefficient. In this work, we propose a novel approach to transformer-based neural samplers in which we generate not a single spin per step but groups of spins. As an additional improvement, we construct a model of approximated probabilities, further improving the efficiency of the algorithm. Despite our approach being computationally heavier than dense networks or CNN-based approaches, we were able to sample larger systems of up to $180 \times 180$ spins in case of the Ising model. The Effective Sample Size of our sampler is $\sim 20$ times larger than that of the previous state-of-the-art neural sampler when trained for the $128 \times 128$ Ising model at critical temperature. Finally, we also test our algorithm on the 2D Edwards-Anderson model, where we train $64\times 64$ spin systems.

</details>


### [4] [Discontinuous BBP transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27992)
*Dario Bocchi,Giulio Biroli,Chiara Cammarota,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Baik-Ben Arous-Peche (BBP)相变在一般条件下可以是不连续的，并为此提供了完整的理论框架。当谱边缘特征值密度以快于线性的速度趋于零时，主特征向量与信号之间的重叠会在临界点处发生跳跃。这一发现使得信号恢复可以在更低的信噪比下实现，但伴随显著的样本间波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Baik-Ben Arous-Peche (BBP)相变描述的是连续过渡，即信号在阈值之上逐渐显现。然而，现有理论未能覆盖特征值密度在谱边缘以更快速率衰减的情形，这限制了我们对低秩结构检测的认识。

Method: 作者在变形高斯系综（deformed Gaussian ensemble）和重加权Wishart系综（reweighted Wishart ensemble）中分析了不连续BBP相变机制，并系统考察了有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）在其中的核心作用。

Result: 当谱边缘特征值密度以快于线性的速度趋于零时，主特征向量与信号的重叠在临界点处发生不连续跳跃。有限尺寸效应导致在渐近阈值之前就出现一个扩展的前临界区域（pre-critical region），其中信息性特征向量已经涌现。

Conclusion: 不连续BBP相变的主要后果是：信号恢复可在远低于连续相变阈值的信噪比下发生，但伴随强烈的样本间变异性（sample-to-sample variability）。这一发现对信号检测具有重要的实际意义。

Abstract: The Baik-Ben Arous-Peche (BBP) transition sets fundamental limits for detecting low-rank structure in noisy high-dimensional data and underlies a wide range of spectral methods in many fields from physics to statistics and data sciences. In standard settings, this transition is continuous, implying that signal recovery emerges gradually above a sharp threshold. We show that BBP transitions can instead be discontinuous in very general settings and provide a full theory of this phenomenon. When the eigenvalue density vanishes faster than linearly at the spectral edge, the overlap between the leading eigenvector and the signal jumps discontinuously at the critical point. We study this mechanism in deformed Gaussian and reweighted Wishart ensembles. We analyze in detail the finite-size effects, which play a central and qualitatively new role in the discontinuous BBP transition. Unlike the continuous BBP transition, we establish the existence of an extended pre-critical region where informative eigenvectors emerge well before the asymptotic threshold. The main consequence-and difference from the continuous BBP transition-is that signal recovery can occur at significantly lower signal-to-noise ratio and it is accompanied by strong sample-to-sample variability. Our results show the relevance and the novelty of the discontinuous BBP transition, and highlight the practical implications for signal detection.

</details>


### [5] [The Synergistic Route to Stretched Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28003)
*Lorenzo Lucarini,Sandro Meloni,Pablo Villegas*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究表明，协同相互作用（synergistic interactions）提供了一条通往非传统临界现象（non-conventional critical phenomena）的新路径，通过互补途径增强活性的扩散机制产生了类似Griffiths相的弛豫速率宽分布、慢动力学和扩展临界性（extended criticality），且该机制在多种网络结构以及包含高阶交互或纯成对非线性动力学的系统中均稳健存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Griffiths相通常与淬火无序（quenched disorder）相关，而阻挫（frustration）导致多稳态和自旋玻璃行为；扩展临界性是否能在其他情境中出现仍是一个悬而未决的问题。本文旨在探索协同相互作用是否能够成为一种不同于无序与阻挫的、产生非传统临界现象的机制。

Method: 通过结合通过互补途径增强活性的扩散机制，作者分析了由此产生的弛豫速率分布，并考察了该机制在不同网络结构下的稳健性。研究同时涵盖了具有明确高阶相互作用（higher-order interactions）的系统以及具有非线性动力学的纯成对（pairwise）系统。

Result: 协同相互作用产生了弛豫速率的宽分布，进而导致类似Griffiths的慢动力学和扩展临界性。该机制在不同网络结构下均表现稳健，且同时存在于具有显式高阶交互的系统与具有非线性动力学的纯成对系统中。

Conclusion: 协同相互作用为产生非传统临界现象提供了一条区别于淬火无序和阻挫的独立路径，扩展了对临界性起源的理解。

Abstract: Griffiths phases are typically associated with quenched disorder, while frustration gives rise to multistability and spin-glass behavior. Whether extended criticality can arise in other contexts remains an open question. Here, we show that synergistic interactions provide a distinct route to non-conventional critical phenomena. By combining spreading mechanisms that reinforce activity through complementary pathways, we uncover a broad distribution of relaxation rates, leading to Griffiths-like slow dynamics and extended criticality. We demonstrate that this mechanism is robust across networks and emerges both in systems with explicit higher-order interactions and in purely pairwise systems with nonlinear dynamics.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.stat-mech'></div>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Triadic Phase Transitions in AI Networks: Composite-Operator Scaling in Cognitive Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27038)
*Eduardo Salazar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于COGENT³模型，证明具有k体自旋关联子（k-body spin correlator）作为集体可观测量（collective observable）的多智能体AI架构（multi-agent AI architectures）展现出复合算子的临界性（composite-operator criticality），其临界指数与所有成对网络普适类（pairwise-network universality classes）定性不同。通过可精确求解的三元伊辛模型（triadic Ising model），推导出形成转变（formation transition）的解析结果，包括交叉温度（crossover temperature）、平均场临界点（mean-field critical point）、形成关联子（formation correlator）的标度行为以及通过Mori-Zwanzig记忆模型得到的可调动力学指数（dynamical exponent）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究大多集中于成对网络（pairwise networks）的临界行为，而对由高阶相互作用（higher-order interactions）驱动的多智能体系统的临界现象尚缺乏系统理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，证明基于k体关联子的多智能体架构会脱离所有已知的成对网络普适类，并给出首个非平凡情形k=3的严格解析结果。

Method: 采用普适性（universality）与平均场（mean-field）论证，将COGENT³的形成转变约化为可精确求解的三元伊辛模型（triadic Ising model）。在{-1,+1}³上推导出最小三元哈密顿量（minimal triad Hamiltonian）的精确配分函数（partition function），并通过独立场论二点函数论证与Mori-Zwanzig记忆模型（Mori-Zwanzig memory ansatz）补充验证临界行为。

Result: 推导出复合算子临界指数β_k = k/2和γ_k = 2-k，其中k≥2时磁化率（susceptibility）有限，k≥3时磁化率消失。得到三元伊辛模型的交叉温度T*=4(J+γw)/ln3和平均场临界点T_c=J+γw；形成关联子Ψ_form标度为(T_c-T)^{3/2}，其共轭磁化率（conjugate susceptibility）在T_c处消失。Mori-Zwanzig记忆模型给出连续可调的动力学指数。

Conclusion: 多智能体AI架构中k体自旋关联子主导的集体可观测行为会产生全新的临界现象普适类，与成对网络系统定性不同。该结果为理解高阶相互作用系统中的临界现象提供了严格的理论基础，并对设计具有特定标度行为的多智能体系统具有指导意义。

Abstract: Multi-agent AI architectures whose dominant collective observable is a $k$-body spin correlator $O_k\equiv\langleφ^k\rangle$ over a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric order parameter exhibit composite-operator criticality with effective exponents $β_k = k/2$ and $γ_k = 2-k$, thereby producing a finite susceptibility for $k\geq2$ and a vanishing susceptibility for $k\geq3$. This is a qualitative departure from all pairwise-network universality classes. We derive these results for the first non-trivial case $k=3$ as presented in COGENT$^3$ (Salazar, 2026). The formation transition of COGENT$^3$ and comparable models, under controlled universality and mean-field arguments, reduces to an exactly solvable triadic Ising model.
  The minimal triad Hamiltonian admits an exact partition function on $\{-1,+1\}^3$, with crossover temperature $T^*=4(J+γw)/\ln 3$ and mean-field critical point $T_c=J+γw$ (gradient coupling cooperatively enhancing order). The formation correlator $Ψ_{\rm form}\equiv\langleφ_iφ_jφ_k\rangle$ scales as $(T_c-T)^{3/2}$. Its conjugate susceptibility vanishes at $T_c$, confirmed by an independent field-theoretic two-point function argument. A Mori-Zwanzig memory ansatz yields a continuously tunable dynamical exponent, completing the composite-operator scaling regime.

</details>


### [7] [Dissipation Mechanisms and Dissipative Phase Transitions of two coupled Fully Connected Quantum Ising models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27072)
*Bidyut Dey,Andrea Nava,Domenico Giuliano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究一个由两个耦合的全连接量子伊辛模型（fully-connected quantum Ising models）构成的开放量子系统中的耗散相变（dissipative phase transitions），发现跳变算符（jump operators）的结构决定了系统表现出平衡态类临界行为还是真正的非平衡临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究开放量子系统中耗散过程的结构如何影响耗散相变的性质，特别是区分平衡态类（equilibrium-like）与真正非平衡（genuinely nonequilibrium）的临界行为。

Method: 采用林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master equation）描述动力学，将相干幺正演化与非相干耗散过程相结合；幺正部分在自洽平均场框架（self-consistent mean-field framework）内处理，有效作用于每个格点上两个耦合自旋的局域希尔伯特空间。分析两类本质上不同的耗散子（dissipators）：第一类中跳变算符定义在平均场哈密顿量的瞬时本征基（instantaneous eigenbasis）上并满足细致平衡条件；第二类通过局域自旋升、降算符实现。

Result: 第一类耗散情况下，参数淬火（parametric quench）导致常规弛豫，而温度淬火（temperature quench）引发动力学相变（dynamical phase transition）并呈现时间上的非解析行为；两种淬火后稳态均为类似平均场哈密顿量热吉布斯态（thermal Gibbs state）的平衡态，耗散相变临界点与平衡相变一致。第二类耗散情况下，稳态为真正非平衡态，相图显著更丰富；当系统-浴耦合足够强时，观察到重入相（reentrant phase），即对称性破缺区域被两个连续的耗散相变所包围。

Conclusion: 耗散过程的结构是控制开放量子系统中出现平衡态类临界行为与真正非平衡临界行为的关键因素。

Abstract: We study dissipative phase transitions in a system of two coupled fully-connected quantum Ising models interacting with an environment. The dynamics is governed by a Lindblad master equation combining coherent unitary evolution and incoherent dissipative processes, where the unitary part is described within a self-consistent mean-field framework effectively acting on the local Hilbert space of two coupled spins at each site.
  We analyze two fundamentally different classes of dissipators. In the first case, the jump operators are defined in the instantaneous eigenbasis of the mean-field Hamiltonian and satisfy a detailed-balance condition. In this setting, the relaxation dynamics depends strongly on the quench protocol: a parametric quench of the Hamiltonian leads to conventional relaxation, whereas a temperature quench gives rise to a dynamical phase transition characterized by nonanalytic behavior in time. Yet, in both cases, the system relaxes toward a steady state determined solely by the post-quench parameters and the bath temperature, which closely resembles a thermal Gibbs state of the mean-field Hamiltonian. As a result, the dissipative phase transition occurs at a critical point consistent with the corresponding equilibrium transition. In contrast, when the dissipators are realized via local spin raising and lowering operators, the steady state is genuinely nonequilibrium, leading to a significantly richer phase diagram. In particular, for sufficiently strong system-bath coupling, we observe a reentrant phase featuring a symmetry-broken region bounded by two continuous dissipative phase transitions.
  Our results evidence how the structure of dissipative processes controls the emergence of equilibrium-like versus genuinely nonequilibrium critical behavior in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [8] [Geometric memory in incomplete phase transitions across dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27779)
*F. Tolea,M. Tolea*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过成核-生长过程建模固态相变中的直接与逆转变，发现了一种由几何阻塞（geometric blocking）和维度性（dimensionality）控制的纯几何记忆机制，并指出二维（2D）几何下的记忆效应强于三维（3D）和三维层状（3DL）几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解释形状记忆合金（shape-memory alloys）中的热记忆效应（thermal memory effect），但更广泛地探讨一级固-固相变（first-order solid-solid transformations）中是否存在一种纯粹由几何因素驱动的记忆机制。

Method: 将直接相变建模为板状晶粒的成核-生长过程（nucleation-and-growth process），板形为正方形（2D）、立方体（3D）或正方形面层片（3DL），并自相似生长至随机最大尺寸或受已形成板片阻挡而停止。逆转变模拟为较小板片优先消失，较大板片在部分回复中保留。引入尺寸质量比（size mass ratio）作为记忆的定量描述符，并计算香农尺寸熵（Shannon size-entropy）以量化构型多样性。

Result: 记忆在所有几何中均表现稳健，但二维（2D）中的记忆效应整体强于三维（3D）或三维层状（3DL）。提供了生长快照、阻滞-再生长循环、尺寸分布及差示扫描量热法（differential scanning calorimetry, DSC）模拟结果。

Conclusion: 识别出在一级固-固相变中存在一种纯几何记忆机制，维度性和几何阻塞是控制相变记忆强度的关键因素。

Abstract: We model a direct solid-state phase transition through a nucleation-and-growth process in which plates have simple, regular shapes - squares, cubes, or square-faced lamellae - and grow homothetically (self-similarly) until they either reach a randomly assigned maximum size or are stopped by impingement with previously formed plates. The reverse transformation is represented by the preferential disappearance of smaller plates, while larger plates are retained during an incomplete reversion. A subsequent direct transformation therefore produces a modified plate-size distribution, a memory effect that forms the main focus of this study. Building upon an earlier two-dimensional (2D) formulation, we extend the model to cubes (3D) and to lamellar plates (3DL) in order to examine how dimensionality affects transformation memory. We introduce a quantitative descriptor of memory, the size mass ratio, and find that memory is robust in all geometries but overall stronger in 2D than in 3D or 3DL. We provide growth snapshots, arrest-regrowth cycles, size distributions, and differential scanning calorimetry simulations, and we compute the Shannon size-entropy to quantify configurational diversity. Although motivated by the thermal memory effect in shape-memory alloys, the model more generally identifies a purely geometric mechanism for memory in first-order solid-solid transformations, highlighting the role of dimensionality and geometric blocking in controlling the strength of transformation memory.

</details>


### [9] [Discrete Lattice Models for Interface Growth on a Complete Graph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27896)
*J. M. Marcos,J. J. Meléndez,R. Cuerno,J. J. Ruiz-Lorenzo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了完全图（complete graph）拓扑结构上的离散界面生长模型，发现受限固-固（RSOS）模型和弹道沉积（BD）模型与对应连续方程存在显著差异，其中BD模型表现出与系统大小正相关的饱和粗糙度及超快生长行为，不再属于Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在评估完全图这一常用于探索统计力学（statistical mechanics）无穷维极限的拓扑结构上，离散晶格模型在何种程度上能够再现其对应连续方程的行为。

Method: 选取属于Edwards-Wilkinson（EW）和KPZ普适类（universality class）的离散界面生长模型，将其定义在完全图上，通过粗糙度（roughness）、高度涨落（height fluctuations）、功率谱（power spectra）及双时间自相关函数（two-time autocorrelation functions）等多个观测量评估其非平凡行为。

Result: RSOS模型表现出与系统大小负相关的饱和粗糙度，与EW和KPZ方程类似；BD模型则表现出与系统大小正相关的饱和粗糙度以及额外的超快生长（ultrafast growth）阶段，使其在完全图上不属于KPZ普适类。两类离散模型的重标度高度涨落均呈现显著的左尾（left tail），表明存在滞后节点（lagging nodes）。

Conclusion: 尽管在完全图上离散模型与连续方程存在某些相似性，但在涨落和长时动力学方面出现重要差异，表明完全图上的离散KPZ模型未必属于KPZ普适类。

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of discrete interface growth models belonging to the Edwards--Wilkinson (EW) and Kardar--Parisi--Zhang (KPZ) universality classes, when defined on a complete graph, a topology commonly used to probe the infinite-dimensional limit of statistical mechanical systems. Our aim is to assess to what extent discrete lattice models reproduce the behavior of their corresponding continuum equations in this highly connected setting. After assessing the trivial behavior shown by some well known cases (like random deposition with surface relaxation or the etching model), we focus on two paradigmatic models associated with the KPZ universality class, the Restricted Solid-on-Solid (RSOS) and Ballistic Deposition (BD) models, and assess non-trivial behavior through several observables including the roughness, height fluctuations, power spectra, and two-time autocorrelation functions. Still, despite similarities with continuum equations, important differences arise in the fluctuations and long-time dynamics. In both discrete models the rescaled height fluctuations display a pronounced left tail, indicating the presence of lagging nodes. While the RSOS model exhibits a saturation roughness that decreases with system size, similarly to the EW and KPZ equations, the BD model exhibits a saturation roughness that increases with system size and an additional ultrafast growth regime, placing it outside the KPZ universality class on a complete graph.

</details>


### [10] [Order by disorder up to arbitrarily high temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28026)
*Ravish Mehta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一类定义在 $\mathbb{Z}^d$ ($d \geq 2$) 上、局域态空间为 $\mathbb{N}_0$ 的经典格点模型（lattice model），在足够高的温度下呈现出长程棋盘序（long-range checkerboard order）。这种序由纯熵机制（entropic mechanism）驱动，而非能量最小化，证明基于 Pirogov–Sinai 理论和 Peierls 界（Peierls bound）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究由纯熵驱动的有序相，特别是高温度下非能量极小构型（如棋盘构型）被统计选择的现象。该工作将 Han–Huang–Komargodski–Lucas–Popov 近期提出的幂律模型推广至更一般的一类相互作用。

Method: 论文对最近邻相互作用 $f : \mathbb{N}_0 \times \mathbb{N}_0 \to [0,\infty)$ 施加了四个结构条件（structural conditions），涵盖了幂律模型作为特例。证明采用 Pirogov–Sinai 理论（Pirogov–Sinai theory），关键步骤是建立一个 Peierls 界。

Result: 在足够高的温度下（即 $\beta \to 0$ 极限附近），模型在 $d \geq 2$ 的 $\mathbb{Z}^d$ 格点上存在长程棋盘序。该有序相不是由能量极小化选择，而是由对占据数（occupation numbers）进行部分迹（partial trace）后的熵贡献所决定。

Conclusion: 纯熵机制可以在经典格点模型中独立于能量驱动长程序，验证了高温度下非平凡有序相的存在性。该结果为一类满足特定结构条件的相互作用提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We prove that a class of classical lattice models on $\mathbb{Z}^d$ ($d \geq 2$) with on-site space $\mathbb{N}_0$ exhibits long-range checkerboard order at sufficiently high temperature. The model has a nearest-neighbour interaction $f : \mathbb{N}_0 \times \mathbb{N}_0 \to [0,\infty)$ satisfying four structural conditions, subsuming the recently introduced power-law model of Han--Huang--Komargodski--Lucas--Popov (arXiv:2503.22789) as a special case. The ordering mechanism is purely entropic: the checkerboard configurations are not energy minimisers, but are selected by the partial trace over occupation numbers in the $β\to 0$ limit. The proof uses Pirogov--Sinai theory and the key input is a Peierls bound.

</details>


### [11] [Strong Mpemba Effect Through a Reentrant Phase Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28117)
*Kristian Blom,Doron Benyamin,Uwe Thiele,Oren Raz,Aljaz Godec*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了反铁磁伊辛模型在磁场中穿过重入相变（reentrant phase transition）的温度淬火（temperature quench）过程，揭示了强正/逆姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）的出现及其与最慢弛豫模式（slowest relaxation mode）选择性激发之间的内在联系，并通过配位数调控证明了重入行为是强姆潘巴效应存在的关键条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索反铁磁伊辛模型在磁场中重入相变区域的温度淬火动力学，验证强姆潘巴效应是否存在于该体系中，并揭示其微观机制及与平衡相行为（equilibrium phase behavior）之间的关联。

Method: 采用配对近似（pair-approximation）方法，通过改变晶格配位数（coordination number）研究重入相变对不同淬火路径弛豫行为的影响，重点分析初始相（顺磁相/反铁磁相）与最慢弛豫模式之间的重叠程度。

Result: 从顺磁相（paramagnetic phase）出发的淬火与慢模的权重为零，呈现强逆姆潘巴效应；从反铁磁相（antiferromagnetic phase）出发的淬火激发了交错模（staggered mode），呈现慢弛豫尾端（slow-relaxation tail）；当配位数改变使得重入行为消失时，强姆潘巴效应也随之消失。

Conclusion: 首次在配对近似下的反铁磁伊辛模型中证实了强正/逆姆潘巴效应的存在，并建立了反常弛豫（anomalous relaxation）与平衡相行为之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We investigate temperature quenches across the reentrant phase transition of the antiferromagnetic Ising model in a magnetic field and show that the strong direct and inverse Mpemba effects arise when quenches terminate in the paramagnetic phase. These anomalous relaxation phenomena originate from the selective excitation of the slowest relaxation mode, which in the paramagnetic phase is purely staggered. Consequently, quenches starting from the paramagnetic phase have zero overlap with the slow mode and exhibit a strong (inverse) Mpemba effect. Quenches from the antiferromagnetic phase excite the staggered mode and display a slow-relaxation tail. By varying the lattice coordination number we show that the strong Mpemba effect disappears in the absence of reentrance. Our results provide the first demonstration of the strong (inverse) Mpemba effect in the antiferromagnetic Ising model based on the pair-approximation, and establish a link between anomalous relaxation and the equilibrium phase behavior.

</details>


### [12] [Domain-wall melting in all-to-all QSSEP from random-matrix theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28151)
*Denis Bernard,Lorenzo Piroli,Stefano Scopa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究全连接量子简单排斥过程（charged SYK₂模型）中畴壁的熔化动力学，利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）求解关联矩阵特征值的Jacobi过程，进而得到平均冯·诺依曼纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）和电荷完全计数统计（full-counting statistics）的精确实时演化；在热力学极限下，量子与经典完全计数统计完全一致，无有限时间修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子排斥过程（quantum simple exclusion process）中的畴壁熔化是理解非平衡量子动力学的重要问题。本文旨在利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）的谱分析结果，精确求解该过程中可观测物理量的实时动力学，并与经典排斥过程进行定量对比。

Method: 首先证明初始带电子系统对应的关联矩阵（correlation matrix）的特征值遵循Jacobi过程（Jacobi process），该过程由一组闭合的随机微分方程（stochastic differential equations）定义。利用该结果，进一步求解所有特征值矩的实时动力学。

Result: 在热力学极限下，得到了平均冯·诺依曼纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）的全显式表达式；并解析计算了电荷的完全计数统计（full-counting statistics）。关键结果是：在热力学极限下，量子与经典简单排斥过程的完全计数统计完全一致，没有任何有限时间修正。

Conclusion: 本文展示了随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）在全连接量子简单排斥过程动力学分析中的有效性；揭示了在热力学极限下量子与经典排斥过程在完全计数统计上的等价性，为理解量子-经典过渡提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the melting of a domain wall in the quantum simple exclusion process with all-to-all hoppings (a.k.a. the charged SYK$_2$ model). We show that the real-time dynamics of physical quantities of interest can be obtained exploiting spectral results in random matrix theory. We first show that the eigenvalues of the correlation matrix corresponding to the initially charged subsystem evolve according to a Jacobi process, which is defined in terms of a closed system of stochastic differential equations. In turn, this observation allows us to obtain the real-time dynamics of all the eigenvalue moments. We present two physical applications. First, we study the dynamics of the averaged von Neumann entanglement entropy, arriving at a fully explicit expression in the thermodynamic limit. Second, we compute analytically the full-counting statistics of the charge. Our formula allows us to perform a thorough comparison with the full-counting statistics of the classical simple exclusion process. Notably, we show that, in the thermodynamic limit, the quantum and classical full-counting statistics coincide, with no finite-time corrections.

</details>


### [13] [Optimal current-based sensing of phonon temperature using a finite reservoir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28155)
*Sindre Brattegard,Stephanie Matern,Mark T. Mitchison,Saulo V. Moreira*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究纳米尺度输运装置中，有限热容的电子库与声子库通过电子-声子耦合交换热量对其温度的影响，提出结合电流测量与有限库热力学框架的测温策略，并证明在长时间极限下监测系统与有限库之间交换的量子可实现最优精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实纳米尺度输运装置中，电子-声子耦合导致有限热容库之间的热交换会影响有限库的温度，但这一温度敏感性在测温（thermometry）中的应用尚未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 将电流计量技术（current metrology）与涵盖有限库（finite reservoirs）的热力学框架相结合。聚焦于一个量子点（quantum dot）与有限库耦合的实验可实现装置，在长时间极限下考虑三种策略：监测量子点与有限库间交换的量子（quanta）、测量从量子点流入无限库的总电流、以及测量量子点的占据数（occupation）。使用费舍尔信息（Fisher information）分析各策略的灵敏度。

Result: 对于大但有限的库，三种策略的费舍尔信息均通过共同因子捕捉有限库对灵敏度的贡献。长时间极限下，监测系统与有限库之间交换的量子可实现最优精度。通过调节栅极电压（gate voltage），可在每种基于电流的策略中实现最大精度。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于有限库的测温框架和电流测量策略，为纳米尺度热电输运中的温度探测提供了优化分析路径，并指出了通过调节栅极电压提升精度的可行方案。

Abstract: In realistic nanoscale transport set-ups, electron-phonon coupling leads to the exchange of heat between phonon baths and electronic reservoirs with finite heat capacities. Such exchange affects the finite reservoir's temperature. However, this sensitivity of the finite reservoir temperature to the exchange of heat with the finite reservoir has remained unexplored for thermometry. Here, we fill this gap by combining current metrology techniques with a thermodynamic framework encompassing finite reservoirs. We focus on an experimentally realizable set-up with a quantum dot coupled to a finite reservoir and consider two distinct current-based strategies in the long time limit, namely monitoring quanta exchanged between the quantum dot and finite reservoir and the measurement of the total current flowing from the quantum dot into an infinite reservoir. A third strategy involves measurements of the quantum dot occupation. For a large but finite reservoir, we show that the Fisher information for all three strategies captures the finite reservoir's contribution to sensitivity through common factors. We also demonstrate that monitoring quanta exchanged between the system and finite reservoir in the long time limit achieves optimal precision. Finally, we provide an optimization analysis that explores how maximal precision can be achieved within each of the current-based strategies by tuning the gate voltage.

</details>

Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的约100.87亿个J/ψ事例，首次观测到衰变过程J/ψ→K⁻Σ⁰Ξ⁻+c.c.，并通过分波分析发现了一个新的双奇异超子Ξ(1720)，其质量约1721.0 MeV/c²、宽度约31.3 MeV，统计显著性超过10σ，自旋宇称最可能为J^P=3/2⁺。同时测定了该衰变道的分支比为(2.68±0.04_stat.±0.17_syst.)×10⁻⁵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索J/ψ衰变中产生的奇异重子激发态，寻找新的双奇异超子（doubly-strange hyperon），以加深对强子谱和量子色动力学（QCD）非微扰区域的理解。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的(10087±44)×10⁶个J/ψ事例样本，对J/ψ→K⁻Σ⁰Ξ⁻+c.c.衰变道进行首次观测，并采用分波分析（partial wave analysis）研究其中涉及的激发态。

Result: 观测到一个新的双奇异超子Ξ(1720)，其质量为1721.0±5.2_stat.±3.4_syst. MeV/c²，宽度为31.3±18.3_stat.±15.4_syst. MeV，统计显著性超过10σ。自旋宇称假设检验表明其自旋宇称（spin-parity）倾向于J^P=3/2⁺。J/ψ→K⁻Σ⁰Ξ⁻+c.c.的分支比确定为(2.68±0.04_stat.±0.17_syst.)×10⁻⁵。

Conclusion: 首次报道了J/ψ→K⁻Σ⁰Ξ⁻+c.c.衰变的观测，发现了一个新的Ξ(1720)共振态，其自旋宇称为J^P=3/2⁺，丰富了双奇异超子谱系。

Abstract: Based on a sample of $(10087 \pm 44) \times 10^6$ $J/ψ$ events collected with the BESIII detector at BEPCII, we report the first observation of the decay $J/ψ\rightarrow K^- Σ^0 \barΞ^++c.c.$. A partial wave analysis is performed to investigate the involved excited states. In addition to the well-established $Ξ(1690)$, a new doubly-strange hyperon $Ξ(1720) $ is observed decaying to $K^- Σ^0$ with a mass of $1721.0 \pm 5.2_{\rm stat.} \pm 3.4_{\rm syst.} ~{\rm MeV}/c^2$ and a width of $31.3 \pm 18.3_{\rm stat.} \pm 15.4_{\rm syst.} ~{\rm MeV}$, with a statistical significance exceeding $10σ$. The spin-parity hypothesis testing across various quantum number configurations reveals that the spin-parity of $Ξ(1720)$ favors $J^P = {\frac{3}{2}}^+$. Furthermore, the branching fraction of $J/ψ\rightarrow K^- Σ^0 \barΞ^++c.c.$ is determined to be $(2.68 \pm 0.04_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.17_{\rm syst.}) \times 10^{-5}$.

</details>


### [15] [Improved results on Higgs boson pair production in the 4b final state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27044)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了利用CMS实验在质心能量13.6 TeV、积分亮度62 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据中，通过四底夸克（4b）末态测量希格斯玻色子对（HH）产生的研究。通过结合分辨（resolved）和融合（merged）两种拓扑分析，在95%置信水平（CL）下给出HH信号强度μ_HH的观测（预期）上限为4.4（4.4），并进一步结合13 TeV数据得到组合上限为4.7（2.8），这是目前4b末态中最严格的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯玻色子对产生是探测希格斯势能中三线性自耦合（trilinear self-coupling）等关键参数的直接途径，对检验电弱对称性破缺机制具有重要物理意义。此前LHC在4b末态中的灵敏度有限，因此需要利用更高能量和更高效的分析方法（如新触发选择和信号提取技术）来提升对HH信号的约束能力。

Method: 利用CMS探测器收集的质心能量13.6 TeV、积分亮度62 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，分别重建H→bb衰变产生的喷注，并将其分为两对小半径喷注（分辨拓扑）和单一大半径喷注（融合拓扑）两种情形进行独立分析。采用改进的触发选择、事件选择和信号提取方法，并将两种拓扑的分析结果进行统计组合；此外还引入了13 TeV数据（138 fb⁻¹）的更新分析及两个能量下数据的联合分析。

Result: 13.6 TeV数据分析得到分辨与融合拓扑组合后观测（预期）95% CL上限μ_HH=4.4（4.4）；相比此前LHC 4b末态结果，等效积分亮度下预期极限在分辨拓扑中提升超过两倍，融合拓扑亦有改善。13 TeV数据更新分析得到观测（预期）上限为10.0（5.9），预期极限改善约25%。两个能量数据组合得到观测（预期）上限为4.7（2.8），并给出了希格斯玻色子三线性自耦合及双希格斯-双矢量玻色子四线性耦合（quartic coupling）的允许范围。

Conclusion: 本文报道的结果是当前LHC在4b末态中对HH信号强度给出的最严格约束，充分体现了新分析方法带来的灵敏度提升，并为后续高统计量Run 3数据及HL-LHC时代的精确测量奠定了重要基础。

Abstract: Measurements of Higgs boson pair (HH) production in the four bottom quark (4b) final state are presented using proton-proton (pp) collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 62 fb$^{-1}$. Events in which the Higgs boson decays, H$\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$, are separately reconstructed as pairs of small-radius jets (resolved), as well as those where they are reconstructed as single large-radius jets (merged), are studied exclusively. Benefiting from new methods in trigger selection, event selection, and signal extraction, the combination of analyses in the resolved and merged topologies gives an observed (expected) upper limit on the HH signal strength, $μ_\mathrm{HH}$, of 4.4 (4.4) at 95% confidence level (CL). Compared to previously published LHC results in the 4b final state, the expected limit with an equivalent integrated luminosity is improved by more than a factor of two in the resolved topology and is better in the merged topology as well. An updated analysis of the resolved topology using 138 fb$^{-1}$ of 13 TeV pp collision data yields an observed (expected) 95% CL upper limit on $μ_\mathrm{HH}$ of 10.0 (5.9), an improvement of about 25% in the expected limit compared to the published results using the same data. Results in the 4b final state with 13 and 13.6 TeV are combined, resulting in an observed (expected) 95% CL upper limit on $μ_\mathrm{HH}$ of 4.7 (2.8). The allowed ranges for the Higgs boson trilinear self-coupling and quartic coupling between two Higgs bosons and two vector bosons are also reported. These are the most stringent constraints achieved in the 4b final state to date.

</details>


### [16] [Energy efficiency of a GPU-based computing system for High Energy Physics experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27523)
*Jiahui Zhuo,Arantza Oyanguren,Álvaro Fernández Casani,Luca Fiorini,Valerii Kholoimov*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出将能源效率（energy efficiency）作为评估高能物理（HEP）实验中基于图形处理器（GPU）的硬件平台与算法优化的新指标。针对LHCb实验的首个高级触发器（HLT1），建立了将吞吐率与GPU核心数、时钟频率、内存带宽及热设计功率等规格关联的计算模型。该模型可推广至其他HEP实验，以辅助决策并实现可持续计算生态系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（HEP）实验面临日益增长的数据处理需求，现有评估指标多侧重于性能（如吞吐率）而忽略了能耗因素。为构建可持续计算生态系统，亟需引入能源效率（energy efficiency）作为统一指标，以同时衡量硬件平台与算法优化的效率。

Method: 以LHCb实验的第一个高级触发器（HLT1）为案例，提出一种将系统吞吐率（throughput）与GPU核心数、时钟频率、内存带宽及热设计功率（thermal design power）等硬件规格相关联的能源效率计算方法。

Result: 建立了一个可量化GPU平台在HEP触发系统中能源效率的计算模型，该模型能够反映吞吐率与关键硬件参数之间的关系。

Conclusion: 所提出的能源效率指标与计算模型可扩展至其他HEP实验，为硬件选型与算法优化提供决策依据，推动可持续计算生态系统的实现。

Abstract: In this paper we introduce the energy efficiency as a new metric for evaluating both hardware platforms based on Graphic Processor Units (GPU), and algorithm optimisations at High Energy Physics (HEP) experiments. We develop a method to compute the energy efficiency for the case of the first high level trigger (HLT1) of the LHCb experiment, relating the throughput with GPU specifications such as the number of cores, clock frequency, memory bandwidth and thermal design power. The model can be extended to other HEP experiments to make decisions and reach sustainable computing ecosystems.

</details>


### [17] [Search for light charged Higgs bosons decaying to charm and strange quarks in $\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$ events in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27795)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），搜索顶夸克对产生过程中轻带电希格斯玻色子（charged Higgs boson H⁺）的信号，假设H⁺衰变为粲夸克（charm quark）和奇异夸克（strange quark），实验观测与标准模型（Standard Model）预期一致，首次在40–50 GeV质量区间给出直接上限，并在70–110 GeV区间给出迄今最严格的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找轻质量带电希格斯玻色子H⁺是超出标准模型（beyond the Standard Model）物理的关键探针，特别是在顶夸克衰变t→H⁺b过程中。本文旨在填补40–160 GeV质量区间内H⁺实验搜索的空白，尤其是40–50 GeV尚无直接限制。

Method: 利用质子-质子对撞数据（√s=13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），选取顶夸克对产生事件，其中一支顶夸克衰变为H⁺b，另一支衰变为W⁺b；H⁺→cs，W⁺→ℓν（ℓ=e, μ）。通过两束轻喷注（light jets，即未通过底夸克标记的喷注）的不变质量谱，在40–160 GeV范围内搜索共振信号。

Result: 观测到的信号产额与标准模型预期一致，未发现显著超出。在95%置信水平下，对分支比B(t→H⁺b)设定上限，范围为0.07%–1.12%，基于B(H⁺→cs)=100%的假设。这是40–50 GeV质量区间的首个直接限制，也是70–110 GeV区间迄今最严格的限制。

Conclusion: 本文在轻质量带电希格斯玻色子搜索中给出了新的实验上限，填补了低质量区域的直接搜索空白，并为未来更高能量或更高亮度下的搜索提供了参照基准。

Abstract: A search is presented for a light charged Higgs boson H$^\pm$ in top quark pair production ($\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$), where one of the top quarks decays to an H$^\pm$ and a bottom quark, while the other decays to a W$^\mp$ boson and a bottom quark. The H$^\pm$ is assumed to decay into a charm and a strange quark, whereas the W$^\mp$ boson decays into a charged lepton (electron or muon) and a neutrino. Results are reported based on proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The analysis probes H$^\pm$ masses in the range 40 to 160 GeV using the invariant mass spectrum of the two light jets, where light jets are defined as jets that do not satisfy the bottom quark tagging requirement. The observed yield is found to be consistent with standard model predictions. Upper limits are set on the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}$(t $\to$ H$^\pm$ b), with values in the range of 0.07$-$1.12% at 95% confidence level, under the assumption that $\mathcal{B}$(H$^\pm$ $\to$ cs) = 100%. These are the first direct limits on charged Higgs bosons produced in top quark decays for masses between 40 and 50 GeV, and the most stringent limits to date in the 70$-$110 GeV range.

</details>


### [18] [The DAMSA Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28133)
*Prithak Bhattarai,Andrew Brandt,Alan Bross,Bradley Brown,Samriddha Chakraborty,Haohui Che,Bhupal Dev,Bhaskar Dutta,Juan V. Estrada,Eric Garcia,Anthony Gomez,Gajendra Gurung,Brian Joshua Gomez Hernandez,Wooyoung Jang,Jay Hyun Jo,Krzysztof Jodłowski,Doojin Kim,Eunsu Kim,Hyunyong Kim,Shin Hyung Kim,Young-Kee Kim,Jing Liu,Chang-Seong Moon,Donna Naples,David Nygren,Minseok Oh,Vittorio Paolone,Hyangkyu Park,Jong-Chul Park,Nathaniel J. Pastika,Rohit Raut,Juergen Reichenbacher,Paul Rubinov,Eunsuk Seo,Veronika Shalamova,Seodong Shin,Melvin Shochet,Adrian Thompson,Yau Wah,Shawn Westerdale,Guang Yang,Un-Ki Yang,Inseok Yoon,Jaehoon Yu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: DAMSA是一种新型短基线加速器/束流倾倒实验，旨在探测暗扇区（dark sector）的短寿命信使粒子（MeV到sub-GeV能区）以及稀有标准模型信号，并通过超短基线设计克服传统束流倾倒实验对快衰变粒子的灵敏度上限。验证实验DPF（DAMSA Path-Finder）计划在SLAC的LESA装置上利用8 GeV电子束寻找衰变为双光子的轴子类粒子（axion-like particles），以验证该方案可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子物理中存在的未解问题，以及传统弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）缺乏确凿实验证据，促使研究者探索暗扇区（dark sector）的轻质量信使粒子。现有长基线束流倾倒实验对快衰变粒子存在灵敏度上限（beam-dump "ceiling"），需要超短基线设计来突破这一限制。

Method: 采用超短基线（ultra-short baseline）的束流倾倒（beam dump）产生方案，结合紧凑型探测器（compact detector），专门优化用于稀有衰变探测，同时抑制高功率质子束固有的强中子本底（neutron-induced backgrounds）。验证实验DPF以轴子类粒子（axion-like particles）衰变为双光子作为基准物理案例，在SLAC的LESA装置上使用8 GeV电子束运行。

Result: DPF概念验证实验的成功实现将确立DAMSA方法的可行性，从而开启一个广泛且强大的物理项目，用于探索短寿命新物理（short-lived new physics）以及此前不可及能区的精确标准模型过程。

Conclusion: DAMSA实验能够探测耦合微弱、在束流倾倒靶中大量产生的MeV到sub-GeV能级暗扇区信使粒子，填补了现有实验在短寿命粒子探测方面的空白。DPF验证实验的完成将为该方案提供关键可行性依据，拓展新物理探索的能区范围。

Abstract: DAMSA (DArk Messenger Searches at an Accelerator) is a novel short-baseline accelerator/beam dump experiment aimed at probing short-lived physics processes, including searches for evidence of a dark sector of particle physics and well-motivated rare Standard Model signals. Motivated by open questions in neutrino physics and the absence of conclusive evidence for conventional weakly interacting massive particles, DAMSA targets MeV-to-sub-GeV dark-sector messengers with feeble couplings that can be produced in abundance at a beam dump/target. By employing an ultra-short baseline, DAMSA is uniquely positioned to overcome the beam-dump "ceiling" that limits sensitivity to fast decaying particles in longer-baseline experiments. The conceptual design emphasizes a beam-dump production scheme combined with a compact detector optimized for rare decays while mitigating intense neutron-induced backgrounds, inherent to high-power proton beams. To validate the experimental strategy and detector technologies, the DAMSA Path-Finder (DPF) proof-of-concept experiment is also proposed, focusing on axion-like particles decaying to two photons, as the benchmark physics case and operating with 8 GeV electron beams at SLAC Linac-to-ESA (LESA) facility. Successful realization of DPF will establish the feasibility of the DAMSA approach, enabling a broad and powerful program to explore short-lived new physics and precision Standard Model processes in a previously inaccessible regime. This paper outlines the technical details of DAMSA's physics goals, key experimental challenges, and how to overcome them.

</details>

### [19] [Light-Cone Structure of Propagation of Entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27170)
*Israel Michael Sigal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 针对一类广泛的局域耦合二分体系统，证明了纠缠传播存在有效光锥（effective light-cone），从而在理想条件下为纠缠传输到远距离位置所需时间提供了严格下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子网络（quantum network）等应用中，需要将纠缠传输到远距离节点或维持远距离纠缠，因此理解纠缠传播的速度极限具有基础性和实际意义。

Method: 基于具有局域耦合（localized couplings）的二分体系统（bipartite systems），通过分析纠缠传播的动力学，严格证明了有效光锥的存在性。

Result: 得到了纠缠传播的有效光锥，并推导出在理想条件下（无损耗、无退相干）将纠缠传输到远距离位置所需时间的硬下界（hard lower bound）。

Conclusion: 该结果对图结构量子网络（graph-structured quantum network）等场景中纠缠的远程传输与维持提供了理论上的速度极限。

Abstract: For a wide class of bipartite systems with localized couplings, we establish existence of an effective light-cone for propagation of entanglement. This result yields a hard lower bound on the time it takes, under ideal conditions (no loss, no decoherence), to transport entanglement to a distant location (say, a node of a graph-structured quantum network), or to maintain it there.

</details>


### [20] [Nonadiabatic Renormalization Group for Strongly Coupled Multiscale Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27381)
*Bing Gu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非微扰的迭代抑制方案——非绝热重整化群（nonadiabatic renormalization group），用于处理强关联量子系统中的多尺度问题。该方法导出了嵌套纤维丛（nested fiber bundle）的量子几何结构，并催生了一种新型张量网络态（tensor network states），其“位点”间共享物理腿，编码超越传统矩阵乘积态（matrix product states）的量子纠缠。文中通过相互作用玻色子模型和第一性原理量子化学（ab initio quantum chemistry）中的相互作用电子问题验证了该方法的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂量子系统往往具有多尺度（multiscale）特性，且不同尺度之间存在强耦合，传统微扰方法难以有效处理。现有方法通常通过“退去”（tracing out）高能自由度来降低问题复杂度，但在强关联（strongly correlated）体系中这一途径可能失效。因此，需要发展一种非微扰（non-perturbative）的多尺度处理方法。

Method: 本文提出非绝热重整化群，其核心思路是迭代地“抑制”（suppressing）而非退去系统的高能快速自由度，从而保留体系中的关键量子关联。该方法在几何上导出嵌套纤维丛结构，每层纤维本身即为下一层的纤维丛。在此基础上，构造了一类新型张量网络态，其特点是不同“位点”之间共享物理腿（physical legs），能够编码超越传统矩阵乘积态的量子纠缠结构。

Result: 新方法在相互作用玻色子模型（interacting boson model）和第一性原理量子化学中的相互作用电子问题两类场景中得到了验证，展示了其处理不同强关联多体问题的适用性。

Conclusion: 非绝热重整化群提供了一种处理强关联量子多尺度系统的非微扰新框架，其几何结构（嵌套纤维丛）和新型张量网络态有望在更广泛的量子多体问题中发挥作用。

Abstract: Complex quantum systems are often multiscale in nature with strong interactions between different scales. We present a novel idea: iteratively suppressing, rather than tracing out, the fast, high-energy degrees of freedom in strongly correlated quantum systems with multiple energy scales in a non-perturbative way, termed nonadiabatic renormalization group. This leads to a quantum geometric structure of a nested fiber bundle, in which each fiber of a layer is itself a fiber bundle of the next layer. The nonadiabatic renormalization group brings a new type of tensor network states that shares physical legs among ''sites'' and encodes quantum entanglement beyond conventional matrix product states. We demonstrate how to apply the nonadiabatic renormalization group to different types of problems, including an interacting boson model and ab initio quantum chemistry with interacting electrons.

</details>


### [21] [Pauli equation in spaces of constant curvature and extended Nikiforov-Uvarov method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27522)
*Abdaljalel E. Alizzi,Zurab K. Silagadze*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文运用扩展的Nikiforov-Uvarov方法处理常曲率空间中含库仑势的Dirac方程的非相对论极限，发现径向方程化为Heun方程，但多项式解存在的必要条件无法满足，从而质疑该方法的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在将扩展的Nikiforov-Uvarov方法应用于常曲率空间（spaces of constant curvature）中含有库仑势（Coulomb potential）的Dirac方程（Dirac equation）的非相对论极限（non-relativistic limit），以检验该方法的适用性及其所得结果的可靠性。

Method: 采用扩展的Nikiforov-Uvarov方法（extended Nikiforov-Uvarov method）求解常曲率空间中Dirac方程在库仑势下的非相对论极限，将径向方程（radial equation）化为Heun方程（Heun equation），并通过量化条件（quantization condition）导出多项式解存在的必要条件。

Result: 量化条件给出的能谱（energy spectrum）与通过Schrödinger方程（Schrödinger equation）得到的无自旋粒子能谱几乎一致，但缺少“几何势”（geometric potential），这证实了Naive非相对论极限与Dirac方程“平方”（squaring）操作之间的非对易性（non-commutativity）。然而，多项式解存在的必要条件无法被满足，从而削弱了结果的可靠性。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，扩展的Nikiforov-Uvarov方法在处理量子力学（quantum mechanics）中的类似问题时价值有限，其可靠性存在根本性问题。

Abstract: We apply the extended Nikiforov-Uvarov method to the non-relativistic limit of the Dirac equation with a Coulomb potential in spaces of constant curvature. In this case, the radial equation reduces to the Heun equation, and the extended Nikiforov-Uvarov method easily yields a quantization condition which leads to necessary condition under which the resulting Heun equation can have polynomial solutions. The energy spectrum implied by the quantization condition is virtually identical to the spectrum of a spinless particle obtained using the Schrödinger equation, except for the absence of the ``geometric potential", confirming the non-commutativity of the naive non-relativistic limit with the ``squaring" of the Dirac equation, first discovered on curved surfaces. However, the necessary conditions for the existence of polynomial solutions cannot be met, and this fact undermines the reliability of the results obtained. This circumstance forces us to conclude that the extended Nikiforov-Uvarov method has limited, if any, value when considering similar problems in quantum mechanics.

</details>


### [22] [A No-Cloning Trade-off Between Black Hole No-Hair and Horizon Smoothness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28050)
*Sudhanva Joshi,Sunil Kumar Mishra*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，黑洞无毛定理（black hole no-hair theorem）可以从幺正性（unitarity）结合半经典假设推导出定量形式；通过迹距离（trace distance）和金刚范数（diamond norm）建立外部位可观测量与视界光滑性（horizon smoothness）之间的权衡不等式（trade-off inequality），揭示外量子毛发（exterior quantum hair）与视界光滑性在幺正演化下定量不相容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统黑洞无毛定理基于广义相对论（general relativity）的唯一性定理推导，但其量子层面的定量约束尚未明确。本文旨在从幺正性和半经典假设出发，建立无毛定理的定量形式，并探究量子毛发与视界光滑性之间的精确关系。

Method: 采用半经典黑洞框架，定义金刚范数偏差ε作为视界光滑性违反（horizon-smoothness violation）的定量度量，内禀保真度（interior fidelity, F_I）衡量下落态被保留的保真度；利用迹距离证明两个同电荷下落态对应的外部位之间的差异被2√(2ε)上界约束；通过逆推得到权衡不等式ε ≥ D_max²/8。

Result: 证明外部位最大可区分度（maximum exterior distinguishability, D_max）与视界光滑性程度之间存在定量权衡：任意预言非零外部位毛发的模型，必须在视界处以可量化的程度违反等效原理（equivalence principle）。同时指出，仅当下落系统预先存在纠缠（pre-existing entanglement）时，量子毛发才可能与幺正性和视界光滑性同时兼容。

Conclusion: 从幺正性和半经典假设导出了黑洞无毛定理的定量版本，明确了外量子毛发与视界光滑性的不相容程度，为量子引力理论中对等效原理违反的定量检验提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The black hole no-hair theorem is traditionally derived from the uniqueness theorems of general relativity. We show that a quantitative form follows from unitarity together with the standard semiclassical assumptions of horizon causality and interior accessibility. For a semiclassical black hole, we prove that the trace distance between exterior states corresponding to two same-charge infalling states is bounded by $2\sqrt{2\varepsilon}$, where $\varepsilon$ quantifies the diamond norm departure of the interior channel from a perfect isometry which is a quantitative measure of horizon-smoothness violation that upper-bounds $1 - F_I$, where $F_I$ is the interior fidelity capturing how faithfully the infalling state is retained. Inverting this relation yields a trade-off inequality, $\varepsilon \geq D_{\max}^2/8$, between the maximum exterior distinguishability $D_{\max}$ and the degree of horizon smoothness. This establishes that observable exterior quantum hair is quantitatively incompatible with exact horizon smoothness under unitary evolution: any model predicting nonzero exterior hair must violate the equivalence principle at the horizon by a quantifiable amount. Pre-existing entanglement with the infalling system is the only channel for quantum hair compatible with both unitarity and horizon smoothness.

</details>


### [23] [Long-lived local quantum coherences from hydrodynamic large deviations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27074)
*Ewan McCulloch,J. Alexander Jacoby,Sarang Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个描述电荷守恒动力学中量子相干性演化的理论框架，揭示了相干性与流体力学大偏差（低电荷熵的空穴）之间的非微扰相互作用，形成类似极化子的复合体。在一维系统中，即使处于无穷温度，相干性的寿命因与空穴结合而显著延长。利用该框架，作者论证了弱噪声极限下Ruelle-Pollicott共振谱的消失，并计算了单粒子格林函数在有无噪声情况下的时空渐近行为，其中无噪声情况下空穴-相干极化子呈现次扩散行为，并给出了相应的扩散指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子相干性在守恒动力学下的演化是量子多体物理的核心问题。现有理论难以处理相干性与流体力学大偏差（即低电荷熵的罕见空穴）之间的非微扰相互作用，这阻碍了对谱性质和Green's函数渐近行为的精确描述。

Method: 作者建立了一个理论框架来刻画不同电荷扇区（charge sectors）之间量子相干性的动力学演化；该框架捕捉了相干性与流体力学大偏差（hydrodynamic large deviations）之间的非微扰相互作用。通过随机电荷守恒电路（random charge-conserving circuits）进行微观推导，并利用张量网络（tensor-network）模拟提供数值证据。

Result: 在一维无穷温度下，相干性寿命因绑定到空穴而得到参数化增强；在弱噪声极限下，所有算子空间扇区中的谱间隙（spectral gap）非微扰地消失，表明不存在有能隙的Ruelle-Pollicott共振；在无噪声情况下，空穴-相干极化子（void-coherence polaron）呈现次扩散（subdiffusion），作者计算了其扩散指数。

Conclusion: 该框架统一描述了相干性与流体力学涨落的耦合，揭示了在电荷守恒系统中量子相干性寿命的拓扑增强机制，并对谱性质与Green's函数的渐近行为给出了非微扰的定量预测。

Abstract: We develop a framework to describe how quantum coherences between distinct charge sectors evolve under generic charge-conserving dynamics. Our framework captures the nonperturbative interactions between quantum coherences and hydrodynamic large deviations -- i.e., rare ``voids'' of low charge entropy. Conditional on surviving, the quantum coherence and its surrounding void form a collective polaron-like object. In one dimension, even at infinite temperature, we show that the lifetime of coherences is parametrically enhanced because they bind to voids. We use our framework to address two fundamental questions about generic quantum dynamics with a conserved charge. First, we argue that gapped Ruelle-Pollicott resonances are absent in the weak-noise limit, even in sectors of operator space that contain no hydrodynamic slow modes: instead, the spectral gap in all sectors vanishes nonperturbatively in the noise strength. Second, we compute the spacetime asymptotics of the dynamical single-particle Green's function, both in the weak-noise regime and in the absence of noise. In the noiseless case, we find that the void-coherence polaron undergoes subdiffusion, with an exponent we calculate. We support our general arguments with a microscopic derivation for random charge-conserving circuits, as well as numerical evidence from tensor-network simulations.

</details>


### [24] [Effective Noise Mitigation via Quantum Circuit Learning in Quantum Simulation of Integrable Spin Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27648)
*Wenlong Zhao,Yimeng Zhang,Yan Guo,Yufan Cui,Zhuohang Wang,Rui-Dong Zhu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于量子电路学习（Quantum Circuit Learning, QCL）的噪声缓解模拟策略，通过训练浅层变分电路近似深层时间演化电路，在保持守恒量和动力学的关键信息下，有效缓解近量子器件的噪声影响，且无需指数级采样开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近量子器件（near-term quantum devices）受噪声限制，深度量子电路的模拟精度严重下降，亟需一种能有效缓解噪声（noise mitigation）且不引入指数级采样开销（exponential sampling overhead）的实用策略。

Method: 基于量子电路学习（Quantum Circuit Learning, QCL），训练一个浅层变分电路（shallow variational circuit）去近似一个更深的、用于时间演化（time-evolution）的原始电路，通过学习系统的守恒荷（conserved charges）以及少量动力学信息（dynamical information）来实现近似。

Result: 在现实噪声模型（realistic noise models）下，与原始电路的含噪模拟相比，学习得到的电路在维持守恒量（conserved quantities）和动力学可观测量（dynamical observables）方面显著更接近真实值。

Conclusion: 量子电路学习（QCL）可作为一种有效的、基于物理信息（physics-informed）的误差缓解（error mitigation）策略，能够生成更短、更鲁棒的量子电路，且无需指数级采样开销。

Abstract: We propose a noise-mitigation quantum simulation strategy for near-term quantum devices based on Quantum Circuit Learning (QCL), which is in particular effective for integrable quantum spin chains. The method trains a shallow variational circuit to approximate a deeper time-evolution circuit by learning the conserved charges and only a small amount of dynamical information in the system. Under realistic noise models, the learned circuit maintains both conserved quantities and dynamical observables significantly closer to their true values than the noisy simulation of the original circuit. This demonstrates QCL as an effective, physics-informed error mitigation strategy, producing shorter, more robust circuits without exponential sampling overhead.

</details>


### [25] [Non-Local Magic Resources for Fermionic Gaussian States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27049)
*Daniele Iannotti,Beatrice Magni,Riccardo Cioli,Alioscia Hamma,Xhek Turkeshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种费米子高斯态非局部稳定子熵的闭式表达式，可在多项式时间内通过约化马约拉纳协方差矩阵的特征值计算，并应用于刻画随机态、XY模型量子临界点和非平衡量子淬火中的非局部魔法（non-local magic）行为，为大规模量子处理器的实验估计提供了可扩展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠（entanglement）和魔法（magic）是捕捉量子多体系统复杂性的基本资源，其中非局部魔法（non-local magic）分离了与纠缠内在关联的不可约非稳定子性质（irreducible nonstabilizerness），但其计算通常需要对整个希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）进行不可行的极小化，使得超过少量量子比特后难以计算。

Method: 该文为费米子高斯态（fermionic Gaussian states）在局域高斯幺正变换（local Gaussian unitaries）下的非局部稳定子熵（non-local stabilizer entropies）推导了一个闭式表达式，该表达式可直接从约化马约拉纳协方差矩阵（reduced Majorana covariance matrix）的特征值在多项式时间内计算。

Result: 在典型随机态中得到了类似佩奇曲线（Page-like curve）的精确结果，在XY模型的量子临界点（quantum critical point）处揭示了对数标度行为，并在非平衡量子淬火（out-of-equilibrium quantum quenches）中建立了魔法产生的准粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）。

Conclusion: 该结果仅依赖于两点关联函数（two-point correlation functions），因此通过费米子阴影断层扫描（fermionic shadow tomography）为在大规模量子处理器中实验估计费米子非局部魔法提供了可扩展的途径。

Abstract: Entanglement and magic are fundamental resources that capture the complexity of quantum many-body systems. Non-local magic isolates the irreducible nonstabilizerness intrinsically tied to entanglement. However, evaluating this quantity generally requires a prohibitive minimization over the full Hilbert space, making it computationally inaccessible beyond a few qubits. Here, we overcome this bottleneck by suggesting a closed-form expression for the non-local stabilizer entropies of fermionic Gaussian states over local Gaussian unitaries, which can be evaluated in polynomial time directly from the eigenvalues of the reduced Majorana covariance matrix. We apply this framework to characterize fermionic non-local magic across diverse physical regimes: we derive an exact Page-like curve for typical random states, reveal logarithmic scaling at the quantum critical point of the XY model, and establish a quasiparticle picture for magic generation during out-of-equilibrium quantum quenches. Crucially, because our result relies solely on two-point correlation functions, it provides a scalable route for the experimental estimation of fermionic non-local magic in large-scale quantum processors via fermionic shadow tomography.

</details>


### [26] [Resolving spurious topological entanglement entropy in stabilizer codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27053)
*Peilun Han,Zijian Liang,Yifei Wang,Bowen Yang,Yingfei Gu,Yu-An Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文识别了拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）中虚假贡献的微观起源，提出一种针对平移不变稳定子码（stabilizer codes）的凹型分区（concave partition）方案来计算Levin-Wen TEE，严格证明该方案不含虚假贡献，并通过双变量自行车码（bivariate bicycle codes）在二分圆柱上的研究揭示了纠缠熵对圆柱周长的敏感依赖性及拓扑任意子的受挫行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑纠缠熵（TEE）是二维有能隙物相中长程纠缠的关键诊断量，但可能受到虚假贡献（spurious contributions）的污染，导致过高估计拓扑序的总量子维度（total quantum dimension）。因此，需要识别虚假贡献的微观起源并设计无偏的TEE计算方法。

Method: 本文针对素数维量子比特（prime-dimensional qudits）的平移不变稳定子码，引入一种凹型分区（concave partition）方案来计算Levin-Wen TEE。此外，在二分圆柱上研究双变量自行车码的纠缠熵行为。

Result: 严格证明了所提出的凹型分区方案不含虚假贡献。双变量自行车码在二分圆柱上的纠缠熵对圆柱周长敏感依赖，揭示了底层任意子（anyons）的拓扑受挫（topological frustration）。

Conclusion: 凹型分区方案为稳定子码提供了一种无虚假贡献的TEE计算途径；圆柱几何中的纠缠熵行为可作为探测拓扑任意子受挫效应的有效探针。

Abstract: Topological entanglement entropy (TEE) is a key diagnostic of long-range entanglement in two-dimensional gapped phases of matter, but it can suffer from spurious contributions that overestimate the total quantum dimension of the underlying topological order. In this work, we identify the microscopic origin of spurious TEE and introduce a concave partition for computing the Levin-Wen TEE of translation-invariant stabilizer codes of prime-dimensional qudits. We rigorously prove that this prescription is free of spurious contributions. As a complementary probe, we study bivariate bicycle codes on a bipartite cylinder and show that the entanglement entropy depends sensitively on the cylinder circumference, revealing topological frustration of the underlying anyons.

</details>


### [27] [Nonlocal nonstabilizerness in free fermion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27055)
*Mario Collura,Benjamin Béri,Emanuele Tirrito*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了纯费米子高斯态的非局域魔法（nonlocal magic），推导了基于子系统协方差矩阵奇异值的纠缠谱下界，并在高斯Haar系综、Kitaev链、随机电路及XY链淬火等情境下分析了其行为与标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子魔法（quantum magic）是衡量量子态偏离稳定化（stabilizer）程度的关键资源，非局域魔法（nonlocal magic）则聚焦于双粒子态在局域基变换后的不可约非稳定化性质（irreducible nonstabilizerness）。现有研究对高斯态（Gaussian states）中非局域魔法的解析刻画尚不充分，尤其在纠缠谱与协方差矩阵奇异值之间的关系上缺乏闭式结果。

Method: 推导了纯费米子高斯态非局域魔法的闭式纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）下界，该下界由子系统限制协方差矩阵（subsystem-restricted covariance matrix）的奇异值（singular values）决定。通过模拟退火（simulated annealing）在局域高斯幺正变换（local Gaussian unitary transformations）轨道上验证结果的最优性。利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中的循环幺正系综（circular unitary ensemble）分析高斯Haar系综的平均非局域魔法及其热力学极限。

Result: 高斯Haar系综的平均非局域魔法是广延量（extensive），热力学极限由随机矩阵理论确定。Kitaev链基态中，非局域魔法在平庸相（trivial phase）和拓扑相（topological phase）深处被抑制，在临界点（critical points）附近达到峰值。随机电路中的非局域魔法呈扩散性增长（diffusive growth）。XY链的XX极限下，非局域魔法与纠缠（entanglement）出现显著分离。

Conclusion: 非局域魔法在高斯态框架下具有可解析计算的下界，其行为在相变点附近增强、在有序相中被抑制，且在某些极限下与纠缠的解耦表明二者刻画了量子态的不同资源维度。

Abstract: Nonlocal magic quantifies the irreducible nonstabilizerness of a bipartite quantum state after optimizing over local basis changes. We study nonlocal magic for pure fermionic Gaussian states, and derive a simple closed-form entanglement spectrum bound in terms of the singular values of the subsystem-restricted covariance matrix. We benchmark our result against simulated annealing over local Gaussian unitary transformations, which supports optimality along the full local Gaussian orbit. For states drawn from the Gaussian Haar ensemble, we show that the average nonlocal magic is extensive and determine its thermodynamic limit using random matrix theory for the appropriate circular unitary ensemble. We also study Gaussian ground states, focusing on the Kitaev chain, and find that nonlocal magic is suppressed deep in both trivial and topological phases and peaks near the critical points. Finally, we investigate Gaussian evolution via random circuits and in quenches with the XY chain. For random circuits, we find that nonlocal magic grows diffusively, while in the XY chain the XX limit reveals a striking separation between nonlocal magic and entanglement.

### [28] [Structure-Aware Transformers for Learning Near-Optimal Trotter Orderings with System-Size Generalization in 1D Heisenberg Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27171)
*Shamminuj Aktar,Reuben Tate,Stephan Eidenbenz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用Transformer编码器模型，基于哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）和特罗特配置（Trotter-configuration）特征，直接预测一维XXZ海森堡模型（XXZ Heisenberg Hamiltonians）的最优特罗特排序（Trotter ordering），无需在推理时计算候选排序的保真度（fidelity）。实验表明，该方法在16至20量子比特（qubits）的外推系统上达到0.00115的平均测试保真度差距，并发现当训练集包含至L=8量子比特时开始出现泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特罗特化（Trotterization）是量子计算机上模拟量子时间演化的标准方法，其中哈密顿量被拆分为局域项并按序施加；当各项不对易（non-commuting）时，排序顺序直接影响模拟的保真度（fidelity）。对于大系统，直接评估所有候选排序的保真度计算成本过高，因此需要一种高效的方法来预测最优排序。

Method: 从哈密顿量对易图（commutation graph）的着色及其群置换中，构造了24个候选排序的集合。训练一个Transformer编码器（transformer encoder），在小系统（3至14量子比特）上学习，直接从哈密顿量和特罗特配置特征预测最优候选排序，推理时不计算候选保真度。训练数据包含3至14量子比特系统，15量子比特系统留作验证。

Result: 在16至20量子比特的外推系统上，模型达到0.00115的平均测试保真度差距（相对于24个候选中的最优值）。训练规模扫描显示，当训练集包含至L=8量子比特时，泛化（generalization）开始出现（在L=9验证），且保真度差距随训练范围扩大而持续减小。

Conclusion: 这是首次将学习模型（learned model）应用于特罗特排序问题，实验结果证明了模型在外推系统上的有效性。该工作为未来基于人工智能（AI）指导的特罗特排序提供了动机，有望推广至不同哈密顿量族和系统类型。

Abstract: Trotterization is a standard approach for simulating quantum time evolution on quantum computers, where the Hamiltonian is split into local terms and each term is applied in sequence. The order of these terms affects the fidelity of the simulation when they do not commute, so the choice of ordering directly impacts the accuracy of the simulation. We study this problem for one-dimensional XXZ Heisenberg Hamiltonians using a structured set of 24 candidate orderings derived from colorings of the Hamiltonian's commutation graph and their group permutations. Finding the best candidate for large systems becomes prohibitive because fidelity evaluation is computationally expensive. In this work, we train a transformer encoder on smaller systems to predict the best candidate ordering for larger systems directly from Hamiltonian and Trotter-configuration features, without computing candidate fidelities at inference time. The model is trained on in-range systems of 3 to 14 qubits with 15-qubit systems held out for validation. Experimental results show that the model reaches a mean test fidelity gap of 0.00115 relative to the best of the 24 candidates on out-of-range systems of 16 to 20 qubits. A training-size sweep further shows that generalization emerges once training includes systems up to L=8 qubits, with validation at L=9, and the gap continues to decrease as the training range grows. To our knowledge, this is the first application of a learned model to Trotter ordering, and it motivates future work on AI-guided Trotter ordering with generalization across Hamiltonian families and system types.

### [30] [Multirate characterization of relaxation mechanisms for two nonequivalent nuclear spins 1/2 in a liquid using maximally entangled pseudo-pure quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27220)
*Georgiy Baroncha,Alexander Perepukhov,Boris V. Fine*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与理论相结合的方法，同时表征了液体分子中两个非等价核自旋（¹H 和 ¹³C）的 8 种弛豫速率，利用基于失谐 Hartmann-Hahn 双共振条件制备的最大纠缠赝纯 Bell 态（Bell PPSs）初始化非对角弛豫本征模，发现非对角弛豫部分源于极弱 J 耦合与涨落远端核自旋的非常规机制，并识别出一个仅由偶极相互作用决定的对角弛豫速率无量纲比，其值具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）中的多速率弛豫表征是一种有前景的复杂分子指纹识别方法，但现有研究通常仅获取少量弛豫速率，缺乏对多弛豫通道的全面同时测量。本研究旨在同时获取两个相邻非等价核自旋的 8 种弛豫速率，并深入理解其微观机制。

Method: 选取液体中化学交换稳定的非等价核自旋对（¹H 和 ¹³C），通过传统反转恢复（inversion recovery）和核Overhauser效应（nuclear Overhauser effect）测量部分弛豫速率；利用基于失谐Hartmann-Hahn双共振条件制备的最大纠缠赝纯Bell态（Bell PPSs）提取非常规弛豫速率，并通过无参数检验验证微观理论的一致性。

Result: 实验成功同时获取了描述该自旋对密度矩阵的 8 种弛豫速率；证明了非对角弛豫的本征模可通过Bell PPSs选择性初始化；发现非对角弛豫部分源于自旋对极弱 J 耦合与涨落远端核自旋的非常规机制；识别出一个仅由磁偶极相互作用决定的对角弛豫速率无量纲比，其普适值与实验及文献数据一致。

Conclusion: 多速率弛豫分析揭示了 NMR 弛豫中存在的非常规机制（涉及远端自旋的弱 J 耦合），并确立了一个由分子内偶极相互作用决定的对角弛豫比普适值，为复杂分子的指纹识别提供了更丰富的弛豫通道信息。

Abstract: Multirate characterization of spin responses in nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) is a promising approach to fingerprinting complex molecules in the presence of multiple relaxation mechanisms. Here we present experimental and theoretical investigations simultaneously accessing 8 relaxation rates describing the density matrix of two adjacent non-equivalent nuclear spins 1/2 ($^1$H and $^{\ 13}$C) belonging to a molecule in a liquid. The selected nuclear pair is stable with respect to chemical exchange. Some of the rates are obtained from conventional measurements of inversion recovery and nuclear Overhauser effect, while other, less conventional ones, are extracted from the relaxation initialized by the maximally entangled pseudo-pure Bell states (Bell PPSs) of the spin pair. The Bell PPSs are created using a hereby introduced method based on a detuned Hartmann-Hahn double resonance condition. Microscopic theory behind the measured relaxation rates is presented, and its consistency is demonstrated by several parameter-free tests. In particular, it is shown both theoretically and experimentally, that the eigenmodes of the off-diagonal relaxation of the two-spin density matrix can be selectively initialized using Bell PPSs. Our multirate analysis suggests that the measured off-diagonal relaxation is partly due to an unconventional mechanism arising from very weak $J$-couplings of the spin pair with fluctuating distant nuclear spins. Furthermore, we identify a dimensionless ratio of diagonal relaxation rates, which is determined exclusively by intra-pair magnetic dipolar interaction and hence possesses a universal value for a broad class of nuclear spin pairs. This value is consistent with both our experiments and other experiments reported in the literature.

### [31] [Magnonic Gottesman-Kitaev-Preskill states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27565)
*Zi-Xu Lu,Gang Liu,Matteo Fadel,Jie Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次提出在混合磁振子-量子比特系统中制备磁振子 Gottesman-Kitaev-Preskill (GKP) 态的方案，利用椭球磁性晶体的几何各向异性实现压缩，并通过腔中介的量子比特控制实现条件位移相互作用，以两轮操作和投影测量制备出三组分和四组分类 GKP 态，并展示了逻辑单量子比特门操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻色量子纠错（Bosonic quantum error correction）通过将逻辑量子比特编码在谐振子中，避免了大规模量子比特阵列的硬件开销。GKP 态因其相空间栅格结构能同时在两个共轭正交分量上抵御小位移错误，但此前尚无磁振子（magnonic）GKP 态的制备方案。

Method: 方案利用一个椭球磁性晶体（ellipsoidal magnetic crystal）通过微波腔有效耦合到超导量子比特。几何各向异性（geometric anisotropy）内禀地压缩磁振子模式，腔中介的量子比特控制实现有效的条件位移（conditional-displacement）相互作用。通过两轮条件位移相互作用和量子比特投影测量，制备出三组分和四组分类 GKP 态。

Result: 成功制备了三组分和四组分磁振子类 GKP（magnonic GKP-like）态，并实现了逻辑 Pauli、Hadamard 和相位门等单逻辑量子比特门操作，完成了近似 GKP 码的逻辑 Pauli 基。

Conclusion: 混合磁振子-量子比特系统（hybrid magnon-qubit systems）被证明是制备玻色编码态（bosonic code states）的有前景平台，可应用于磁振子容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computation）和量子传感（quantum sensing）。

Abstract: Bosonic quantum error correction encodes a logical qubit in an oscillator, avoiding the hardware overhead of large qubit arrays. Among such encodings, Gottesman-Kitaev-Preskill (GKP) states are paticularly powerful because their phase-space grid structure protects against small displacement errors simultaneously in both conjugate quadratures. Here we provide the first protocol for preparing magnonic GKP states, which involves an ellipsoidal magnetic crystal effectively coupled to a superconducting qubit via a microwave cavity. The geometric anisotropy intrinsically squeezes the magnon mode, while the cavity-mediated qubit control realizes an effective conditional-displacement interaction. We show that two rounds of a conditional-displacement interaction and a qubit projective measurement yield three- and four-component magnonic GKP-like states. We also show how to realize single logical qubit gate operations, such as Pauli, Hadamard and phase gates, completing the logical Pauli basis of the approximate GKP code. Our results establish hybrid magnon-qubit systems as a promising platform for preparing bosonic code states, with applications in magnonic fault-tolerant quantum computation and quantum sensing.

### [32] [Observation of Universal Spectral Moments and the Dynamic Dispersive-to-Proliferative Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27585)
*Jia-Xin Zhong,Chang Shu,Nan Cheng,Jee Woo Kim,Kai Zhang,Kai Sun,Yun Jing*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过声学实验证明，在非厄米（non-Hermitian）晶格中，谱矩（spectral moments）作为体态可观测量对边界几何具有鲁棒性，不受趋肤效应（skin effect）引起的谱重构影响；并发展了一种环计数理论（loop-counting theory）解释有限尺寸修正，揭示了谱矩不变性导致的从色散到增殖的体态动力学转变，挑战了PT对称性破缺必然导致动力学不稳定的传统认知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非厄米系统中，谱对边界条件高度敏感（边界敏感，boundary-sensitive），但体态物理（bulk physics）未必如此。该研究旨在寻找一种在有限非厄米晶格中对边界几何鲁棒的体态可观测量，以弥合热力学极限与有限系统之间的鸿沟。

Method: 采用统一声学平台（unified acoustic platform），结合全谱重构（full spectral reconstruction）和时域测量，对一维、二维和三维非厄米晶格进行实验探测。同时发展环计数理论，以边界缺失环（missing boundary loops）解释有限尺寸偏差，并推导标度律（scaling law）。

Result: 实验表明，在不同边界几何下谱矩几乎保持不变，而对应的复频谱（complex spectra）因趋肤效应发生显著差异。环计数理论定量捕获了有限尺寸修正，并预测了标度律，实验验证了该标度律。进一步发现，基于体态矩结构（bulk moment structure）而非谱边界敏感性，系统可呈现从色散（dispersive）到增殖（proliferative）的体态动力学转变。

Conclusion: 谱矩可作为有限非厄米物质的实用体态描述符（bulk descriptors），即使在PT对称性破缺（$\mathcal{PT}$-broken）的谱区域，局部体态动力学仍可保持稳定（色散），推翻了PT破缺必然导致指数放大和不稳定（增殖）的传统预期。该结果为在真实波动型非厄米器件中提取和控制本征体态行为开辟了新路径。

Abstract: In non-Hermitian systems, spectra can be maximally boundary-sensitive, yet bulk physics need not be. Here we experimentally show that spectral moments provide boundary-robust bulk observables in finite non-Hermitian lattices, even when the spectra undergo dramatic geometry-dependent reshaping due to the skin effect. Using a unified acoustic platform with full spectral reconstruction and time-domain access, we probe one-, two- and three-dimensional lattices and demonstrate that spectral moments remain nearly invariant across distinct boundary geometries while the corresponding complex spectra differ strongly. To connect the thermodynamic theorem to realistic finite systems, we develop a loop-counting theory that identifies the physical origin of finite-size deviations in terms of missing boundary loops, quantitatively captures the corrections, and predicts a scaling law, which we verify experimentally. Beyond acoustic spectroscopy, we reveal a counterintuitive dynamical consequence of moment invariance: a dispersive-to-proliferative bulk transition governed by bulk moment structure rather than spectral boundary sensitivity. As a result, local bulk dynamics can remain stable (dispersive) even in a $\mathcal{PT}$-broken spectral regime, challenging the conventional expectation that $\mathcal{PT}$ breaking necessarily implies feedback-induced dynamical instability (proliferation) through exponentially amplifying spectral components. These results establish spectral moments as practical bulk descriptors for finite non-Hermitian matter and open a route to extracting and controlling intrinsic bulk behavior in realistic wave-based non-Hermitian devices.

Motivation: 在传统无源（passive）系统中，观测磁振子-极化激元（magnon-polariton）系统中不同非线性吸引子（attractor）之间的受控转变通常需要强外部驱动，实验上极具挑战。本文旨在利用主动系统（active system）在低功率下实现并观测吸引子跃迁现象。

Method: 通过将自振荡微波腔（self-oscillating microwave cavity）与钇铁石榴石（YIG）球体耦合，形成主动磁振子-极化激元系统。利用反馈回路提供内部微波驱动，通过Kerr频率牵引（Kerr frequency pulling）和Suhl介导的磁振子-磁振子散射（Suhl-mediated magnon-magnon scattering）增强有效非线性。结合实验标定参数进行不动点（fixed-point, FP）稳定性分析，并通过调节增益跨越不同相区进行实验观测。

Result: 稳定性分析揭示了包含多个不稳定不动点相和三相点（triple-point）区域的丰富不动点景观。实验首次观测到双稳态（bistability）的爆炸性增长，以及随后在微瓦功率下向多频极限环（multifrequency limit cycles）、梳状/分形谱（comb-like/fractal spectra）和宽带混沌动力学（broadband chaotic dynamics）的转变。在临界点附近，磁场触发的非线性发射态开关产生了高达裸旋磁响应（bare gyromagnetic response）162倍的光谱偏移。

Conclusion: 主动磁振子-极化激元系统通过实现低功率吸引子跃迁和吸引子开关放大光谱响应，为非线性微波信号生成、高精度传感和神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Magnon-polaritons provide a room-temperature platform for investigating nonlinear cavity quantum electrodynamics in the microwave domain, but experimentally observing controlled transitions among distinct nonlinear attractors remains challenging in conventional passive systems, where strong external driving is usually required. Here we report the observation of attractor transitions in an active magnon-polariton formed by a self-oscillating microwave cavity coupled to a yttrium iron garne (YIG) sphere. The feedback loop supplies an internal microwave drive, while Kerr frequency pulling and Suhl-mediated magnon-magnon scattering produce an enhanced effective nonlinearity. Stability analysis using experimentally calibrated parameters reveals a rich fixed-point (FP) landscape with multiple unstable-FP phases and a triple-point region. By tuning gain across these phases, we observe the first experimental evidence of explosive growth of bistability, followed by transitions to multifrequency limit cycles, comb-like/fractal spectra, and broadband chaotic dynamics at microwatt powers. Near a critical point, magnetic-field-triggered switching between nonlinear emission states produces spectral shifts up to 162 times the bare gyromagnetic response. By enabling low-power attractor transitions and attractor-switching-amplified spectral response, active magnon-polaritons open opportunities for nonlinear microwave signal generation, high-precision sensing, and neuromorphic computing.

</details>


### [34] [Timescales for Deep and Full Thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27749)
*Tabea Herrmann,Felix Fritzsch,Arnd Bäcker*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟比较了本征态热化假说（ETH）的两种扩展形式——全热化（full thermalization）与深度热化（deep thermalization），发现在混沌多体量子动力学中二者均呈现指数弛豫，但深度热化中所有矩以相同速率弛豫（约等于ETH描述的自关联函数弛豫率），而全热化中高阶关联函数弛豫更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越本征态热化假说（ETH）所描述的孤立量子系统趋向热平衡的基本图景，探索两种扩展形式——深度热化（deep thermalization）与全热化（full thermalization）——之间的差异及其动力学特征。

Method: 在混沌多体量子动力学的典范模型中进行大规模数值研究（extensive numerical studies），系统比较深度热化与全热化两种扩展方案的弛豫行为。

Result: 两种扩展均呈现指数弛豫（exponential relaxation）；深度热化中所有矩（moments）以相同速率弛豫，该速率近似等于ETH所描述的自关联函数（autocorrelation function）的弛豫率；全热化中高阶关联函数（higher order correlation functions）趋于平衡的速度更快。

Conclusion: 在更高阶层次上，全热化比深度热化更快达到热平衡，表明二者在热化动力学速率上存在本质差异。

Abstract: Isolated quantum systems typically approach thermal equilibrium as described by the Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis (ETH). Going beyond this involves either higher order correlators (full thermalization) or the formation of state designs, i.e., the approach of moments of state ensembles after a projective measurement towards thermal equilibrium (deep thermalization). We compare these two extensions of ETH using extensive numerical studies within a paradigmatic model for chaotic many-body quantum dynamics. For this we find exponential relaxation for both extensions: For deep thermalization all moments relax with the same rate, which approximately equals the relaxation rate of the autocorrelation function captured by ETH. In contrast, higher order correlation functions in full thermalization approach equilibrium faster. This means that at higher orders full thermalization is faster than deep thermalization.

</details>


### [35] [Geometric complexity in thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27858)
*Tan Van Vu,Keiji Saito*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于几何复杂度（geometric complexity）推导出经典随机映射与量子通道（quantum channel）执行误差的下界，证明状态重置（state-reset）操作实现零误差需要发散几何复杂度，从而在经典与量子领域建立了热力学第三定律（third law of thermodynamics）的一种通用不可达性原理（unattainability principle）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学第三定律禁止在有限步骤中将物理系统冷却到绝对零度，但现有量化结果仅针对特定状态间转移，缺乏一种与动力学无关、适用于状态无关重置映射（state-agnostic reset map）的通用下界。

Method: 通过分析几何流形（geometric manifold）上映射的连续路径，推导出经典随机映射或量子通道的几何复杂度与执行误差（execution error）之间的权衡关系（trade-off relation）。

Result: 证明了任何经典随机映射或量子通道的几何复杂度受其执行误差下界约束；状态重置操作实现零误差要求几何复杂度发散，其中几何复杂度统一涵盖了无限时间、能量成本或控制带宽等不同物理资源。

Conclusion: 该不可达性原理在经典与量子领域均成立，为热力学控制与量子计算（quantum computation）中重置操作的物理实现建立了严格的几何极限。

Abstract: The third law of thermodynamics forbids cooling a physical system to absolute zero in a finite number of operational steps. Although this unattainability principle has been quantified for specific state-to-state transitions, a universal, dynamics-independent bound for implementing a state-agnostic reset map remains elusive. In this work, we unveil the fundamental limits of physical map implementation by deriving a trade-off relation based on geometric complexity. By analyzing continuous paths of maps on a geometric manifold, we prove that the geometric complexity of any classical stochastic map or quantum channel is bounded from below by its execution error. As a consequence, we show that achieving zero error in a state-reset operation requires a divergent geometric complexity -- a unified measure that naturally incorporates disparate physical resources, including infinite time, energetic cost, or control bandwidth. This unattainability principle holds universally across both classical and quantum regimes, establishing a strict geometric limit on the physical realization of reset operations in thermodynamic control and quantum computation.

</details>

### [36] [Geodesically Complete Curvature-Bounce Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27103)
*Damien A. Easson*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在闭合（$k=+1$）FRW宇宙学框架下，构建了一个由单一标准标量场驱动、无奇点且测地线完备的反弹+暴胀（bounce-plus-inflation）宇宙学模型。该模型无需引入奇异物质或外推的暴胀前史，反弹由正曲率而非奇异能动张量支撑，物质场全程满足平均零能量条件（ANEC），暴胀阶段的观测预测（$n_s$、$r$）符合当前宇宙微波背景约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准暴胀宇宙学通常需要假设一个不完整的暴胀阶段与更奇异的早期历史相连接，而完整宇宙学背景应避免初始奇点。作者希望利用近期关于非静态FRW宇宙学中只有正空间曲率才能实现无奇点、测地线完备且满足ANEC的结论，构建一个完全基于广义相对论（general relativity）与常规物质场的完整早期宇宙模型。

Method: 采用闭合FRW度规（$k=+1$）与单个规范标量场（canonical scalar field）加正真空偏移势作为物质源；反弹机制依赖正空间曲率而非奇异能动张量；通过直接演化闭合宇宙红外扰动（infrared perturbations），跟踪张量与标量模式在反弹和暴胀阶段的传播行为，并与标准慢滚暴胀的观测预言进行对比。

Result: 标量场全程满足零能量条件（NEC），仅违反强能量条件（SEC）；模型在反弹与暴胀阶段保持亚普朗克尺度；在$N_*=55$和$N_*=60$时给出标量谱指数$n_s$和张量标量比$r$的预测值（$n_s=0.9617,\, r=0.0045$与$n_s=0.9650,\, r=0.0037$），与当前观测约束一致；闭合宇宙红外扰动的直接演化显示张量与标量模式均能正常穿越反弹并进入暴胀期，物理曲率扰动以标准方式冻结。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了闭合FRW分支下由完备性与ANEC兼容性所选择的完整早期宇宙宇宙学的最小显式实现。它表明无需引入异常高能物理或奇异物质，仅靠正空间曲率即可在广义相对论框架内构建无奇点、测地线完备的反弹-暴胀连贯图像。

Abstract: The early universe need not be described by an incomplete inflationary phase connected to a separate, more exotic prehistory. Recent results show that, within non-static FRW cosmology, only positive spatial curvature permits a nonsingular, geodesically complete universe with ANEC-respecting matter. We construct a geodesically complete closed $k=+1$ bounce-plus-inflation cosmology in ordinary general relativity, sourced by a single canonical scalar field with a positive vacuum offset. The bounce is supported by curvature rather than exotic stress energy: the matter content satisfies the NEC throughout and violates only the strong energy condition, as in any accelerated expansion. The solved branch remains sub-Planckian and evolves onto a curvature-diluted slow-roll phase with inflationary observables consistent with current constraints. The pivot-scale predictions are $n_s=0.9617$, $r=0.0045$ at $N_*=55$ and $n_s=0.9650$, $r=0.0037$ at $N_*=60$. Direct evolution of closed-universe infrared perturbations shows regular tensor and scalar propagation through the bounce and inflationary era, with the physical curvature perturbation freezing in the standard way. This gives a minimal explicit realization of a complete early-universe cosmology in the closed FRW branch selected by completeness and ANEC compatibility.
