### [37] [A Cosmological Uncertainty Relation and Late-Universe Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27771)
*Savvas M. Koushiappas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出宇宙尺度因子（scale factor）满足一种形变对易关系（deformed commutation relation），导致宇宙大小和膨胀速率无法同时精确测量。该形变修正了弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equation），通过单一自由指数决定宇宙学行为：正指数产生晚期暗能量（dark energy），负指数实现非奇点经典反弹（non-singular classical bounce），从而统一描述暗能量和宇宙起源，无需引入新粒子或场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学模型或依赖新粒子/场来解释暗能量和宇宙奇点问题，缺乏基于量子引力（quantum gravity）的统一描述。本文旨在从量子力学对易关系的形变出发，在不引入新自由度的前提下，同时解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀和早期大爆炸奇点（Big Bang singularity）的消除。

Method: 基于尺度因子的形变对易关系（deformed commutation relation），将量子力学的不确定性原理推广到宇宙学尺度；由此推导出修正的弗里德曼方程，其中包含几何修正项。该模型仅有一个自由指数参数，其正负分别对应不同的宇宙学阶段。

Result: 当指数为正时，模型预言晚期暗能量状态方程参数 $w > -1$，可用当前及下一代巡天（survey）检验；当指数足够负时，产生非奇点经典反弹（non-singular classical bounce），消除大爆炸奇点。模型保持标度不变的原初功率谱（scale-invariant primordial power spectrum），且形变的特征尺度由宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon）而非普朗克长度（Planck length）设定。

Conclusion: 宇宙加速膨胀可能是量子引力在宇宙学视界处的宏观印记（macroscopic imprint）。该形变在晚期宇宙中具有普遍适用性，膨胀历史（expansion history）是其主要可观测特征，无需引入新粒子或场。

Abstract: We propose that the size of the universe and its rate of expansion cannot be simultaneously specified with arbitrary precision, a quantum mechanical statement encoded in a deformed commutation relation for the scale factor. The deformation modifies the Friedmann equation by adding a geometric correction to the expansion rate, and the sign and magnitude of a single free exponent determine the cosmological behavior. When the exponent is positive, the model predicts late-time dark energy with $w > -1$, testable with current and next-generation surveys. When the exponent is sufficiently negative, the same deformation produces a non-singular classical bounce that resolves the Big Bang singularity. The model introduces no new particles or fields and preserves a scale-invariant primordial power spectrum. The deformation has a natural interpretation as a horizon-scale phenomenon, with the cosmological horizon, and not the Planck length, setting its characteristic scale. The late-universe regime is then its generic application, with the expansion history as the primary observable signature. Cosmic acceleration may be the macroscopic imprint of quantum gravity at the cosmological horizon.

</details>


### [38] [Finding the one: identifying the host of compact binary mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28132)
*Alberto Salvarese,Hsin-Yu Chen,Daniel E. Holz*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出通过聚焦引力波事件定位体积内最明亮星系的方法来识别恒星质量致密双星并合的主星系，并利用这些星系的红移与引力波数据推断的亮度距离估算哈勃常数（Hubble constant）。针对三个定位良好的LVK事件（S250207bg、GW190814、S250830bp），在筛选最亮1%星系后分别仅找到1、1和4个候选星系，随机关联概率为29%-36%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找恒星质量致密双星并合（compact binary mergers）的主星系有助于研究其形成历史并测量关键宇宙学参数如哈勃常数。然而，目前除GW170817外，大部分事件缺乏电磁对应体，且LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）网络提供的定位体积较大，使得主星系识别极具挑战性。

Method: 利用星系光度（galaxy luminosity）示踪质量或恒星形成率、从而与并合宿主概率相关的特点，将分析限制在每个引力波事件定位体积内最明亮1%的星系（阈值L_th ~ 10^11 h^{-2} L_⊙），并结合星系红移与LVK观测推断的亮度距离（luminosity distance）来估算哈勃常数。

Result: 针对三个定位良好的LVK事件S250207bg、GW190814和S250830bp，分析分别只找到1、1和4个宿主候选星系，且这些星系与引力波事件无关的随机概率为29%-36%。

Conclusion: 该方法在当前事件中识别效率有限，但随LVK探测器网络灵敏度提升和定位精度改善，该策略将在未来观测运行中变得更为有效，有望对并合形成历史提供约束并测量哈勃常数。

Abstract: Finding the host galaxies of stellar-mass compact binary mergers will open a new window for studying their formation histories and measuring key cosmological parameters, such as the Hubble constant. To date, only one merger, GW170817, has had its host galaxy confidently identified through electromagnetic counterpart observations. The large localization volumes from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) network, combined with the lack of electromagnetic emission for most events, make host identification challenging. However, as the sensitivity of the gravitational-wave (GW) detector network improves, events are becoming increasingly well localized. Furthermore, galaxy luminosity traces mass or star formation rate, and thus correlates with the probability of hosting a merger. Focusing on the most luminous galaxies within the localization volumes of the best-localized GW events, we estimate the corresponding Hubble constant for each galaxy by combining its redshift with the luminosity distance inferred from LVK observations. For the well-localized LVK events \texttt{S250207bg}, \texttt{GW190814}, and \texttt{S250830bp}, we find only $1$, $1$, and $4$ galaxies, respectively, when restricting the analysis to the most luminous $1\%$ of galaxies above $L_{\rm th} \sim 10^{11} h^{-2} L_{\odot}$ in each event's localization volume and adopting a broad $H_0$ prior. The probability of these galaxies being random, and not associated with the GW events, is $29$-$36\%$ across the three events. We encourage further follow-up observations of these candidate host galaxies. We expect this approach to become increasingly powerful in future LVK observing runs, enabling constraints on merger formation histories and measurements of the Hubble constant.

</details>


### [39] [Primordial black hole dark matter from axion inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27496)
*Gabriele Franciolini,Nadir Ijaz,Marco Peloso*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文重新研究了由赝标量耦合暴胀子的U(1)规范场产生原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）的机制。通过在均匀反作用区域中使用数值计算的规范模式函数、采用最先进的PBH丰度计算并纳入密度涨落统计不确定性，作者发现即使暴胀子梯度能量密度高度次主导（仅占动能10⁻⁴–10⁻³），PBH仍可构成小行星质量范围内的全部暗物质；该过程不可避免地会产生可被LISA探测到的随机引力波背景，从而间接区分不同的密度涨落统计模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献在计算赝标量耦合规范场产生PBH时，尚未系统考虑均匀反作用区域（homogeneous backreaction regime）下数值计算的规范模式函数、最先进的PBH丰度计算方法以及密度涨落统计不确定性对结果的影响。本文旨在填补这些空白，更准确地评估该机制产生PBH并解释暗物质的能力。

Method: 研究在均匀反作用区域框架下，采用数值计算出的规范模式函数（gauge mode functions）处理规范场的动力学；使用当前最先进的PBH丰度计算方法（state-of-the-art PBH abundance calculations）；并纳入密度涨落统计不确定性（uncertainty in the statistics of δρ）对结果的影响。

Result: PBH可以在小行星质量范围（asteroidal mass range）内解释全部暗物质，即使暴胀子梯度能量密度高度次主导（仅为动能的10⁻⁴–10⁻³），这验证了反作用方案（backreaction scheme）的有效性。该机制不可避免地产生一个随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background），其振幅可被LISA探测到，并可用于间接区分不同的密度涨落统计模型。

Conclusion: 均匀反作用区域下的数值计算支持赝标量耦合规范场机制作为小行星质量范围PBH暗物质起源的可行性，同时预测了一个可被LISA检验的引力波信号，为区分不同统计模型提供了观测途径。

Abstract: We revisit the production of primordial black holes (PBHs) by a U(1) gauge field with a pseudo-scalar coupling to the inflaton. We improve upon the existing literature by working in the homogeneous backreaction regime with numerically computed gauge mode functions, adopting state-of-the-art PBH abundance calculations, and incorporating the uncertainty in the statistics of $δρ$. We find that PBHs can account for all of the dark matter in the asteroidal mass range, even when the inflaton gradient energy density is highly subdominant ($10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$ of the kinetic energy), supporting the validity of the backreaction scheme. This mechanism also unavoidably generates a stochastic gravitational wave background with an amplitude that will be measured at LISA and that will allow to indirectly discriminate between different statistics of $δρ$.

</details>

### [40] [A nanoionic diode: Equilibrium rectifying junction enabling large and stable resistance variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28029)
*Chuanlian Xiao,Joachim Maier*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种处于完全接触平衡状态的新型整流器（rectifier），即使缩小至纳米尺度并在高温或极长等待时间下也不会发生漂移。该器件基于混合导体（mixed conductors）和纳米离子（nanoionic）机制，利用TiO₂薄膜与Ru衬底界面处的"工作分担机制（job-sharing mechanism）"存储锂离子和电子，实现了电流开关比高达6-7个数量级的优异功能，并且易于制备和电化学调控特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二极管（diode）依赖冻结掺杂分布（frozen doping profiles），属于非平衡器件（non-equilibrium devices），在纳米尺度下受高温或长时间等待时会发生漂移。因此，需要开发一种处于平衡态的纳米级整流器以克服上述局限。

Method: 采用混合导体思路，使用纳米级TiO₂薄膜负载于Ru衬底上，利用界面处"工作分担机制"使Li离子存储在TiO₂侧、电子存储在Ru侧，从而实现类似肖特基二极管（Schottky diode）但掺杂剂（dopant）具备适中迁移率的整流器结构。

Result: 该纳米离子器件展现出优异的整流功能，电流开关比（on-off ratio）可超过6-7个数量级；并且具有制备简便、可通过电化学方法调控特性的额外优势。

Conclusion: 所提出的新型整流器在完全接触平衡下工作，克服了传统二极管在纳米尺度下的漂移问题，为开发稳定、可调控的纳米级电子器件提供了新方向。

Abstract: We report on a new type of rectifier which is in full contact equilibrium and thus, if down-sized to the nanoscale, shows no drift even if exposed to elevated temperatures and/or extreme waiting times. This is in contrast to existing diodes which rely on frozen doping profiles and are hence non-equilibrium devices. Our rectifiers are related to Schottky diodes but employ "dopants" whose mobilities are high enough to follow the electrical field quickly but low enough to not compete with the electrons in terms of conductivities. In order to realize such a device based on mixed conductors, we use nanosized TiO2 films on Ru as a substrate which can store Li at the interface according to a job-sharing mechanism (Li-ions on the TiO2 side, electrons on the Ru side). The excellent functionality of this nanoionic device is demonstrated (e.g., current on-off ratio can exceed 6-7 orders of magnitude) and the additional advantages stressed (such as ease of preparation and tuning the characteristics electrochemically).

</details>

### [41] [Multi-messenger emission from choked jets in collapsar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27257)
*Zegarelli Angela,Pais Matteo,Peretti Enrico,Celli Silvia*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过相对论性非电阻磁流体动力学（non-resistive magnetohydrodynamics, MHD）模拟，研究了大质量恒星死亡过程中形成的受阻喷流（choked jets）在蓝超巨星和红超巨星前身星中的等离子体物理过程，包括喷流受阻的参数空间、强激波处的带电粒子加速率与效率，以及由此产生的高能中微子和电磁暂现源的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大质量恒星死亡过程中，部分喷流未能成功逃离恒星包层（即受阻喷流），其能量耗散到增压茧（pressurized cocoon）中，可能产生相对论性外流。该过程的等离子体物理机制及其作为高能中微子和电磁暂现源（electromagnetic transients）的潜力尚不明确，有待系统研究。

Method: 采用相对论性、非电阻磁流体动力学模拟，对包含受阻喷流的塌缩大质量恒星系统进行等离子体物理研究。通过模拟界定喷流受阻的参数空间，并量化强激波（strong shocks）处带电粒子的加速率与加速效率。

Result: 明确了喷流受阻的参数空间范围；定量给出了强激波处带电粒子的加速率和加速效率；指出蓝超巨星和红超巨星前身星均为喷流受阻的有力候选天体。

Conclusion: 受阻喷流在超巨星前身星中可能有效产生高能中微子和电磁暂现源，需进一步结合观测进行验证。

Abstract: The death of massive stars produces central accreting compact objects and sometimes relativistic jets. Not all jets escape the stellar envelope: unsuccessful, or choked, jets dissipate their energy into a pressurized cocoon, which expands and may break out as a mildly relativistic outflow. We investigate the plasma physics of collapsing massive stars hosting choked jets through relativistic, non-resistive magnetohydrodynamical simulations. We delineate the parameter space for jet choking and quantify the acceleration rate and efficiency of charged particles at strong shocks, which are potential sources of high-energy neutrinos and electromagnetic transients. Our study focuses on blue and red supergiant progenitors, both promising candidates for jet choking.

### [42] [Topological and self-dual vortices in a double sigma model with Maxwell coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27021)

Method: 构建(2+1)维时空中双O(3)-西格玛模型与麦克斯韦场最小耦合（minimally coupled）的拉格朗日量；进行BPS分析推导自对偶方程；结合解析与数值方法验证涡旋解的存在性与性质。

Result: 两个西格玛场属于同一拓扑扇区（topological sector）；势能呈周期余弦形式；理论支持通量量子化（quantized flux）的磁涡旋；数值解显示场轮廓光滑、空间局域化，磁场与能量密度均正则且局域。

Conclusion: 双O(3)-西格玛模型在BPS框架下可合并为单一拓扑扇区，支持自对偶磁涡旋解，且该解在物理上具有光滑局域化与正则性特征。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a double O(3)-sigma model minimally coupled to a Maxwell field in (2+1)-dimensional spacetime and investigate the existence of self-dual magnetic vortex solutions. An analysis of the Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) property reveals that both sigma fields belong to the same topological sector and that the potential assumes a periodic cosine-like form. Furthermore, the theory supports the emergence of magnetic vortices with quantized flux, described by two nonlinear O(3)-sigma sectors that effectively combine into a single topological sector in the BPS regime. In addition, we analytically verify the consistency of the BPS structure and its asymptotic behavior. Within this framework, numerical vortex solutions confirm that the field profiles are smooth and spatially localized, with both the magnetic field and the energy density remaining regular and localized.

### [43] [Tidal Response and Thermodynamics of Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27046)
*Itamar Cohen,Dina Meylakh,Michael Smolkin,Israel Warszawiak*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从规范不变框架和黑洞热力学两个视角，重新审视了黑洞的 Love 数（Love numbers），提出了一种不依赖标准匹配流程或 Regge-Wheeler 方程的短程自由度积分方法，并揭示了 Love 数在黑洞热力学中控制极化与热力学修正的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞 Love 数的计算通常依赖标准匹配程序或 Regge-Wheeler 方程及其主场（master field），缺乏规范不变的直接导出框架；同时，Love 数在黑洞热力学中的物理角色尚未被充分阐明。本文旨在填补这两个空白。

Method: 首先，发展了一个显式规范不变（gauge-invariant）的框架，通过直接积分掉任意时空维度下静态黑洞（static black hole）的短程自由度（short-distance degrees of freedom），得到有效点粒子作用量（effective point-particle action）及相应的 Love 数，无需标准匹配程序或 Regge-Wheeler 方程。其次，通过分析 Schwarzschild 黑洞在多种外部扰动下的行为，研究 Love 数在黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）中的作用。

Result: Love 数决定了黑洞在外界扰动下的诱导极化（induced polarization），并控制了其热力学性质的主要修正（leading corrections）。

Conclusion: Love 数在黑洞热力学中具有明确的物理意义，即控制黑洞的诱导极化与热力学修正，从而建立起引力响应理论与黑洞热力学之间的桥梁。

Abstract: In this work, we revisit black hole Love numbers from two complementary perspectives. First, we develop a manifestly gauge-invariant framework that directly integrates out the short-distance degrees of freedom of a static black hole in arbitrary spacetime dimensions. This approach yields the effective point-particle action and its associated Love numbers without relying on the standard matching procedure or on the Regge-Wheeler equation and its associated master field. Second, we investigate the role of Love numbers in black hole thermodynamics by analyzing a Schwarzschild black hole subjected to various types of external perturbations. We show that Love numbers govern the induced polarization of the black hole and control the leading corrections to its thermodynamic properties, thereby clarifying their physical significance in black hole thermodynamics.

### [44] [Optimal Architecture and Fundamental Bounds in Neural Network Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27050)
*Zhengkang Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在神经网络场论（neural network field theory, NNFT）中发现了一个此前未被探索的架构自由度 $α$，该自由度在无限宽极限下保持理论不变，但显著影响有限宽关联函数计算中的误差。研究表明，$α=0$ 是最优选择，能最小化方差并消除红外敏感修正；同时指出，即使在该最优设定下，偏差与方差的相对误差仍随距离指数增长，方差从根本上限制了信噪比，类似格点场论（lattice field theory）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将场论与神经网络结合（NNFT）是新兴方向，但此前未系统研究其有限宽效应（finite-width effects）对关联函数计算精度的影响，特别是架构选择如何影响误差行为。

Method: 识别并参数化了一个架构自由度 $α$，该自由度在无限宽极限下保持理论不变，但在有限宽情形下影响关联函数计算的误差特性。针对有质量标量场（massive scalar field）进行理论分析与数值验证。

Result: $α=0$（即传播子加权的神经元动量与恒定神经元振幅）为最优选择，能最小化有限宽方差，并唯一消除相互作用理论中的红外敏感修正。即使在 $α=0$ 下，偏差与方差的相对误差在超过关联长度（correlation length）后随距离指数增长。

Conclusion: 偏差可通过外推到无限宽消除（已数值验证），方差则构成信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）的基本上限，与格点场论中的情形类似。这些结果为将 NNFT 发展为场论数值研究的实用工具指明了方向。

Abstract: Neural network field theory (NNFT) represents fields as neural networks and samples field configurations by drawing network parameters from a probability distribution. We identify a previously unexplored architectural freedom in NNFT, parameterized by $α$, that leaves the infinite-width theory invariant but dramatically affects finite-width errors in the calculation of correlation functions. For a massive scalar field, we show that $α=0$, corresponding to propagator-weighted neuron momenta and constant neuron amplitudes, is optimal: it minimizes finite-width variance and uniquely removes IR-sensitive corrections in the interacting theory. Even at $α=0$, relative errors from both bias and variance grow exponentially with distance beyond the correlation length. The bias can be removed by extrapolating to infinite width, which we demonstrate numerically, while the variance imposes a fundamental bound on the achievable signal-to-noise ratio as in lattice field theory. These results chart a path toward developing NNFT into a practical tool for the numerical study of field theories.

### [45] [A Timelike Quantum Focusing Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27054)

TL;DR: 本文提出广义复杂度（generalized complexity）概念，类似于广义熵（generalized entropy），用于描述存在不可忽略量子效应（如蒸发黑洞）情形下的全息复杂度动力学。通过引入基于复杂度的类时测地线汇量子扩张（quantum expansion），研究了类时量子聚焦猜想（timelike quantum focusing conjecture）的推论，发现对于特定类别的余维-0 场论复杂度测度，类时聚焦条件可导出基于复杂度的量子强能条件（quantum strong energy condition）以及与协变熵界（covariant entropy bound）类似的复杂度界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，在存在量子效应的全息设置（如蒸发黑洞）中，标准的复杂度概念可能不足以描述其动力学。为此，作者试图推广复杂度概念，提出一种类似于广义熵的广义复杂度，以更准确地刻画此类系统中的全息复杂度行为。

Method: 从广义复杂度概念出发，为类时测地线汇（timelike geodesic congruences）引入基于复杂度的量子扩张量，并在此基础上提出并检验类时量子聚焦猜想（timelike quantum focusing conjecture）的物理后果。

Result: 对于满足条件的余维-0（codimension-0）场论复杂度测度，类时聚焦条件可推导出两类重要结果：其一是基于复杂度的量子强能条件（quantum strong energy condition），其二是类似于协变熵界（covariant entropy bound）的复杂度界。

Conclusion: 本文展示了广义复杂度在全息复杂度动力学中的适用性，揭示了复杂度与量子能量条件之间存在深层联系，并为建立复杂度版的协变熵界提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Recent proposals suggest that a notion of generalized complexity, analogous to generalized entropy, may be necessary for understanding the dynamics of holographic complexity in settings where quantum effects are non-negligible, such as evaporating black holes. Beginning with a notion of generalized complexity, we introduce a complexity-based quantum expansion for timelike geodesic congruences, and investigate the consequence of a timelike quantum focusing conjecture. We find that for a suitable class of codimension-0 field theory complexity measures the timelike focusing condition implies a complexity-based quantum strong energy condition as well as a complexity bound which is analogous to the covariant entropy bound.

### [46] [Perturbative Coulomb branches on $\mathbb{R}^3\times S^1$: the global D-term potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27066)
*Arash Arabi Ardehali,Daniel J. Resnick*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过zeta正规化（zeta-regularization）处理Kaluza-Klein模式产生的D项耦合，得到了手性4d 𝒩=1规范理论在ℝ³×S¹上约化后3d 𝒩=2库仑支（Coulomb branch）上的微扰势能公式，填补了该领域的关键空白，并展示了数据科学技术在模空间结构分析中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆紧致化（circle compactification）下的手性超对称规范理论中，库仑支上的微扰势能公式长期缺失，已有间接方法无法提供全局视角，难以捕捉瞬子鞍点（holonomy saddles）及进行系统分析。

Method: 对Kaluza-Klein模式生成的D项耦合进行zeta正规化，推导出3d 𝒩=2库仑支上的微扰势能公式；并利用数据科学技术（如RANSAC超平面检测）对势能零点轨迹进行数值分析，从而提取模空间（moduli space）结构。

Result: 所得公式为手性理论的圆紧致化提供了库仑支的全局描述，能够识别微扰超对称真空（perturbative SUSY vacua），并复现了之前从超共形指标（superconformal index）的Cardy极限中得到的约化结果；即使在阿贝尔理论（abelian theories）中也产生了新结果。

Conclusion: 该势能公式填补了手性4d 𝒩=1理论圆约化的重要空白，为SCFT/VOA对应等方向的圆约化研究提供了ℝ³×S¹上的直接计算途径；附录还阐明了该势能与指标Cardy极限中某函数之间的关系，类比于4d 𝒩=2预势（prepotential）与Nekrasov配分函数极限的关系。

Abstract: We find the perturbative potential on the 3d $\mathcal{N}\!=\!2$ Coulomb branch arising from a chiral 4d $\mathcal{N}\!=\!1$ gauge theory on $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$, zeta-regularizing the D-term couplings generated by the Kaluza-Klein modes. This fills a significant gap in the literature on circle-compactified SUSY gauge theories. Unlike earlier indirect approaches to the circle reduction of chiral theories, our formula provides a global view of the Coulomb branch, necessary for capturing holonomy saddles and for systematic implementation. The zero locus of the potential identifies perturbative SUSY vacua, and we show how data-analysis techniques (such as RANSAC hyperplane detection) numerically extract the structure of the moduli space when this locus is extended. Our formula yields new results even in abelian theories, and offers a new perspective on several earlier observations in the context of the Cardy limit of the superconformal index. In particular, circle reductions (of interest in the SCFT/VOA correspondence) found earlier from limits of the index can now be reproduced on $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$. An appendix shows how our 3d $\mathcal{N}\!=\!2$ potential is related to a function arising in the Cardy limit of the index analogously to how the 4d $\mathcal{N}\!=\!2$ prepotential arises in a limit of the Nekrasov partition function.

</details>


### [47] [Holographic realization of higher-spin Carrollian free fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27068)
*Ethan D'Arcy,Arnaud Delfante,Stefan Fredenhagen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过全息对偶在三维渐近平直（高自旋）引力中实现了Carroll自由场结构，构造了将反德西特对角规范推广到平直时空的边界条件，揭示了渐近对称性中由Carrollian屏蔽荷生成的纯规范冗余，并建立了Carrollian Miura变换，将物理可观测量表达为天球自由标量场，从而在平直空间引力与Carrollian Coulomb气体描述之间建立了具体联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了一类将反德西特对角规范（diagonal gauge of Anti-de Sitter）推广到平直时空的边界条件；通过分析渐近对称性，将其分解为物理变换与由Carrollian屏蔽荷（Carrollian screening charges）生成的纯规范冗余；引入Carrollian Miura变换（Carrollian Miura transformations），将物理可观测量表达为天球自由标量场（celestial free scalars）。

Result: 建立了平直空间（高自旋）引力与Carrollian Coulomb气体描述之间的具体联系，实现了Carrollian自由场结构的全息体态实现。

Conclusion: 该结果为平直时空全息对偶的量子化提供了一条有前景的途径，表明渐近平直时空中的高自旋引力可以通过Carrollian场论框架进行全息描述。

Abstract: We provide a holographic bulk realization of Carrollian free-field structures arising in three-dimensional asymptotically flat (higher-spin) gravity. We construct a class of boundary conditions that generalizes the diagonal gauge of Anti-de Sitter to flat spacetimes. We show that the associated asymptotic symmetries decompose into genuine physical transformations and pure gauge redundancies, the latter being generated by Carrollian screening charges. This structure leads to a bulk-born realization of Carrollian Miura transformations, expressing physical observables in terms of celestial free scalars. Our results establish a concrete link between flat space (higher-spin) gravity and a Carrollian Coulomb gas description, thereby providing a promising route toward the quantization of flat holography.

### [48] [Oscillators from non-semisimple walled Brauer algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27087)
*Sanjaye Ramgoolam,Michał Studziński*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入受限布拉特利图（restricted Bratteli diagrams）来研究有壁布饶尔代数（walled Brauer algebras）$B_N(m,n)$在非半单（non-semisimple）区域 $N < m+n$ 中的表示维数修正，发现其生成函数由无限塔简谐振子的配分函数（partition function）控制，并讨论了在规范理论（gauge theory）和量子信息论（quantum information theory）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有壁布饶尔代数在酉群（unitary groups）$U(N)$的薛尔-外尔对偶（Schur–Weyl duality）中起核心作用，并在 AdS/CFT 对偶和量子信息论等应用中有重要意义。在稳定区域（stable regime）$N \ge m+n$ 中该代数是半单的且表示理论已清晰，但在 $N < m+n$ 的非半单区域中，张量空间上的表示具有非平凡核（non-trivial kernel），维数发生修正，需系统方法描述这些修正。

Method: 通过修改标准布拉特利图构造受限布拉特利图，利用稳定区域的表示论数据系统计算非半单区域的维数修正。特别地在 $N=m+n-l$ 且 $l$ 远小于 $m,n$ 的条件下，证明受限图具有稳定性（stability property），从而有效计数导致维数修正的路径。

Result: 在 $N=m+n-l$ 且 $l$ 较小的区域中，受限布拉特利图表现出稳定性，能有效计数维数修正路径。令人惊奇的是，这些路径的生成函数由无限塔简谐振子的配分函数所控制。

Conclusion: 该工作为规范理论中矩阵不变量（matrix invariants）的正交基构造及量子信息论的相关应用提供了理论工具，说明了非半单区域中表示维数修正的结构可被统一描述。

Abstract: The walled Brauer algebras $B_N(m,n)$ govern Schur--Weyl duality for unitary groups $U(N)$ acting on mixed tensor spaces $V_N^{\otimes m}\otimes \overline{V}_N^{\otimes n}$ and play an important role in applications ranging from AdS/CFT to quantum information theory. In the stable regime $N\ge m+n$ the algebra is semisimple and its representation theory is well understood. For $N<m+n$, however, $B_N(m,n)$ becomes non-semisimple. The representation of the algebra on tensor space has a non-trivial kernel and the corresponding quotient algebra is semisimple, with representation dimensions differing from those in the stable regime.
  We introduce \emph{restricted Bratteli diagrams}, obtained by modifying the standard Bratteli diagrams for $B_N(m,n)$. This construction provides a systematic way to use representation-theoretic data from the stable regime to compute the dimension modifications arising in the non-semisimple regime. In the regime $N=m+n-l$, with $l$ small compared to $m,n$, we show that the restricted diagrams exhibit a stability property and enable an efficient counting of the paths responsible for these dimension corrections.
  Remarkably, the resulting generating functions are governed by the partition function of an infinite tower of simple harmonic oscillators. We briefly discuss implications for the construction of orthogonal bases of matrix invariants in gauge theory and related applications in quantum information theory.

### [49] [BPS spectra of $\operatorname{tr}[Ψ^p]$ matrix models for odd $p$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27164)
*Miguel Tierz*

Conclusion: 费米子矩阵模型即使在Casimir可解性丧失后仍保持高度结构化的荷分辨谱因子化，秩回文性与模p指标分析提供了严格的解析控制。单迹矩阵模型相比N=2 SYK具有更丰富的BPS谱结构（指标超出与更宽的荷支撑），表明两者具有不同的量子引力或全息对应内涵。

We prove rank palindromicity $r_R=r_{N^2-p-R}$ from the exterior top-degree pairing; at $(5,5)$, the ten low-charge ranks and the minimal divisibility condition $(1+x)\mid\mathcal{R}_{5,5}$ determine the remaining middle rank, and direct computation confirms the full generating function. A rank-projection tower gives rigorous lower bounds on the projection-fortuitous cohomology. In matched $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK examples at $N_f=16$, the BPS count saturates the index floor, whereas the single-trace matrix model has nonzero index excess and broader charge support.

### [52] [Phase-Space Contractions of Carrollian Black-Hole Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27449)

Conclusion: 通过适当的标度变换（α+γ=1），可以在Carroll极限下获得非退化的有限热力学第一定律，其中温度趋于零而熵发散，但热力学量的组合保持有限，这为Carrollian黑洞热力学提供了自洽的相空间描述。

Abstract: We study Carrollian limits of Schwarzschild-AdS black-hole thermodynamics using covariant phase space. Allowing the cosmological constant to vary, we derive the extended Iyer-Wald identity and identify the renormalized bulk term proportional to \(δΛ\) with the generator-normalized thermodynamic volume contribution \(V_ξ\,δP\). We show that the Carroll limit contracts the full thermodynamic phase space together with the metric. For fixed Newton constant, the Lorentzian generator \(\partial_t\) collapses to a zero-norm direction as \(c\to0\), yielding a degenerate sector with vanishing Hamiltonian variation, temperature and volume. Introducing \(ξ_λ=c^{-α}\partial_t\) and \(G=c^γG_C\), we find that the extended first law scales as \(c^{1-α-γ}\), so finite phase-space contractions require \(α+γ=1\). Abstract: We consider non-equilibrium evolution of non-Gaussian fluctuations in a hydrodynamic system undergoing a boost-invariant expansion described by Bjorken flow. Abstract: We study the celestial three-gluon amplitude in a dilaton background through the Mellin-Liouville formulation proposed by Stieberger, Taylor and Zhu (STZ). This uniquely fixes the operator normalization and the parameter dictionary, and leads to a controlled expansion in the Liouville coupling $b$. Starting from the full Liouville DOZZ three-point function, we derive the leading and first subleading terms in the $b^2$ expansion. Abstract: We develop the ODE/IM correspondence for the higher-order Mathieu equation arising from the quantum Seiberg-Witten curve of the pure $SU(r+1)$ ${\cal N}=2$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory. The dependence of the moduli parameters is found to be encoded in the boundary conditions of the Y-functions at $θ\to -\infty$. Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）证明光子具有动量空间中的非平凡量子度量（quantum metric），并推导了考虑该度量后的半经典作用量与运动方程。在折射率空间变化的介质中，量子度量会在折射率的二阶导数阶数上引起光线轨迹偏移，可视为光学的非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect）；在弯曲时空下，量子度量还会在波长的非线性阶数上修正引力透镜效应，这体现了位置空间几何与动量空间几何之间的相互作用。

Motivation: 光子作为规范玻色子，其量子几何性质（尤其是量子度量）尚未得到充分研究。本文旨在揭示光子是否具有非平凡的量子度量，以及该度量如何修正光在半经典层面的运动行为。

Method: 采用路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）作为理论框架，推导包含量子度量（quantum metric）贡献的半经典作用量（semiclassical action）和运动方程（equations of motion）。

Result: 在折射率空间变化的介质中，量子度量在折射率$n(\mathbf{x})$的二阶导数阶数上引起光线轨迹偏移，类比为光学的非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect）。在弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中，量子度量在波长的非线性阶数上对引力透镜（gravitational lensing）产生修正，形成引力非线性霍尔效应（gravitational nonlinear Hall effect）。

Conclusion: 光子确实具有非平凡的动量空间量子度量，该度量在介质和引力场景中均可对光的传播产生可观测的修正效应。这些效应源于位置空间几何与动量空间几何之间的耦合，拓展了传统半经典光学的理论框架。

Abstract: Using the path-integral formalism, we show that photons possess a nontrivial quantum metric in momentum space. We derive the semiclassical action and equations of motion by taking into account the quantum metric. In media with a spatially varying refractive index $n(\mathbf{x})$, the quantum metric induces a shift in the trajectory of light at second order in derivatives of $n$, which may be regarded as a nonlinear Hall effect of light. The quantum metric also gives rise to corrections to gravitational lensing in curved spacetime at the nonlinear order in wavelength. This gravitational nonlinear Hall effect results from the interplay between the geometry of position space and that of momentum space.

</details>


### [57] [BV quantization of $φ^3$-theory on $λ$-Minkowski space: Tree-level correlation functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28114)
*Djordje Bogdanović,Marija Dimitrijević Ćirić,Stefan Djordjević,Richard J. Szabo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用 Batalin-Vilkovisky (BV) 形式论，在 λ-闵可夫斯基空间（λ-Minkowski space）上对标量场论的量子化进行综述，比较了标准量子化与编织量子化（braided quantization）两种方案在 φ³-理论中的树图级三点和四点关联函数。标准量子化基于普通 L∞-代数，而编织量子化基于编织 L∞-代数；在四点函数中，标准量子化产生两类不等价费曼图，而编织量子化仅产生一类，非对易性仅通过依赖于外部动量的整体相位因子进入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非对易几何（noncommutative geometry）背景下，需要在 λ-闵可夫斯基空间这种非对易时空上对标量场论进行量子化，并系统比较不同量子化方案（标准 BV 与编织 BV）之间的异同，特别是前者基于普通 L∞-代数而后者基于编织 L∞-代数。

Method: 采用 Batalin-Vilkovisky (BV) 形式论对 φ³-理论进行量子化，分别使用标准量子化方案（基于普通 L∞-代数）和编织量子化方案（基于编织 L∞-代数），并计算两种方案下的树图级三点和四点关联函数。

Result: 对于三点函数，两种方案均可计算树图级关联函数；对于四点函数，标准量子化导致两类不等价费曼图且具有不同的非对易贡献，而编织量子化仅产生一类费曼图，非对易性仅通过一个依赖于外部动量的整体相位因子体现。

Conclusion: 在 λ-闵可夫斯基空间上的 φ³-理论中，标准 BV 量子化与编织 BV 量子化在四点关联函数层面显示出结构性差异，编织量子化方案具有更简洁的费曼图分类，非对易效应对关联函数的修正更为统一。

Abstract: We review the quantization of scalar field theory on $λ$-Minkowski space using the Batalin--Vilkovisky (BV) formalism. We consider $φ^3$-theory in two different quantization schemes: standard and braided. While standard BV quantization is based on an ordinary $L_\infty$-algebra, braided BV quantization is based on a braided $L_\infty$-algebra. We compare the tree-level three-point and four-point correlation functions in the two approaches. For the four-point function, standard quantization leads to two inequivalent classes of diagrams with different noncommutative contributions, whereas braided quantization yields only a single class of diagrams with noncommutativity entering solely through an overall phase factor depending on the external momenta.

### [58] [Couch-Torrence conformal inversion, supersymmetry and conserved charges for D3-branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27815)
*Mohammad Akhond,Massimo Bianchi,Antonio Cristofaro,Fabio Riccioni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过 Couch-Torrence 共形反演（conformal inversion）建立了 D3-膜及其束缚态时空中 Newman-Penrose 标量荷与 Aretakis 标量荷之间的精确匹配，并利用 Type IIB 超引力的未破缺超对称性将标量（复膨胀子）荷推广到更高自旋的荷，特别是确定了无穷维渐近旋量荷并给出了反演映射。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功建立了 Newman-Penrose 标量荷与 Aretakis 标量荷之间的精确匹配；通过超对称性将复膨胀子（complex dilaton）标量荷关联到更高自旋的守恒荷；确定了与 dilatino 涨落（dilatino fluctuations）相关的无穷维渐近旋量荷，并给出了其反演映射。

Conclusion: Couch-Torrence 反演不仅能匹配标量渐近荷，还能借助超对称性扩展到更高自旋的荷，表明该映射在高维和超引力框架下具有普适性，为理解渐近对称性与视界对称性之间的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: An asymptotically flat spacetime in $D=4$ can be mapped via Couch-Torrence conformal inversion to the geometry around an extremal non-expanding and non-rotating horizon. At the linearized level, an infinite tower of conserved Newman-Penrose charges can be found at null-infinity, while infinitely many Aretakis charges are conserved in the near-horizon. Couch-Torrence inversion allows one to establish a matching between the two sets of asymptotic charges. In this work we construct the Newman-Penrose and Aretakis scalar charges in higher-dimensional geometries of D3-branes in $D=10$ and D3-brane bound states in $D=4$ and $D=5$ and establish a precise matching between them through the inversion. By exploiting the residual unbroken supersymmetry of Type IIB supergravity, we demonstrate that it is possible to relate scalar (complex dilaton) charges to higher spin charges. In particular, we determine infinite towers of conserved asymptotic spinorial charges associated with the dilatino fluctuations, and determine the map through inversion.

### [59] [Some Properties and Uses of the Species Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27835)
*Luis E. Ibáñez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文围绕“物种标度（Species Scale）”在量子引力（Quantum Gravity）中的模依赖性展开两个主题：一是证明BPS保护的R²ⁿ算符的单圈Wilson系数满足拉普拉斯型本征值方程，并指出这构成若干Swampland猜想的根源；二是利用物种标度作为紫外截断计算no-scale模的单圈势，发现势能在模空间中的“沙漠点（desert points）”处取极小值，可能实现Kähler模的稳定化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物种标度（Species Scale）是研究量子引力（Quantum Gravity）中有效场论一致性的重要概念。本文旨在揭示其模依赖性（moduli dependence）对两类问题的影响：BPS算符的量子修正与模稳定化（moduli stabilization）机制。

Method: 在第一部分，通过求解BPS保护的R²ⁿ算符的单圈Wilson系数所满足的拉普拉斯型本征值微分方程（eigenvalue differential equations）进行分析，覆盖了不同超对称（SUSY）生成元数目和维度的理论。在第二部分，以物种标度为紫外截断（UV cut-off），对GKP-like Type IIB 4d orientifolds中的no-scale模进行单圈势求和，同时计入轻模和重塔（tower）模式。

Result: 单圈Wilson系数满足形式为 $\mathcal{D}^2_{\bf {\cal M}} \mathcal{F}^{(d)}_n = η_d\, \mathcal{F}^{(d)}_n$ 的拉普拉斯型方程，这解释了Swampland距离猜想（Swampland Distance Conjecture）中的指数行为和塔标度的衰减界限。单圈势具有通用形式 $V_{1-loop}\sim g^2m_{3/2}^2M_p^2(g^{i{\bar i}}(\partial_iΛ)(\partial_{\bar i}Λ))/Λ^2$，在模空间中的“沙漠点”处存在极小值，在大模区指数衰减，中间存在一个德西特（dS）山丘。

Conclusion: 物种标度的模依赖性为Swampland猜想提供了更深层的动力学根源。导出的单圈势有望在具现象学意义的4d Type IIB orientifolds中实现部分或全部Kähler模（Kähler moduli）在沙漠点的稳定化。

Abstract: The 'Species Scale' has proved to be an important concept when studying consistent effective actions in Quantum Gravity. This is a short summary of my contribution to the Corfu Summer Institute in September 2025, in which I covered two topics, both related in different ways to the fact that the Species Scale is moduli dependent. In the first, based on work done in collaboration with C. Aoufia and A. Castellano, we show how the one-loop Wilson coefficients $\mathcal{F}_n^{(d)}$ multiplyiing BPS protected ${\cal R}^{2n}$ operators obey Laplace-like eigenvalue differential equations of the form $\mathcal{D}^2_{\bf {\cal M}} \mathcal{F}^{(d)}_n = η_d\, \mathcal{F}^{(d)}_n$. This is true both for $n=2$ with 32 and 16 SUSY generators in 10,9,8 dimensions and theories with 8 SUSY generators in 6,5,4 dimensions $(n=1)$. We argue that this fact is at the root of some Swampland conjectures put forward in the past, like bounds on the dumping rates for the tower scales and the exponential behaviour in the Swampland Distance Conjecture. For the second topic, based on work done in collaboration with G.F. Casas, we discuss the one loop potential of the no-scale moduli in GKP-like Type IIB 4d orientifolds. To compute this potential we sum both over light and heavy (tower) modes using the Species Scale as a UV cut-off. We find a generic form $V_{1-loop}\sim g^2m_{3/2}^2M_p^2(g^{i{\bar i}}(\partial_iΛ)(\partial_{\bar i}Λ))/Λ^2$, with $Λ$ the Species Scale. This has minima at the $desert$ $points$ in moduli space and exponentially decreases at large moduli, with a dS hill in between. We argue that this potential may lead to the stabilisation of some or all Kahler moduli at the desert points in 4d Type IIB orientifolds of phenomenological interest.

</details>


### [60] [Towards Systematics of Calabi-Yau Landscape for String Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28189)
*George K. Leontaris,Pramod Shukla*

TL;DR: 这篇综述探讨了卡拉比-丘三维流形（Calabi-Yau threefolds）的几何拓扑在弦现象学（string phenomenology）全局模型构建中的核心作用，特别分析了其除子（divisors）与曲线（curves）拓扑如何影响KKLT、LVS等模稳定化方案中的有效标量势，并讨论了多场通胀模型中纤维模（fibre moduli）的几何约束与耦合问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦现象学的全局模型构建中，卡拉比-丘三维流形的具体几何特征对有效理论的可实现性至关重要，但现有研究往往缺乏对几何拓扑如何影响模稳定化（moduli stabilization）及暴胀（inflation）模型的系统性分析。

Method: 采用现象学家友好（phenomenologist-friendly）的视角，系统综述了卡拉比-丘三维流形的除子和曲线拓扑在KKLT（Kachru-Kallosh-Linde-Trivedi）和LVS（Large Volume Scenario）等标准模稳定化方案中生成有效标量势（effective scalar potentials）的作用；随后针对最小LVS暴胀模型（如纤维暴胀，fibre inflation），分析了卡拉比-丘三维流形的具体几何特征带来的挑战，特别关注暴胀子场范围界限（inflaton field-range bound）问题。

Result: 指出在纤维暴胀模型中，当多个纤维模共同驱动暴胀时，可以避免单个模接近其凯勒锥边界（Kähler cone boundary），从而获得足够的e-fold数（efolds），实现成功的多场暴胀（multi-field inflation）。

Conclusion: 卡拉比-丘三维流形的几何细节对弦现象学中的模稳定化和暴胀模型构建具有决定性影响；多场方法可以有效缓解纤维暴胀中由凯勒锥边界引起的场范围限制问题。

Abstract: In this review, we discuss the relevance and impact of studying Calabi-Yau threefolds in the context of global model building in string phenomenology. First, taking a phenomenologist-friendly approach, we review how the topologies of the various divisors and curves of the compactifying CY threefolds play a crucial role for generating the various ``suitable" classes of effective scalar potentials, within the framework of the popular moduli stabilization schemes such as KKLT and LVS. Subsequently, we discuss the impact of the specifics of the CY threefold geometries in the minimal LVS inflationary models such as fibre inflation, in particular, along the challenges such as the inflaton field-range bound. In this regard, we discuss a multi-field approach in which several fibre moduli assist to drive successful inflation having a sufficient number of efolds, without getting close to their individual Kähler cone boundaries.

### [61] [Covariant Locally Localized Gravity and vDVZ Continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28194)
*Hao Geng,Moritz Merz,Lisa Randall*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明Karch-Randall膜世界理论在零引力子质量极限下，配分函数对应的是一个无质量引力子和一个解耦的大质量矢量场的理论，而非基本的Randall-Sundrum II模型，并基于完全协变描述的单圈配分函数计算给出了证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明AdS_d膜上的有质量引力子在树图（tree-level）水平上具有平滑的零质量极限，且该光滑性被推测在量子水平仍然成立。本文旨在从配分函数（partition function）层面严格验证这一极限的量子行为，并厘清极限理论的具体组成。

Method: 推导出d维引力理论的完全协变（fully covariant）描述，并在此基础上计算单圈配分函数（one-loop partition function），从而分析零质量极限下的理论结构。

Result: 零质量极限下的配分函数对应于一个无质量引力子（massless graviton）和一个解耦的大质量矢量场（massive vector field），而非基本的Randall-Sundrum II（RSII）模型。该极限理论中包含的额外矢量自由度仅与引力耦合，其余部分解耦。

Conclusion: 该结果支持了AdS_d膜上大质量引力子源自自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）的猜想，与其全息对偶（holographic dual）描述一致。此外，该结果对纠缠岛（entanglement islands）物理具有潜在重要含义。

Abstract: The Karch-Randall braneworld concerns the physics of an AdS$_{d}$ brane embedded in an ambient gravitational AdS$_{d+1}$ spacetime. The gravitational theory induced on the AdS$_{d}$ brane has a very light but massive graviton. It has been established that the zero graviton mass limit of the $d$-dimensional graviton propagator is smooth at tree-level. Furthermore, this smoothness was conjectured to persist to the quantum level. This conjecture suggests that the massive graviton on the AdS$_{d}$ brane is due to spontaneous symmetry breaking, which is consistent with its holographic dual description. In this letter, we show that the zero mass limit of the partition function is a theory of a massless graviton and a decoupled massive vector. The zero mass limit is not the basic Randall-Sundrum II model, but a theory with these additional decoupled vector degrees of freedom coupled only to gravity. The proof relies on deriving the fully covariant description of the $d$-dimensional gravity theory which enables us to compute the one-loop partition function. At the end, we comment on the implications of this result to the physics of entanglement islands.

### [62] [Ratio-Dependent Contrarian Activation in Opinion Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27226)
*Serge Galam*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Galam多数决模型（Galam Majority Model）中引入混合型反向者（mixed contrarians），其激活依赖于局部讨论组中多数/少数比例。通过解析推导出固定点、稳定性及完整二维相图，发现均匀反向者结果是其特例，并揭示了多种新的颠覆性策略以改变最终意见格局。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有意见动力学模型通常假设反向者（contrarians）行为均匀一致，未考虑反向者激活强度随局部多数/少数比例变化的情形。本文旨在引入比例依赖的混合型反向者机制，探索其对异质群体意见演化的影响。

Method: 基于Galam多数决模型，将讨论组大小限制为3，引入两类反向者：比例参数$c_{3,0}$（对应3:0配置）和$c_{2,1}$（对应2:1配置），并推导出显式更新方程（update equation）。通过解析方法求解固定点（fixed points）并分析其稳定性（stability），构建完整的二维动力学相图（two-dimensional landscape）。

Result: 当$c_{3,0} = c_{2,1} = c$时，退化为均匀反向者（uniform contrarians）的原始结果。混合反向者机制可产生两类新策略：一是确保初始支持率较高的意见获胜（majority/minority ending）；二是产生50/50的单吸引子动力学（single attractor dynamics），此时胜者随机，与初始支持率无关。

Conclusion: 混合型反向者机制显著拓展了意见动力学的可能结果，为设计破坏性干预策略（disruptive strategies）提供了更广泛的选择空间，可用于操控群体意见的最终走向。

Abstract: I study the impact of mixed contrarians on the opinion dynamics of an heterogenous population with conformists using Galam Majority Model. Activation of contrarians is a function of the ratio majority/minority in the local groups of discussion. Restricting the group size to 3, two types of contrarians are included in respective proportions $c_{3,0}$ for configurations with ratio 3 to 0 and $c_{2,1}$ for ratio 2 to 1. I then derive the explicit update Equation and obtained analytically the fixed points, their stability, and the resulting full two-dimensional landscape of the dynamics of opinion. Setting $c_{3,0} =c_{2,1} = c$ recovers the original results obtained with uniform contrarians. The findings allow for considering a wide spectrum of new disruptive strategies to secure either a majority/minority ending ensuring the opinion having the larger initial support to win, or a single attractor dynamics at fifty/fifty, which implies a random winner regardless of initial supports.

</details>

### [63] [The Hawking Singularity Theorem for Hölder Continuous Metrics with $L^p$-Bounded Curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27023)
*Michael Kunzinger,Moritz Reintjes,Roland Steinbauer,Inés Vega-González*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了洛伦兹度量在低正则性条件下的霍金奇点定理，将结果从Lipschitz正则性推广到W^{1,p}空间，并建立了相应的迈尔斯定理低正则性版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典霍金奇点定理要求度量具有较高正则性（通常至少为C^{1,1}或Lipschitz），而低正则性条件下的奇点定理尚不完整。本文旨在将霍金定理推广到W^{1,p}正则性的洛伦兹度量，其中p>2n，n为时空维度，从而突破Lipschitz正则性障碍。

Method: 采用两种技术结合：一是基于椭圆型RT方程（elliptic RT-equations）的正则化方法，将度量的正则性提升一个导数阶；二是对先前使用的流形卷积（manifold convolution）进行改进。引入一种新的涂抹化平均曲率（smeared-out notion of mean curvature），以适应正则化前后的低正则性度量与W^{2,p}超曲面。

Result: 在适当的里奇下界（lower Ricci bounds）和平均曲率上界（upper mean curvature assumptions）条件下，建立了霍金定理的两个版本：一是全局双曲版本，给出从类空柯西超曲面（spacelike Cauchy hypersurface）的时间间隔上界；二是紧致类空超曲面版本，导致类时RT-测地线不完全性（timelike RT-geodesic incompleteness）。此外，证明W^{1,p}洛伦兹度量在L^p有界曲率下是因果plain（causally plain）的，并在黎曼设定下证明了相应的迈尔斯定理（Myers's theorem）低正则性版本。

Conclusion: 成功将霍金奇点定理推广到W^{1,p}正则性的洛伦兹度量，建立了低正则性条件下的几何与因果结构描述，为广义相对论中更粗糙度量的奇点分析提供了严格的数学基础。

Abstract: We prove a low-regularity version of Hawking's singularity theorem for Lorentzian metrics in $W^{1,p}$ with Riemann curvature in $L^p$, where $p>2n$ and $n$ the dimension of spacetime. This extends previous results beyond the Lipschitz regime. Under suitable lower Ricci bounds and upper mean curvature assumptions, expressed in terms of temporal functions, we establish both the globally hyperbolic version of Hawking's theorem, in the form of an upper bound on the time separation from a spacelike Cauchy hypersurface, and the version with a compact achronal spacelike hypersurface, yielding timelike RT-geodesic incompleteness.
  The proof combines regularisations, based on the elliptic RT-equations, to raise the regularity of the metric by one derivative, with a refinement of the previously used manifold convolution. We introduce a new smeared-out notion of mean curvature adapted to the low metric regularity before, and the $W^{2,p}$-hypersurfaces arising after regularisation. As further consequences, we show that $W^{1,p}$-Lorentzian metrics with $L^p$-bounded curvature are causally plain, and we prove a corresponding low-regularity version of Myers's theorem in the Riemannian setting.

</details>


### [64] [Agnostically decoding gravitational wave model deficiencies in GWTC-3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27185)
*Guillaume Dideron,Suvodip Mukherjee,Luis Lehner*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文使用SCoRe分析流程，基于第三次引力波瞬变目录（Third Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog，GWTC-3）中信噪比最高的30个事件，搜索引力波数据中与源相关的系统性偏差，发现质量阈值假设在约2.5 M☉到60 M☉范围内被数据所排除（贝叶斯因子0.16–0.5），且额外交叉相关功率的分布与噪声统计一致（贝叶斯因子0.07）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波数据为检验致密天体并合模型提供了独特途径，特别是在强引力与高曲率区域，可能存在偏离广义相对论（General Relativity，GR）或未考虑的物理效应的微小偏差。这些偏差虽然难以建模，但有望在探测器之间以及观测事件群体中表现出相关性，因此需要一种系统性方法来搜寻这类与源相关的偏差信号。

Method: 本文应用了最近开发的SCoRe分析流程（SCoRe analysis pipeline），该流程通过聚焦探测器间的相关功率（correlated power）并联合多个事件的结果来搜寻源依赖的偏差。具体而言，研究基于GWTC-3中30个最高信噪比的事件，检验是否存在一个质量阈值（mass-scale），在该阈值上下引力波特征表现出不同的偏差模式。

Result: 设定不同的阈值质量后，贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）范围为0.16–0.5，不支持在约2.5 M☉到60 M☉之间存在任何质量阈值的假设。额外交叉相关功率（excess cross-correlated power）分布的整体贝叶斯因子为0.07，与预期的噪声统计一致。

Conclusion: 当前数据不支持在约2.5 M☉到60 M☉范围内存在一个与源相关的质量阈值，表明在该质量区间内，引力波事件的物理性质未表现出显著的二分性偏差。额外交叉相关功率的分布亦未偏离噪声预期，进一步强化了这一结论。

Abstract: Gravitational Wave (GW) data bring an exceptional avenue to test the underlying models of coalescing compact objects. In the regime of strong gravity and high curvature, they allow the exploration of minute deviations from the best-fit models, which are difficult to uncover with other observational modalities. These deviations can stem from departures from General Relativity (GR) or unaccounted astrophysical effects. They may not be explainable within the current description of GW strain data, or may simply be difficult to model. However, they are expected to be correlated between detectors and across the population of observed events. The recently developed SCoRe analysis pipeline leverages these properties by focusing on the correlated power between detectors and combining results from multiple events. In this paper, we apply the framework on the Third Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog to search for source-dependent deviations. In particular, we explore whether there is evidence for a mass-scale in the observed events, which can act like a line of demarcation in their physical properties by exhibiting a deviation that is different above and below this mass-scale. This mass scale dependency naturally arises in gravitational theories described through effective field theories, due to environmental effects or in scenarios involving exotic compact objects, where the GW signature can differ from the standard binary black holes in GR. Using the 30 highest Signal-to-Noise Ratio events in the catalog, we find Bayes factors ranging from 0.16--0.5 (depending on where the threshold mass is set), thus disfavoring the hypothesis of existence of any mass-scale between $\sim 2.5$ M$_\odot$ and $60$ M$_\odot$. We also compute the distribution of excess cross-correlated power across events and find a Bayes factor of $0.07$, which agrees with expected noise statistics.

### [65] [Bound-State Resonances of Schwarzschild-de Sitter Black Holes: Analytic Treatment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27377)
*Qi-Dong Chen,Chong-Bin Chen,Guo-Qing Huang,Fu-Wen Shu,Tieguang Zi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Mashhoon的反转势阱束缚态共振框架，解析推导了Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS)黑洞的束缚态共振特征方程及其闭合解析解。研究证明：高度激发态的无限退定域化是渐近平直Schwarzschild系统的普适特征，而SdS黑洞仅支持有限数量的束缚态共振能级，这一有限性阻止了无限退定域化，揭示了不同渐近背景下黑洞共振结构的根本差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Völkel的数值分析发现，高度激发的束缚态会迅速退定域化、变得极弱束缚且波函数对远场扰动高度敏感，这挑战了准正则模式（QNMs）作为光环区局域激发的传统解释。本文旨在从解析角度解释这一反直觉现象，并将研究从渐近平直Schwarzschild黑洞扩展至Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS)黑洞。

Method: 推导了SdS时空中激发束缚态共振的特征方程，并获得了共振能量的紧凑闭合解析表达式。通过在$Λ→0$极限下将SdS导出的谱与Schwarzschild黑洞的近期结果进行比对验证。

Result: 在$Λ→0$极限下，SdS导出的谱与Schwarzschild黑洞结果一致。解析证明高度激发共振态的快速无限退定域化是渐近平直Schwarzschild系统的普适特征。更重要的是，SdS黑洞仅支持有限数量的束缚态共振能级，与渐近平直情形下的无限谱形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: SdS黑洞共振能级的有限性意味着共振本征函数的振荡区域存在上界，从而阻止了无限退定域化。这一结果揭示了不同渐近背景（平坦vs. de Sitter）下黑洞共振结构的根本性区别。

Abstract: Inspired by Mashhoon's framework connecting black hole quasi-normal modes (QNMs) to bound-state resonances in inverted potentials, V$\ddot{\text{o}}$lkel's recent numerical analysis of asymptotically flat Schwarzschild black holes revealed a counterintuitive phenomenon: highly excited bound states rapidly delocalize, become extremely weakly bound, and exhibit wavefunctions highly sensitive to far-field perturbations. This challenges the conventional interpretation of QNMs as localized excitations of the light-ring region. To analytically explain this phenomenon and extend the investigation to Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) black holes, we derive the characteristic equation for excited bound-state resonances in SdS spacetime and obtain compact closed-form analytical expressions for their resonance energies. In the $Λ\rightarrow 0$ limit, our SdS-derived spectrum aligns perfectly with recent results for Schwarzschild black holes. We analytically demonstrate that the rapid and infinite delocalization of highly excited resonances is a universal feature of asymptotically flat Schwarzschild systems. More significantly, we prove that SdS black holes support only a finite number of bound-state resonance levels -- in sharp contrast to the infinite spectrum of the asymptotically flat case. This finiteness implies an upper bound on the oscillatory domain of the resonance eigenfunctions in SdS geometries, thereby preventing infinite delocalization and offering a fundamental distinction in the resonance structure of black holes in different asymptotic backgrounds.

Conclusion: Paneitz算符在四维标量场情形下与模拟引力理论等价，存在不稳定性问题；未来的理论构建需考虑高阶导数修正，并满足引力波观测对传播速度的限制。

Abstract: The Paneitz operator is a dimension-4 conformally invariant fourth-order differential operator that has recently attracted attention for possible cancellations of the vacuum energy. Thus, it exhibits the usual instabilities of mimetic gravity. ### [67] [Boltzmann equation in the $2{\frac12}$-post-Newtonian approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27575)
*Gilberto M. Kremer*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后牛顿近似是连接广义相对论与经典流体力学或气体动理论的重要桥梁，但已有工作多局限于较低阶近似。本文旨在将动理论方法推广至$2\frac12$后牛顿阶，以更精确地描述引力场中的相对论气体行为。

Method: 基于$2\frac12$后牛顿近似理论，将玻尔兹曼方程和麦克斯韦-尤特纳平衡分布函数展开至$1/c^7$阶，据此计算粒子四流和能量-动量张量的各分量，并推导相应的欧拉流体力学方程。

Result: 得到了$2\frac12$后牛顿近似下质量、质量-能量和动量密度的欧拉流体力学方程，并发现能量守恒定律可由总能量密度的流体力学方程导出，该方程是质量密度和质量-能量密度的流体力学方程的组合。

Conclusion: 成功将引力场中相对论气体的动理论描述扩展至$2\frac12$后牛顿阶，明确了该阶近似下各守恒律与流体力学方程之间的内在关系。

Abstract: Within the framework of the post-Newtonian $2\frac12$ approximation theory, a kinetic theory for relativistic gases in the presence of gravitational fields is developed. The Boltzmann equation and the equilibrium Maxwell-Jüttner distribution function are determined up to $1/c^7$--order, which are used to calculate the components of the particle four-flow and energy-momentum tensor and to find the Eulerian hydrodynamic equations for the mass, mass-energy, and momentum densities in the $2\frac12$--post-Newtonian approximation. The energy conservation law follows from the hydrodynamic equation for the total energy density, which is a combination of the hydrodynamic equations for the mass and the mass-energy densities.

### [68] [Constraining Dipole Radiation with Multiband Gravitational Waves from Eccentric Binary Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27734)
*Han Wang,Lijing Shao*

TL;DR: 该研究首次构建了一个同时包含轨道偏心率（eccentricity）和理论无关的偶极辐射（dipole radiation）修正的多波段贝叶斯推断（multiband Bayesian inference）管道，用于分析恒星质量双黑洞（stellar-mass binary black holes）。结果表明，偶极参数、啁啾质量（chirp mass）和偏心率之间存在强简并（degeneracy），这会显著削弱偶极约束；但对于类似GW231123的信号，结合天琴（TianQin）或LISA一年的观测与下一代地面探测器网络的先验信息，仍可将偶极参数约束至$|b|\lesssim\mathcal{O}(10^{-7})$量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首次提出了一个多波段贝叶斯推断管道，同时纳入轨道偏心率和理论无关的偶极辐射修正，用于分析恒星质量双黑洞系统。

Result: 发现了偶极参数、啁啾质量和偏心率之间存在强简并，这显著削弱了包含偏心率时的偶极约束。然而，对于一个类似GW231123的源，结合天琴或LISA一年的观测及下一代探测器网络的地面先验信息，仍可在含噪数据下将偶极参数约束至$|b|\lesssim\mathcal{O}(10^{-7})$量级。

Conclusion: 多波段双黑洞观测为检验理论无关的偶极辐射提供了一个有前景且独特的渠道，同时也突显了在未来引力精密测试（precision tests of gravity）中需要更完整的波形建模。

Abstract: Dipole-radiation-like deviations from general relativity are most prominent during the early inspiral of compact binaries, making space-ground multiband observations a potential probe of such effects. In the same regime, orbital eccentricity can leave a significant imprint on the waveform and is therefore essential for robust dipole-radiation constraints. For the first time we present a multiband Bayesian inference pipeline for stellar-mass binary black holes that simultaneously incorporates eccentricity and a theory-agnostic dipole-radiation correction. We find strong degeneracies among the dipole parameter, chirp mass, and eccentricity, which substantially weaken the inferred dipole constraints when eccentricity is included. Even so, for a GW231123-like source, one year of TianQin or LISA observation with ground-informed priors from a next-generation detector network can still constrain the dipole parameter to $|b|\lesssim\mathcal{O}(10^{-7})$ under inference with noisy data. Our results show that multiband binary black hole observations provide a promising and distinct channel for testing theory-agnostic dipole radiation, while also highlighting the need for more complete waveform modeling in future precision tests of gravity.

### [69] [Cosmological Tensions as Consistency Conditions for f(Q) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27773)
*Amare Abebe*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出宇宙学中的H₀与S₈张量应被视为全局一致性约束，构成由背景膨胀（H₀）、结构增长振幅（S₈）和增长红移依赖（增长指数γ）组成的“一致性三角”。以f(Q)引力为测试案例，通过贝叶斯和动力系统分析发现，虽然f(Q)模型能缓解个别张量，但三者同时一致的要求严重限制其参数空间，仅少数子类可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学中H₀和S₈张量已成为统计显著且鲁棒的观测矛盾，不再孤立存在。需要将这些张量重新理解为对底层宇宙学模型的全局一致性约束，而不仅仅是局部问题。

Method: 以f(Q)引力为测试案例，选取幂律、指数和对数三类最佳研究的函数族，综合运用贝叶斯分析和动力系统分析。随后简要考察体粘滞（bulk-viscous）扩展模型作为物质自由度受约束的代表性示例。

Result: f(Q)模型能缓解个别张量，但H₀、S₈和增长指数三者同时满足一致性的要求严重限制了可行参数空间。体粘滞扩展模型同样受到该一致性要求的约束。只有限制性的一小部分f(Q)子类在全局约束下仍具竞争力。

Conclusion: 宇宙学张量应被解释为全局一致性条件，而非孤立的异常。ΛCDM的可行扩展必须满足跨多探针的一致性约束。在该框架下，仅少数f(Q)子类模型保持竞争力。

These tensions are no longer isolated anomalies but increasingly appear as global consistency constraints on the underlying cosmological model, defining what we will refer to here as a \emph{consistency triangle} of background expansion ($H_0$), structure-growth amplitude ($S_8$), and the redshift-dependence of growth - summarised by the growth index $γ$, or equivalently the shape of $fσ_8(z)$. The third vertex is non-trivial because in modified-gravity scenarios with a redshift-dependent effective gravitational coupling, growth amplitude and growth shape evolve independently, breaking the rigid coupling characteristic of $Λ$CDM. In this work, we use $f(Q)$ gravity as a test case for this emerging paradigm. By drawing on a focused set of recent Bayesian and dynamical-system analyses of the three best-studied functional families - power-law, exponential, and logarithmic - we show that while $f(Q)$ models can alleviate individual tensions, the requirement of simultaneous consistency across $H_0$, $S_8$ and the growth index severely restricts the viable parameter space. A bulk-viscous extension is then briefly examined as a representative illustration of how additional matter-sector freedom is constrained by the same consistency requirement. Our reading of the current literature supports the view that cosmological tensions should be interpreted as global consistency conditions, and that viable extensions of $Λ$CDM must satisfy this multi-probe constraint \cite{CosmoVerse,DiValentino2025Corfu}. Within this framework, only a restricted subset of $f(Q)$ models remains competitive.

Abstract: In this paper, we employ the Comisso-Asenjo magnetic reconnection (MR) mechanism to investigate energy extraction from a rapidly rotating five-dimensional Kerr black hole (BH) with single- and two-rotation configurations. We analyze the efficiency, phase-space structure of accelerated and decelerated plasma energies, and the extracted power as functions of the spin parameter, reconnection location, plasma magnetization, and magnetic field orientation. We show that MR significantly enhances energy extraction from a five-dimensional BH with a single rotation and that the extraction efficiency is higher in the single rotation configuration than in the two-rotation case. We also evaluate the extraction rate and compare it with the Blandford-Znajek (BZ) mechanism, showing that the extracted power can exceed that of the BZ process in the single-rotation configuration. Our analysis shows that MR can significantly improve energy extraction in five-dimensional Kerr BHs with a single rotation, making them promising candidates for powering high-energy astrophysical phenomena.

### [71] [Spin-Induced Nonlinear Scalarization of Kerr Black Holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27811)
*Meng-Yun Lai,Hyat Huang,Jutta Kunz,Yun Soo Myung,De-Cheng Zou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注线性标量化机制，而对纯粹非线性标量化（nonlinear scalarization）的理解尚不充分。本文旨在探讨在没有线性快子不稳定性时，非线性标量化能否在克尔黑洞中发生，以及其动力学和稳态解的相空间结构。

Method: 首先在固定克尔背景上分析解耦标量场动力学（decoupled scalar dynamics），研究高斯-博内不变量随自旋的变化。然后通过完全考虑反作用的数值方法构造稳态标量化黑洞解，并确定其在自旋-质量平面上的存在区域。

Result: 足够快的旋转（阈值χ=0.5）使高斯-博内不变量在极点附近出现负的近水平区域，从而提供非线性标量增长的几何俘获机制。稳态解在自旋-质量平面上占据一个有限的高自旋低质量楔形区域（wedge）；在高自旋端标量毛（scalar hair）增强并趋近近极端（near-extremal）区域，在低自旋边界（χ→0.5）标量场被强烈抑制并趋近弱毛极限（weak-hair limit）。

Conclusion: 在无线性不稳定性的EsGB模型中，克尔黑洞可以通过纯非线性机制发生标量化，其解的空间结构是一个高自旋低质量楔形区域，与传统的线性自旋诱导自发标量化行为显著不同。

Abstract: We investigate spin-induced scalarization of Kerr black holes in an Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet (EsGB) model that does not admit a linear tachyonic instability of the scalar-free solution. The scalarization mechanism is therefore genuinely nonlinear. We first analyze the decoupled scalar dynamics on fixed Kerr backgrounds and show that sufficiently rapid rotation modifies the Gauss-Bonnet invariant such that a negative near-horizon region develops near the poles. This region provides a geometric trapping mechanism for nonlinear scalar growth, which becomes effective above a threshold spin $χ=0.5$. We then construct stationary scalarized black hole solutions with full backreaction and determine their domain of existence. We find that the solutions occupy a finite low-mass high-spin wedge in the spin-mass plane. This is in contrast to spin-induced spontaneous scalarization, where the scalarized solutions form a narrow band. In this wedge, toward the high-spin end, the scalar hair becomes stronger, and the solutions approach a near-extremal regime, while toward the low-spin boundary, the scalar field is strongly suppressed and approaches a weak-hair limit as $χ\to 0.5$.

</details>


### [72] [Regular ultracompact objects with anti-de Sitter cores as polymerized vacuum solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27880)
*Hongguang Liu,Ioannis Soranidis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）的启发，系统推导了一类通过反德西特核（anti-de Sitter core）实现正则化的规则黑洞解（regular black hole solutions）及其无视界对应体。这些几何构型通过聚合化真空解（polymerized vacuum solutions）得到，利用辅助尘埃场（dust field）作为参考时钟，结合球对称系统的超局域性（ultralocality），推导出静态真空度规函数的普适表达式，并构建了四维协变完备化拉格朗日量，表明其属于广义扩展模仿引力（generalized extended mimetic gravity）模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）为量子引力效应提供了一种可能的正则化机制，但如何系统性地构造规则黑洞解并理解其与有效截断（effective truncations）的关系仍是一个开放问题。本文旨在建立一种系统性的推导框架，以生成具有反德西特核（anti-de Sitter core）的规则黑洞几何及其无奇点对应体。

Method: 利用辅助的相对论尘埃场（dust clock）作为解参量化（deparameterization）的参考时钟，结合球对称系统中引力波缺失所导致的超局域性（ultralocality），将动力学分解为独立的壳层自由度（shell degrees of freedom）。在Lemaitre-Tolman-Bondi壳哈密顿量（shell Hamiltonian）的因子化形式约束下，推导出静态真空度规函数的普适表达式。通过有限阶有效截断（finite-order effective truncations）分析反弹（bounce）的编码机制，并在一般情形下推导显式物理哈密顿量，最后构造四维协变完备化拉格朗日量。

Result: 该框架生成的规则黑洞解由其质量唯一确定，并满足Birkhoff型定理（Birkhoff-type theorem）。尘埃场仅作为参考时钟，不源化所考虑的真空几何。反弹（bounce）的存在性信息可能被有限阶有效截断所遗漏。四维协变完备化拉格朗日量属于广义扩展模仿引力（generalized extended mimetic gravity）模型类。

Conclusion: 本文提供了从圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）启发式聚合化真空解到规则黑洞几何的系统性推导路径，澄清了有效截断（effective truncations）对反弹（bounce）特征捕捉的局限性，并将所得模型纳入广义扩展模仿引力（generalized extended mimetic gravity）的理论框架中。

Abstract: We present a systematic derivation of regular black hole solutions - and their horizonless counterparts - that achieve regularization via an anti-de Sitter core. These geometries emerge as polymerized vacuum solutions inspired by loop quantum gravity, constituting effective quantum gravity configurations that admit a Birkhoff-type theorem and are uniquely determined by their mass. Using an auxiliary relational dust clock, together with the absence of gravitational waves in spherical symmetry, we exploit the structural ultralocality of the system to decompose the dynamics into independent shell degrees of freedom. The dust field acts as a reference clock for deparameterization and does not source the vacuum geometries considered here. These assumptions tightly constrain the Lemaitre-Tolman-Bondi shell Hamiltonian to a factorized form and the static vacuum metric function to a universal expression. We examine the possibility of a bounce and analyze how its presence is encoded, or missed, in finite-order effective truncations of the full model. The procedure for deriving the explicit physical Hamiltonian is described for a generic case before specializing to a specific model of interest. Finally, we construct a four-dimensional covariant completion of the spatially covariant Lagrangian, showing that it belongs to the class of generalized extended mimetic gravity models.

</details>


### [73] [Probing mass inflation in polymerized vacuum regular black holes via colliding null shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27897)
*Hongguang Liu,Ioannis Soranidis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了一类具有退化内视界的内极端正则黑洞解，这些解源于圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）的聚合化（polymerized）真空构型。研究表明，该类内极端视界仅存在于理论参数确定的精细调谐质量值下。基于此构造及相应的非退化正则黑洞解，文章利用内视界附近的碰撞零壳（null-shell）设置，对四维时空中的质量膨胀（mass inflation）现象进行了通用分析，识别了质量膨胀显著化的条件，并考察了最小长度尺度（minimal length scale）对该行为的影响，最后评论了上述构型在零壳扰动下的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典广义相对论中的黑洞解存在奇点和内视界不稳定性等问题，圈量子引力等量子引力理论期望提供正则化修正。本文旨在推导内极端正则黑洞解，并系统分析这类量子引力修正构型中的质量膨胀现象及其稳定性。

Method: 利用圈量子引力启发的聚合化方法构造内极端正则黑洞解，并证明该解在考虑框架内满足Birkhoff型定理（Birkhoff-type theorem），具有唯一性。通过碰撞零壳设置，在四维时空中对质量膨胀现象进行通用分析，检验最小长度尺度的影响。

Result: 内极端视界构型仅在由理论参数确定的精细调谐质量值下存在。识别了质量膨胀显著化的条件，并阐明了圈量子引力所引入的最小长度尺度如何影响质量膨胀行为。

Conclusion: 所构造的内极端正则黑洞解在特定质量参数下存在；质量膨胀行为受量子引力修正调控；在零壳扰动分析框架下，对该类构型的稳定性进行了初步评估。

Abstract: We derive a class of inner-extremal regular black hole solutions characterized by a degenerate inner horizon. These geometries arise as polymerized vacuum configurations inspired by loop quantum gravity and constitute effective quantum-gravity solutions that admit a Birkhoff-type theorem, rendering them unique within the considered framework. We show that such inner-extremal horizon configurations exist only for a finely tuned value of the mass determined by the parameters of the theory. Building on this construction, together with the corresponding non-degenerate regular black hole solutions, we perform a generic analysis of the mass inflation phenomenon in four-dimensional spacetimes using a colliding null-shell setup near the inner horizon. We identify the conditions under which mass inflation becomes significant and examine how the presence of a minimal length scale affects this behavior, with particular emphasis on the case where such a scale is motivated by loop quantum gravity. Finally, we comment on the stability of these configurations under the null-shell perturbations considered in our analysis.

### [74] [Rotation-Induced Pressure Anisotropy in Newtonian White Dwarfs: Sequences and Applicability Criteria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27956)
*Aray Muratkhan,Saken Toktarbay,Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出一种一维牛顿约化模型（reduced model），通过有效压强各向异性（effective pressure anisotropy）将均匀自转编码进白矮星的流体静力平衡（hydrostatic balance）中，从而快速计算冷白矮星的结构与全局序列，避免使用二维求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统处理白矮星自转需要二维轴对称计算，计算成本较高。作者希望引入一种快速的一维方法，在不显著损失精度的前提下捕捉均匀自转对白矮星结构的影响。

Method: 模型基于定常欧拉方程（stationary Euler equation）导出离心修正项 $Δ_{\rm rot}(r)=\frac{1}{3}ρ(r)Ω^2 r^2$，其中利用 $\langle\sin^2θ\rangle=2/3$ 进行角度平均，将自转离心支撑等效为压强各向异性引入流体静力平衡。采用钱德拉塞卡简并电子物态方程（Chandrasekhar degenerate-electron equation of state），在中心密度 $ρ_c \in [10^6, 10^{11}]~{\rm g\,cm^{-3}}$ 和自转代理参数 $f \le 0.35$ 范围内扫描计算。通过亚开普勒诊断量 $\max(Ω/Ω_K)$、$\max(ε)$ 以及内部小量测度 $A_{10^{-2}}$ 检验模型适用性。

Result: 模型预测限制质量（limiting mass）和半径随自转代理参数 $f$ 单调增加；在 $f = 0.35$ 时质量增益约在百分量级。所有扫描参数下的亚开普勒诊断量均小于1，表明模型在慢速至中等自转范围内具有合理性。

Conclusion: 该一维约化模型适合作为慢速至中等均匀自转条件下冷白矮星的简化牛顿基准（reduced Newtonian benchmark），但无法替代完整的轴对称自转恒星计算。

Abstract: We introduce a fast, one-dimensional Newtonian {reduced model} to capture uniform rotation in cold white dwarfs, encoding centrifugal support as an effective pressure anisotropy. Using $Δ_{\rm rot}(r)=\frac{1}{3}ρ(r)Ω^2 r^2$ derived from the stationary Euler equation with $\langle\sin^2θ\rangle=2/3$, the model incorporates rotation into hydrostatic balance without a two-dimensional solver. Applying the Chandrasekhar degenerate-electron equation of state, we compute interior structures and global sequences for $ ρ_c \in [10^6, 10^{11}]~{\rm g\,cm^{-3}} $ with rotation proxies $f \le 0.35$, finding monotonic increases in limiting mass and radius, with a percent-level mass gain at $f = 0.35$. We quantify applicability using sub-Keplerian diagnostics evaluated on the rotating configurations, $\max(Ω/Ω_K)$ and $\max(ε)$, together with a bulk-interior smallness measure $A_{10^{-2}}\equiv \max_{p_r/p_c\ge 10^{-2}}(Δ_{\rm rot}/p_r)$. Within the scanned domain these diagnostics remain below unity. The model is therefore best viewed as a reduced Newtonian benchmark for slow-to-moderate rotation, not as a replacement for fully axisymmetric calculations of rotating stars.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纯爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）加正宇宙学常数（positive cosmological constant）的框架下，研究4+1维径向对称引力波引力坍缩能否形成接近极端（extremal）的黑洞，并探讨宇宙学背景下黑洞热力学第三定律（third law of black hole thermodynamics）是否成立。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在4+1维时空中对具有宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon）的规则初始数据进行演化，追踪径向对称引力波坍缩导致的黑洞形成过程，并通过特征粘合（characteristic gluing）框架对结果进行分析。

Result: 引力坍缩形成的黑洞质量超过极端值（即de Sitter空间中史瓦西黑洞的最大质量，对应黑洞视界与宇宙学视界重合）的99%。数值结果与特征粘合框架吻合，并显示出宇宙学背景下黑洞热力学第三定律可能不成立的迹象。

Conclusion: 在正宇宙学常数的4+1维纯爱因斯坦引力中，径向对称引力波坍缩可以形成质量极其接近极端值的近极端黑洞；研究结果倾向于表明，宇宙学环境下的黑洞热力学第三定律可能失效。

Abstract: We numerically study a formation of near extremal horizons from a gravitational collapse of radially symmetric gravitational waves in $4+1$ dimensions within the framework of pure Einstein gravity with positive cosmological constant. Evolution of a regular initial data with cosmological horizon leads to a formation of a black hole with mass exceeding $99\%$ of the extremal value corresponding to the black hole and cosmological horizons coinciding.
  We demonstrate how our results fit within the framework of characteristic gluing, and present some evidence that the third law of black hole thermodynamics may not hold in the cosmological context, where the extremality corresponds to the maximal mass of the Schwarzschild black hole in de--Sitter space.

### [76] [On mass inflation and thin shells in quasi-topological gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27980)
*Francesco Di Filippo,David Kubiznak,Aravindhan Srinivasan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究（重新求和后的）拟拓扑引力理论（quasi-topological gravity）中的零测地线交结条件（null junction conditions），发现标准分布理论下不存在零厚度薄壳（null thin shells），进而指出传统质量暴涨不稳定性（mass inflation instability）推导在此类理论中不适用。正则黑洞内视界稳定性问题仍然悬而未决，需采用不依赖薄壳或真空条件的更精细分析方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析（重新求和后的）拟拓扑引力理论中的零测地线交结条件，验证标准分布理论（standard distributional theory）下零厚度薄壳的存在性。

Result: 在所分析的正则黑洞纯引力解中，不存在零厚度薄壳。因此，传统基于薄壳的质量暴涨不稳定性推导在拟拓扑引力中不成立。

Conclusion: 拟拓扑引力中正则黑洞内视界的稳定性问题仍是一个开放问题，需采用不依赖薄壳或真空假设的更精细分析方法加以解决。

Abstract: We study the null junction conditions in (re-summed) quasi-topological gravity theories, showing that no null thin shells exist within the realms of standard distributional theory for the pure gravity regular black hole solutions we have analyzed. This implies that the usual derivation of the mass inflation instability, which makes use of null thin shells, is not applicable in these theories. The problem of stability of inner horizons of regular black holes in quasi-topological gravity is hence still open and must be addressed with a more refined analysis, which does not rely on thin shells or the vacuum condition.

### [77] [Beyond the Separatrix: Analytic Continuation of Darwin Variables for Plunging Geodesics in Schwarzschild Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28140)
*Francisco M. Blanco*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）Darwin变量，构建了一个统一的运动学描述框架，适用于史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中的束缚（bound）、散射（scattering）和陷入（plunging）三类测地线（geodesic），并演示了该变量体系在跨越分界线（separatrix）时的连续演化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Darwin变量虽然能方便地参数化径向运动，但在分界线处失效，且无法直接推广到陷入轨道（plunging trajectories）。作者旨在构建一组解析延拓的变量，统一描述所有类型的test-particle运动，并解决分界线处的参数化断裂问题。

Method: 对Darwin变量进行解析延拓，得到一组实参数化（real parameterization），统一描述束缚、散射和陷入三类史瓦西测地线。随后将该变量体系应用于一个简单的非测地演化（non-geodesic evolution）——在常外力驱动下能量与角动量变化的toy model，以演示变量在跨越分界线时的连续轨道演化能力。

Result: 成功构造了Darwin变量的解析延拓，实现了对束缚、散射和陷入三类测地线的统一实参数化。在toy model中，利用拓展后的变量，仅使用单个轨道相位变量（single orbital phase variable）即可在分界线两侧连续地跟踪轨道演化，包括从束缚轨道过渡到陷入轨道的过程。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析延拓Darwin变量为史瓦西时空中所有类型test-mass motion提供了统一的运动学描述，并具备跨越分界线的连续演化能力。该方法有望为更复杂的物理模型（如辐射反作用力驱动下的极端质量比旋进系统）提供数学工具基础。

Abstract: We study geodesic motion of a test particle in Schwarzschild spacetime. Bound and scattering geodesics are commonly described using Darwin variables, which provide a convenient parametrization of the radial motion. However, this description breaks down at the separatrix and does not extend straightforwardly to plunging trajectories. We construct an analytic continuation of Darwin variables that yields a real parametrization of bound, scattering, and plunging Schwarzschild geodesics, thereby providing a unified kinematical description of all types of test-mass motion. As a proof of concept, we then apply these variables to a simple non-geodesic evolution in which the energy and angular momentum are driven by a constant external force. This toy model is not intended to represent a physical radiation-reaction model, but rather to illustrate how the extended variables can be used to follow an orbit through a transition to plunge using a single orbital phase variable across the separatrix.

</details>


### [78] [Cosmology of fractional gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28188)
*Iván Salvador-García,Gianluca Calcagni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了经典分数引力（classical fractional gravity）的宇宙学，这是一种基于自伴分数达朗贝尔算子（self-adjoint fractional d'Alembertian operator）的非局域理论。推导了任意分数指数γ下的经典协变非局域运动方程，并将其简化为均匀各向同性宇宙学背景下的弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）。发现德西特（de Sitter）时空是精确稳定解，反弹解（bouncing solutions）由幻影流体或鬼流体维持，不同形式因子的表示给出完全相同的解，确认了分数场论形式因子存在一个普适类（universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典分数引力是一种非局域（nonlocal）理论，基于自伴分数达朗贝尔算子，为紫外完备（ultraviolet-complete）的量子引力理论提供基础。此前该理论的宇宙学后果尚未被研究，本文填补了这一空白。

Method: 从经典协变非局域运动方程出发，针对任意分数指数γ推导一般形式，然后将其约化到均匀各向同性（homogeneous and isotropic）宇宙学背景下的弗里德曼方程。通过分析不同形式因子的表示来检验解的等价性。

Result: 德西特时空是精确稳定解；反弹解由幻影流体（phantom fluid, w<-1）或鬼流体（ghost fluid, ρ<0）维持，后者伴随一种新类型的有限未来奇点（finite-future singularity）出现在气压指标（barotropic index）中。不同形式因子表示给出完全相同的解，证实分数场论的表述依赖于形式因子的一个普适类。

Conclusion: 分数引力宇宙学展现出德西特稳定解和反弹解等多种有趣行为，且形式因子存在普适类，表明分数场论（fractional field theories）的表述具有稳健性。这些初步结果与模拟分数量子引力时空几何的多分数宇宙学模型（multi-fractional cosmological models）进行了比较。

Abstract: This is a first study of the cosmology of classical fractional gravity, a nonlocal proposal endowed with self-adjoint fractional d'Alembertian operators which serves as the basis for an ultraviolet-complete theory of quantum gravity. We derive the classical covariant nonlocal equations of motion for an arbitrary fractional exponent $γ$ and reduce them to the Friedmann equations on a homogeneous and isotropic cosmological background. We find that de Sitter is an exact stable solution and that bouncing exact solutions are sustained by phantom ($w<-1$) or ghost ($ρ<0$) fluids, in the latter case with a new type of finite-future singularity in the barotropic index. Different representations of the form factor give exactly the same solutions, thus confirming that the formulation of fractional field theories relies on a universality class of form factors. We compare these preliminary results with what obtained in multi-fractional cosmological models mimicking the spacetime geometry of fractional quantum gravity.

</details>

### [79] [Measurement of the top quark pair production cross section in PbPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27091)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了在铅-铅（PbPb）碰撞中顶夸克对（$\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$）产生的包容性截面，利用CMS实验在5.36 TeV每核子对质心能量下采集的数据，测量了双轻子末态的产生截面，并与次次领头阶（NNLO）量子色动力学预言一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在重离子碰撞中首次测量顶夸克对产生截面，以检验微扰量子色动力学（perturbative quantum chromodynamics）在极端高密度核物质环境下的预测能力，并探索碰撞冲击参数（impact parameter）对顶夸克产生的影响。

Method: 基于CMS实验在2023年采集的积分亮度为1.58 nb$^{-1}$的铅-铅碰撞数据，利用双轻子末态（dilepton final states），通过拟合结合衰变电子与缪子运动学性质及底夸克喷注多重度的多变量鉴别器（multivariate discriminator）进行测量。

Result: 测得的$\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$产生截面$σ_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}} = 3.42^{+0.54}_{-0.51}(\text{stat})^{+0.50}_{-0.43}(\text{syst})\ \mu$b，以及Drell–Yan产生截面$σ_\text{DY}$和二者比值$R_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}/\mathrm{DY}}$均与次次领头阶（NNLO）预言一致；三个观测量还在中心与半中心碰撞中分别测量以研究冲击参数依赖性。

Conclusion: 顶夸克对产生截面及其相关观测量与NNLO微扰量子色动力学计算在多种核子部分子分布函数（nuclear parton distribution functions）下相符，表明顶夸克产生在重离子碰撞中可由标准模型理论准确描述。

Abstract: The inclusive cross section for top quark pair ($\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$) production in lead-lead (PbPb) collisions is reported for the first time at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of 5.36 TeV. The analysis uses data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 1.58 nb$^{-1}$ collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC in 2023. The $\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$ production cross section, $σ_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}} $ = 3.42$^{+0.54}_{-0.51}$(stat)$^{+0.50}_{-0.43}$(syst) $μ$b, is measured in dilepton final states using a fit to a multivariate discriminator that combines the decay electron and muon kinematic properties with the multiplicity of bottom quark jets. The result is consistent with perturbative quantum chromodynamics calculations at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) accuracy employing several nuclear parton distribution functions. In addition, the Drell$-$Yan production cross section ($σ_\text{DY}$) for dilepton masses above 10 GeV and the ratio of $\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$ to DY cross sections ($R_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}/\mathrm{DY}}$) are found to be compatible with the NNLO predictions. The observables $σ_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}}$, $σ_\text{DY}$, and $R_{\mathrm{t\bar{t}}/\mathrm{DY}}$ are measured separately for central and semicentral PbPb collisions to investigate for the first time the dependence of top quark production on the collision impact parameter.

</details>
