### [80] [The effect of Van der Waals interaction on the microstructure of EPD deposits: a simulation study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26987)
*Rémi Martin,Sandrine Duluard,Céline Merlet*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于粒子模拟（particle-based simulations）研究了电泳沉积（electrophoretic deposition）过程中粒子自聚集（self-cohesion）对不同电场强度下沉积层微观结构（microstructure）的影响，发现高电场下自聚集效应会消失，沉积机制由此从聚集主导转变为体积排斥主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电泳沉积因工艺简单、可单步制备厚涂层而广受欢迎，但其可调参数众多（电场、浓度、黏度等），参数选择困难。现有粒子模型研究大多忽略粒子间的自聚集（self-cohesion）效应，而这种效应对沉积最终结构可能至关重要。

Method: 采用基于粒子的计算机模拟方法，系统研究了不同外加电场强度下，粒子自聚集对沉积层形貌和微观结构的影响。

Result: 自聚集效应确实改变了沉积层的微观结构，包括基底附近区域和沉积层内部；在高电场条件下，当电场强度超过某一临界值时，自聚集对微观结构的影响基本消失。

Conclusion: 电泳沉积存在两种机制：当电场较低时，沉积受聚集效应影响显著；当电场超过临界强度后，沉积机制转为体积排斥效应主导，自聚集的影响可忽略。

Abstract: Electrophoretic deposition is a method of choice for generating coatings thanks to its ease of implementation and its ability to produce coatings of relatively large thicknesses in a single step process. While this process also benefits from a large number of tunable parameters to adapt the coating to each application (applied electric field, particle concentration, viscosity of the suspension, etc...), such a freedom can lead to the selection of parameters being an overwhelming task. A better fundamental understanding of the microscopic phenomena and mechanisms at play during deposition can provide clues for the more efficient design of optimized coatings. Particle-based models, allowing for the simulation of deposit microstructures for various process parameters, are particularly interesting to get insights in such systems. Nevertheless, such studies are rare and usually do not involve the possibility of self-cohesion between particles, while it seems crucial for the final structure of the deposit. Here, we use particle-based simulations to study the influence of aggregation on the deposit formed for different applied electric fields. We show that the self-cohesion indeed leads to different microstructures, both in the close vicinity of the substrate and in the bulk of the deposit, and relate this to the mechanical signature of the deposits. Our results reveal that at high electric field, the influence of self-cohesion on resulting microstructures essentially vanishes beyond a critical field strength. This marks the transition between a deposition regime affected by aggregation to a regime largely dominated by volume exclusion effects.

</details>


### [81] [Thin film synthesis of SrZn2P2 with SrI2 post-annealing for enhanced crystallinity and optoelectronic quality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26995)
*Sita Dugu,Shaham Quadir,Christopher P. Muzzillo,Zhenkun Yuan,Smitakshi Goswami,Xiaojing Hao,Jialiang Huang,Guillermo Esparza,Baptiste Julien,David Fenning,Jifeng Liu,Geoffroy Hautier,Andriy Zakutayev,Sage R. Bauers*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了采用射频共溅射法合成纯相 SrZn2P2 薄膜，并发现 SrI2 辅助退火能显著促进晶粒生长、增强光致发光强度和均匀性，从而为 Zintl 磷化物半导体提供了一种可推广的微观结构调控策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三元 Zintl 磷化物（ternary Zintl phosphides）是薄膜光电器件中前景良好的光吸收半导体，但其微观结构和光电质量的调控策略尚不充分。本文旨在探索有效的后处理工艺来优化其性能。

Method: 在 PH₃ + Ar 气氛中采用射频共溅射（radio-frequency co-sputtering）合成 SrZn2P2 薄膜，并通过掠入射 X 射线散射（grazing-incidence X-ray scattering）和拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）确认物相；进一步采用卤化物辅助退火（halide-assisted annealing）处理，并与快速热退火或成形气体退火进行对比。

Result: 光学测量显示薄膜在直接带隙能量（~1.8 eV）附近具有强吸收和近带边光致发光（near-band-edge photoluminescence）。SrI2 处理在保持相纯度的同时显著促进了晶粒生长并减小了衍射峰展宽；在 450 °C 下退火显著增强了光致发光的强度和空间均匀性。

Conclusion: 卤化物辅助退火是一种有效的 SrZn2P2 薄膜微观结构调控路径，为将 Zintl 磷化物半导体推向光电器件应用提供了一种可推广的加工策略。

Abstract: Ternary Zintl phosphides are promising light-absorbing semiconductors for thin-film optoelectronic applications, but strategies for controlling their microstructure and optoelectronic quality remain underexplored. Here, we report the synthesis of phase-pure SrZn2P2 thin films using radio-frequency co-sputtering in a PH3 + Ar atmosphere and investigate the impact of post-growth processing on their structural and optical properties. Grazing-incidence X-ray scattering and Raman spectroscopy confirm the formation of crystalline SrZn2P2 films over a finite compositional window. Optical measurements reveal strong absorption near the direct-band-gap energy (~1.8 eV) and near-band-edge photoluminescence. Further, we have studied the effects of chemically compatible halide-assisted annealing. It is found that SrI2 treatments lead to pronounced grain growth and reduced diffraction peak broadening while preserving phase purity, in contrast to rapid thermal or forming-gas annealing. Notably, annealing with SrI2 at 450 °C significantly enhances both the intensity and spatial uniformity of the photoluminescence, thus connecting the observed microstructural consolidation with improved radiative recombination. Our study demonstrates that halide-assisted annealing provides an effective pathway for microstructural control in SrZn2P2 thin films and highlights a generalizable processing strategy for advancing Zintl phosphide semiconductors toward optoelectronic applications.

</details>


### [82] [Contrasting Effects of Functionalization in Binary and Medium-Entropy MXene Coatings for Corrosion Protection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27114)
*Aqsa Fayyaz,Ulises Martin Diaz,Jianyu Dai,Homero Castaneda,Chenglin Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究受珍珠母结构启发，设计了四种MXene体系增强的多层环氧防腐涂层。多层结构形成致密层状网络，增加扩散曲折度并引入电活性表面。电化学阻抗谱（EIS）证实涂层电阻从约10³提升至约10⁸ Ohm/cm²，性能排序为：P-(TiVCrMo)C₃ > O-Ti₃C₂Tₓ > O-(TiVCrMo)C₃ > P-Ti₃C₂Tₓ。密度泛函理论（DFT）计算揭示了表面化学、电子结构与成分熵之间的微妙平衡对防腐性能的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在富含氯化物的环境中保护钢铁基础设施需要开发可规模化且环境友好的防腐涂层。

Method: 受珍珠母（nacre）启发的多层环氧涂层，采用四种MXene体系（P-(TiVCrMo)C₃、O-Ti₃C₂Tₓ、O-(TiVCrMo)C₃、P-Ti₃C₂Tₓ）进行增强。通过电化学阻抗谱（EIS）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算分别从实验和理论层面分析涂层性能及表面反应机制。

Result: 多层设计使涂层电阻从约10³提升至约10⁸ Ohm/cm²；性能层级为P-(TiVCrMo)C₃ > O-Ti₃C₂Tₓ > O-(TiVCrMo)C₃ > P-Ti₃C₂Tₓ；DFT计算表明P-Ti₃C₂强吸附O₂，氧端基（oxygen termination）通过部分钝化Ti位点稳定表面，而P-(TiVCrMo)C₃的多金属电子结构促进含氧物种吸附并形成保护性氧化物。

Conclusion: 表面化学、电子结构（electronic structure）与成分熵（compositional entropy）之间的精细平衡是设计下一代MXene基防腐涂层的核心，此类涂层在海洋和工业环境中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Developing scalable and environmentally benign anticorrosion coatings is critical for protecting steel infrastructure in chloride-rich environments. Here, a nacre-inspired multilayer epoxy coating reinforced with four MXene systems is investigated. This architecture forms a dense lamellar network that increases diffusion tortuosity and introduces electroactive surfaces for ion interactions. Electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) confirms that the multilayer design increases coating resistance from ~103 to ~108 Ohm/cm2. A clear performance hierarchy was observed: P-(TiVCrMo)C3 > O-Ti3C2Tx > O-(TiVCrMo)C3 > P-Ti3C2Tx. Density functional theory (DFT) calculations reveal that P-Ti3C2 strongly adsorbs O2, indicating higher surface reactivity, while oxygen termination stabilizes the surface by partially passivating Ti sites. In contrast, P-(TiVCrMo)C3 exhibits strong adsorption of oxygen-containing species due to its multi-metal electronic structure, promoting the formation of protective oxides. These results highlight the delicate balance of surface chemistry, electronic structure, and compositional entropy in designing next-generation MXene-based anticorrosion coatings for marine and industrial environments.

</details>


### [83] [First-Principles Thermodynamic Analysis of Ternary Chalcogenide Phase Change Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27120)

Method: 基于奥斯特瓦尔德规则（Ostwald's rule）提出热力学框架；利用第一性原理（first-principles）计算系统评估三元硫系混合物沿二元-二元结线（binary-binary tie lines）及其多晶型（polymorphs）的能量学；通过比较基态（ground-state）和亚稳态（metastable）结构，评估宽组分空间内的相稳定性、混溶性（miscibility）及类GST多晶型介导的结晶路径可能性。

Result: 计算再现了GST及相关体系中已知的行为，并识别出若干具有类似特征的有前景候选混合物。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了某些PCM体系比其他体系更有利的内在原因，并将热力学多晶型筛选（thermodynamic polymorph screening）确立为未来发现新型PCM的实用路径。

Abstract: Chalcogenide phase-change materials (PCMs) are important for nonvolatile memory and reconfigurable photonic technologies. The GeTe-Sb2Te3 mixture system, commonly referred to as GST, is the most well-known PCM family, but new PCMs are needed to broaden the accessible property space while retaining fast switching. Here, we propose a thermodynamic framework, motivated by Ostwald's rule, for understanding and identifying PCM materials. Since direct modeling of phase-transition dynamics is computationally expensive, Using first-principles calculations, we systematically evaluate the energetics of ternary chalcogenide mixtures along binary-binary tie lines and their polymorphs. By comparing ground-state and metastable structures, we assess phase stability, miscibility, and the likelihood of GST-like polymorph-mediated crystallization pathways across a broad composition space. The calculations reproduce known behavior in GST and related systems and identify several promising candidate mixtures with similar features. These results provide insight into why some PCM systems are more favorable than others and establish thermodynamic polymorph screening as a practical route for future PCM discovery.

### [84] [Practical Insights to Thin Film Dewetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27192)
*Karim Gadelrab,Stefan Reimann-Zitz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用格子玻尔兹曼方法（LBM）在润滑理论框架下系统量化了薄膜厚度、表面能、润湿性和分子间力对去湿动力学（dewetting kinetics）和长时间形貌的影响，识别出主曲线标度律，并发现去湿时间对膜厚具有强幂律敏感性，而对接触角中等变化依赖性较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 薄膜（thin liquid films）的失稳与破裂动力学对涂覆性能（coating performance）有重要影响，但各物理参数（膜厚、表面能、润湿性、分子间力）如何系统调控去湿动力学和长时间形貌尚缺乏定量理解。

Method: 采用润滑理论框架（lubrication-theory framework）下的格子玻尔兹曼方法模拟（lattice Boltzmann method, LBM），系统量化膜厚、表面能、润湿性和分子间力的影响。

Result: 识别出去湿时间的主曲线标度律（master-curve scalings），膜厚具有强幂律敏感性，接触角中等变化影响较弱；破裂后达到有物理意义的覆盖度平台（coverage plateau），该平台值与材料参数相关；长时间演化服从经典粗化标度律（coarsening scaling laws），表面能主导畴密度。

Conclusion: 基于润滑理论的模型能够为涂覆鲁棒性评估、成型材料及表面工程策略提供预测性设计指导。

Abstract: Thin liquid films exhibit rich instability and rupture dynamics that critically impact coating performance across many applications. In this work, we use the lattice Boltzmann method (LBM) simulations within a lubrication-theory framework to systematically quantify how film thickness, surface energy, wettability, and intermolecular forces govern dewetting kinetics and long-time morphology. Master-curve scalings are identified for the time to dewet, revealing a strong power-law sensitivity to film thickness and a comparatively weak dependence on moderate variations in the contact angle. Following rupture, the film reaches a physically meaningful coverage plateau, whose magnitude correlates with material parameters and provides a practical window for morphological stabilization prior to coarsening. Long-time evolution obeys classical coarsening scaling laws, with surface energy controlling domain density. These results demonstrate that lubrication-based models can deliver predictive design guidance for evaluating coating robustness and forming materials and surface engineering strategies. Source code is available at https://github.com/Zitzeronion/Swalbe.jl.

### [85] [Dual role of core electrons in electronic friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27236)
*Runfeng Zhou,Emilio Artacho*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time time-dependent density functional theory, rt-TDDFT）对铍自辐照体系中的电子阻止本领进行第一性原理计算，发现布拉格峰（Bragg peak）出现因芯电子（core electrons）存在而产生的独特精细结构。该结构的出现源于芯电子的双重效应：一方面提供额外的耗散通道，另一方面通过弹丸核从宿主核捕获电子的过程抑制价电子激发，而非泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）。该机制与水中芯电子增强价激发的shake-up效应形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡态多壳层快离子/物质体系中的能量耗散问题尚未被充分理解，电子阻止本领（electronic stopping power, $\mathcal{S}_\text{e}$）作为电子摩擦（electronic friction）的关联可观测量，是理解该问题的关键。

Method: 采用实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time time-dependent density functional theory, rt-TDDFT），对所有电子进行显式处理，对铍自辐照体系的电子阻止本领$\mathcal{S}_\text{e}$进行第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）。

Result: 计算揭示出布拉格峰（Bragg peak）呈现一种标准半经验模型无法捕捉的独特精细结构；芯电子的激发提供了额外耗散通道，同时抑制了价电子激发；弹丸核从宿主核捕获电子的过程导致了这一抑制，而非泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）。

Conclusion: 提出了芯电子在弹丸能量耗散中的双重作用机制，与水中观测到的shake-up效应相反，为理解芯电子在物质能量耗散中的作用和重要性提供了新视角。

Abstract: Non-equilibrium energy dissipation in multi-shell swift-ion/matter systems remains a fundamental yet incompletely understood problem, with electronic stopping power $\mathcal{S}_\text{e}$ as a relevant observable for electronic friction. Using real-time time-dependent density functional theory, we perform first-principles calculations of $\mathcal{S}_\text{e}$ for beryllium self-irradiation with explicit treatment of all electrons. Our results reveal a Bragg peak exhibiting a distinct structure which lies beyond the reach of standard semi-empirical models. We attribute its appearance to a dual effect of the presence of core electrons, by which their excitation provides an additional dissipation channel while simultaneously suppressing valence electron excitations. An electron capture process by the projectile's core from the host cores is behind such suppression, rather than Pauli blocking. This dual mechanism contrasts with the shake-up effect reported for water, whereby the inclusion of core electrons enhances valence excitation. Our work provides a new perspective on the effect and importance of core electrons in projectile energy dissipation in matter.

</details>


### [86] [Ultrafast Sliding Ferroelectric Switching in Bilayer Hexagonal Boron Nitride Revealed by Deep Learning Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27342)
*Yinan Wang,Poyen Chen,Teruyasu Mizoguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过整合微调 MACE 机器学习势（machine learning potential, MLP）与等变图卷积神经网络（equivariant graph convolutional neural network, EGCNN）用于实时玻恩有效电荷（Born effective charge, BEC）预测，构建了全数据驱动的耦合原子级框架，对 AB 堆叠双层六方氮化硼（bilayer hexagonal boron nitride, h-BN）在外加电场下的非平衡分子动力学进行了大规模模拟。研究表明，相干单畴刚性滑动可在 5 ps 内完成，是一种物理上可行的超快极化翻转机制，并再现了与实验定性一致的干净铁电迟滞回线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层六方氮化硼（bilayer hexagonal boron nitride, h-BN）中的滑移铁电性（sliding ferroelectricity）为下一代非易失性存储器提供了有前景的方向，但电场驱动极化翻转（polarization switching）的原子级动力学机制仍不清楚。

Method: 提出了一种全数据驱动的耦合原子级框架，整合了微调后的 MACE 机器学习势（MACE machine learning potential, MLP）与等变图卷积神经网络（equivariant graph convolutional neural network, EGCNN）用于实时玻恩有效电荷（Born effective charge, BEC）预测。采用严格的实空间路径积分极化形式（real-space path-integral polarization formalism），并结合状态约束高斯卷积背景提取（state-constrained Gaussian convolution background extraction）过程，从占主导的介电背景中分离出本征自发极化。

Result: 模拟发现，相干单畴刚性滑动（coherent single-domain rigid sliding）可在 5 ps 内完成，是一种物理可行的超快翻转机制。该方法成功再现了干净的铁电迟滞回线（ferroelectric hysteresis loops），其形状与实验观察定性一致。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了 AB 堆叠双层六方氮化硼中电场驱动极化翻转的原子级机制，证实了刚性滑动作为超快翻转途径的可行性，为理解滑移铁电体的动力学行为提供了新的计算途径。

Abstract: Sliding ferroelectricity in bilayer hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) offers compelling prospects for next-generation non-volatile memory, yet the atomistic dynamics of electric-field-driven polarization switching remain poorly understood. Here, we present a fully data-driven, coupled atomistic framework that integrates a fine-tuned MACE machine learning potential (MLP) with an equivariant graph convolutional neural network (EGCNN) for real-time Born effective charge (BEC) prediction, enabling large-scale non-equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations of AB-stacked bilayer h-BN under applied electric fields. By implementing a rigorous real-space path-integral polarization formalism combined with a state-constrained Gaussian convolution background extraction procedure, we successfully isolate the intrinsic spontaneous polarization from the dominant dielectric background. Our simulations reveal that coherent single-domain rigid sliding, completing within 5 ps, constitutes a physically viable ultrafast switching mechanism, and reproduces clean ferroelectric hysteresis loops whose shape is qualitatively consistent with experimental observations.

</details>


### [87] [Phase-Transition Induced Domain Evolution and Magnetization Dynamics in FePt/FeRh Bilayers for Efficient Heat-Assisted Magnetic Recording](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27370)

Conclusion: FePt/FeRh双层膜中矫顽力的降低主要由相变诱导的畴壁迁移率（domain wall mobility）和界面磁相互作用的耦合作用主导，而非本征各向异性的软化；这一机制实现了在降低热负荷下的高效磁化翻转，使FePt/FeRh异质结构成为先进HAMR介质的有前景候选材料。

Abstract: Achieving ultrahigh recording densities with low power consumption is a central challenge for next generation heat assisted magnetic recording (HAMR), as conventional L10 FePt media require intense laser heating due to their high coercivity (Hc) and high Curie temperature (700 K). Here, we address this issue using FePt/FeRh bilayers, where the antiferromagnetic to ferromagnetic transition of FeRh near 350 K generates strong interfacial exchange coupling that assists magnetization switching in the FePt layer. Temperature dependent MFM directly captures phase transition induced domain evolution, showing a 30% reduction in domain size and enhanced phase contrast. TR-MOKE measurements reveal only a minor (0.4 T) modification of the effective anisotropy field during phase transition, confirming that the intrinsic anisotropy of FePt remains largely preserved. These results demonstrate that the reduction in Hc in FePt/FeRh bilayers is primarily governed by phase transition induced domain wall mobility coupled with interfacial magnetic interactions, rather than by intrinsic anisotropy softening. This mechanism provides a pathway toward efficient magnetization switching under reduced thermal load, making FePt/FeRh heterostructures promising candidates for advanced HAMR media.

### [88] [The optical phonoelectric effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27524)
*D. Choi,M. Först,M. Fechner,M. Buzzi,X. Deng,Z. Zeng,K. H. Martens,D. Prabhakaran,C. Putzke,P. Moll,P. G. Radaelli,A. Cavalleri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种名为“光声电效应（optical phonoelectricity）”的新机制：通过光激发光学声子畸变，在无机械应变的情况下实现类压电效应。在弱压电材料BPO₄中，该效应通过声子整流（phonon rectification）诱导电极化，其建立速度比传统压电效应快四个数量级（受光速限制），且最大极化强度远超应变断裂极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统压电效应（piezoelectricity）存在三个内在局限：响应建立速度受限于声速、效应强度不可调谐、最大幅度受限于材料断裂。本文旨在克服这些限制，探索一种无应变、超快、可调谐的类压电响应机制。

Method: 在弱压电材料BPO₄中，通过光激发光学声子畸变（photo-excited optical phonon distortions）驱动声子整流（phonon rectification）过程，从而实现无机械应变条件下的电极化。该方法利用光与晶格振动耦合，在宏观体积内建立类压电响应。

Result: 实验实现了光声电效应（phonoelectricity），该效应在宏观体积内建立的速度比传统压电响应快四个数量级（最终受光速限制），且最大诱导极化强度估计远超应变断裂极限下可达到的值。

Conclusion: 超快光声电效应为量子材料中的光学调控以及器件应用开辟了新机遇，克服了传统压电效应在速度、可调谐性和幅度方面的根本限制。

Abstract: Piezoelectricity is a technologically important property of certain insulators in which mechanical strain induces an electrical polarization. However, the rate at which a piezoelectric response can be established over a macroscopic volume is limited by the sound velocity, constraining applications in high-bit-rate transduction and sensing. Furthermore, the strength of the piezoelectric effect is not readily tunable, as it depends on intrinsic anharmonic coupling between strain and intra-unit-cell distortions in a given material. Lastly, the maximum amplitude of the effect is bounded by material fracture, which sets in already at percent level strain values. Here we overcome these limitations by realizing a strain-free, piezoelectric-like response driven solely by photo-excited optical phonon distortions. We demonstrate such optical phonoelectricity in the weak piezoelectric BPO$_4$, in which we induce electrical polarization through phonon rectification. This effect is established over macroscopic volumes with four orders of magnitude higher speed than piezoelectric responses, ultimately limited by the speed of light. The maximum induced polarization is estimated to be far in excess of that attainable through strain at the fracture limit. Ultrafast phonoelectricity opens up new opportunities for optical control in quantum materials, but also for device applications.

Abstract: While machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) accelerate phonon dispersion calculations, merely identifying dynamical instabilities in computationally predicted materials is insufficient; automated pathways to resolve them are required. VibroML employs an energy-guided genetic algorithm that vastly outperforms traditional soft-mode following, efficiently navigating the potential energy surface to uncover diverse, dynamically stable polymorphs. As 0 K harmonic stability does not guarantee macroscopic viability, an automated molecular dynamics workflow evaluates finite-temperature structural retention. VibroML also couples with ProtoCSP, our combinatorial structure prediction engine, to stabilize frustrated crystal topologies via targeted alloying, successfully rescuing functional perovskite networks like Cs$_2$KInI$_6$ and KTaSe$_3$. Demonstrating broader applicability, we mined the Alexandria database -- where ~50% of quaternary and 99.5% of quinary elemental combinations lack any structural entries -- to identify thousands of abandoned, high-symmetry stoichiometries. Deploying ProtoCSP's "cold start" retrieval and VibroML's evolutionary search on a sample, we successfully identified dynamically stable low-symmetry candidates. Conclusion: 该工作为拓扑磁体中声子驱动的自旋-电荷-晶格耦合提供了一个统一的粗粒化理论框架，有助于理解在微波激发下斯格明子晶格中由晶格形变产生的宏观涌现电场行为。

Abstract: We discuss modulation phasons as a possible source of unusual elastic behavior of five-layer modulated (10\,M) martensite of the Ni-Mn-Ga shape memory alloy. This material exhibits anomalous macroscopic shear compliance along specific planes perpendicular to the modulation vector, and this compliance disappears when the modulations become incommensurate. Using a simple mechanical model, we show that modulation phasons in Ni-Mn-Ga can have macroscopic mechanical manifestations, and that the resulting 'mechanical phasons' can relax external shear loadings for commensurate and weakly incommensurate modulations, but not for strongly incommensurate modulations. ### [93] [The second altermagnet candidate in organic conductors: $κ$-(BEDT-TTF)$_2$$m$-HOOCC$_6$H$_4$SO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27746)
*Kohei Tokura,Takato Masuta,Kazushi Aoyama,Hiroki Akutsu,Yasuhiro Nakazawa,Scott S. Turner*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于紧束缚能带计算（tight-binding band calculation）分析了κ-m-SBA的转移积分比t'/t；通过磁化测量观测到弱铁磁转变；并结合数值计算验证能带自旋分裂（spin splitting of energy bands）这一交变磁体特征。

Result: κ-m-SBA在100 K时的t'/t为1.01，表明自旋结构接近等边三角形（t'/t=1）；在T_N=14 K处发生由倾斜反铁磁自旋结构引起的弱铁磁转变；数值计算证实该材料存在能带自旋分裂。

Conclusion: κ-m-SBA是继κ-Cl之后有机导体中第二个交变磁体候选材料，扩展了交变磁体（altermagnet）在有机导体领域的材料体系。

Tight-binding band calculations of $κ$-$m$-SBA provide a $t'/t$ of 1.01 at 100 K, indicating that the spin structure is closely aligned to an equilateral triangle ($t'/t= 1$). While most $κ$-type BEDT-TTF-based salts become spin liquids due to the spin frustration caused by the triangular lattice, $κ$-$m$-SBA surprisingly shows a weak ferromagnetic transition at $T_\mathrm{N} = 14$ K due to a canted antiferromagnetic (AFM) spin structure. This was theoretically predicted by Naka et al. in 2019, who demonstrated that $κ$-type organic conductors can be candidates for altermagnetism if they display such order. Consequently, $κ$-$m$-SBA can be considered the second candidate for altermagnetism in organic conductors. Furthermore, numerical calculations demonstrate a characteristic of altermagnets in $κ$-$m$-SBA, namely spin splitting of energy bands.

*Radmir Karamov,Tagir Karamov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于物理引导特征工程与数据增强（data augmentation）的小样本机器学习工作流，用于校正浅层纳米压痕（shallow nanoindentation）中的尺寸效应（indentation size effect, ISE）。基于约700组钢试样实验数据，通过岭回归、随机森林、XGBoost和神经网络（neural network, NN）进行建模，其中约束神经网络在隔离测试集上达到R²>0.98、RMSE=0.470 GPa、MAPE=5.4%的效果，优于经典Nix-Gao方法，尤其在浅层压痕区表现稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 浅层纳米压痕是表征薄膜、单相及体积受限材料力学性能的重要手段，但测量硬度常因压痕尺寸效应（indentation size effect, ISE）、接触面积误差和针尖几何伪影而偏高。经典ISE修正方法如Nix-Gao模型需依赖深压痕线性区域，在仅有浅层测量数据时不可靠。因此，该研究旨在探索如何利用小规模实验数据集，通过物理引导的特征工程与数据增强来预测参考硬度，实现ISE校正。

Method: 实验收集了约700组来自三种钢参考试样的压痕数据（硬度范围2–6.5 GPa），并基于物理动机进行数据增强（data augmentation），模拟仪器噪声、批次漂移和局部多相边界混合。输入空间结合Oliver-Pharr标准参数与力学描述符，包括压痕功分配、H/E_r（硬度与约化弹性模量之比）以及面积不变柔量代理量P_max/S²。采用岭回归（Ridge Regression, RR）、随机森林（Random Forest）、XGBoost和神经网络（Neural Network, NN）四种模型进行训练，并以第四种钢试样（采用阶梯载荷测试）作为隔离验证集。

Result: 硬度映射具有非线性特征：岭回归（线性模型）失败，而非线性模型在内部验证中均达到R²>0.98。约束架构为64-8-64的神经网络表现最佳，在隔离钢试样上达到RMSE=0.470 GPa、MAPE=5.4%。与Nix-Gao分析不同，该神经网络在浅层压痕区域仍能给出稳定估计。SHAP（Shapley Additive Explanations）与潜空间分析表明，模型主要依赖面积不变描述符和能量基描述符。

Conclusion: 该研究验证了基于物理引导特征工程与数据增强的小样本机器学习工作流对钢材料ISE校正的可行性。该方法无需依赖深压痕的线性区域，在浅层压痕区表现优于经典Nix-Gao方法，为任意体积受限材料的数据高效力学表征提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Shallow nanoindentation enables mechanical characterization of thin films, individual phases and other volume-constrained materials, but measured hardness is often inflated by the indentation size effect (ISE), contact-area errors and tip-geometry artifacts. Classical ISE corrections such as the Nix-Gao require a deep linear regime and are unreliable when only shallow measurements are used. This study investigates how a small experimental dataset can be used to predict a reference hardness with physics-guided feature engineering and augmentation. Approximately 700 experimental indentations were collected from three steel reference specimens covering a hardness range of 2-6.5 GPa and augmented using physically motivated variations representing instrumental noise, session-level drift, and local multiphase boundary blending. The input space combined Oliver-Pharr values with mechanics descriptors, including indentation work partitioning, ($H\text{/}E_{r}$), and the area-invariant compliance proxy ($P_{\max}\text{/}S^{2}$). Ridge Regression (RR), Random Forest, XGBoost, and Neural Networks (NN) were evaluated using a quarantined fourth steel specimen tested at staggered loads. The hardness mapping was nonlinear: RR failed, whereas nonlinear models achieved ($R^2 > 0.98$) internally. A constrained (64-8-64) NN gave the best results, reaching RMSE = 0.470 GPa, MAPE = 5.4% on the quarantined steel. Unlike Nix-Gao analysis, the NN produced stable estimates in the shallow regime. SHAP and latent-space analysis showed reliance on area-invariant and energy-based descriptors. The results demonstrate the feasibility of a this workflow for ISE correction in steels using small datasets and suggest a pathway toward data-efficient characterization of any volume constrained materials.

</details>


### [95] [Theory for the mixed alkali effect in glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27873)
*Justus Leiber,Quinn Emilia Fischer,Sven Lohmann,Philipp Maass*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于热激活跳跃输运（thermally activated hopping transport）和无序位能景观（disordered site energy landscapes）的理论，自洽地结合统计力学与动力学，解释混合碱玻璃（mixed alkali glasses）中离子输运的非线性混合效应，并通过模拟和实验验证了该理论的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合碱效应（mixed alkali effect）表现为不同类型移动离子混合后离子输运性质的非线性变化，其背后的统计力学和动力学机制尚不清晰，需要建立统一的理论框架加以解释。

Method: 基于无序位能景观中的热激活跳跃输运，构建了包含联合概率密度（joint probability density）、广义费米分布（generalized Fermi distributions）及非对角Onsager系数（nondiagonal Onsager coefficients）的理论模型，并结合动理学蒙特卡洛模拟（kinetic Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证。

Result: 理论表明，即使两种离子的位能分布完全相同，混合碱效应仍可出现；关键因素在于不同离子占据同一位置时位能不同。引入错配能（mismatch energy）可增强该效应，而位能的空间关联（spatial correlations）是主离子迁移率随替代以超指数形式下降的必要条件。理论适用于混合碱磷酸盐玻璃的电导激活能。

Conclusion: 该理论自洽地统一了统计力学与动力学视角，准确刻画了混合碱效应的本质机制，并与动理学蒙特卡洛模拟及实际玻璃体系的电导实验数据高度吻合。

Abstract: The mixed alkali or mixed mobile ion effect in glasses manifests itself by strong nonlinear variations of ionic transport properties upon mixing of different types of mobile ions. We develop a theory for this effect based on thermally activated hopping transport in disordered site energy landscapes that consistently incorporates the statistical-mechanical and kinetic aspects of a mobile ion mixture. This includes a consideration of the joint probability density of site energy states, generalized Fermi distributions for mean site occupations, and cross-terms in the current response described by nondiagonal Onsager coefficients. The theory shows that a mixed alkali effect can arise even when the two ion species share identical site energy distributions. It suffices that sites have distinct energies when occupied by ions of different type. Taking into account that a mismatch energy is needed for ions of one type to occupy sites adapted to the other type, the mixed alkali effect becomes stronger. Spatial correlations between site energies are needed for the mobility of the majority ion to decrease stronger than exponential upon replacement by the minority ion. The theory agrees well with kinetic Monte Carlo simulations. Application to mixed alkali phosphate glasses yields good agreement with measured conductivity activation energies.

</details>

Method: 利用有机材料数据库（OMDB）构建包含15,000余个单点第一性原理计算（single-point first-principles computations）的训练数据集；对机器学习原子间势模型CHGNet进行微调（fine tuning）；实现位点替换工作流（site substitution workflow），基于QMOF数据库中的结构原型识别新型高磁性MOFs。

Conclusion: 研究表明，结合有机材料数据库和微调后的机器学习原子间势，可有效克服有机材料模拟的计算挑战，并拓展至新型高磁性MOFs的发现，弥补了现有基础模型中有机材料训练数据不足的局限。

Abstract: The potential to utilize metal-organic frameworks as a replacement for rare earth materials as well as in technological applications has prompted increased interested in this material class. The simulation of organic materials, including metal-organic frameworks (MOFs), represents a computational challenge due to an increased average number of atoms in the unit cell. Compounding this challenge, modern materials databases are generally limited to inorganic structures due to their utility in modern technologies such as batteries and integrated circuits. Machine-learning tools appear ideally suited to study these systems. However, organic materials are generally underrepresented in the training sets of foundational models. In this work we leverage the the Organic Materials Database (OMDB) to create a training dataset comprised of more than 15,000 single-point first-principles computations for finetuning machine learned interatomic potentials. Specifically, we fine tune CHGNet and implement a site substitution workflow to identify novel, highly magnetic, MOFs from structural prototypes within the QMOF database.

### [97] [Fragment-Constrained Charge Equilibration for Charge-Aware Machine Learning Potentials at Electrochemical Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27910)
*Akhil Reddy Peeketi,Blas P Uberuaga,Travis E Jones*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种可微分的软片段约束电荷均衡（Soft-FQEq）方法，使反应性机器学习原子间势（MLIP）能够恢复电极-电解质界面的电化学势梯度，克服了全局电荷均衡（QEq）方法无法维持双电层界面梯度的根本缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电化学界面的预测模拟需要能同时捕捉反应性键重排、长程静电以及反映电极与电解质电子区分的电荷分布，但现有基于全局电荷均衡（global QEq）的电荷感知机器学习原子间势（charge-aware MLIPs）会将电极与电解质置于同一电化学势，无法保留双电层（double layer）所需的界面梯度，并允许电子不相连区域间产生虚假电荷转移。

Method: 将片段识别（fragment identification）本身构造为原子几何的可微分函数，提出软片段约束电荷均衡（Soft-FQEq）求解层（solver layer），以恢复反应性MLIP中的片段分辨电荷守恒（fragment-resolved charge conservation）。该层从共享原子特征网络（atomic-feature network）中接收每原子电负性（per-atom electronegativity）、源电荷（source charge）、短程能量（short-range energy）与软键连通性（soft bond connectivity）四个标量MLP读出值，返回均衡电荷及每片段化学势（per-fragment chemical potential）。在IrO2/H2O/Na+/ClO4-界面上基于HIP-NN特征网络与DFT能量、力和DDEC6电荷训练。

Result: 训练后的模型恢复了清晰的电极到电解质的每原子电化学势梯度。在相同训练权重下，将片段约束求解器替换为全局QEq进行推理时，该梯度坍缩为近似均匀分布，直接证明全局QEq无法维持该梯度，而片段化公式（fragment formulation）可以恢复它。

Conclusion: Soft-FQEq通过将片段识别可微化，在反应性MLIP中实现了片段约束电荷均衡，能有效恢复电化学界面的电势梯度，为电化学界面的预测模拟提供了关键方法论进展。

Abstract: Predictive simulation of electrochemical interfaces requires atomistic models that capture reactive bond rearrangements, long-range electrostatics, and charge distributions reflecting the electronic distinctness of electrode and electrolyte. Existing charge-aware machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) built on global charge equilibration (QEq) settle electrode and electrolyte at a common electrochemical potential, leaving no room for the interfacial gradient that the double layer requires and admitting spurious charge transfer between electronically disconnected regions. Per-fragment charge equilibration is the established remedy in classical molecular dynamics, but reliance on predefined molecular topology has confined it to non-reactive systems. We lift this restriction by making fragment identification itself a differentiable function of atomic geometry, yielding soft fragment-constrained charge equilibration (Soft-FQEq) -- a solver layer that restores fragment-resolved charge conservation in reactive MLIPs. The layer consumes four scalar MLP readouts from a shared atomic-feature network -- per-atom electronegativity, source charge, short-range energy, and a soft bond connectivity -- and returns equilibrated charges together with per-fragment chemical potentials. We implement Soft-FQEq as an extension of the hippynn framework on a HIP-NN feature network and train it on DFT energies, forces, and DDEC6 charges for IrO2/H2O/Na+/ClO4- interfaces. The trained model recovers a clear electrode-to-electrolyte gradient in the per-atom electrochemical potential. With the same trained weights but the fragment-constrained solver replaced by global QEq at inference, this gradient collapses to an essentially uniform profile, directly showing that the gradient cannot be sustained within global QEq while the fragment formulation recovers it.

</details>


### [98] [Anharmonic phonon coupling enabled by local inversion symmetry breaking at domain walls in ferroelastic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28066)
*Seyyed Jabbar Mousavi,Vivek Unikandanunni,Niccolo Sellati,Paolo Barone,Martina Basini,Steven L. Johnson,Andrey Shalit,Peter Hamm,Mattia Udina,Thomas Feurer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用二维拉曼-太赫兹光谱（two-dimensional Raman-terahertz spectroscopy）直接证明了铁弹材料LaAlO$_3$中由于畴壁处反演对称性破缺（inversion symmetry breaking）所导致的局域非简谐声子耦合（anharmonic phonon coupling）的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁弹材料（ferroelastic materials）中畴壁（domain walls）处可能发生局域反演对称性破缺，从而改变声子选择定则并允许局域非简谐声子耦合，但缺乏直接实验证据。

Method: 采用二维拉曼-太赫兹光谱技术，对铁弹LaAlO$_3$进行实验测量，分析二维光谱中的交叉峰（cross-peaks）信号。

Result: 二维光谱中的交叉峰来源于$A_{1g}$拉曼活性声子与$E_g$声子之间的力学非简谐性（mechanical anharmonicity）和电学非简谐性（electrical anharmonicity）；其中$E_g$声子因铁弹畴壁处的局域反演对称性破缺而获得了有限的红外活性（infrared activity）。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了铁弹材料中复杂的晶格动力学行为，并展示了二维拉曼-太赫兹光谱在探测微弱对称性破缺及内禀弱非简谐信号方面的潜力。

Abstract: In ferroelastic materials, spontaneous symmetry breaking leads to the formation of twin domains. Although the bulk crystal typically remains centrosymmetric, inversion symmetry can be locally broken at the domain walls, potentially changing phonon selection rules and enabling local anharmonic phonon coupling. Here we report direct evidence of such anharmonic coupling in ferroelastic LaAlO$_3$ using two-dimensional Raman-terahertz spectroscopy. We attribute the cross-peaks observed in the two-dimensional spectra to both mechanical and electrical anharmonicity between the $A_{1g}$ Raman-active phonon and the $E_g$ phonon, which acquires finite infrared activity through local inversion symmetry breaking at ferroelastic domain walls. These findings provide new insight into the complex lattice dynamics of ferroelastic materials and highlight the potential of two-dimensional Raman-terahertz spectroscopy to uncover subtle symmetry breaking through the detection of intrinsically weak anharmonic signals.

### [99] [Quantifying Thermal, Photovoltage, and Defect Contributions to Transient Absorption of Ta$_{3}$N$_{5}$ Photoanodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28094)
*Johannes Dittloff,Lukas M. Wolz,Matthias U. Quintern,Laura I. Wagner,Matthias Kuhl,Johanna Eichhorn,Ian D. Sharp*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过微秒到秒级瞬态吸收光谱（transient absorption spectroscopy）结合互补光学光谱方法，系统解耦了Ta₃N₅薄膜中来自晶格加热、静电效应和缺陷态的贡献，阐明了光生载流子激发与弛豫机制，并量化了热动力学、表面光电压动力学及缺陷电荷态再分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ta₃N₅是一种广泛研究的太阳光驱动水氧化（solar-driven water oxidation）光阳极材料，但其性能受限于短载流子寿命（carrier lifetime）和缺陷介导的复合（defect-mediated recombination）。尽管瞬态吸收光谱被广泛用于探测光电极中的载流子动力学，但由于光谱贡献重叠，谱峰归属常存在歧义。因此，需要一种系统方法解耦不同物理过程的贡献。

Method: 本研究结合了微秒到秒时间尺度的瞬态吸收光谱与互补光学光谱技术，对Ta₃N₅薄膜进行表征。通过光反射谱（photoreflectance）识别能带结构中的关键临界点，并利用电位依赖性测量区分近边漂白特征（bleach features）源于能带展平（band flattening）与表面光电压弛豫（surface photovoltage relaxation）。通过将瞬态吸收光谱与独立测量的热和静电组分拟合，实现对热动力学和光电压动力学的定量分析。

Result: 光反射谱揭示了Ta₃N₅能带结构中的三个临界点：2.14 eV和2.27 eV的两个各向异性近边跃迁（anisotropic near-edge transition），以及约2.80 eV的高能跃迁，这些均与主要的瞬态吸收特征高度吻合。首次报道了2.80 eV处的光致吸收（photo-induced absorption），归因于泵浦诱导的晶格加热（pump-induced lattice heating）。电位依赖性测量显示，近边漂白特征源于泵浦诱导的能带展平及随后的表面光电压弛豫。亚带隙响应（sub-bandgap response）揭示缺陷电荷态（defect charge state）的再分布。

Conclusion: 所提出的热、静电和缺陷介导贡献的解耦方法，能够量化微秒到秒时间尺度下Ta₃N₅中的热动力学和光电压动力学，并为功能性半导体光电极（semiconductor photoelectrode）中的光激发与弛豫机制提供了广泛适用的见解。

Abstract: Ta$_{3}$N$_{5}$ is among the most intensively studied photoanode materials for solar-driven water oxidation, yet its performance often remains limited by short carrier lifetimes and defect mediated recombination. Although transient absorption spectroscopy is widely used to probe carrier dynamics in photoelectrodes, spectral assignments are frequently ambiguous due to overlapping contributions. Here, microsecond-to-second transient absorption of Ta$_{3}$N$_{5}$ thin films is combined with complementary optical spectroscopies to disentangle contributions from lattice heating, electrostatics, and defect states. Photoreflectance reveals three critical points in the Ta$_{3}$N$_{5}$ band structure, including two anisotropic near-edge transitions at 2.14 eV and 2.27 eV and a higher-lying transition near 2.80 eV, all closely aligned with dominant transient absorption features. A previously unreported photo-induced absorption at 2.80 eV is attributed to pump-induced lattice heating, while potential-dependent measurements reveal that near-edge bleach features arise from pump-induced band flattening and subsequent surface photovoltage relaxation. Fitting transient absorption spectra with independently measured thermal and electrostatic components enables quantification of both thermal and photovoltage dynamics, while the sub-bandgap response provides insight into the redistribution of defect charge states. Thus, this approach to quantifying thermal, electrostatic, and defect-mediated contributions to microsecond-to-second transient absorption provides broadly applicable insights into photoexcitation and relaxation mechanisms in functional semiconductor photoelectrodes.

### [100] [Yukawa screening derivation of the bond-valence rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28099)
*Michael L. Whittaker,Pan Wang,Chunhui Li,Naman Katyal,Piotr Zarzycki*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文从屏蔽库仑静电作用（screened Coulomb electrostatics）中推导出键价模型（bond-valence model）的指数形式，将键价柔软度（bond-valence softness）解释为电子屏蔽长度（electronic screening length），从而将键价从经验拟合规则转变为可迁移的局域屏蔽电荷响应描述符，并通过对大量阳离子-氧物种键价参数的拟合以及第一性原理电荷密度的比较，验证了该理论预测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 键价模型虽被广泛用于估算晶体中的键强度，但其键长指数依赖形式一直缺乏基于具体物理相互作用的推导，这使得该模型停留在经验拟合规则层面，缺乏物理基础与可迁移性。

Method: 作者从屏蔽库仑静电作用出发，证明键价模型的指数形式是其领头阶（leading-order）极限；通过将键价柔软度参数解释为电子屏蔽长度，构建了一个可用于预测键价参数随离子电荷（ionic charge）与配位数（coordination number）变化的理论框架，并利用94种阳离子-氧物种的150个拟合键价以及第一性原理（first-principles）电荷密度数据进行验证。

Result: 理论预测与94种阳离子-氧物种中150个拟合键价的丰度加权决定系数（abundance-weighted coefficient of determination）为0.986；键价壳半径（bond-valence shell radius）与电子屏蔽云的比较显示，在10种碱金属与碱土金属氧化物中决定系数为0.9998，在其他21种二元氧化物中为0.967。

Conclusion: 广泛使用的键价模型实际上是离子固体中屏蔽静电作用的领头阶表达式，从而为其提供了明确的物理基础与可迁移的预测能力。

Abstract: The bond-valence model is a standard way to estimate bond strengths in crystals, but its exponential dependence on bond length has lacked a derivation from a specific physical interaction. We show that this form emerges as the leading-order limit of screened Coulomb electrostatics and that the fitted bond-valence softness can be interpreted in terms of an electronic screening length. This turns bond valence from an empirical fitting rule into a transferable descriptor of local screened charge response across coordination environments. The resulting theory predicts how the bond-valence parameters should vary with ionic charge and coordination number, and that prediction agrees with 150 fitted valences from 94 cation-oxygen species, including 68 in fourfold coordination and 82 in sixfold coordination, at an abundance-weighted coefficient of determination of 0.986. A comparison with first-principles charge densities shows that the bond-valence shell radius tracks the electronic screening cloud with coefficients of determination of 0.9998 for ten alkali and alkaline-earth oxides and 0.967 for 21 other binary oxides whose nearest-neighbor environments match the theory's assumptions. The widely used bond-valence model is thus the leading-order expression of screened electrostatics in ionic solids.

</details>


### [101] [Radio Frequency Field-Induced Enhancement of Detection Sensitivity in Silicon Nanowire Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28100)
*Ang Liu,Jingsong Shang,Jiangang J. Du,Shyamsunder Erramilli,Pritiraj Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于硅纳米线场效应晶体管（silicon nanowire field-effect transistor）中挠曲电共振（flexoelectric resonance）的生物传感方法。通过施加射频电场诱导纳米线产生应变梯度，在共振频率下放大挠曲电极化，从而增强对生物分子结合引起的表面电荷变化的检测灵敏度。以C反应蛋白（C-reactive protein）为模型，实验观察到灵敏度提升一个数量级，且在生理高盐环境下有效抑制德拜屏蔽（Debye screening），无需样品稀释即可实现直接检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生理体液中生物标志物的灵敏检测常受德拜屏蔽（Debye screening）限制——该效应会抑制传感器表面的静电信号，导致传统检测方法在高离子强度环境下灵敏度不足。

Method: 在硅纳米线场效应晶体管（silicon nanowire field-effect transistor）中施加射频电场（radiofrequency field），诱导纳米线产生应变梯度（strain gradients），从而在共振频率（resonant frequencies）下放大挠曲电极化（flexoelectric polarization），增强电导测量对生物分子结合引起的小表面电荷变化的灵敏度。同时，高频电场扰动电双层（electrical double layer），降低高离子强度环境中的德拜屏蔽效应。

Result: 以C反应蛋白（C-reactive protein）为模型生物标志物的实验中，相比常规操作，检测灵敏度提升一个数量级：施加射频调制时电导增加62%，而无调制时仅增加30%。

Conclusion: 挠曲电共振（flexoelectric resonance）可作为一种通用策略，在生理相关条件下提升纳米级生物传感性能，实现无需样品稀释的直接生物标志物检测。

Abstract: Sensitive biomarker detection in physiological fluids is often limited by Debye screening, which suppresses electrostatic signals at sensor surfaces. Here we report a sensing approach based on flexoelectric resonance in silicon nanowire field-effect transistors. An applied radiofrequency field induces strain gradients in the nanowires, generating flexoelectric polarization that is amplified at resonant frequencies. This effect enhances the sensitivity of conductance measurements to small surface charge variations associated with biomolecular binding. Using C-reactive protein as a model biomarker, we observe an order-of-magnitude improvement in detection sensitivity compared to conventional operation, with a 62% conductance increase versus 30% without radiofrequency modulation. The high-frequency field also perturbs the electrical double layer, reducing Debye screening in high-ionic-strength environments. These combined effects enable direct biomarker detection without sample dilution. This work establishes flexoelectric resonance as a general strategy for improving nanoscale biosensing performance in physiologically relevant conditions.

</details>


### [102] [From Narrow-gap Semiconductor to Metallic Altermagnet: Optical Fingerprints of Co-Doped FeSb$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28105)
*R. Mathew Roy,M. Povolotskiy,J. Kirschke,C. Prange,Y. Xia,V. Sundaramurthy,P. Puphal,M. Pinteric,M. van de Loo,A. Kreyssig,T. Zhang,A. E. Böhmer,M. Dressel,M. Wenzel*

TL;DR: 通过适量钴替代（~15%）将关联窄带隙半导体FeSb₂转变为可在室温下持续存在的金属态交变磁性（altermagnetic）材料；光谱学与第一性原理计算揭示了源于非相对论性自旋分裂和自旋-轨道耦合能带分裂的低能带间跃迁，以及增强的电子-声子耦合与局域反演对称性破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用适度钴替代（~15%）掺杂调控FeSb₂；利用红外光学电导谱（infrared optical conductivity）测量低能带间跃迁；结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算分析自旋分裂能带结构和自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）效应。

Result: 掺杂后在0.1 eV附近出现低能带间跃迁，且随Co浓度增加而增强；DFT表明这些跃迁完全源于交变磁性自旋排序，产生了~0.2 meV的非相对论性自旋分裂带和~5 meV的自旋-轨道耦合能带分裂；Co替代还导致红外活性声子呈现Fano线型与模式杂化，反映电子-声子耦合增强及局域反演对称性破缺，但交变磁性自旋对称性保持完整。

Conclusion: 载流子调控的FeSb₂可作为探索金属态d波交变磁性（metallic d-wave altermagnetism）及其与晶格自由度（lattice degrees of freedom）耦合的实验平台。

Abstract: The realization of bulk metallic altermagnetism has remained elusive despite the growing number of candidate materials. Here, we present evidence that moderate cobalt substitution ($\sim$15%) drives the correlated narrow-gap semiconductor FeSb$_2$ into a metallic altermagnetic state persisting up to room temperature. The infrared optical conductivity reveals low-energy interband transitions near 0.1 eV that emerge upon doping and grow with Co concentration. Density functional theory calculations show that these transitions originate exclusively from altermagnetic spin ordering, with spin split bands ($\sim$0.2 meV) of non-relativistic origin, together with spin-orbit coupling induced band splitting of the order of $\sim$5 meV near the Fermi level. Co substitution further leads to Fano lineshapes and mode mixing in the infrared-active phonons, reflecting enhanced electron-phonon coupling and local inversion symmetry breaking, while leaving the altermagnetic spin symmetry intact. Our results establish carrier-tuned FeSb$_2$ as a platform for exploring metallic $d$-wave altermagnetism and its coupling to lattice degrees of freedom.

### [103] [Machine Learning and Molecular Simulations Reveal Mechanisms of ZIFs Polymorph Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28106)

Abstract: Zn(imidazolate)$_2$ metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) exhibit a remarkable degree of polymorphism. There is now wide consensus in the research community that these MOFs are solvothermally formed via non-classical nucleation mechanisms, in which pre-nucleation clusters are first formed, followed by an intermediate amorphous structure that subsequently reorganizes to yield the final crystalline MOF. However, no study up to date has uncovered which part of the synthesis process determines the final polymorph obtained. In this work, path collective variable metadynamics simulations performed with a partially reactive force field give insights into mechanistic and thermodynamic aspects of the self-assembly of these MOFs. Databases of transient and intermediate synthesis structures are built from the simulations. By developing and applying neural network classifiers over these databases, it is found that both pre-nucleation clusters and the amorphous intermediate structures are polymorph-dependent. These results suggest that polymorph selection happens as early as the pre-nucleation cluster stage.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 释放外延SrRuO3薄膜的衬底以驱动铁弹畴细化；使用关联显微术，包括介观电子通道衬度成像（ECCI）和原子分辨扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）进行表征；结合第一性原理（ab initio）计算验证边界处的倾斜场插值行为。

Conclusion: 在薄膜形态下，金属氧化物为容纳产生极性织构的纳米尺度铁弹畴提供了一个稳健平台。

Engineering polar textures in a conducting magnet holds promise for reconfigurable spin orbit coupling and magnetoelectric functionality. Here we show that releasing epitaxial SrRuO3 films from their substrates drives a hierarchy of ferroelastic domain refinement from micrometre to nanometre length scales, and that this structural reorganisation spontaneously generates two distinct classes of emergent polar texture that are ubiquitous across the freestanding membrane. Using correlative microscopy from mesoscale electron channelling contrast imaging (ECCI) to atomic resolution scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM), we demonstrate that electric polarisation emerges selectively at translation-inequivalent antiphase boundaries (APBs). At these boundaries multicomponent aac tilt field undergoes Neel-like interpolation that preserves the in-phase tilt component and amplifies roto flexoelectric coupling, while translation-equivalent boundaries remain nonpolar. The Neel like interpolation at hard APBs and Ising like collapse of all tilt components at easy APBs is corroborated with ab initio calculations. While embedded 90 ferroelastic walls provide an additional mechanistically distinct source of electric polarisation resulting in polar nanoclusters (4 nm). These distinct nanotextures at 90 walls from via elastic accommodation of strain mismatch between variants and rotostriction as the tilt field interpolates across the boundaries. These findings show that, in a membrane form, metal oxides provide a robust platform for hosting nanoscale ferroelastic domains that generate polar textures.

### [106] [Multi-scale calculation of light-induced structural changes in low-angle twisted bilayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28143)
*Rafael R. Del Grande,David A. Strubbe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过结合经典力场弛豫和第一性原理GW/Bethe-Salpeter激发态力（excited state forces），揭示了1.1°扭转双层WSe₂中光致层间距变化的微观机制：面内应变软化层间力常数，同时增强激发态力，二者协同使得扭转体系的光致层间距变化比完美堆叠体系更强，证明扭转双层过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）中的激子-声子相互作用可被调控。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将经典力场弛豫（classical force field relaxation）与基于第一性原理GW/Bethe-Salpeter方程（GW/Bethe-Salpeter equation）的激发态力（excited state forces, ESF）计算相结合，克服了莫尔原胞过大的计算瓶颈。

Result: 弛豫结果表明：小角度扭转诱导出面内应变场（in-plane strain field），AB区域足够大可作为周期性AB堆叠双层WSe₂模拟，且层间力常数相对于完美AB堆叠变软。ESF计算表明：面内应变增大了面外激发态力。两个效应（层间力常数弱化与ESF的应变依赖性）共同导致扭转双层WSe₂中光致层间距变化强于完美堆叠情形。

Conclusion: 扭转双层TMD中的激子-声子相互作用可被扭转角调控，并可通过实验观测，使其成为研究光致材料变化的优异平台。

Abstract: Exciton-phonon interactions in transition metal dichalcogenides (TMD) are strong and lead to phenomena such as coherent phonon generation. When stacked and twisted, their properties can be tuned by the twisting angle. In experiments with 1.1$^\circ$ twisted 2L WSe$_2$, a change of 0.1 Å in the interlayer distance was observed when light was shone on this material, and here we explain the microscopic mechanism behind this. Theoretical works to study such systems are limited because the Moiré unit cell is too large. To overcome this, we combined classical force field relaxations with our implementation of ab initio GW/Bethe-Salpeter excited state forces (ESF). From the relaxations we found that the low-angle twisting induced an in-plane strain field, the AB regions are large enough to be simulated as periodic AB stacked 2L WSe2, and the interlayer force constant becomes softer in relation to the perfect AB stacking. From the ab initio ESF we obtained that the in-plane strain increases the out of plane ESFs. Those two effects combined, the weakening of the interlayer force constant and strain dependence of the ESF, make light-induced changes in the interlayer distance of twisted 2L WSe2 stronger than in the perfectly stacked case, in agreement with experimental observations. Therefore, our results show that the exciton-phonon interactions can be tuned in twisted 2L TMDs and can be observed experimentally, which makes those materials excellent platforms to study light-induced changes in materials.

### [107] [Strong coupling between quantized magnon modes in a YIG microstucture and microwaves in a superconducting resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28145)
*Seth W. Kurfman,Philipp Geyer,Anoop Kamalasanan,Karl Heimrich,Kwangyul Hu,Paul Tharnier,Frank Heyroth,Michael Flatté,Georg Schmidt*

Conclusion: 该研究所发展的制备技术和器件几何结构能够以显著降低的功率，在不同磁场强度和方向下确定性利用微米级YIG结构中的多个受限磁振子模式。这为在微米尺度YIG磁元件上实现高效的基于磁振子的强耦合片上实验建立了基础性路径。

Abstract: Strong-coupling experiments based on magnons enable the exploration into on-chip demonstrations involving numerous long-lived excitations. Yttrium iron garnet (YIG) has been considered for decades as a gold standard material for magnonics due to its low-loss magnonic properties. While YIG has successfully demonstrated strong-coupling in macroscopic device geometries, the strong coupling of magnons in truly sub-10 micron YIG structures to date has not yet been realized. This obstacle is due to the difficulty producing large enough effective magnonic mode volume necessary primarily due to thickness limitations of YIG deposition and device fabrication techniques. Here, we demonstrate the use of a microplatelet of YIG, manufactured from a single crystal of YIG via focused ion beam (FIB) techniques, placed on a constricted inductive line of an optimized superconducting lumped element LC resonator to achieve strong coupling between numerous magnon modes and the LC resonator photons. These experimental findings are qualitatively backed by micromagnetic simulations and quantitatively supported by analytical calculations to identify the magnon modes corresponding to the experimentally observed anti-crossings in the microwave transmission signal. Further, we show that these anti-crossings remain even at incredibly low device input powers ($\leq 10$ fW). The fabrication techniques and device geometry enable the deterministic use of numerous confined magnon modes in micron-scale YIG structures for various magnetic field strengths and orientations at substantially reduced device powers. The results here establish a foundational path forward to achieving efficient magnon-based strong-coupling experiments in micron-scale YIG magnetic elements for effective on-chip studies.

</details>


### [108] [Uniaxial strain-driven ferroelastic domain control in LaAlO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28183)
*Matthias Roeper,Robin Buschbeck,Jakob Wetzel,Tobias Ritschel,Anna-Lena Hofmann,Vladyslav Kovtunovych,Mike N. Pionteck,Javier Taboada-Gutiérrez,Alexey B. Kuzmenko,Martina Basini,Vivek Unikandanunni,Iuliia Kiseleva,Jochen Geck,Susanne C. Kehr,Maximilian Lederer,Simone Sanna,Lukas M. Eng,Samuel D. Seddon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过在单晶LaAlO₃中施加原位单轴应变（uniaxial strain），实现了铁弹畴结构（ferroelastic domain structure）的连续、可逆操控，并结合原子力显微镜、X射线衍射、拉曼光谱与第一性原理计算，完整揭示了从菱方R3̄c基态向正交Fmmm相的应变驱动畴演化过程，建立了单轴应变作为铁弹畴工程可控参量的技术路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多铁性氧化物中的畴壁（domain walls）在纳米电子与光子器件中具有重要应用价值，但现有对畴群体的控制手段局限于局部操控或热移除，缺乏连续、可逆的全局调控方法。

Method: 采用原位单轴应变（in-situ uniaxial strain）作用于单晶LaAlO₃，结合原子力显微镜（AFM）、X射线衍射（XRD）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）以及第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），系统表征孪晶畴群体（twin domain population）在应变驱动下的微观演化过程。

Result: 在低于0.5%的应变条件下，观察到显著的表面平坦化与大规模畴重组；完整映射了从菱方R3̄c相向正交Fmmm相的应变驱动转变路径；证明了单轴应变可作为技术上可访问的铁弹畴工程控制参数。

Conclusion: 该工作为实现LaAlO₃基异质结构中畴架构的主动实时编程开辟了新途径，对应变可调超导界面（strain-tunable superconducting interfaces）、纳米尺度声子-极化激元光学（nanoscale phonon-polariton optics）以及超快晶格控制（ultrafast lattice control）具有潜在影响。

Abstract: Multiferroic domain walls in functional oxides exhibit properties distinct from the bulk and are increasingly exploited as active elements in nanoelectronic and photonic devices. Deterministic control of domain populations has typically remained limited to local control, or removal with temperature. Here we demonstrate continuous, reversible manipulation of the ferroelastic domain structure in single-crystal LaAlO$_3$ using in-situ uniaxial strain. Combining atomic force microscopy, X-ray diffraction, and Raman spectroscopy with first-principles calculations we map the complete microscopic evolution of the twin domain population through the strain-driven transition from the rhombohedral $R\bar{3}c$ ground state toward the predicted orthorhombic $Fmmm$ phase. Applied strains below $0.5\%$ produce pronounced surface flattening and large-scale domain reorganisation, establishing uniaxial strain as a technically accessible control parameter for ferroelastic domain engineering. These results open a route to active, real-time programming of domain architectures in LaAlO$_3$-based heterostructures, with implications for strain-tunable superconducting interfaces, nanoscale phonon-polariton optics, and ultrafast lattice control.

</details>

### [109] [When Two Loops Matter: Electroweak Precision in the SMEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26817)
*Lukas Born,Admir Greljo,Anders Eller Thomsen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）的维度-6算符中识别出一种新的次领头阶重整化效应，该效应通过大反常维度在双圈阶诱导顶希格斯耦合κ_t对W玻色子质量的偏移，使得电弱精密可观测量成为κ_t的强力间接探针，并对未来Tera-Z和Giga-W工厂（如FCC-ee）的数据解释至关重要，该效应可在简单的可重整双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）中维度-6算符的次领头阶（next-to-leading order）重整化效应，并揭示其对电弱精密可观测量（electroweak precision observables）的直接影响，从而为顶希格斯耦合（top-Higgs coupling）κ_t的间接探测提供新的理论工具。

Method: 通过计算维度-6希格斯-汤川算符（Higgs-Yukawa operator）的双圈阶（two-loop order）反常维度（anomalous dimension），分析该算符对W玻色子质量的偏移效应，并在可重整的双希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs doublet model, 2HDM）中实现该效应。

Result: 发现维度-6希格斯-汤川算符通过大反常维度在双圈阶诱导W玻色子质量的偏移，从而将电弱精密可观测量转化为κ_t的强力间接探针。

Conclusion: 该次领头阶重整化效应对未来Tera-Z和Giga-W工厂（如FCC-ee）数据的一致解释不可或缺，为κ_t的间接探测提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: We identify a novel next-to-leading order renormalization effect in the dimension-six SMEFT with direct phenomenological impact. The Higgs-Yukawa operator that modifies the top-Higgs coupling $κ_t$ induces a shift in the $ W $ mass at two-loop order through a large anomalous dimension, rendering electroweak precision observables a powerful indirect probe of $κ_t$. We show that this effect is essential for the consistent interpretation of data from future Tera-$Z$ and Giga-$W$ factories such as FCC-ee. The effect is realized in a simple renormalizable two-Higgs doublet model.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠缠作为量子理论的基本现象，近期已在高能物理过程中被观测到。这为在相对论性（relativistic）区域探测量子效应开辟了新途径，但也带来了概念性与技术性挑战。现有方法在分析自旋-自旋纠缠时，由于相对论运动使自旋与动量耦合，且所研究粒子的动量无法实验控制，因此需要改进。

Method: 基于阴影层析（shadow tomography）技术，发展了一个通用理论框架，用于表征对撞机实验中的自旋-自旋关联，从而更有效地分析自旋-自旋纠缠。

Result: 以欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）上的顶夸克对产生为例，展示了该形式体系的应用，作为概念验证（proof of concept）。该框架具有通用性与灵活性。

Conclusion: 该框架可被直接应用于更复杂的末态（final states）和包含更多粒子的系统，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Entanglement, a fundamental phenomenon of quantum theory, has recently been observed in processes in high-energy physics. This opens new avenues for probing quantum effects in relativistic regimes, but also poses conceptual and technical challenges. We develop a general framework based on shadow tomography techniques for characterising spin-spin correlations in collider experiments. This improves the analysis of spin-spin entanglement, where relativistic motion couples spin and momentum and the momenta of the investigated particles are not under experimental control. As a proof of concept we illustrate the application of our formalism to top quark pair production at the Large Hadron Collider at CERN. The framework, however, is general and flexible and can be readily applied to more complex final states and systems with more particles.

</details>

### [112] [Theoretical and Experimental Constraints in the $μ$--$τ$ Four-Lepton Sector of the SMEFT: implications to neutrino self interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27716)
*Aadarsh Singh,G. D'Ambrosio,Sudhir K. Vempati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在μ-τ扇区研究维数六SMEFT四轻子算符，综合比较幺正性、正性和实验约束三种方法，发现全局拟合主导部分算符系数而NA64μ主导另一方向，并将界限转化为有效四中微子耦合，排除了哈勃张力所驱动的强自相互作用的重中介体紫外完备化方案，同时承认轻中介体场景不受此分析约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 维数六SMEFT四轻子算符同时控制带电轻子散射和中微子自相互作用，后者在宇宙学张力（如哈勃张力）中有潜在重要性，但直接实验室探针对其约束较弱，因此需要系统性比较不同约束手段的有效性。

Method: 基于华沙基（Warsaw basis）系数[Cℓℓ]2222、[Cℓℓ]2233和[Cℓℓ]2332，采用三类约束方法：(1) 从2→2分波分析（partial-wave analysis）得到的微扰幺正性（perturbative unitarity）；(2) 自旋求和的正性和（positivity sum rules）；(3) NA64μ实验界限及全局拟合（global fit）的实验约束。此外还考虑了重整化群（renormalization-group）在1 GeV至30 TeV能标间的跑动效应。

Result: 全局拟合对[Cℓℓ]2222和[Cℓℓ]2332的约束最强，NA64μ对[Cℓℓ]2233给出领先界限，且该方向的幺正性线进入约200 GeV的对撞能量范围。重整化群跑动对系数的修正不超过10%。转化为有效四中微子耦合Geff后，上限远小于哈勃张力（Hubble tension）所预期的强相互作用区域。

Conclusion: 在维数六SMEFT有效范围内且无算符间精细抵消（tuned cancellations）的前提下，排除了强νμ-νμ和νμ-ντ自相互作用的重中介体紫外完备化（UV completion）；宇宙学上激发的轻中介体场景不受此分析约束。基于SMEFT的NA64μ界限复现了文献中已有的专用Z'分析结果。

Abstract: We study the dimension-six SMEFT four-lepton operators in the $μ$--$τ$ sector. These operators control both charged-lepton scattering and neutrino self-interactions, the latter being weakly constrained by direct laboratory probes despite their importance for cosmological tensions. We compare three classes of constraints on the Warsaw-basis coefficients $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2222}$, $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2233}$, and $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2332}$. We use perturbative unitarity from $2\!\to\!2$ partial-wave analysis, spin-summing positivity sum rules, and the experimental bounds from NA64$μ$ and the global fit~\cite{Falkowski:2017pss}. We find that the global fit dominates for $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2222}$ and $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2332}$, while NA64$μ$ provides the leading bound on $[C_{\ell\ell}]_{2233}$, with the unitarity line for this direction entering the range of collider energies near $200~\mathrm{GeV}$. Renormalization-group running between $1~\mathrm{GeV}$ and $30~\mathrm{TeV}$ modifies these coefficients by up to $10\%$. Translating these bounds onto the effective four-neutrino coupling $G_\mathrm{eff}$, we find values many orders of magnitude smaller than the strongly interacting regime motivated by the Hubble tension; this excludes heavy-mediator UV completions of strong $ν_μ$--$ν_μ$ and $ν_μ$--$ν_τ$ self-interactions within the validity of the dimension-six SMEFT and in the absence of tuned cancellations between operators, while leaving the cosmologically motivated light-mediator scenarios unconstrained by this analysis. Finally, we comment on the bounds these coefficients place on a leptophilic $L_μ- L_τ$ $Z'$ UV completion. Our SMEFT-based current and projected NA64$μ$ bounds reproduce the dedicated $Z'$ analyses already available in the literature.

*Motoi Endo,Syuhei Iguro,Satoshi Mishima*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了涉及轨道激发粲强子的b→c τ ν̄半轻子衰变求和规则，分析了与小速度极限的偏差，发现激发态强子参与时偏差增大，张量贡献效应显著，但当前形状因子约束不足，需改进强子输入以获得稳健的轻子普适性比值预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索涉及轨道激发粲强子（orbitally excited charm hadrons）的半轻子过程b→c τ ν̄中的求和规则（sum rules），以理解重夸克对称性（heavy quark symmetry）在非极限情况下的行为，并为轻子普适性（lepton universality）比值的精确计算奠定基础。

Method: 从重夸克对称性在振幅层次（amplitude level）导出的关系出发，构建求和规则连接这些衰变过程；随后考察与小速度极限（small-velocity limit, SV limit）的偏差，并进行数值分析。

Result: 数值分析显示，一旦激发态强子参与，与SV极限的偏差通常会增大，其中张量贡献（tensor contributions）常引发显著效应；但当前相关形状因子（form factors）的约束尚不充分。

Conclusion: 要使得这些求和规则对相应的轻子普适性比值（lepton-universality ratios）产生稳健预言，进一步改进强子输入（hadronic inputs）是必不可少的。

Abstract: We study semileptonic sum rules for $b \to c τ\overlineν$ transitions involving orbitally excited charm hadrons. Starting from the amplitude-level relation implied by the heavy quark symmetry, we construct sum rules relating these decays. We then examine deviations from the small-velocity limit. Our numerical analysis shows that the deviations generally increase once excited hadrons are involved, with tensor contributions often inducing sizable effects. At present, however, the relevant form factors are not yet sufficiently constrained. Further improvements in the hadronic inputs are essential for these sum rules to yield robust predictions for the corresponding lepton-universality ratios.

Abstract: We investigate the photoproduction of the tensor meson $f_2(1270)$ on the proton within a Regge-based framework, focusing on the reaction $γp \to p f_2(1270)$ in the few-GeV energy region. The production mechanism is modeled through the exchange of vector-meson Regge trajectories in the $t$-channel, including both $ρ$ and $ω$ exchanges with phenomenologically motivated couplings. The scattering amplitudes are derived using Reggeized propagators and effective hadronic vertices, allowing for the calculation of differential cross sections in the narrow-width approximation. We further extend the analysis to the $π^+π^-$ invariant mass distribution by incorporating a relativistic Breit--Wigner description of the $f_2(1270)$ resonance.

### [115] [Deeply virtual pion production through two-loop order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28164)
*Wen Chen,Feng Feng,Yu Jia,Qing-Tao Song,Guang Tang,Zhe-Yu Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了深度虚介子产生（DVMP）过程在广义Bjorken极限下的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD辐射修正，发现双圈QCD修正显著为正，能大幅改善微扰QCD预言与JLab实验数据的一致性，并进一步研究了该修正对横向单自旋不对称性（TSSA）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度虚介子产生（DVMP）是提取核子广义部分子分布（GPDs）的重要过程渠道，对揭示核子的三维内部结构至关重要。然而，此前相关过程的微扰QCD计算尚未达到次次领头阶（NNLO）精度，需要更精确的理论预言以匹配实验需求。

Method: 在广义Bjorken极限（$Q^2\gg |t|, \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}^2$）下，基于共线因子化框架（collinear factorization framework），在领头扭度（leading twist）精度下首次计算了深度虚π介子产生（DVπP）过程 $\gamma_L^* p\to \pi^+ n$ 和 $\gamma_L^* p\to \pi^0 p$ 的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD辐射修正。

Result: 双圈QCD修正为正且幅度显著；纳入该修正后，微扰QCD预言与JLab现有实验数据的一致性得到大幅改善。此外，还展示了该修正对JLab、EIC和EicC实验基准运动学下横向单自旋不对称性（TSSA）的影响。

Conclusion: 次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD辐射修正对于深度虚介子产生过程（DVMP）的理论预言至关重要，能够显著提升与实验数据的吻合程度，并有助于在未来的电子-质子（$ep$）散射设施上更精确地提取核子的广义部分子分布（GPDs）。

Abstract: Deeply virtual meson production (DVMP) is among the most prominent channels to extract the nucleon's generalized parton distributions (GPDs) at $ep$ scattering facilities such as {\tt JLab} and the upcoming {\tt EIC/EicC} experiments, which plays a vital role in unravelling the three-dimensional internal structure of nucleon. In this work we calculate for the first time the next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD radiative corrections to the DV$π$P processes $γ_L^* p\to π^+ n$ and $γ_L^* p\to π^0 p$ in the generalized Bjorken limit $Q^2\gg \vert t\vert, Λ_{\text{QCD}}^2$, accurate at the leading twist within collinear factorization framework. The impact of the two-loop QCD corrections appears to be positive and substantial, including which considerably improves the agreement between the perturbative QCD prediction and the available {\tt JLab} data. In addition to the differential longitudinal DV$π$P cross section, we also study the impact of the two-loop QCD corrections on the transverse single-spin asymmetries (TSSA) in some benchmark kinematics at {\tt JLab}, {\tt EIC} and {\tt EicC}.

### [116] [$\mathcal{H}$olographic $\mathcal{N}$aturalness and Information See-Saw Mechanism for Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26982)
*Andrea Addazi,Giuseppe Meluccio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的理论框架——全息自然性（Holographic Naturalness），将德西特熵（de Sitter entropy）解释为由引力瞬子模空间中的轻相干自由度——“hairons”——所携带，并以此统一解释中微子质量生成与宇宙学常数问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特熵的微观起源是量子引力中与宇宙学常数问题相关的核心谜题，现有理论缺乏对其微观自由度的明确物理解释。

Method: 基于欧几里得德西特瞬子（$S^4$）构造了一类新的轨形引力瞬子（orbifold gravitational instanton）$S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$，其中$N$对应德西特熵；利用Wilson环（Wilson loops）产生的$\mathbb{Z}_N$对称性确保模式可区分性，从而导出正确的熵值。

Result: Hairons质量约为哈勃尺度（Hubble scale）且相互作用可忽略，表明德西特真空是一种玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）；中微子质量通过引力拓扑自然产生，无需标准模型之外的新物理；拓扑自由度$N \sim M_\text{P}^2/\Lambda \sim 10^{120}$同时提供全息熵计数和$1/N$信息跷跷板机制（information see-saw）来解释中微子质量。

Conclusion: 预测了中微子超流凝聚形成库珀对（Cooper pair）作为冷暗物质、通过QCD复合轴子（composite axion）解决强CP问题、中微子质量随时间演化追踪暗能量演化，以及在高能宇宙射线和高磁场实验中可观测的唯象学信号。

Abstract: The microscopic origin of the de Sitter entropy remains a central puzzle in quantum gravity related to the cosmological constant problem. Within $\mathcal{H}$olographic $\mathcal{N}$aturalness, we propose this entropy is carried by light, coherent degrees of freedom - "hairons" - emerging as moduli of gravitational instantons on orbifolds. From the Euclidean de Sitter instanton ($S^4$), we construct a new class of orbifold gravitational instantons, $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$, where $N$ corresponds to the de Sitter entropy. The moduli space dimension scales linearly with $N$, and we identify these moduli with hairon fields. A $\mathbb{Z}_N$ symmetry from Wilson loops ensures mode distinguishability, yielding the correct entropy. Hairons acquire a mass of the order of the Hubble scale with negligible interactions, suggesting the de Sitter vacuum is a Bose-Einstein condensate of these excitations. We then unify the neutrino mass generation with the cosmological constant via gravitational topology. The small neutrino mass emerges naturally without new physics beyond the Standard Model. The gravitational Chern-Simons structure and anomaly force a topological Higgs mechanism, leading to neutrino condensation via $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ instantons. The topological degrees $N \sim M_\text{P}^2/Λ\sim 10^{120}$ provide both a holographic entropy counting and a $1/N$ information see-saw mechanism for neutrino masses. Predictions: (i) neutrino superfluid condensation forming Cooper pairs below meV as cold dark matter; (ii) resolution of the strong CP problem via a QCD composite axion; (iii) time-varying neutrino masses tracking th dark energy evolution; (iv) signatures in astroparticle physics, ultra-high-energy cosmic rays and high magnetic field experiments.

</details>


### [117] [New gravitational-wave templates for metastable cosmic strings: Loop breaking versus network collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28097)
*Doa Hashemi Asl,Kai Schmitz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了亚稳宇宙弦（metastable cosmic strings）产生的引力波背景（gravitational-wave background, GWB）信号，强调需区分两种不同的时间尺度——环断裂时间尺度（t_LB）和网络坍缩时间尺度（t_NC），并将GWB信号推广至包含弦张力Gμ及两个时间尺度的三参数模型，从而统一了标准亚稳弦与准稳弦（quasi-stable strings）的建模，并在大t_LB/t_NC比值极限下导出了与数值结果高度吻合的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大统一理论（grand unified theories, GUTs）普遍预言亚稳宇宙弦的存在，这类弦被认为是解释2023年脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）信号中引力波背景的潜在来源。现有模型对亚稳弦的两种关键时间尺度（t_LB与t_NC）的区分不够清晰，导致GWB信号的描述不够准确。

Method: 论文通过严格区分环断裂时间尺度（t_LB）和网络坍缩时间尺度（t_NC），分析了两种尺度相近或相远的条件及其对GWB信号的影响。在此基础上，将GWB信号的描述推广为包含弦张力Gμ、t_LB和t_NC的三参数模型，从而统一了标准亚稳弦与准稳弦的建模。在大t_LB/t_NC比值极限下，推导了GWB谱的紧凑解析表达式。

Result: 建立了三参数模型，能够统一描述标准亚稳弦和准稳弦的GWB信号；在大t_LB/t_NC比值极限下，得到的解析GWB谱与文献中的数值结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的亚稳弦GWB谱新模板可直接用于未来PTA数据集的分析，为解释观测到的引力波背景信号提供更准确的工具。

Abstract: Metastable cosmic strings are a common prediction of grand unified theories and act as a source of a gravitational-wave background (GWB) that can explain the 2023 pulsar timing array (PTA) signal. In this paper, we revisit the GWB signal from metastable strings, emphasizing the need to carefully distinguish between two different time scales: (i) t_LB, the time scale of loop breaking because of spontaneous monopole nucleation on closed string loops, and (ii) t_NC, the time scale of network collapse when string segments attached to monopoles begin to enter the Hubble horizon. We discuss under which conditions these two time scales are similar or far apart from each other and illustrate the resulting consequences for the GWB signal. In doing so, we generalize the description of the GWB signal from metastable strings to a three-parameter model in terms of the string tension Gμand the time scales t_LB and t_NC, which allows us to unify the modeling of standard metastable strings with what is known as quasi-stable strings. In the limit of a large t_LB/t_NC ratio, we, moreover, derive a compact analytical expression for the predicted GWB spectrum in excellent agreement with numerical results in the literature. We thus conclude that our new templates for the GWB spectrum from metastable strings can be readily used in the analysis of future PTA data sets.

Method: 将标准模型扩展一个实规范单态标量场（real gauge-singlet scalar field），针对标量质量 0 < m_φ < 40 GeV 的范围，推导希格斯玻色子衰变到两个及三个标量末态的分析表达式；要求所有衰变率之和不超过标准模型总衰变宽度，导出关于单态真空期望值（vacuum expectation value）v_φ 的四阶不等式作为全局约束。

Result: 该四阶不等式在整个质量范围内给出混合角的统一上界 cosθ < 0.12–0.13，与现有直接搜寻限值互补；在更强的独立混合约束（如 cosθ < 0.1）下，预测奇异衰变率上界分别为 Γ_{h→φφ} < 0.06 MeV 和 Γ_{h→φφφ} < 5×10⁻⁶ MeV。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过要求奇异衰变率之和不超过标准模型希格斯总衰变宽度，可获得对单态标量模型参数的有效全局约束，为轻标量粒子的实验搜寻提供了新的理论边界。

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenology of the Standard Model extended by a real gauge-singlet scalar field, focusing on exotic Higgs decay channels. For a light scalar mass in the range \(0 < m_φ < 40\) GeV, the Higgs boson can decay to both two and three scalar final states. We derive analytical expressions for these decay rates and impose a global constraint on the model parameters by requiring that their sum does not exceed the total Standard Model Higgs boson decay width. This requirement translates into a fourth-order inequality with respect to the singlet vacuum expectation value, \(v_φ\). We demonstrate that satisfying this inequality imposes an upper bound of \(\cos θ< 0.12 - 0.13\) across the entire mass range, providing a complementary constraint to existing direct search limits. Utilizing stronger independent constraints on the mixing (e.g., \(\cos θ< 0.1\)), we then predict upper bounds on the individual exotic decay rates as a function of \(m_φ\) as \(Γ_{h \rightarrow φφ} < 0.06\) MeV and \(Γ_{h \rightarrow φφφ} < 5 \times 10^{- 6}\) MeV, respectively.

### [119] [Thermal Spectra Without Detailed Balance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27926)
*Xingjian Lu,Shuzhe Shi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文论证，微观发射核（emission kernel）的结构本身即可在无需探针粒子热化（thermalization）的条件下产生热谱，并提出了一个基于核的判据，用以区分真正的探针-介质交换平衡与仅由核结构导致的热谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，热谱（thermal spectrum）是探针粒子与周围介质达到细致平衡（detailed balance）的标志。本文旨在检验这一解释的普适性，并探究微观发射核如何影响宏观谱的生成。

Method: 通过研究微观发射核对宏观谱的决定作用，作者在 3+1 维时空下分析了发射核属于热简并类（thermally degenerate class）的情形，并以低能汤姆孙散射（low-energy Thomson scattering）为例进行具体说明。

Result: 研究发现，在 3+1 维中，当发射核属于热简并类时，无需探针热化即可产生精确的热谱。在低能汤姆孙散射中，微分截面仅依赖散射角而不依赖曼德尔施塔姆变量 s，正是这种简并核的典型实例。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一个基于发射核的判据，用于区分真正的探针-介质交换平衡与由发射核结构本身产生的热谱，从而修正了热谱必然对应热化平衡的传统解读。

Abstract: A thermal spectrum is often taken as a signature that the emitted probe has reached detailed balance with the surrounding medium. We show that this interpretation is not generally valid by studying how the microscopic emission kernel determines the macroscopic spectrum. In $3+1$ dimensions, a simple thermal spectrum can be generated without probe thermalization when the relevant kernel belongs to a thermally degenerate class. A representative case is realized when the differential cross section depends on the scattering angle but carries no additional dependence on the Mandelstam variable $s$, as in low-energy Thomson scattering. Our results provide a kernel-based criterion for distinguishing genuine probe--medium exchange equilibrium from thermal spectra produced by the structure of the emission kernel itself.

Method: 计算了双层石墨烯中通过大质量中介子（massive mediator）的暗物质-电子散射率，并分析了散射率随靶材相对于银河系暗物质风（Galactic dark matter wind）取向的恒星日变化。

Result: 仅需约0.5 mg·年的暴露量即可探测到新的参数空间；双层石墨烯的各向异性响应函数导致散射率产生显著的恒星日调制（sidereal-day modulation），尤其对亚MeV质量暗物质信号明显。

Abstract: Novel target materials with anisotropic response will play a key role in detecting low-mass dark matter in upcoming experiments. Bilayer graphene is one such material that has been proposed for the detection of sub-MeV mass dark matter particles via electronic excitations. In this work, we calculate scattering rate via a massive mediator in bilayer graphene. With an exposure as small as $\sim$ 0.5 mg-year, bilayer graphene can probe new regions of the parameter space. The anisotropic response function of bilayer graphene leads to a sidereal-day modulation in the scattering rate, depending on its orientation with respect to the Galactic dark matter wind. We find significant modulation in the scattering rate for sub-MeV mass dark matter, demonstrating bilayer graphene's promise for a future experiment. We hope that our work will motivate the community to investigate bilayer graphene as a novel target material, and that it may lead us to discover the particle nature of dark matter.

### [121] [Species-Resolved Scaling of Azimuthal Anisotropy: Constraining Attenuation, Collective Expansion, and Hadronic Dynamics in Hydrodynamic Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27254)
*Roy Lacey*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本研究基于iEBE-VISHNU模拟的Pb+Pb碰撞事件，构建了区分粒子种类的方位角各向异性标度函数（scaling functions），发现其在横动量、中心度、粒子种类和束流能量下呈现稳健塌缩，并通过能量依赖的衰减基线β₀和中心度依赖的有效衰减修正，实现了与数据定义参考的定量一致，从而为流体动力学响应提供了定量约束探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对方位角各向异性（azimuthal anisotropy）中不同粒子种类、横动量（transverse momentum）、中心度（centrality）和束流能量（beam energy）之间的标度关系缺乏系统性理解，亟需构建统一的标度函数框架以揭示背后的流体动力学响应机制。

Method: 利用逐事件（event-by-event）iEBE-VISHNU模拟，针对Pb+Pb碰撞在$\sqrt{s_{NN}}=2.76$和$5.02$~TeV两个能量下，从已识别粒子的定向流$v_2$和三角流$v_3$出发，构建区分粒子种类的方位角各向异性标度函数（scaling functions），并引入能量依赖的衰减基线（attenuation baseline）$β_0$和中心度依赖的有效衰减修正。

Result: 标度函数在不同横动量、中心度、粒子种类和束流能量下表现出稳健塌缩（robust collapse），基于标度参数化与数据定义参考实现了定量一致；在中心到中等中心碰撞中依赖能量相关的衰减基线β₀，而在更外围碰撞中需引入中心度依赖的有效衰减修正，且对质心碰撞能量$\sqrt{s_{NN}}$仅有弱依赖。

Conclusion: 该标度框架（scaling framework）可为流体动力学响应（hydrodynamic response）提供定量约束探针，有助于解耦并约束对方位角各向异性的耦合贡献，并揭示由状态方程（EOS）驱动的集体膨胀、有限系统寿命以及强子再散射（hadronic re-scattering）三者间的相互作用。

Abstract: Species-resolved azimuthal anisotropy scaling functions are constructed from identified particle $v_2$ and $v_3$ obtained from event-by-event iEBE-VISHNU simulations for Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=2.76$ and $5.02$~TeV. The scaling functions exhibit a robust collapse across transverse momentum, centrality, particle species, and beam energy, indicating a common and tightly constrained scaling structure. High scaling fidelity yields quantitative agreement with the data-defined reference through an energy-dependent attenuation baseline $β_0$ in central to mid-central collisions and a centrality-dependent modification of the effective attenuation in more peripheral collisions, with only a weak dependence on $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$. The multiplicity dependence of the extracted scaling parameters reflects the interplay of EOS-driven collective expansion, finite system lifetime, and hadronic re-scattering. These results demonstrate that the scaling framework provides a quantitative, constraint-driven probe of the hydrodynamic response, enabling the disentanglement and constraint of the coupled contributions to azimuthal anisotropy.

### [122] [Unmasking Hidden Wigner's Symmetry from First Principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27144)
*Phong Dang,Daniel Langr,Tomas Dytrych,Jerry P. Draayer,David Kekejian*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文展示了基于手征有效场论（$\chi$EFT）推导的核子间相互作用中，维格纳超多重态对称性（Wigner's supermultiplet symmetry）的显著主导性，并通过第一性原理对称性适应模型（SAM）证明该对称性在核结构中的体现，揭示了抑制的自旋-同位旋极化率，为削减无核芯壳模型（NCSM）基组规模提供了策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理对称性适应模型（Symmetry Adapted Model, SAM）进行从头计算（\textit{ab initio}），在不施加任何模型空间先验约束的条件下，分析$\rm ^4He$、$\rm ^6Li$和$\rm ^6He$波函数在$\rm U(4)$不可约表示（irreducible representations）上的分布。

Result: 大多数$\rm ^4He$、$\rm ^6Li$和$\rm ^6He$的波函数高度集中于少量$\rm U(4)$不可约表示中；自旋-同位旋极化率（spin-isospin polarizability）受到抑制。

Conclusion: 该对称性的涌现特征为削减无核芯壳模型（No-Core Shell Model, NCSM）中爆炸性增长的多体基组提供了可行策略，同时保留计算可观测量所需的重要物理组态。

Abstract: We present quantitative evidence that high-quality internucleon forces derived from $χ$EFT exhibit a striking dominance of Wigner's supermultiplet symmetry, without invoking the large-$N_c$ limit of QCD or assumptions about specific nuclei. We trace the manifestation of this symmetry in nuclear structure using the \textit{ab initio} Symmetry Adapted Model (SAM) and identify suppressed spin-isospin polarizability. Our calculations show that a majority of $\rm ^4He$, $\rm ^6Li$, and $\rm ^6He$ wave functions is concentrated in a few $\rm U(4)$ irreducible representations, without imposing any \textit{a priori} constraints on the model space. This emergent feature points to a strategy for reducing explosive many-body bases of the NCSM while retaining physically important configurations needed to compute observables.
