### [123] [Lorentz-FitzGerald Contraction as the Unique Closure Condition for Moving Spherical-Harmonic Cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27525)
*Shiva Meucci*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在力学波介质中运动的共振腔要保持球谐相位闭合（spherical-harmonic phase closure），其边界的唯一变形就是洛伦兹-菲茨杰拉德收缩（Lorentz–FitzGerald contraction），并由此导出共振周期膨胀（period dilation），从而为构造性相对论纲领（constructive relativity program）提供了缺失的唯一性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在菲茨杰拉德、洛伦兹和亥维赛发起的构造性相对论纲领中，一直缺乏一个严格的证明，说明洛伦兹运动学（Lorentzian kinematics）不仅是与力学波介质中相位闭合相一致的，而是被其唯一要求的。本文旨在填补这一缺失的唯一性定理。

Method: 本文通过分析在无耗散波速为 $c$ 的力学波介质中以速度 $v=βc$ 运动的共振腔，推导腔内射线往返相位 $Φ(θ)$ 与边界半径 $r(θ)$ 的关系式，并施加 $Φ(θ)$ 与角度 $θ$ 无关的条件（即保留球谐本征结构（spherical-harmonic eigenstructure）的必要条件），从而唯一确定边界的洛伦兹纵横比（aspect ratio）。

Result: 唯一确定的边界变形为 $a_\parallel/a_\perp = 1/γ = \sqrt{1-β^2}$，即洛伦兹-菲茨杰拉德收缩。将这一边界代入往返时间，无需额外假设即得到共振周期膨胀 $T = γT_0$。

Conclusion: 收缩与膨胀均源于同一力学约束——运动下本征结构的保持。这构成了构造性相对论纲领的缺失唯一性定理：洛伦兹运动学被相位闭合所唯一要求。

Abstract: We prove that the Lorentz--FitzGerald contraction is the unique deformation of a resonant cavity moving through a mechanical wave medium that preserves spherical-harmonic phase closure. For a cavity moving at speed $v = βc$ through a medium supporting nondispersive wave propagation at speed $c$, the round-trip phase of an internal ray at angle $θ$ to the motion depends on the boundary radius $r(θ)$ according to $Φ(θ) = 2k\,r(θ)\sqrt{1-β^2\sin^2θ}/(1-β^2)$. Requiring $Φ(θ)$ to be independent of $θ$ -- the necessary condition for retaining a spherical-harmonic eigenstructure -- uniquely fixes the Lorentzian aspect ratio \[ \frac{a_\parallel}{a_\perp} = \frac{1}γ = \sqrt{1-β^2}. \] Substituting this unique boundary into the round-trip time yields the resonant period dilation $T = γT_0$, without additional assumptions. Both results -- contraction and dilation -- follow from a single mechanical constraint: preservation of eigenstructure under motion. This is the missing uniqueness theorem of the constructive relativity program initiated by FitzGerald, Lorentz, and Heaviside: the proof that Lorentzian kinematics are not merely consistent with, but uniquely required by, phase closure in a mechanical wave medium.

</details>

### [124] [Momentum-Space Entanglement Signatures and Spinon Breakdown in the $J_1$-$J_2$ Zig-Zag Heisenberg Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27048)
*Tom Oeffner,Ludwig Bordfeldt,Andreas Feuerpfeil,Lukas Elter,Tobias Helbig,Tobias Hofmann,Martin Greiter,Ronny Thomale*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过动量空间纠缠（momentum-space entanglement）分析，研究了 $J_1$-$J_2$ 锯齿形自旋链（zig-zag spin chain）中自旋子（spinon）准粒子的鲁棒性。结果表明，在高度阻挫（frustrated）区域，双自旋子描述（double-spinon description）在广泛参数范围内保持稳健，且自旋子稳定性存在显著不对称性：铁磁耦合（$J_1<0$）为边缘无关（marginally irrelevant），将分数化（fractionalization）维持至螺旋相深处；反铁磁耦合（$J_1>0$）为边缘相关（marginally relevant），更早导致禁闭（confinement）。最终分数化描述的崩溃由一连串链间激发（inter-chain excitations）驱动，表现为尖锐的基态动量移动。本文建立了动量截断纠缠分析作为追踪自旋子准粒子鲁棒性的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在高度阻挫的锯齿形自旋链中，自旋子准粒子（spinon quasiparticles）在何种参数条件下保持稳健，以及其最终崩溃的机制。

Method: 采用动量空间纠缠分析（momentum-space entanglement analysis）方法；在高度阻挫区域将系统建模为两条耦合的海森堡链（Heisenberg chains），并提出双自旋子描述（double-spinon description）；将系统视为两个耦合的 SU(2)$_1$ Wess-Zumino-Witten 模型进行分析。

Result: 对于小的 $J_2$，退禁闭自旋子（deconfined spinons）在液态-二聚体转变（liquid-dimer transition）之后仍持续存在，直至马朱姆达尔-高希点（Majumdar-Ghosh point）附近才塌缩。在高度阻挫区域，双自旋子描述在广泛参数范围内保持稳健。自旋子稳定性存在鲜明不对称性：铁磁耦合（$J_1<0$）为边缘无关，维持分数化至螺旋相；反铁磁耦合（$J_1>0$）为边缘相关，更早引发禁闭。分数化描述的最终崩溃由连续链间激发谱驱动，表现为尖锐的基态动量移动。

Conclusion: 动量截断纠缠分析（momentum cut entanglement analysis）可作为追踪自旋子准粒子鲁棒性的有效工具；将锯齿形海森堡链视为两个耦合的 SU(2)$_1$ Wess-Zumino-Witten 模型，为强阻挫量子磁体提供了超越退耦合极限的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the resilience of spinon quasiparticles in the $J_1$-$J_2$ zig-zag spin chain ($J_2>0$) from the viewpoint of momentum-space entanglement. For small $J_2$, we show that deconfined spinons survive well past the liquid-dimer transition before eventually collapsing towards the Majumdar-Ghosh point. In the highly frustrated zig-zag regime ($J_2 \gg |J_1|$), we model the system as two coupled Heisenberg chains and by Fourier transforming each subchain individually, a framework we dub the double-spinon description. While continuum field theories predict that this decoupled phase is strictly unstable to any finite inter-chain coupling, our analysis reveals that the double-spinon description remains robust over an extensive parameter regime. Notably, we find a stark asymmetry in spinon stability reflecting the underlying renormalization group flow: ferromagnetic coupling ($J_{1} < 0$) is marginally irrelevant and sustains fractionalization deep into the spiral phase, whereas antiferromagnetic coupling ($J_{1} > 0$) is marginally relevant and drives confinement much earlier. The ultimate breakdown of this fractionalized description is driven by a continuum of inter-chain excitations which manifests itself as a sharp ground-state momentum shift distinct from macroscopic thermodynamic phase boundaries. Our results establish momentum cut entanglement analysis as a tool to trace the quasiparticle resilience of spinons, as we show that treating the zig-zag Heisenberg chain as two coupled SU(2)$_1$ Wess-Zumino-Witten models provides a theoretical framework for strongly frustrated quantum magnets applicable beyond the decoupled limit.

</details>


### [125] [Local Current Algebra for the HK Universality Class](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27051)
*Yuting Bai,Philip W. Phillips*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过引入满足 $\mathfrak{su}_1(2)$ 仿射李代数（affine Lie algebra）的局域实空间流（local real-space current）哈密顿量，消除了掺杂莫特绝缘体中 Hatsugai-Kohmoto（HK）模型的非局域性，从而回应了该模型的关键批评，并展示了流代数（current algebra）在强相互作用系统中的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hatsugai-Kohmoto（HK）模型在描述掺杂莫特绝缘体（doped Mott insulator）时存在非局域性（non-locality）问题，这一缺陷是该模型受到的主要批评。本文旨在通过构造一个局域流哈密顿量来消除这一非局域性。

Method: 通过 Bjorken-Johnson-Low（BJL） prescription 处理反常对易子（anomalous commutators），建立局域实空间流哈密顿量与原始费米子场（fermionic fields）表述之间的对应关系。该流哈密顿量满足 $\mathfrak{su}_1(2)$ 仿射李代数（affine Lie algebra）。

Result: 从流哈密顿量计算得到的电荷磁化率（charge susceptibility）与由基本费米子场计算的结果完全相同。这表明 HK 模型在实空间中是局域的，尽管以费米子场表述时表现为非局域形式。

Conclusion: 该工作消除了对 HK 模型非局域性的关键批评，同时强化了流代数（current algebras）在强相互作用（strong interactions）系统研究中的工具价值。

Abstract: We show that a Hamiltonian in terms of the local real-space currents obeying an $\mathfrak{su}_1(2)$ affine Lie algebra eliminates the non-locality in the Hatsugai-Kohmoto model for a doped Mott insulator. We establish this local correspondence through the Bjorken-Johnson-Low prescription for anomalous commutators. With this result, we show that the charge susceptibility computed from the current Hamiltonian is identical to that with the elemental Fermionic fields. Consequently, the HK model is local in real space, though not in terms of the Fermionic fields, thereby eliminating the key criticism of this model and reinforcing the utility of current algebras for strong interactions.

</details>


### [126] [Topological phase transitions in twisted bilayer graphene/hBN from interlayer coupling and substrate potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27304)
*Huiwen Wang,Wei Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了六方氮化硼对齐的双层转角石墨烯（TBG/hBN）中通过改变层间跳跃强度（w₀, w₁）和hBN诱导的交错势（staggered potential）引发的拓扑相变（topological phase transitions），绘制了陈数（Chern number）相图，发现了多个高陈数态（C = 3, 4, 5），并阐明了各相变对应的能带反转机制与贝里曲率（Berry curvature）演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TBG/hBN体系中的拓扑性质对连续模型（continuum model）中的多个材料参数高度敏感，但此前缺乏对参数联合作用的系统性理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供全面的拓扑相变研究。

Method: 通过改变层间跳跃强度（w₀, w₁）和hBN诱导的交错势（staggered potential），在考虑/不考虑hBN莫尔势（moiré potential）两种情况下，系统扫描实验相关的大范围参数空间，绘制陈数（Chern number）相图。

Result: 揭示了拓扑景观（topological landscape）的逐步丰富，包括多个高陈数态（C = 3, 4, 5）。每个拓扑相变与C₃对称（C₃-symmetric）k点、高对称动量或抛物线接触点处的不同能带反转机制（band-inversion mechanisms）相关联，并清晰地反映在贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的演化中。

Conclusion: 本文结果为解释现有实验观测提供了理论见解，阐明了驱动这些拓扑相变的机制，并有助于在TBG/hBN及相关莫尔体系（moiré systems）中探索拓扑态（topological states）。

Abstract: Twisted bilayer graphene aligned with hexagonal boron nitride (TBG/hBN) hosts rich topological and correlated quantum phases, such as (fractional) Chern insulators, whose character is dictated by the topology of the moiré flat band. This topology is highly sensitive to several material parameters in the continuum model, yet a systematic understanding of their combined influence has been lacking. Here, we present a comprehensive study of topological phase transitions in TBG/hBN by varying the interlayer hopping strengths ($w_0, w_1$) and hBN-induced staggered potential, both with and without the hBN moiré potential. We map out Chern number phase diagrams across a broad, experimentally relevant parameter space, revealing a progressive enrichment of the topological landscape including multiple high-Chern number ($C$ = 3, 4, and 5) states. Each transition is linked to distinct band-inversion mechanisms at generic $C_3$-symmetric k points, high-symmetry momenta, or parabolic touchings, clearly reflecting in the evolution of the Berry curvature. Our results offer theoretical insights that help interpret existing experimental observations, elucidate the mechanisms driving these topological phase transitions and facilitate the exploration of topological states in TBG/hBN and related moiré systems.

### [127] [Exotic Spin Excitation Continuum in a Weakly Coupled Quantum Chainsaw Antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27310)
*Asiri Thennakoon,Prena Chaudhary,Sankha Subhra Bakshi,Tommy Park,Tristen Lowrey,Daniel Pajerowski,Christina Hoffmann,Junghong H. He,Hiroaki Ueda,Collin Broholm,Gia-Wei Chern,Seung-Hun Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过非弹性中子散射实验，在Ti基量子反铁磁体Cs₈LiNa₃Ti₁₂F₄₈中发现了具有本征方向性的分数化激发（fractionalized excitations），表明一维临界性（one-dimensional criticality）的痕迹可以在二维晶格中持续存在，从而建立了各向异性分数化（anisotropic fractionalization）作为量子无序态的一种独特组织原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子磁体中分数化激发通常与二维拓扑序（topological order）或一维临界性相关，但这两个不同机制如何跨越维度交叉（dimensional crossover）相互联系尚不清楚。本文旨在探索这种联系，并研究是否存在一种介于一维与二维之间的中间态。

Method: 对Ti基量子反铁磁体Cs₈LiNa₃Ti₁₂F₄₈的单晶样品进行非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）实验。该材料中Ti³⁺（3d¹, S=1/2）离子在扭曲的kagome平面内发生反铁磁相互作用，形成弱耦合的自旋-1/2链锯（chainsaws）网络，实现维度挫败（dimensional frustration）的调控区间。

Result: 磁激发谱在整个测量的动量与能量相空间中呈现强连续谱（continuum）；动态自旋关联函数（dynamic spin correlation function）在动量空间中表现出杆状散射（rod-like scattering），表明磁关联具有准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）性质。

Conclusion: 实验结果指向具有本征方向性（intrinsically directional character）的分数化激发，证明一维临界性的特征可在二维晶格中持续存在。研究工作确立了各向异性分数化作为量子无序态（quantum-disordered states）的一种独立组织原则。

Abstract: Collective motions in strongly interacting magnets involve many spins and are often described in terms of integer-spin excitations. However, in certain cases, the collective motion can behave as if these integer excitations break apart into smaller, particle-like entities with unusual properties. Such fractionalized excitations in quantum magnets are commonly associated either with topological order in two dimensions or with criticality in one dimension. It remains unclear how these distinct mechanisms are connected across a dimensional crossover. Here we investigate the Ti-based quantum antiferromagnet, $Cs_{8}LiNa_{3}Ti_{12}F_{48}$, in which $Ti^{3+}$ ($3d^{1}$, $S=1/2$) ions interact antiferromagnetically within distorted kagome planes. Our inelastic neutron scattering study on a single crystal reveals a frustrated network of weakly coupled spin-$1/2$ chainsaws, realizing a regime of dimensional frustration in which interchain couplings fail to establish coherent two-dimensional order. The magnetic excitation spectrum exhibits a strong continuum spanning the full measured momentum and energy phase space. In addition, the dynamic spin correlation function displays rod-like scattering in momentum space, indicating a quasi-one-dimensional nature of the magnetic correlations. These results point to fractionalized excitations with intrinsically directional character, demonstrating that signatures of one-dimensional criticality can persist within a two-dimensional lattice. Our findings establish anisotropic fractionalization as a distinct organizing principle for quantum-disordered states.

</details>


### [128] [Constructing Bulk Topological Orders via Layered Gauging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27363)
*Shang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“分层规范构造（layered gauging construction）”的物理直观方法，通过堆叠多个k维量子系统层并逐层施加对角规范操作，系统性地从k维广义对称性生成(k+1)维拓扑序（涵盖液态拓扑序与分形子拓扑序），并在多种对称性类型（包括常规、高形式、子体系、反常、非阿贝尔、不可逆对称性）中成功验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解含对称性的量子相与量子相变是量子多体物理的核心目标。拓扑全息术（topological holography）为此提供了强大范式，但现有的体态构造方法依赖复杂的数学形式，难以适用于某些对称性类型。因此需要一种更直观、通用的构造方法。

Method: 该方法将k维量子系统的多个层堆叠成(k+1)维结构，然后对每对最近邻层之间作用的一种对角对称性（diagonal symmetry）依次进行规范（gauging）。具体操作细节取决于所涉及的对称性类型。

Result: 在多种空间维度的实例中成功实现了该方法，涉及的对称性包括常规、高形式（higher-form）、子体系（subsystem）、反常（anomalous）、非阿贝尔（nonabelian）和不可逆（noninvertible）对称性。例如，从2d plaquette Ising模型的子体系对称性导出了X-cube模型及各向异性分形子拓扑序；从1d中的反常Z2对称性构造了实现双半子拓扑序（double semion topological order）的新型正方晶格模型。

Conclusion: 该方法具有高度普适性，能够系统性地从各种广义对称性生成拓扑序，为拓扑全息术提供了一种物理直观且便于实际应用的构造框架。

Abstract: Understanding quantum phases and phase transitions in the presence of symmetries is a central objective of quantum many-body physics. A powerful modern paradigm for investigating this problem is topological holography, which relates symmetries in $k$ dimensions to "bulk" topological orders in $(k+1)$ dimensions. While conceptually profound, most existing bulk construction methods rely on sophisticated mathematical formalisms and can be difficult to apply to certain symmetry types. In this work, we propose a physically intuitive and versatile method, termed the layered gauging construction, to systematically generate $(k+1)$-dimensional (liquid or fracton) topological orders from $k$-dimensional generalized symmetries. Roughly speaking, the prescription is to stack many layers of $k$-dimensional quantum systems with certain symmetries into a $(k+1)$-dimensional pile, and then sequentially gauge a diagonal symmetry acting on each nearest-neighbor pair of layers. The detailed procedure depends on the specific symmetry types. We have successfully implemented the method in a number of examples in different spatial dimensions, with symmetries that are conventional, higher-form, subsystem, anomalous, nonabelian, or noninvertible. We hence conjecture the method to be very general. For example, from the subsystem symmetry of the $2d$ plaquette Ising model, we derive the X-cube model and also an anisotropic fracton topological order. Additionally, starting from an anomalous $\mathbb Z_2$ symmetry in $1d$, we construct a new square lattice model realizing the double semion topological order.

</details>


### [129] [Evidence for interior-gap pair-density-wave state in Kondo-Heisenberg chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27440)
*Yuto Hirose,Shunsuke C. Furuya,Yasuhiro Tada*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过一维Kondo-Heisenberg模型的密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算，证明其超导相实现了一种由强关联产生的内隙配对密度波（interior-gap PDW）态，并揭示了与常规内隙超导不同的动力学起源机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内隙超导（interior-gap superconductivity）作为一种在费米面失配条件下可能存在的奇特配对态，长期以来仅在理论层面被讨论，尚未在规范的强关联模型中得到实现。本文旨在探索一维Kondo-Heisenberg模型中是否能够出现这种态。

Method: 采用无限密度矩阵重整化群（infinite DMRG, iDMRG）和有限DMRG方法，对自旋S=1/2和S=3/2的一维Kondo-Heisenberg链进行数值计算，分析配对密度波（pair-density-wave, PDW）关联函数和动量分布函数n(k)的结构特征。

Result: 在自旋能隙区域内，PDW关联是主导的体超导关联。动量分布函数n(k)呈现出内隙物理特征的重构结构：S=1/2链中仅表现为凸起（hump），而S=3/2链中则发展为清晰的凹陷（dip），强有力地支持了内隙类凹陷结构的解释。有限DMRG数据表明，边界效应会显著改变实空间关联，因此直接计算热力学极限对识别内在体动量结构和主导关联通道至关重要。

Conclusion: 一维Kondo-Heisenberg模型的超导相确实实现了内隙PDW态。与基于预先存在费米面（Fermi surface）失配的传统内隙超导方案不同，该体系始于单一裸传导电子费米面，额外的低能单粒子结构通过Kondo耦合与主导的PDW关联动态地同时涌现。

Abstract: Interior-gap superconductivity has long been discussed as an exotic paired state in the presence of Fermi-surface mismatch, but its realization in canonical strongly correlated models has remained elusive. Here we present evidence that the superconducting phase of one-dimensional Kondo-Heisenberg models realizes an interior-gap pair-density-wave (PDW) state generated by strong correlations. Combining infinite density-matrix-renormalization-group (iDMRG) and finite DMRG calculations for $S=1/2$ and $S=3/2$ chains, we show that the PDW correlation is the dominant bulk superconducting correlation in the spin-gapped regime and that the momentum distribution function $n(k)$ exhibits a reconstructed structure characteristic of interior-gap physics. In particular, while the feature in $n(k)$ for the $S=1/2$ chain is only hump-like, the corresponding structure in the $S=3/2$ chain develops into a clear dip, strongly supporting the interpretation in terms of an interior-gap-like dip structure. Unlike conventional interior-gap scenarios based on a mismatch between preexisting Fermi surfaces, the present system starts from a single bare conduction-electron Fermi surface, and the additional low-energy single-particle structure emerges dynamically together with the dominant PDW correlation through the Kondo coupling. Finite DMRG data further demonstrate that boundary effects can substantially modify real-space correlations in this gapless one-dimensional system, making a direct thermodynamic-limit calculation essential for identifying the intrinsic bulk momentum structure and the dominant correlation channel.

</details>


### [130] [Chern number reversal and emergent superconductivity in rhombohedral graphene induced by in-plane magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27788)
*Xiaozhou Zan,Hangzhe Li,Jiawei Guo,Gengdong Zhou,Kangyao Chen,Cihan Gao,Zijun Xu,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Anqi Wang,Jie Shen,Jinsong Zhang,Zhida Song,Yayu Wang*

TL;DR: 本文报道在hBN对齐的八层菱方石墨烯摩尔超晶格中，发现了稳健的量子反常霍尔（QAH）态及三种非常规超导相，并通过位移场和面内磁场实现了QAH陈数反转、超导相调控及自旋三重态配对证据的获取。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验构建了hBN对齐的八层菱方石墨烯摩尔超晶格（moire superlattice），通过施加位移场（displacement field）和面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field），分别对电子掺杂和空穴掺杂载流子区域进行电输运测量。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了菱方石墨烯摩尔超晶格作为拓扑态与超导态共存的高度多功能平台，并凸显了面内磁场作为一种强大的原位调控手段，可用于新型量子器件的工程设计。

Abstract: Rhombohedral graphene with topological flat bands offers an ideal platform for realizing correlated and topological quantum phases. Here we investigate hBN aligned eight-layer rhombohedral graphene moire superlattices, which host a robust quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) state alongside three unconventional superconducting phases. For electron-doped carriers away from the moire potential, we observe QAH Chern number reversal driven by the displacement fields and in plane magnetic fields. For hole-doped carriers near the moire superlattice, the three superconducting phases exhibit distinctively different in plane magnetic field responses: one is weakly enhanced, the second is strongly suppressed, and the third exclusively induced by in plane magnetic field. The isotropic in plane magnetic field response in the QAH regime points to interplay between orbital magnetism and spin-orbit coupling, and the field-emergent superconductivity provides compelling evidence for spin-triplet pairing. Our work demonstrates a highly versatile platform for coexisting topological and superconducting states, and highlights in plane magnetic field as a powerful in-situ control knob for engineering novel quantum devices.

### [131] [Magnetic excitation spectrum and hierarchy of magnetic interactions in ErFeO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27857)
*Dnyaneshwar R. Bhosale,Piotr Fabrykiewicz,Devashibhai Adroja,Martin Meven,Astrid Schneidewind,Michal Stekiel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用飞行时间中子谱学（time-of-flight neutron spectroscopy）全面研究了 ErFeO₃ 正铁氧体的激发谱，区分了 Fe³⁺ 亚晶格的自旋波激发（~9–65 meV）与 Er³⁺ 离子的晶格电场（CEF）激发（<36 meV），通过线性自旋波理论提取了关键交换参数，并揭示了由 Er³⁺-Er³⁺ 交换耦合引起的色散以及 Er³⁺-Fe³⁺ 相互作用导致的 Kramers 简并劈裂，最终给出了正铁氧体中相互作用的层级特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 ErFeO₃ 正铁氧体的自旋动力学（spin dynamics）及其低能激发行为，特别是 Fe³⁺ 和 Er³⁺ 亚晶格之间的相互作用如何影响磁基态（magnetic ground state）和低温自旋排布。

Method: 采用飞行时间中子谱学（time-of-flight neutron spectroscopy）测量激发谱，并结合线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）拟合自旋波色散关系与谱权重，同时利用低能入射中子的高能量分辨率解析 Er³⁺ 离子 CEF 能级的色散与劈裂。

Result: 激发谱包含两个组分：Fe³⁺ 亚晶格的自旋波激发（~9–65 meV）和 Er³⁺ 的 CEF 激发（<36 meV）；Fe 自旋波色散由线性自旋波理论很好地描述；Er³⁺ CEF 能级的色散源于 Er³⁺ 离子间的交换耦合（exchange coupling），而 Kramers 简并劈裂由 Er³⁺ 与 Fe³⁺ 亚晶格的相互作用引起；偶极相互作用（dipolar interaction）和反对称交换相互作用（antisymmetric exchange interaction）对低温自旋排布有重要影响。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了 ErFeO₃ 自旋动力学的详细图像，揭示了正铁氧体（orthoferrite）中不同相互作用尺度之间的层级结构（hierarchy of interaction scales）。

Abstract: We report a comprehensive investigation of the excitation spectrum of ErFeO$_3$ orthoferrite by means of time-of-flight neutron spectroscopy. The spectrum consists of two distinct components: strongly dispersive spin wave excitations of the Fe$^{3+}$ sublattice spanning $\approx$~9 - 65 meV, and crystal electric field (CEF) excitations of Er$^{3+}$ ions below 36 meV. The observed spin wave dispersions and spectral weight are well captured within linear spin wave theory, enabling extraction of the key Fe-Fe exchange parameters. Low-energy incident neutrons with their enhanced energy resolution, further revealed the dispersive character and splitting of Kramers-degenerate CEF levels. We show that the dispersion is caused by the exchange coupling between Er$^{3+}$ ions, while the degeneracy is lifted by interactions between the Er$^{3+}$ and Fe$^{3+}$ sublattices. We further explore the influence of dipolar and antisymmetric exchange interactions with the focus on the magnetic ground state of ErFeO$_3$, with particular attention to the low-temperature spin arrangement. Taken together, our results provide a detailed account of the spin dynamics in ErFeO$_3$ and reveal a hierarchy of interactions scales characteristic for orthoferrites.

</details>


### [132] [Dimensionality-Driven Electronic and Orbital Transitions Mediating Interfacial Magnetism in LaNiO3/CaMnO3 Observed In Situ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28054)
*B-A. Courchene,A. Hampel,S. Beck,J. R. Paudel,J. D. Grassi,L. A. Lapinski,A. M. Derrico,M. Terilli,M. Kareev,C. Klewe,A. Gloskovskii,C. Schlueter,S. K. Chaluvadi,F. Mazzola,I. Vobornik,P. Orgiani,J. Chakhalian,A. J. Millis,A. X. Gray*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验与理论计算相结合，揭示了LaNiO3/CaMnO3超晶格中电子限域（electronic confinement）驱动金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）、轨道极化反转（orbital-polarization crossover）以及界面磁矩的调控机制，建立了氧化物异质结中电子、轨道与磁自由度之间的直接可调耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索氧化物界面（oxide interfaces）中电荷转移（charge transfer）、轨道重构（orbital reconstruction）与维度限域（dimensional confinement）的相互作用如何产生涌现磁态，从而为纳米尺度自旋电子材料（nanoscale spintronic materials）中关联电子行为的工程化提供途径。

Method: 采用原位合成（in situ synthesis）、偏振依赖角分辨光电子能谱（polarization-dependent angle-resolved photoelectron spectroscopy）、X射线磁圆二色性（X-ray magnetic circular dichroism）以及第一性原理电子结构计算（first-principles electronic-structure calculations），对LaNiO3/CaMnO3超晶格（superlattices）进行系统研究。

Result: LaNiO3厚度减小导致金属-绝缘体转变，伴随电子相干性丧失（loss of electronic coherence）和轨道极化反转；这些变化削弱了界面电荷转移，抑制了CaMnO3中界面Mn磁矩（interfacial Mn magnetic moment），表明涌现铁磁态（emergent ferromagnetic state）直接受LaNiO3中电子限域控制。绝缘态与轨道重构可通过密度泛函理论结合动力学平均场理论（DFT+DMFT）重现。

Conclusion: 该研究在氧化物异质结（oxide heterostructures）中建立了电子、轨道与磁自由度之间的直接且可调谐的耦合关系，为关联电子系统的设计与调控提供了实验和理论依据。

Abstract: Emergent magnetic states at oxide interfaces arise from the interplay of charge transfer, orbital reconstruction, and dimensional confinement, offering a route to engineered correlated-electron behavior in nanoscale spintronic materials. Here, we combine in situ synthesis, polarization-dependent angle-resolved photoelectron spectroscopy, X-ray magnetic circular dichroism, and first-principles electronic-structure calculations to investigate LaNiO3/CaMnO3 superlattices. We show that reducing the LaNiO3 thickness drives a metal-insulator transition accompanied by loss of electronic coherence and an orbital-polarization crossover in the ultrathin limit. These changes weaken charge transfer across the interface and suppress the interfacial Mn magnetic moment in CaMnO3, revealing that the emergent ferromagnetic state is directly governed by electronic confinement in LaNiO3. The insulating state and orbital reconstruction are reproduced by density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory. Together, these results establish a direct and tunable coupling among electronic, orbital, and magnetic degrees of freedom in oxide heterostructures.

### [133] [Positive mass theorem for initial data sets with arbitrary ends](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26978)
*Tin-Yau Tsang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文利用谱正标量曲率（spectral PSC）概念证明了渐近平坦初始数据集的正能量定理，进而通过渐近双曲流形的因果性定量屏蔽定理，确立了满足主能量条件（dominant energy condition）的完备渐近双曲流形的正质量定理，并推广至具有特定对称性的渐近局部双曲末端流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将广义相对论中的正质量定理（positive mass theorem）从渐近平坦情形推广至渐近双曲流形（asymptotically hyperbolic manifold）及渐近局部双曲（asymptotically locally hyperbolic）情形，以完善引力系统的能量-动量正定性理论。

Method: 首先引入 He-Shi-Yu、Bi-Hao-He-Shi-Zhu 以及 Brendle-Wang 提出的谱正标量曲率（spectral PSC）概念，证明渐近平坦初始数据集的正能量定理；随后证明关于渐近双曲流形能量-动量矢量（energy-momentum vector）因果性质的定量屏蔽定理（quantitative shielding theorem）。

Result: 建立了满足主能量条件（dominant energy condition）的完备渐近双曲流形的正质量定理（positive mass theorem）；作为推论，获得了具有特定对称性的渐近局部双曲末端流形的相应结果。

Conclusion: 谱正标量曲率框架可有效推广正质量定理至渐近双曲几何背景，且该结果可进一步拓展至更一般的渐近局部双曲情形。

Abstract: We showed a positive energy theorem for asymptotically flat initial data sets with the concept of spectral PSC by He-Shi-Yu, Bi-Hao-He-Shi-Zhu and Brendle-Wang. Then, we proved a quantitative shielding theorem concerning the causal property of the energy-momentum vector of an asymptotically hyperbolic manifold. As a result, we established the positive mass theorem for complete asymptotically hyperbolic manifolds satisfying the dominant energy condition. As corollaries, we also obtained corresponding results for manifolds with asymptotically locally hyperbolic ends with a certain symmetry.

### [134] [On the Quantisation of Linear Gauge Theories on Lorentzian Manifolds: Maxwell's Theory via Complete Gauge Fixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27026)
*Gabriel Schmid*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了全局双曲流形（globally hyperbolic manifolds）上的双曲型微分算子、线性规范理论（linear gauge theories）及其量子化，涵盖了非局部相互作用的柯西问题、规范固定（gauge fixing）下约束双曲动力学的约化，以及麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell’s theory）中基于新型霍奇分解（Hodge decomposition）的哈达玛态（Hadamard states）存在性证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典双曲型方程通常仅限于局部相互作用，但数学物理多个领域强烈需要处理非局部相互作用；线性规范理论的运动方程一般非双曲型，须通过规范固定才能归结为约束双曲动力学，其柯西问题与量子化需要系统分析；麦克斯韦理论中哈达玛态的存在性问题长期以来缺少基于初始数据层面规范固定的构造方案。

Method: 第一部分从第一性原理（first principles）出发处理对称双曲系统（symmetric hyperbolic systems）及正态双曲算子（normally hyperbolic operators）的柯西问题，并进一步证明耦合非局部势（nonlocal potentials）情形下的适定性（well-posedness）；第二部分对线性规范理论进行详尽分析，展示其通过规范固定约化为约束双曲系统的过程；第三部分在初始数据层面引入新的规范固定方法，利用完整黎曼流形（complete Riemannian manifolds）上索伯列夫空间（Sobolev spaces）中微分k-形式的霍奇分解来抑制非物理自由度，并借助伪微分算子（pseudodifferential calculus）构造态。

Result: 证明了全局双曲流形上对称双曲系统耦合非局部势的柯西问题的适定性；给出了线性规范理论在全局双曲时空（globally hyperbolic spacetimes）中柯西问题与经典相空间（classical phase space）的完整分析，辅以多个物理关注示例；在麦克斯韦理论中，通过初始数据的规范固定方法成功证明了哈达玛态的存在性。

Conclusion: 论文将双曲型方程从局部相互作用推广至非局部情形，建立了线性规范理论中约束双曲动力学的完整理论框架，并为麦克斯韦理论的量子化提供了新的哈达玛态构造方案，推进了弯曲时空量子场论（algebraic quantum field theory）中规范理论的处理方法。

Abstract: This thesis is devoted to the study of hyperbolic differential operators on globally hyperbolic manifolds, linear gauge theories and their quantisation.
  In the first part, we treat the Cauchy problem for symmetric hyperbolic systems and normally hyperbolic operators on globally hyperbolic manifolds from first principles. Although hyperbolic equations are usually studied with local interactions, there are strong motivations from several areas of mathematical physics to consider also nonlocal interactions. As an intermezzo, we therefore take a small deviation from the classical local theory and prove well-posedness of the Cauchy problem for symmetric hyperbolic systems coupled to a broad class of nonlocal potentials.
  The second part presents a detailed exposition of linear gauge theories in globally hyperbolic spacetimes. Linear gauge theories are yet another deviation from the concept of hyperbolicity: the corresponding equations of motion are generically non-hyperbolic; however, can always be reduced to a constrained hyperbolic dynamics once an appropriate gauge fixing procedure has been applied. We give a thorough analysis of their Cauchy problem and classical phase space, complemented by a detailed discussion of many examples of physical interest, and discuss their quantisation following the algebraic approach to quantum field theory.
  The final chapter is devoted to the quantisation of Maxwell's theory on globally hyperbolic spacetimes, with the goal of proving the existence of Hadamard states. The novelty of our approach lies in a new gauge-fixing procedure at the level of initial data, which allows us to suppress the unphysical degrees of freedom. This gauge is achieved by means of a new Hodge decomposition for differential k-forms in Sobolev spaces on complete Riemannian manifolds, while states are constructed using tools from pseudodifferential calculus.

</details>


### [135] [The quantum group structure of long-range integrable deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27189)
*Koen Schouten,Marius de Leeuw*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从量子群（quantum group）理论的角度，描述了均匀杨-巴克斯特可积自旋链（Yang-Baxter integrable spin chains）在变形参数一阶展开下的长程形变（long-range deformations），证明形变通过扭结（twist）代数结构实现，并由此得到非结合代数和非平凡德林菲尔德结合子（Drinfeld associator），后者编码了长程相互作用项。变形后的量子群包含一个大的微扰结合子结构，并显式给出满足RLL关系和杨-巴克斯特方程（Yang-Baxter equation）至一阶的拉克斯算子（Lax operators）和R矩阵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子可积自旋链已知存在由局域、升维（boost）和双局域算子生成的大族长程形变，但背后的量子群结构尚未被认识。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立长程形变的量子群理论描述。

Method: 引入称为代数荷密度（algebraic charge densities）的代数元素；通过对底层量子群代数结构施加扭结（twist）来获得形变，并分析由此产生的非结合代数结构及德林菲尔德结合子（Drinfeld associator）。讨论微扰结合子结构以确保可积性。

Result: 长程形变通过量子群代数的扭结实现，导致一个一般非结合且具有非平凡德林菲尔德结合子的代数；该结合子编码了长程相互作用项。变形后的量子群显式给出满足RLL关系和杨-巴克斯特方程至一阶的拉克斯算子和R矩阵。此外，提出未形变荷密度的代数元素显式表达式猜想。

Conclusion: 该工作为长程形变可积自旋链提供了系统的量子群理论框架，揭示了形变的代数根源，并为后续研究高阶形变及更一般模型奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Quantum integrable spin chains are known to possess a large family of long-range deformations generated by the local, boost and bilocal operators. Although these deformations are well-understood on the level of the pairwise commuting charges, the underlying quantum group structures had not yet been recognised. In this paper, we provide a quantum group-theoretical description for the family of long-range deformations of arbitrary homogeneous Yang-Baxter integrable spin chains up to first order in the deformation parameter. In particular, we show that the deformations are obtained via a twist of the algebraic structure of the underlying quantum group. This twisting results in a generally non-associative algebra that has a non-trivial Drinfeld associator. The Drinfeld associator is then shown to encode the information about the long-range interaction terms for the integrable spin chain. Moreover, the deformed quantum group is shown to contain a large perturbatively associative substructure, thus ensuring the perturbative integrability of the long-range model. The deformed quantum group provides explicit expressions for the Lax operators and R-matrices of the long-range deformed models, which manifestly satisfy the RLL relation and the Yang-Baxter equation up to first order in the deformation parameter. In order to derive the results, we introduce algebra elements that we call the algebraic charge densities. As a side result, we provide a conjecture for the explicit expressions of the undeformed charge densities in terms of these algebra elements.

</details>


### [136] [Dynamical delocalization in disordered 2D Chern insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27194)
*Gianluca Panati,Constanza Rojas-Molina,Vincenzo Rossi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在一般随机势微扰下的二维陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）中存在表现出动力学退局域化（dynamical delocalization）的能量。通过利用陈数（Chern number）整数值跳跃和平均谱投影（averaged spectral projections）在能量与无序参数下的连续性，证明无序存在时拓扑指标（topological index）的鲁棒性，并结合已有动力学局域化方法给出相图细节。新颖之处在于能在无序参数（而非仅能量参数）中展示动力学退局域化，从而证明即使在无序强度导致能隙闭合时仍存在安德森金属-绝缘体转变（Anderson metal-insulator transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无序存在的情况下，二维陈绝缘体中的动力学退局域化现象尚未被一般性证明。本文旨在填补这一空白，并进一步揭示拓扑相图与无序诱导的金属-绝缘体转变之间的关联。

Method: 利用陈示性数（Chern character）整数值的跳跃以及平均谱投影在能量和无序参数上的连续性，证明拓扑指标在无序下的鲁棒性，再与已有的动力学局域化证明方法结合，分析模型的相图。

Result: 证明了在一般随机势微扰下的二维陈绝缘体中存在动力学退局域化的能量；能够在无序参数中（而非仅限于能量参数）展示动力学退局域化；证明了即使能隙因无序强度而闭合，仍然存在安德森金属-绝缘体转变。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种新的方法论，可在无序参数中证明动力学退局域化，从而更全面地刻画无序拓扑系统中的相图，深化了对安德森金属-绝缘体转变与拓扑结构之间关系的理解。

Abstract: We show the existence of energies exhibiting dynamical delocalization in discrete 2D Chern insulators perturbed by a random potential in a general setting. Our proof exploits two main features of the model: jumps in the integer value of the Chern character and continuity of averaged spectral projections in both energy and disorder parameters. This allows us to show robustness of the topological index in the presence of disorder, which, combined with existing methods to prove dynamical localization, allows us to provide detailed information on the phase diagram of the model. The novelty of our approach is that we are able to show dynamical delocalization in the disorder parameter, and not only in the energy parameter, which allows to prove Anderson metal-insulator transition even when spectral gaps close due to the strength of disorder.

</details>


### [137] [Hamilton--Jacobi theory for non-conservative field theories in the $k$-contact framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27670)
*Javier de Lucas,Julia Lange,Xavier Rivas,Cristina Sardón*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在共定向 k-接触几何（co-oriented k-contact geometry）框架下，为包含耗散系统的非保守经典场论发展了一套 Hamilton–Jacobi 理论，提出了演化 k-接触 k-向量场，发展了 z-不依赖与 z-依赖两类 Hamilton–Jacobi 方法，并通过多个具体实例验证了理论的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典场论中的耗散系统（dissipative systems）缺乏统一的几何框架来描述，现有接触 Hamilton–Jacobi 理论仅适用于 k=1 的情形且存在技术假设限制，亟需将其推广至更一般的场论情景。

Method: 在共定向 k-接触几何框架下，引入演化 k-接触 k-向量场（evolution k-contact k-vector fields）以扩展接触演化形式到场论；发展两类 Hamilton–Jacobi 理论：z-不依赖方法（基于底流形 $(\bigoplus^kT^*Q)\times\mathbb{R}^k\to Q$ 上的可积 k-向量场重构动力学）和 z-依赖方法（基于底流形 $(\bigoplus^kT^*Q)\times\mathbb{R}^k\to Q\times\mathbb{R}^k$ 上的可积 k-向量场）。

Result: 详细推导了耗散变量呈仿射依赖的 Hamilton 函数情形；展示了耗散变量的二次依赖可结构性扩展应用范围；恢复了 k=1 时普通接触 Hamilton–Jacobi 理论作为特例，并去除了先前公式中的若干技术假设；通过电报/Klein–Gordon 方程、耗散 Hunter–Saxton 方程等实例验证了理论。

Conclusion: 该工作为非保守经典场论尤其是耗散系统提供了统一的几何 Hamilton–Jacobi 描述框架，通过 k-接触几何推广了标准理论，并去除了此前存在的技术限制，具有更广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: This article develops a Hamilton--Jacobi theory for non-conservative classical field theories, with particular emphasis on dissipative systems, in the framework of co-oriented k-contact geometry. We introduce evolution k-contact k-vector fields, extending the contact evolution formalism to field theories, and analyse the corresponding Hamilton--De Donder--Weyl equations. Moreover, we develop two distinct families of Hamilton--Jacobi theories: a z-independent approach, based on the reconstruction of the dynamics from an integrable k-vector field defined on the base manifold of $(\bigoplus^kT^*Q)\times\mathbb{R}^k\to Q$, and a z-dependent approach, where the integrable k-vector field is defined on the base manifold of $(\bigoplus^kT^*Q)\times\mathbb{R}^k\to Q\times\mathbb{R}^k$. We develop in detail the important case of Hamiltonian functions with affine dependence on the dissipative variables, show how quadratic dependence on these variables can be used structurally to enlarge the range of applications, and recover the ordinary contact Hamilton--Jacobi theory as the particular case k=1, while removing some technical assumptions appearing in previous formulations. Our theory is illustrated through several representative examples, including the telegrapher/Klein--Gordon equation, a dissipative Hunter--Saxton equation, a simple dissipative non-regular first-order field model, and a relativistic thermodynamic model.

</details>


### [138] [Hypergeometric Functions of Nilpotent Operators: Functional Collapse and Structural Depth at Exceptional Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27834)
*Ramon Moya*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限维空间中幂零算子（nilpotent operator）的超几何函数（hypergeometric function），发现当自变量为幂零算子时，广义超几何函数 pFq 退化为至多 m 次的多项式，无需解析收敛条件；并建立了“幂零深度准则”（nilpotent depth criterion），用以刻画非厄米量子力学中例外点（exceptional point）处哈密顿量的 Jordan 深度（Jordan depth）缩减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于非厄米量子力学（non-Hermitian quantum mechanics）中例外点（exceptional point）的代数结构，即哈密顿量在该点处不可对角化、呈现 Jordan 块形式。作者希望利用幂零算子的超几何函数来理解和控制例外点处 Jordan 深度的变化。

Method: 在复数域上的结合代数中，考虑幂零指数为 m+1 的幂零算子 N；证明任意广义超几何函数 pFq(N) 退化为至多 m 次的多项式（“函数塌缩”，functional collapse）；进一步提出“幂零深度准则”（nilpotent depth criterion，定理 2）：若形式级数 F 的首个非常数系数出现在次数 r≥1，则 F(N)−F(0)I 的幂零指数不超过 ceil((m+1)/r)。

Result: 定理 3 给出例外点处哈密顿量 H=λI+N 的结论：若 F 在 λ 处解析且接触阶（contact order）为 r，则 F(H) 将 Jordan 深度从 m+1 缩减至不超过 ceil((m+1)/r)。具体推论包括：时间演化算子 e^{tH} 对所有 t≠0 保持完整 Jordan 深度；具有 m+1 阶零点的函数消灭整个 Jordan 结构；修正预解式（modified resolvent）的极点阶数从 m+1 降至最多 m+1−r。3×3 Jordan 块数值示例验证了界的紧致性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了幂零算子超几何函数“函数塌缩”的一般框架，给出了例外点处 Jordan 结构受函数接触阶调控的精确上界，为非厄米量子力学中例外点附近算符行为的代数分析提供了系统性工具。

Abstract: We study hypergeometric functions of nilpotent operators in finite-dimensional settings, motivated by the algebraic structure of exceptional points in non-Hermitian quantum mechanics. Our starting point is the following exact result: if N is a nilpotent operator of index m+1 in an associative algebra over C, then every generalized hypergeometric function pFq evaluated at N reduces to a finite polynomial in N of degree at most m, without any analytic convergence requirement. This "functional collapse" is distinct from the classical parameter-termination mechanism and arises purely from the nilpotent structure of the argument. The main result is a "nilpotent depth criterion" (Theorem 2): if the first non-constant coefficient of a formal series F appears in degree r >= 1, then the nilpotent part F(N) - F(0)I has nilpotency index bounded above by ceil((m+1)/r). We apply this criterion to Hamiltonians at exceptional points, where H = lambda I + N with N^{m+1} = 0. Theorem 3 establishes that a function F analytic at lambda reduces the Jordan depth of the exceptional point from m+1 to at most ceil((m+1)/r), where r is the contact order of F at lambda. As consequences: the time evolution operator e^{tH} preserves the full Jordan depth for all t != 0; a function with a zero of order m+1 at lambda annihilates the entire Jordan structure; and the order of the pole of the modified resolvent is reduced from m+1 to at most m+1-r. Results are illustrated with explicit 3x3 Jordan block computations for 1F1, 2F1, and the time evolution operator, confirming sharpness of the bounds.

</details>


### [139] [No-Go Theorem for Quasiparticle BEC in the Spin-Boson Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27904)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在泛函积分表示（functional integral representations）与预解代数（resolvent algebra）框架下，分析了自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson model）在有限温度下发生玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）的可能性。尽管零模引出的半双线性形式形式上允许类似自由玻色气体的BEC分量，但基于arxiv:1207.4621的定义，对于中等平衡态（moderate equilibrium states），论文证明了一个BEC的不存在定理（no-go theorem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-玻色子模型中准粒子是否会在有限温度下发生玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）尚不明确。由于零模导致的半双线性形式在形式上暗示了BEC存在的可能性，而先前工作（arxiv:1207.4621）指出准粒子不发生BEC，因此需要严格的论证来排除这一可能性。

Method: 采用泛函积分表示（functional integral representations）和预解代数（resolvent algebra）作为理论框架，并依据arxiv:1207.4621中关于中等平衡态（moderate equilibrium states）的定义和形式体系进行分析。

Result: 在自旋-玻色子模型中，零模（zero mode）引出了一个与自由玻色气体类似的半双线性形式（sesquilinear form），形式上允许BEC型分量的存在。但针对中等平衡态，论文推导出了BEC的不存在定理（no-go theorem）。

Conclusion: 自旋-玻色子模型在中等平衡态下不存在有限温度的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC），验证了之前工作中关于准粒子不发生BEC的论断。

Abstract: We analyze the possibility of Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) at finite temperature in the spin-boson model within the frameworks of functional integral representations and the resolvent algebra. Because a sesquilinear form arising from the zero mode appears, analogous to the case of the free Bose gas, a BEC-type component is also formally present in the spin-boson model. However, according to arxiv:1207.4621, quasiparticles do not undergo BEC, so an argument is needed to exclude this possibility. In particular, for moderate equilibrium states defined by following the formulation of that paper, a no-go theorem for BEC is obtained.

</details>


### [140] [Constrained Symplectic and Contact Hamiltonian Systems: A Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27940)
*Callum Bell,David Sloan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统阐述了奇异理论（singular theories）在预辛流形（pre-symplectic manifolds）和预切触流形（pre-contact manifolds）上的几何结构，并发展了相应的约束算法（constraint algorithms），以确定存在一致哈密顿演化（Hamiltonian evolution）的相空间（phase space）允许子集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异理论因其拉格朗日描述（Lagrangian description）或哈密顿描述（Hamiltonian description）中存在退化性（degeneracies），需要系统实施约束才能获得良定义的动力学（well-defined dynamics）。辛框架（symplectic framework）适用于保守力学系统，但具有耗散效应（dissipative effects）的理论需在切触几何（contact geometry）框架下讨论，因此亟需建立统一的几何约束算法。

Method: 本文采用几何方法，首先分别构建预辛流形和预切触流形的底层几何结构，然后针对每种几何结构发展相应的约束算法，以确定相空间中存在一致哈密顿演化的允许子集。

Result: 针对预辛流形和预切触流形，分别建立了相应的约束算法，能够系统性地确定相空间中满足一致哈密顿演化的可允许子集。

Conclusion: 每种约束算法的讨论均以具体示例收尾，验证了所提出几何框架和算法的有效性。

Abstract: Singular theories, characterised by the presence of degeneracies in their Lagrangian or Hamiltonian descriptions, require the systematic implementation of constraints in order to obtain well-defined dynamics. While the symplectic framework provides the standard geometrical setting for conservative mechanical systems, those theories which exhibit dissipative effects are most appropriately discussed within the context of contact geometry. In this review, we present the geometrical structure underlying pre-symplectic and pre-contact manifolds, and develop the corresponding constraint algorithms that determine the admissible subset of phase space upon which consistent Hamiltonian evolution exists. We then close the discussion of each of the constraint algorithms with an example.

### [141] [Integrable systems from Poisson reductions of generalized Hamiltonian torus actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.12051)
*L. Feher,M. Fairon*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一组充分条件，确保具有对称群 $K$ 的可积系统（integrable system）在商泊松空间（quotient Poisson space）$M/K$ 的稠密开子集上仍保持可积性，并应用到紧李群（compact Lie group）双上的约化系统及平坦联络模空间（moduli space of flat connections）上的可积系统等若干开放问题中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在约化过程中，原本在较大相空间 $M$ 上可积的系统不一定会保持可积性，因此需要系统性的充分条件来保证约化后的系统仍然是可积的，特别是当相空间携带准泊松（quasi-Poisson）双向量且对称群具有 $\mathrm{U}(1)^{\ell_1} \times \mathbb{R}^{\ell_2}$ 形式时。

Method: 通过在流形 $M$ 上构建具有对称群 $K$ 的可积系统，并假设该未约化系统拥有生成 $\mathrm{U}(1)^{\ell_1} \times \mathbb{R}^{\ell_2}$ 恰当有效作用的“作用量变量（action variables）”，证明这些作用量变量可以下降到约化系统中，从而建立约化系统可积性的充分条件。由于群的形式以及 $P_M$ 可能是准泊松双向量，该方法被概括为广义哈密顿环面作用（generalized Hamiltonian torus action）。

Result: 该条件保证了约化系统在商泊松空间 $M/K$ 的稠密开子集上是可积的，且由于 $\mathrm{U}(1)^{\ell_1} \times \mathbb{R}^{\ell_2}$ 恰当哈密顿作用产生的大量不变量，约化系统通常具有超可积（superintegrable）性。论文通过多种例子验证了该框架，并成功解决了有关紧李群双上约化系统的可积性开放问题，包括余切丛（cotangent bundle）、海森堡双（Heisenberg double）和准泊松双（quasi-Poisson double）。此外，还利用准泊松方法给出了平坦联络模空间上可积系统的多个应用。

Conclusion: 该充分条件为对称群约化下可积性的保持问题提供了一个通用框架，并展示了其在紧李群双约化和平坦联络模空间可积系统中的应用价值，为这些领域的开放问题提供了解决方案。

Abstract: We develop a set of sufficient conditions for guaranteeing that an integrable system with a symmetry group $K$ on a manifold $M$ descends to an integrable system on a dense open subset of the quotient Poisson space $M/K$. The higher dimensional phase space $M$ carries a bivector $P_M$ yielding a bracket on $C^\infty(M)$ such that $C^\infty(M)^K$ is a Poisson algebra. The unreduced system on $M$ is supposed to possess `action variables' that generate a proper, effective action of a group of the form $\mathrm{U}(1)^{\ell_1} \times \mathbb{R}^{\ell_2}$ and descend to action variables of the reduced system. In view of the form of the group and since $P_M$ could be a quasi-Poisson bivector, we say that we work with a generalized Hamiltonian torus action. The reduced systems are in general superintegrable owing to the large set of invariants of the proper Hamiltonian action of $\mathrm{U}(1)^{\ell_1} \times \mathbb{R}^{\ell_2}$. We present several examples and apply our construction for solving open problems regarding the integrability of systems obtained previously by reductions of master systems on doubles of compact Lie groups: the cotangent bundle, the Heisenberg double and the quasi-Poisson double. Furthermore, we offer numerous applications to integrable systems living on moduli spaces of flat connections, using the quasi-Poisson approach.

</details>


### [142] [Spherical singularities in compactified Ruijsenaars--Schneider systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18023)
*L. Feher,H. R. Dullin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类通过约化SU(n)拟哈密顿对偶（quasi-Hamiltonian double）构造的刘维尔可积系统（Liouville integrable systems）。这些系统存在于维数为2(n-1)的紧致连通辛流形上，可解释为紧致化三角Ruijsenaars–Schneider系统。根据参数y的取值，系统分为两类：类型(i)为环面系统（toric systems）；类型(ii)的全局连续作用变量仅在相空间稠密开子集上生成哈密顿环面作用。本文重点研究类型(ii)中位于稠密环面作用域补集内的作用映射纤维（即T^{n-1}动量映射的纤维），证明所有此类“奇异纤维”均为光滑连通的各向同性子流形（isotropic submanifolds），并给出了纤维作为SU(n)子群在另一子群作用下的商空间的模型。以n≥4且π/(n-1) < y < π/(n-2)的最简类型(ii)案例为例，确定了作用变量填充的多面体顶点，并证明这些情形下“奇异顶点”上的纤维微分同胚于S^3 ≃ SU(2)。该结果丰富了具有球面奇异性（spherical singularities）的刘维尔可积系统案例集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前通过约化SU(n)拟哈密顿对偶构造了一类刘维尔可积系统，它们在不同参数取值下表现出截然不同的结构：类型(i)为环面系统，类型(ii)则仅在相空间稠密开子集上存在连续作用变量生成的哈密顿环面作用。本文的核心动机是深入研究类型(ii)中那些位于稠密环面作用域补集内的奇异纤维（singular fibers），以揭示系统的全局辛几何结构。

Method: 首先将奇异纤维定义为作用映射（即T^{n-1}动量映射）在稠密环面作用域补集内的纤维。通过分析这些纤维的几何性质，证明它们是光滑连通的各向同性子流形。利用SU(n)子群在另一子群作用下的商空间构造纤维模型。选取n≥4且π/(n-1) < y < π/(n-2)的最简类型(ii)案例进行具体计算，确定作用变量填充的多面体的顶点，并验证奇异顶点上的纤维微分同胚于S^3 ≃ SU(2)。

Result: 证明所有奇异纤维都是光滑连通的各向同性子流形。给出了纤维作为SU(n)特定子群在另一子群作用下的商空间的模型。在n≥4且π/(n-1) < y < π/(n-2)的最简类型(ii)案例中，确定了作用变量填充的多面体的顶点，并证明这些奇异顶点上的纤维微分同胚于S^3 ≃ SU(2)。

Conclusion: 该研究丰富了具有球面奇异性（spherical singularities）的刘维尔可积系统（Liouville integrable systems）的案例集，为理解类型(ii)紧致化三角Ruijsenaars–Schneider系统的奇异纤维结构提供了系统性的几何刻画。

Abstract: We investigate certain Liouville integrable systems constructed earlier via reduction of the quasi-Hamiltonian double of $\mathrm{SU}(n)$. These systems live on compact connected symplectic manifolds of dimension $2(n-1)$ and can be interpreted as compactified trigonometric Ruijsenaars--Schneider systems. Depending on the value of a parameter $0<y< π$, they arise in two drastically different forms: in type (i) these are toric systems, while in the type (ii) cases they possess globally continuous action variables that generate a Hamiltonian torus action (only) on a dense open subset of the phase space. The principal goal of the paper is to study those fibers of the action map (alias the $\mathbb{T}^{n-1}$ momentum map) which are contained in the complement of the domain of the densely defined torus action occurring in the type (ii) cases. We demonstrate that all such `singular fibers' are smooth connected isotropic submanifolds. We also work out a model of the fibers as quotient spaces of certain subgroups of $\mathrm{SU}(n)$ with respect to an action of another subgroup. The general results are exemplified by determining the vertices of the polytope filled by the action variables in the simplest type (ii) cases that appear for any $n\geq 4$ with $π/(n-1) <y < π/(n-2)$, and proving that the fibers over the `singular vertices' are diffeomorphic to $S^3 \simeq \mathrm{SU}(2)$ in these cases. In this way, our findings enrich the set of examples of Liouville integrable systems with spherical singularities.

### [143] [Optical effects in Gaseous Electron Multipliers (GEMs)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27399)
*D. Edgeman,F. M. Brunbauer,M. Gardner,D. Loomba,P. A. Majewski,T. Marley,L. Millins,T. Neep,K. Nikolopoulos,J. Schueler,E. Tilly,W. Thompson*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验室测量和Geant4模拟，系统研究了基于GEM的光学时间投影室（OTPC）中由于GEM衬底导光引起的光学展宽效应，发现玻璃GEM的展宽最强，最高可使模拟粒子径迹的强度和宽度分别增加约26%和31%，从而解释了MIGDAL实验中观测到的径迹异常。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对三种类型的GEM衬底（玻璃、陶瓷和FR4）进行实验室测量，检验雪崩过程中GEM孔内产生的闪烁光（scintillation light）穿过衬底并从邻近孔出射的光学展宽（optical broadening）效应；同时使用Geant4模拟复现实验结果，并量化真实电荷雪崩中的光学展宽。

Conclusion: 玻璃GEM衬底的导光效应是导致MIGDAL OTPC中径迹强度和宽度大于预期的可能原因，且该效应预计在基于GEM的所有OTPC中普遍存在。

Abstract: Optical time projection chambers (OTPCs) are well suited for applications that require the highest spatial resolution for particle track reconstruction. The MIGDAL experiment uses a glass GEM-based OTPC and observes a systematic excess in both the intensity and width of particle tracks in its optical readout, when compared with charge readout simulations. One hypothesis is that scintillation light produced inside a GEM hole during the avalanche propagates through the GEM substrate and exits neighboring holes. We present lab measurements testing this hypothesized optical broadening effect in three types of GEM substrates: glass, ceramic, and FR4. Our observations quantify this optical broadening and demonstrate it to be strongest in glass GEMs. Additionally, we use Geant4 simulations to both reproduce our observations and quantify optical broadening effects in realistic charge avalanches. Applying our glass GEM effects to simulated particle tracks yields increases of track intensity and widths by up to around 26% and 31%, respectively. This may explain the larger than expected intensity and track widths observed in the MIGDAL OTPC and is expected to be an observed effect in all GEM-based OTPCs.

### [145] [AutoREC: A software platform for developing reinforcement learning agents for equivalent circuit model generation from electrochemical impedance spectroscopy data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27266)
*Ali Jaberi,Yonatan Kurniawan,Robert Black,Shayan Mousavi M.,Kabir Verma,Zoya Sadighi,Santiago Miret,Jason Hattrick-Simpers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 AutoREC，一个基于强化学习（reinforcement learning, RL）的开源 Python 工具包，能够从电化学阻抗谱数据中自动生成等效电路模型（equivalent circuit models, ECMs）。实验表明，该工具在合成数据集上成功率超过 99.6%，并能泛化到多种真实实验数据上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的等效电路模型（ECM）识别依赖人工试错，需要领域专家且难以规模化，尤其不适合自主实验管道（如自驱动实验室）的高通量需求，因此亟需一种自动化的 ECM 生成方法。

Method: 将 ECM 构建形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（Markov Decision Process, MDP）中的序列决策问题；采用带优先经验回放（prioritized experience replay）的双深度 Q 网络（Double Deep Q-Network），并设计了专用的死循环缓解策略（dead-loop mitigation strategy），以高效探索复杂的电路生成动作空间。

Result: 在合成数据集上成功率达到 99.6% 以上，并在来自电池、腐蚀、析氧反应和 CO₂ 还原系统的未见实验 EIS 数据上展现出强大的泛化能力。

Conclusion: AutoREC 被定位为一种自适应、数据驱动的 ECM 生成平台，有望集成到自动化电化学工作流中，未来可通过策略改进进一步缓解当前局限性。

Abstract: This paper introduces AutoREC, an open-source Python package for developing reinforcement learning (RL) agents to automatically generate equivalent circuit models (ECMs) from electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) data. While ECMs are a standard framework for interpreting EIS data, traditional identification is typically based on manual trial-and-error, which requires domain experts and limits scalability, particularly in autonomous experimental pipelines such as self-driving laboratories. AutoREC addresses this challenge by formulating ECM construction as a sequential decision-making problem within a Markov Decision Process framework. It implements a Double Deep Q-Network with prioritized experience replay, along with a dedicated dead-loop mitigation strategy, to efficiently explore a complex action space for circuit generation. To demonstrate the capabilities of the platform, we trained an RL agent using AutoREC and evaluated its strengths and limitations across diverse datasets, while also discussing possible strategies to mitigate these limitations in future agent designs. The trained agent achieved a success rate exceeding $99.6\%$ on synthetic datasets and demonstrated strong generalization to unseen experimental EIS data from batteries, corrosion, oxygen evolution reaction, and CO$_2$ reduction systems. These results position AutoREC as a promising platform for adaptive and data-driven ECM generation, with potential for integration into automated electrochemical workflows.

</details>

### [146] [Radio signal generation in milliseconds: enabling multi-parameter reconstruction of ultra-high-energy cosmic rays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27684)
*Arsène Ferrière*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于机器学习的仿真器（emulator），能够替代计算密集型的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，在毫秒级内高精度重现超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs）的无线电信号，并基于马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法实现宇宙射线性质的重构，在GRANDProto300实验中达到8.9%的电磁能量分辨率和0.08°的角度分辨率，并成功应用于真实数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs，能量超过$10^{18}$ eV）的无线电探测技术近年来已成熟，但精确的无线电信号模拟依赖于ZHAireS和CoREAS等蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）代码，这些模拟虽然关键但计算代价极高，限制了重构效率。

Method: 构建一个基于机器学习（machine learning）的仿真器（emulator）来替代传统蒙特卡洛模拟；利用ZHAireS对GRANDProto300实验布局进行模拟来训练该仿真器；采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法，将实测信号与仿真器生成的信号进行比对，从而重构初级宇宙射线的性质。

Result: 该仿真器在毫秒级时间内完成高精度信号模拟，较传统数小时的蒙特卡洛模拟大幅加速；在GRANDProto300实验布局上，电磁能量分辨率达到8.9%，角度分辨率达到0.08°，与当前最优（state-of-the-art）重构性能相当。

Conclusion: 该方法在真实数据上成功重建了GP300原型探测器探测到的宇宙射线候选事件，验证了其在实际观测场景中的有效性，表明基于机器学习的仿真器有望大幅提升UHECR无线电探测的数据分析效率。

Abstract: In recent years, radio detection of ultra-high-energy cosmic rays (UHECRs), with energies above $10^{18}$ eV, has become an established technique. The radio emissions can be simulated with high accuracy using Monte Carlo codes such as ZHAireS and CoREAS. These simulations are essential but are computationally intensive. In this work, we present a machine-learning-based emulator that reproduces radio signal simulations with high accuracy in milliseconds rather than hours. Primary particle properties can then be reconstructed by comparing measured signals to emulated traces using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo approach. Using ZHAireS simulations carried out over the GRANDProto300 experiment layout, the method achieves an 8.9\% resolution on electromagnetic energy and a 0.08° angular resolution, matching state-of-the-art reconstruction performance. Finally, we apply the method on real data, successfully reconstructing cosmic-ray candidates detected by the GP300 prototype.

### [147] [A benchmark for binary star interaction with a supermassive black hole in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27429)
*Megha Sharma,Alexander Heger,Daniel J. Price,Emilio Tejeda,Evgeni Grishin,Luis A. Manzaneda,Alessandro A. Trani*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文对比了后牛顿近似（post-Newtonian, PN）与标量微扰背景度规（scalar perturbation to a background metric）两种方案，用于求解包含超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的恒星质量双星三体问题。研究发现，对于一百万倍太阳质量的黑洞，两种近似方案统计上一致；但对十亿倍太阳质量的黑洞，不同方案在双星间距和偏心率上出现分歧。其中，成对后牛顿（pair-wise PN）方法在所有测试情形下均导致近心点间距减小，可靠性最差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大多数星系中心存在超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole, SMBH），其周围存在恒星及其双星系统。准确描述这一三体系统的动力学行为，对于理解极端质量比旋近（extreme mass ratio inspiral, EMRI）等天体物理过程至关重要，但不同数值近似方案在强引力场下的可靠性尚不明确。

Method: 采用两种数值方案求解包含双星与SMBH的三体问题：后牛顿近似（PN）方案和标量微扰背景度规（metric-with-perturbation）方案。PN方案内部测试了三种不同形式：爱因斯坦-英菲尔德-霍夫曼方程（Einstein-Infeld-Hoffman equation）、三体中两体PN项成对实现（pair-wise PN）以及阿诺维特-德塞-米斯纳哈密顿量（Arnowitt-Deser-Misner Hamiltonian）。分别针对一百万倍和十亿倍太阳质量黑洞进行测试，并开展统计研究。

Result: 对于一百万倍太阳质量黑洞，两种近似方案在恒星质量双星的相互作用上统计匹配；成对后牛顿（pair-wise PN）方法在所有测试条件下均导致近心点（pericentre）间距减小。对于十亿倍太阳质量黑洞，不同方案在双星间距减小和偏心率（eccentricity）变化上出现分歧，但若双星间距较大或远离黑洞，由于广义相对论效应减弱，该分歧消失。

Conclusion: 不同数值方案在超大质量黑洞附近的计算结果需要谨慎解读；成对后牛顿（pair-wise PN）方法是求解该问题最不可靠的方案。在利用模拟理解极端质量比旋近（EMRI）时，双星越靠近黑洞，越应警惕不同公式间的系统性偏差。

Abstract: Most galaxies have supermassive black holes (SMBH) at their centres, surrounded by stars with binary systems also present in this environment. We use two schemes - post-Newtonian (PN) and a scalar perturbation to a background metric to numerically solve the three-body problem of a binary with a SMBH. We test three different PN formulations for the PN scheme: The Einstein-Infeld-Hoffman equation, pair-wise implementation of two-body PN-terms for three bodies and the Arnowitt-Deser-Misner Hamiltonian. We compare these approaches for one million solar mass and one billion solar mass black holes, and find a statistical match between the two approximations for stellar mass binary interacting with a million solar mass black hole. We also perform a statistical study for encounters with this black hole, and find that the higher order PN formulation matches with metric-with-perturbation scheme. However, we find a decrease in separation of the binary, and eccentricity variations between different schemes around the billion solar mass black hole. This behaviour is not present if binary has a large separation or is further away from the black hole due to decreased general-relativistic effects. We find that the pair-wise PN method results in a decrease in separation at pericentre in all test cases irrespective of the distance from the black hole or mass of the black hole, making this the least reliable method for solving this problem. Our work highlights the need for caution when interpreting the results in different formulations around SMBHs. This also shows that when understanding extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs) using simulations, one should beware as the binary gets closer to the black hole.

</details>

### [149] [Superconductivity-Enabled Conversion of Ferromagnetic Resonance into Standing Spin Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27076)
*Ya. V. Turkin,N. G. Pugach,F. M. Maksimov,A. S. Pakhomov,A. I. Chernov,V. I. Belotelov,S. N. Polulyakh,V. S. Stolyarov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论证明了传统扩散型超导体能够将铁磁绝缘体中的均匀铁磁共振（FMR）模式转换为垂直驻立自旋波（PSSWs），并建立了包含自旋三重态库珀对和Abrikosov涡旋的微观理论来精确描述这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体可在无焦耳耗散下传输自旋，但超导体与绝缘磁体中短波长磁振子（magnons）之间的相干耦合尚未被充分探索。

Method: 实验上采用Bi取代铁石榴石/Nb双层膜结构进行微波传输测量；理论上构建了将准经典Keldysh–Usadel超导凝聚体描述与Landau–Lifshitz–Gilbert动力学自洽耦合的微观理论。

Result: 在Nb的超导转变温度以下，微波传输谱出现一个位于均匀FMR峰附近的新共振特征；理论分析表明，该转换依赖于两个关键机制：由自旋极化三重态库珀对（triplet Cooper pairs）介导的界面自旋转移矩（spin-transfer torque），以及由Abrikosov涡旋产生的深度依赖有效场（电磁邻近效应）。

Conclusion: 理论计算的磁化率（susceptibility）准确复现了实测线形，证明超导电性可作为磁性绝缘体中交换驻立波模式的有效控制手段。

Abstract: Superconductors can transport spin without Joule dissipation, yet their coherent coupling to short-wavelength magnons in insulating magnets remains largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate experimentally and theoretically that a conventional diffusive superconductor can enable the conversion of the uniform ferromagnetic-resonance (FMR) mode into perpendicular standing spin waves (PSSWs) in an adjacent ferrimagnetic insulator. In Bi-substituted iron-garnet/Nb bilayers, the microwave transmission develops an additional resonance feature that appears only below the Nb transition temperature and lies close to the uniform FMR peak. A microscopic theory that self-consistently couples the quasiclassical Keldysh--Usadel description of the superconducting condensate to the Landau--Lifshitz--Gilbert dynamics shows that the conversion requires two ingredients: (i) an interfacial spin-transfer torque mediated by spin-polarized triplet Cooper pairs and (ii) a depth-dependent effective field produced by Abrikosov vortices (electromagnetic proximity). The resulting susceptibility reproduces the measured lineshapes and establishes superconductivity as an active control knob for exchange standing-wave modes in magnetic insulators.

### [150] [Phase Stability of Superfluid $^{3}\mathrm{He}$ in Anisotropic Aerogel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27098)
*J. W. Scott,D. Park,X. Yuan,W. P. Halperin*

Method: 采用含温度依赖各向异性的金兹堡-朗道模型（temperature dependent anisotropic Ginzburg-Landau model）对实验观察到的磁场无关转变温度Tx进行理论描述。

Result: 发现超流氦-3的矢量自由度会在一个与磁场无关的转变温度Tx处发生自发重取向（spontaneously reorient）。

Conclusion: 各向异性无序能够取向超流氦-3的矢量自由度并影响其相稳定性；所提出的温度依赖各向异性金兹堡-朗道模型可定量描述该自发重取向转变。

Abstract: The A and B phases of superfluid 3 He have vector degrees of freedom that reflect their characteristic broken symmetries, respectively chiral and spin-orbit rotation axes. Anisotropic disorder in the superfluid, imbibed in uniformly strained silica aerogel, orients these degrees of freedom, thereby affecting phase stability. These degrees of freedom have been found to spontaneously reorient at a field-independent transition temperature Tx , that can be accounted for with a temperature dependent anisotropic Ginzburg-Landau model.

### [151] [Magnetic Quantum Criticality inside the Superconducting State Revealed by Penetration Depth Scaling with Local $T_{\mathrm c}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27507)
*Yusuke Iguchi,Kaede Inoh,Ryosuke Koizumi,Makoto Yokoyama*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过扫描SQUID显微镜测量锌掺杂CeCoIn₅的超导态磁穿透深度，发现其中存在一个磁量子临界点，并利用局部超导转变温度而非名义掺杂浓度参数化，提取出超过清洁自旋密度波值的临界指数，揭示了无序修正的量子临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子临界点（quantum critical point）通常隐藏于非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）的掺杂不均匀性中，难以精确表征。本研究旨在通过局域测量方法，规避掺杂不均匀性带来的歧义，从而揭示超导态内部固有的量子临界行为。

Method: 使用扫描SQUID显微镜（scanning SQUID microscopy）测量掺杂Zn的CeCoIn₅，获取局域超导转变温度T_c和零温磁穿透深度λ(0)。通过以局域T_c而非名义Zn替代浓度对λ(0)进行参数化，消除掺杂不均匀性的影响，进而提取临界指数（critical exponent）。

Result: 在超导态中观测到一个磁量子临界点，表现为零温磁穿透深度λ(0)的显著峰值。提取的临界指数超过清洁自旋密度波（clean spin-density-wave）的理论值，表明体系处于无序修正的量子临界区（disorder-modified quantum critical regime）。λ(0)的增强反映了超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）的抑制，与临界标度行为一致。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种在非常规超导体中，克服掺杂不均匀性影响、揭示内在量子临界行为的有效方法。

Abstract: We demonstrate a magnetic quantum critical point embedded within the superconducting state of Zn-doped CeCoIn$_5$, revealed by a pronounced peak in the magnetic penetration depth at zero temperature $λ(0)$. Using scanning SQUID microscopy, we determine the local superconducting transition temperature $T_{\mathrm c}$ and $λ(0)$. By parameterizing $λ(0)$ in terms of the local $T_{\mathrm c}$ rather than nominal Zn substitution, we circumvent the ambiguity caused by doping inhomogeneity and enable a more precise extraction of the critical exponent. The extracted exponent exceeds the clean spin-density-wave value, indicating a disorder-modified quantum critical regime. The enhancement of $λ(0)$ reflects the suppression of the superfluid stiffness and is consistent with critical scaling. Our approach provides a route to uncover intrinsic quantum critical behavior hidden by inhomogeneity in unconventional superconductors.

</details>


### [152] [Critical temperatures and critical currents of wide and narrow quasi-one-dimensional superconducting aluminum structures in zero magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27822)
*V. I. Kuznetsov,O. V. Trofimov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该实验首次发现，在零磁场下，准一维超导铝结构的宽度越窄，其临界温度和临界电流密度越低，这可能归因于脏污纵向边界上的退配对中心（depairing centers）效应增强。此外，首次观察到开关临界电流随温度的变化可由两种函数描述：在电阻性正常-超导（N-S）转变底部以下符合Kupriyanov-Lukichev理论，在转变顶部附近则呈线性关系并与约瑟夫森临界电流一致，此时结构中形成SNS约瑟夫森结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究准一维超导铝薄膜结构在零磁场下的临界温度与临界电流随结构尺寸变化的规律，特别关注宽度减小对超导性能的影响机制。

Method: 测量了相同厚度、不同宽度（宽与窄）的准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）超导铝薄膜结构在零磁场下的临界温度、临界开关电流（switching current）和重俘获电流（retrapping current）。

Result: 首次发现结构越窄，临界温度（critical temperature）和临界电流密度（critical current density）越低；温度依赖的开关临界电流在大多数情况下可由两个函数分段近似。

Conclusion: 窄结构的超导性能退化可能与脏污纵向边界上的退配对中心（depairing centers）效应增强有关；在N-S转变顶部附近，结构中形成的SNS（超导体-正常金属-超导体）约瑟夫森结决定了开关电流的线性温度依赖关系。

Abstract: We measured the critical temperatures and critical switching and retrapping currents of wide and narrow thin-film quasi-one-dimensional superconducting aluminum structures of the same thickness in zero magnetic field. For the first time, we found that the narrower the structure, the lower the critical temperature and critical current density in the structure. Probably, the influence of depairing centers that are on dirty longitudinal boundaries of the structure, is the stronger than the narrower the structure. It is found for the first time that, in most cases, the temperature-dependent switching critical current in both structures is approximated by two functions. At temperatures below the temperature corresponding to the bottom of the resistive N-S transition of structures, the switching critical current is described by the Kupriyanov-Lukichev theory. At temperatures close to the top of the N-S transition, the switching current is linear with temperature and coincides with the critical Josephson current. At these temperatures, Josephson SNS junctions are formed in structures.

</details>


### [153] [Shift of the maxima of the critical currents of different polarity relative to the zero magnetic flux along the flux axis in a superconducting asymmetric aluminum ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27848)
*V. I. Kuznetsov,O. V. Trofimov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过实验测量了由超导非对称铝环串联结构产生的交流电压整流效应，并首次提出一个基于半环间动力学电感（kinetic inductance）差异的温度依赖相位偏移模型，成功解释了临界电流极大值随磁通偏移的现象，并解决了长期存在的实验矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验发现，非对称铝环结构中不同极性的临界电流极大值沿磁通轴方向发生相反偏移，但该偏移的物理起源长期未得到解释，且不同测量结果之间存在难以调和的矛盾。

Method: 构建由超导非对称铝环串联而成的结构，施加磁通和低频交流电流（不含直流分量），测量交流电压的整流效应。提出一个基于宽、窄半环（具有相同长度和厚度）无量纲动力学电感之差的温度依赖相位偏移模型。

Result: 模型表明，当两个半环的临界电流密度不同时，相位偏移不为零；而这种临界电流密度的差异只有在两个半环具有不同临界温度时才可能实现。该模型很好地描述了临界电流极大值随温度的偏移行为。

Conclusion: 该模型不仅成功解释了长期悬而未决的临界电流偏移问题，还消除了此前在非对称铝环结构中不同测量结果之间的极端矛盾，为理解超导非对称环的整流机制提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We measured the rectification of an ac voltage in a structure of superconducting circularly-asymmetric aluminum rings in series, permeated with a magnetic flux and biased with a low-frequency alternating current (without a dc component). This rectification is due to the shift of the maxima of the critical currents of different polarity relative to the zero flux in opposite directions along the flux axis in the asymmetric ring. For the first time, we propose a model for a temperature-dependent phase shift equal to difference between dimensionless kinetic inductances of wide and narrow semirings having the same length and thickness. The shift is not zero in the case of different critical currents densities in both semirings. This is possible only in a situation of different critical temperatures of both semirings. The model describes well the temperature-dependent shift of the maxima of the critical currents, answers the long-standing mysterious challenge of the shift and removes extremely strange contradiction between the results of different measurements, previously found in circularly-asymmetric aluminum structures.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 实验观测到的反常开关电流行为无法由现有理论（包括金茨堡-朗道理论）完整描述，表明该结构可能涉及新的物理机制。

Abstract: We measured unusual critical currents as functions of temperature in the zero field and as functions of a magnetic field perpendicular to the substrate surface at a given temperature close to the critical temperature in thin-film long quasi-one-dimensional superconducting aluminum two-width structures consisting of narrow and wide wires with different critical temperatures. It is found that the experimental critical switching current as a function of the field at a given temperature, determined by the appearance of a dc voltage on a short section of the structure, is nonlocal (dependent on electron transport in the area containing the junction line between the narrow and wide wires). When current flows through the narrow and wide wires of the structure, the switching currents, experimental and calculated within the framework of the Ginzburg-Landau theory, differ radically from each other. A nonzero switching current exists in high fields greater than the maximum critical magnetic field in a quasi-one-dimensional superconducting wire. In the aluminum two-width structures studied here, the unusual measured switching current challenges description by known theories.

Abstract: Superconductivity in strontium titanate has remained enigmatic for more than 50 years. Transport measurements in patterned devices reveal puzzling phenomena, including width-independent critical currents and anomalous pairing suggestive of one-dimensional behavior, but direct local probes of the patterned interface and its superconducting response have been lacking. Here we use ultralow-temperature non-contact atomic force microscopy, dissipation spectroscopy, and Kelvin probe force microscopy to locally probe signatures of superconductivity in patterned LAO/STO devices. ### [156] [Enhancement of superconducting stiffness in hybrid superconducting-metallic bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28187)
*J. E. Ebot,Lorenzo Pizzino,Sam Mardazad,Johannes S. Hofmann,Thierry Giamarchi,Adrian Kantian*

TL;DR: 本文通过研究部分自旋极化的1D安德森或近藤晶格模型，论证了在远离半填充的掺杂体系中，金属储层能够显著增强超导配对层的超导近长程有序，并揭示了对超导增强起关键作用的“配对限制”与“刚度限制”两种机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用强耦合（strong-coupling）方法研究部分自旋极化的1D安德森晶格（Anderson lattice）或近藤晶格（Kondo lattice）模型，在远离半填充（away from half-filling）的掺杂区分析超导与密度-密度关联（density-density correlations）之间的竞争。

Result: 掺杂打破了超导主导关联与密度-密度关联的共存，使超导占据优势；在该掺杂区间，超导近长程有序（superconducting near-long-range order）在热力学极限下不会被小电荷能隙（charge gap）所阻碍；超导增强对金属层参数有复杂依赖，可出现配对限制（pairing-limited）与刚度限制（stiffness-limited）两种不同机制；通过粒子-空穴变换（particle-hole transformation），结果还揭示了重费米子近藤晶格材料中反铁磁与面内（easy-plane）磁性之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 本文首次为Kivelson双层提案在掺杂条件下提供了明确的强耦合证据，同时为重费米子材料中的磁性竞争提供了此前缺乏的见解，并为该提案的综合性间接检验开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Boosting superconductivity by metallic reservoirs is the essence of Kivelson's bilayer proposal.
  One layer provides pairing to the electrons, while the weakly coupled metal provides additional phase coherence to those pairs by mediating extended-range pair-pair coupling.
  Demonstrating significant and unambiguous performance gains with strong-coupling methods for such set-ups had been difficult.
  In the present work, we study these systems doped away from half-filling, corresponding to a partially spin-polarized 1D Anderson- or Kondo-lattice.
  We show that this breaks the coexistence of dominant superconducting and density-density correlations decisively in favour or the former.
  Consequently, we provide evidence that in this doped regime, superconducting near-long-range order is not precluded by a small charge-gap in the thermodynamic limit, as we have recently shown to be the case at half-filling [JE Ebot $et$ $al.$, arXiv:2602.11153 [cond-mat.supr-con]].
  We study the complex manner in which the enhancement of superconductivity in the pairing layer depends on the parameters of the metal, and especially that both pairing-limited and stiffness-limited regimes may appear in these systems.
  In addition to superconducting bilayers, our results are relevant, via a particle-hole transformation, for heavy-fermion Kondo-lattice materials in magnetic fields, as we provide previously lacking insight on the competition between antiferromagnetic and easy-plane magnetism, as well as a route for comprehensive indirect tests of Kivelson's bilayer proposal well beyond previous capabilities.

### [158] [Confinement-Connectivity Coupling Enables High-Efficiency Piezoionic Transduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27240)
*Tofayel Ahammad Ovee,Daniel Kroeger,Jean-François Louf*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种限域-连通性（confinement-connectivity）设计策略，通过超分子聚乙烯醇-甘油-葫芦[5]脲（PVA-glycerol-CB[5]）介孔网络与层状正-中-负（Negative-Neutral-Positive）架构，同时增大孔隙率并减小孔径，约束离子再分布并维持大离子储库，实现了~180 mV和~9 mA的压电离子输出，并可在小鼠坐骨神经中诱发同步肌电反应，无需外部电源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用超分子聚乙烯醇-甘油-葫芦[5]脲（PVA-glycerol-CB[5]）构建介孔网络，并设计层状负-中-正（Negative-Neutral-Positive）架构，同时提高孔隙率并减小特征孔径，实现限域与连通性的耦合。

Result: 压缩产生的峰值输出约为~180 mV和~9 mA，并可在小鼠坐骨神经中诱发同步肌电反应（electromyographic responses），无需外部电源。这表明限域-连通性耦合而非体电导率（bulk conductivity）是压电离子转导的关键。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了限域-连通性耦合作为压电离子水凝胶的材料设计框架，证明通过调控孔隙连通性与限域效应可主导压电离子转导（piezoionic transduction），为机械驱动的生物电子接口提供了新路径。

Abstract: Piezoionic hydrogels offer a route to mechanically driven bioelectronic interfaces, but their output is limited by rapid, symmetric ion redistribution that dissipates charge gradients. In biological electrocytes, efficient signal generation arises from the coupling of ion selectivity with spatial confinement that regulates transport. Here, we introduce a confinement-connectivity design strategy for piezoionic hydrogels, implemented through a supramolecular poly(vinyl alcohol)-glycerol-cucurbit[5]uril (PVA-glycerol-CB[5]) mesoporous network with a layered Negative-Neutral-Positive architecture that simultaneously increases pore fraction while reducing characteristic pore size. This architecture constrains ionic redistribution while maintaining a large mobile-ion reservoir, enabling deformation-driven charge separation. Compression generates peak outputs of ~180 mV and ~9 mA and elicits synchronized electromyographic responses in the mouse sciatic nerve without external power. These results establish confinement-connectivity coupling, rather than bulk conductivity, as a materials design framework in which coupling pore connectivity and confinement governs piezoionic transduction.

### [159] [Electrically Tunable Terahertz Chirality from Quantum Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27294)
*Sobhan Subhra Mishra,Thomas CaiWei Tan,Faxian Xiu,Ranjan Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何（quantum geometry）通过贝里曲率（Berry curvature）调控电荷动力学，可产生非常规输运和光学响应；在拓扑半金属中，这种几何效应通过费米口袋（Fermi pockets）采样，理论上可通过费米面（Fermi surface）调谐实现电控，但此前仅局限于直流输运领域，缺乏在太赫兹频段的电控能力。

Method: 对三维狄拉克半金属Cd₃As₂施加静电门控，重塑光致弗洛凯外尔节点（photoinduced Floquet Weyl nodes）周围的费米口袋；利用激发几何中固有的π/2相位锁定，结合门控对贝里曲率驱动线性偏振分量的选择性调制，实现偏振态在整个庞加莱球（Poincaré sphere）上的调控。

Result: 门控调谐选择性调制了由贝里曲率驱动的线性偏振太赫兹分量，在正偏压和负偏压下分别实现了最高60%和49%的调制幅度；正交的光子拖曳（photon-drag）偏振分量保持不变；在+10 V偏压下实现了近圆偏振（χ≈-42°）。

Conclusion: 费米面调谐是实现可编程量子几何控制（programmable quantum geometric control）手性太赫兹发射的通用途径，为太赫兹光电器件的主动调控提供了新方案。

Abstract: Quantum geometry encoded in the momentum space structure of electronic wavefunctions, governs charge dynamics through Berry curvature, enabling unconventional transport and optical responses. In topological semimetals, this geometry is sampled over Fermi pockets, suggesting electrical control by Fermi surface tuning, yet such control has remained largely limited to DC transport. Here we show that electrostatic gating of the 3D Dirac semimetal Cd3As2 reshapes Fermi pockets surrounding photoinduced Floquet Weyl nodes, enabling electrical control of terahertz (THz) emission chirality. Gate tuning selectively modulates the Berry curvature driven linearly polarized THz component by up to 60% and 49% at positive and negative bias, respectively, while the orthogonal linearly polarized photon-drag component remains unchanged. With the two orthogonal fields intrinsically phase-locked at \sfracπ{2} by the excitation geometry, the selective gate-tuned amplitude control enables the polarization tuning across the Poincaré sphere, achieving near-circular polarization (χ\approx-42°) at +10 V. These results establish Fermi surface tuning as a general route to programmable quantum geometric control of chiral terahertz emission.

### [160] [Low-Energy Purification of Crystal Defects by Rydberg Excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27331)
*Shiva Kant Tiwari,Tijs Karman,Valentin Walther*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 发展了一个Rydberg激子-杂质散射的多通道理论（multichannel theory），系统分析捕获（capture）、弹性散射（elastic scattering）以及激子态间非弹性跃迁（inelastic transitions）这三种竞争渠道的贡献。

Result: 高碰撞能下（常规单光子激发条件），净化效率低于Langevin捕获预测值，归因于强弹性散射（包括显著的光辉散射（glory scattering））和非弹性再分布；超低碰撞能下进入仅s波（s-wave）贡献的量子区，捕获增强而弹性和非弹性通道被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 可通过简并双光子激发（degenerate two-photon excitation）产生可调反冲的偶宇称Rydberg激子来进入该量子区，从而实现高效净化，并为在远宽于原子气体实验的碰撞能范围内系统探索激子-杂质散射提供新途径。

Abstract: Recent experiments show that optically generated Rydberg excitons in cuprous oxide can neutralize charged impurities, strongly reducing stray electric fields and effectively purifying the crystal. Here, we develop a multichannel theory of Rydberg exciton-impurity scattering that resolves the competing roles of capture, elastic scattering, and inelastic transitions between excitonic states. We find that at high collision energies, as effective under conventional single-photon excitation, purification is reduced relative to Langevin capture. These collisions are accompanied by inelastic redistribution and dominant elastic scattering, including pronounced glory scattering, which suppress purification efficiency. We identify a quantum regime at ultralow collision energies favorable for purification, where only the s-wave contributes: capture is enhanced while elastic and inelastic channels are strongly suppressed. This regime can be accessed via degenerate two-photon excitation of even-parity Rydberg excitons with tunable recoil, additionally enabling the systematic exploration of exciton-impurity scattering over a wide range of collision energies beyond what is readily achievable in atomic counterparts in atomic gas experiments.
