### [161] [Mobile Exceptional Points Generate Momentum-Space Switching Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27417)
*Jung-Wan Ryu,Chang-Hwan Yi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现可移动的奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）会在动量空间中产生切换域（switching domains），将布里渊区划分为具有不同能带切换行为的区域，并引入能带置换不变量（band-permutation invariant）来描述这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验已能在多种物理系统中可控地产生和操纵奇异点（EPs），这自然引出一个关键问题：当EPs在循环调制下变得可移动时，会涌现出何种新的能带拓扑结构。

Method: 采用最小二能带晶格模型（two-band lattice model），引入能带置换不变量（band-permutation invariant）来判断本征模式在一个调制周期后是否发生交换。切换区域边界由扩展参数空间中EP轨迹的投影决定，该空间结合了晶体动量（crystal momentum）和调制参数。

Result: 随着调制强度增加，切换域逐渐扩大并最终覆盖整个布里渊区（Brillouin zone），导致全局能带切换（global band switching）。该切换域结构进一步在含损耗材料的光子晶体（photonic crystal）中得到验证。

Conclusion: 这些结果通过实现EP驱动现象的可控运动，为非厄米拓扑学（non-Hermitian topology）开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs), non-Hermitian degeneracies where both eigenvalues and eigenvectors coalesce, play a central role in the topology of non-Hermitian spectra. Recent advances have enabled the controlled creation and manipulation of EPs in a wide range of physical systems, raising the question of what new band topology emerges when EPs become mobile under cyclic modulation. Here we show that mobile EPs generate momentum-space switching domains that partition the Brillouin zone into regions with distinct band-switching behavior. Using a minimal two-band lattice model, we introduce a band-permutation invariant that determines whether eigenmodes exchange after one modulation cycle. The boundaries between switching regions arise from the projection of EP trajectories in an extended parameter space combining crystal momentum and the modulation parameter. As the modulation strength increases, the switching domains expand and eventually cover the entire Brillouin zone, resulting in global band switching. The predicted switching-domain structure is further demonstrated in a photonic crystal with lossy materials. These results open a new avenue within non-Hermitian topology by enabling the engineering of EP-driven phenomena through their controlled motion.

</details>


### [162] [Curvature-induced nonlinear anomalous Hall effect in thin magnetic shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27544)
*Maria Teresa Mercaldo,Mario Cuoco,Carmine Ortix*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过几何弯曲（geometric bending）在中心对称铁磁体中工程化量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）的实部和虚部，利用曲率诱导的应变梯度打破反演对称性，激活轨道Rashba耦合，从而产生受量子度量（quantum metric）和Berry曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）分别主导的各向异性非线性反常霍尔效应（NAHE）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何在中心对称铁磁体中突破对称性约束，实现量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）实部和虚部——即量子度量（quantum metric）和Berry曲率（Berry curvature）——在光电子和非线性输运实验中的可调控响应。

Method: 通过引入几何弯曲（geometric bending）导致壳层厚度方向的曲率诱导应变梯度，打破结构反演对称性并激活轨道Rashba耦合（orbital Rashba coupling）；结合面内磁化与自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），产生具有非平凡量子几何的自旋织构（spin textures）。

Result: 当磁化方向与外加电场对齐时，量子度量（quantum metric）主导的内禀非线性反常霍尔效应（NAHE）达到最大；当几何变形进一步破坏面外方向的二重旋转对称时，出现由Berry曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）控制的另一NAHE分量，其最大值出现在磁化垂直于驱动电场的方向。

Conclusion: 弯曲铁磁壳层可作为工程化各向异性非线性输运的平台，并提供选择性探测量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）两个分量的实验途径。

Abstract: Optoelectronic and nonlinear transport experiments probe the quantum geometric tensor of Bloch states, whose real and imaginary components -- the quantum metric and the Berry curvature -- are typically constrained by symmetry. Here, we show that geometric bending provides a route to engineer such responses in centrosymmetric ferromagnets. Curvature-induced strain gradients across the shell thickness break inversion symmetry and activate an orbital Rashba coupling. In the presence of in-plane magnetization and spin-orbit coupling, this generates spin textures with a nontrivial quantum geometry, leading to an intrinsic nonlinear anomalous Hall effect (NAHE) governed by the quantum metric and maximized when the magnetization aligns with the applied electric field. When geometric deformations further break twofold rotational symmetry around the out-of-plane axis, an additional NAHE emerges, maximal for magnetization perpendicular to the driving electric field and governed by the Berry curvature dipole, thus giving access to the imaginary component of the quantum geometric tensor. These results establish curved ferromagnetic shells as a platform for engineering anisotropic nonlinear transport and for selectively probing both components of the quantum geometric tensor.

</details>


### [163] [Quantum Scalar Spin Chirality in Coplanar Kagome Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27632)
*Nanse Esaki,Gyungchoon Go,Se Kwon Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明，反铁磁体中的量子涨落可以在零温下、甚至在共面有序磁体中产生标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）。在具有共面基态自旋构型的kagome反铁磁体中，当描述涨落的哈密顿量中有效的类时间反演反幺正对称性（effective time-reversal-like antiunitary symmetry）被破坏，且经典基态的磁点群允许其存在时，零温下就会出现由量子涨落诱导的标量自旋手性。标量自旋手性涨落会随着温度升高而进一步增长，其大小可达到与非共面自旋结构预测的静态手性相当的水平，突显了其在共面自旋系统中的物理意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子涨落能否在零温下、共面有序的反铁磁体中诱导出标量自旋手性，从而拓展对手性现象产生机制的理解。

Method: 以kagome反铁磁体为模型系统，分析其共面基态自旋构型；考察描述涨落的哈密顿量中有效时间反演反幺正对称性的破缺条件，并结合经典基态的磁点群对称性分析，论证零温下量子涨落诱导标量自旋手性的可行性。

Result: 在满足对称性破缺条件时，kagome反铁磁体的共面基态中确实存在由量子涨落诱导的零温标量自旋手性；该手性涨落随温度升高而进一步增大，其幅度可与非共面自旋结构中的静态标量自旋手性相比拟。

Conclusion: 量子涨落可在共面有序磁体中诱导出显著的标量自旋手性，这种涨落驱动的效应在共面自旋系统中具有重要的物理意义，可能对理解相关磁性材料的行为提供新的视角。

Abstract: We theoretically demonstrate that quantum fluctuations inherent to antiferromagnets can generate scalar spin chirality at zero temperature even in coplanar ordered magnets. In a kagome antiferromagnet with coplanar ground-state spin configurations, the quantum-fluctuation-induced scalar spin chirality is shown to arise at zero temperature when an effective time-reversal-like antiunitary symmetry is broken in the Hamiltonian describing fluctuations, and a magnetic point group of the classical ground state allows for its presence. The scalar spin chirality fluctuations are shown to grow further with increasing temperature by thermally excited magnons. These scalar spin chirality fluctuations can reach a magnitude comparable to the static one predicted for noncoplanar spin structures, highlighting their physical implications in coplanar spin systems.

### [164] [Size-Limited Room Temperature Single-Photon Emission from Sidewall-Treated Fractional Dimension InGaN Quantum Dots: Determined by Density-of-States-Corrected Ultrafast Carrier Dynamics and Improved Signal-to-Noise Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27718)
*Pratim K. Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文首次在化学和光电化学刻蚀的In0.14Ga0.86N量子点中，于室温下实现了双激子-激子级联衰变产生的单光子发射，并建立了一个基于量子点表面与几何结构的广义物理框架，用以预判室温单光子发射概率，最优性能可逼近激子玻尔半径（约3 nm）尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室温下单光子发射（room-temperature single-photon emission, SPE）是量子光子学的重要目标，但现有材料在室温下实现高纯度单光子发射仍面临背景噪声和载流子动力学瓶颈，亟需从物理机制上阐明量子点尺寸与表面效应对发射性能的系统影响。

Method: 采用化学和光电化学刻蚀技术在垂直GaN纳米线中制备位置可控的In0.14Ga0.86N量子点（quantum dots, QDs），通过分析直径依赖的双激子-激子（biexciton-exciton）动力学，结合表面复合、Auger复合速率和态密度修正，研究不同量子点尺寸下的单光子发射行为。

Result: 量子点直径大于35 nm时，表面复合导致非均匀展宽；直径小于35 nm时，态密度修正的Auger复合成为双激子主要衰变路径，抑制热展宽并设置单光子发射阈值；直径小于9 nm时，Auger复合速率远超其他衰变速率，通过单次Auger衰变实现多光子抑制；湿法处理可降低侧壁表面态，最小化激子表面复合概率并最大化双激子态填充概率，提高单光子纯度。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个广义物理框架，可基于量子点表面与几何结构预判单光子发射概率，直至激子玻尔半径（约3 nm）尺度，为设计和开发下一代高纯度室温单光子发射半导体量子点提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Room-temperature single-photon emission (SPE) resulting from a biexciton-exciton cascaded decay is demonstrated for the first time from chemically and photoelectrochemically etched site-controlled In0.14Ga0.86N quantum dots (QDs) embedded in vertical GaN nanowires. Diameter-dependent biexciton-exciton dynamics are analysed to determine the eligibility of QD as a single-photon emitter. The signal-to-noise ratio degrades with increasing QD diameter. Background noise photons pose a bottleneck to achieving SPE. This is also explained from a carrier dynamics perspective. Surface recombination contributes to inhomogeneous broadening at QD diameters larger than 35 nm. Below 35 nm, density-of-states-corrected Auger gradually becomes the principal biexciton-decay route with further reduction in QD diameter, thereby quenching the possibility of thermal broadening and setting a threshold for SPE. Below 9 nm, the Auger recombination rate becomes manyfold of other decay rates, causing multi-photon suppression via single Auger decay to form an exciton. Surface recombination probability of this exciton is minimized while biexciton state filling probability is maximized by reducing sidewall surface states through wet-treatment. These improve biexciton state preparation and enhance the single-photon purity of the exciton towards the exciton Bohr radius (3 nm) regime. Far away from this regime, higher-order autocorrelations to characterize quantum emission involving multi-photon events are discussed. This study establishes a generalized physical framework for predetermining SPE probability as a function of QD surface and geometry down to the exciton Bohr radius regime, with practical implementations. This work shows the pathway to design and develop next-generation semiconductor QDs for high-purity room-temperature SPE.

</details>

The cross section of the nanowire has a hexagonal geometry. ### [166] [Spin-coherence characterization of boron vacancy defects in hexagonal boron nitride with broadband microwave pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27843)

TL;DR: 本研究通过在同位素富集的六方氮化硼（hBN）薄膜上实现亚GHz拉比振荡，测量了带负电的硼空位（VB-）缺陷的自旋相干时间T2* = 13.8 ns和T2 = 108.7 ns，为范德华薄膜中自旋缺陷的相干性评估提供了有效方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用同位素富集的hBN薄膜直接贴在窄金线上，实现VB-的亚GHz拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）。通过强微波脉冲进行Ramsey干涉（Ramsey interference）和Hahn回波（Hahn echo）测量。

Result: Ramsey干涉信号呈高斯型衰减，得到T2* = 13.8 ns。Hahn回波测量给出T2 = 108.7 ns以及拉伸因子（stretch factor）α = 1.25。

Conclusion: 实验结果明确了VB-的自旋相干特性，并为评估具有宽共振线宽（broad resonance linewidths）的范德华（van der Waals）薄膜中自旋缺陷的相干性提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Negatively charged boron vacancy (VB-) defects in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) are promising for nanoscale-proximity quantum sensing. To evaluate their performance, it is important to characterize the spin coherence times T2* and T2. In this study, we realized sub-GHz Rabi oscillations of VB- using an isotopically enriched hBN thin film directly stamped onto a narrow gold wire. Using these strong microwave pulses, we performed Ramsey interference and Hahn echo measurements. The Ramsey interference signal showed Gaussian-like decay, yielding T2* = 13.8 ns. The Hahn echo measurement gave T2 = 108.7 ns and a stretch factor of α= 1.25. These results experimentally clarify the spin coherence properties of VB- and provide an effective method for evaluating the coherence of spin defects in van der Waals thin films with broad resonance linewidths.

Abstract: We report the formation of large-scale steady-state whirlpools in a GaAs-based two-dimensional electron liquid and demonstrate them by straightforward transport measurements. A whirlpool forming inside a circular cavity adjoining a wide conducting channel appears as a negative four-terminal resistance over a broad range of temperatures and cavity sizes. The effect scales with the Gurzhi length, in quantitative accord with the hydrodynamic analogy. Obtained results firmly establish this analogy and probe the limits of its applicability.

### [168] [Theory of quantum decoherence in macroscopic topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27946)
*Xian-Peng Zhang,Yan-Qing Feng,Wanxiang Feng,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套完整理论，定量研究量子退相干（quantum decoherence）如何影响宏观拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）中的量子自旋霍尔效应（quantum spin Hall effect），发现退相干诱导的修正与杂质密度呈二次方关系，揭示了一种基于退相干的二阶斜散射（second-order skew-scattering）这一全新的外在自旋霍尔效应机制，并预言退相干诱导的自旋霍尔电导率与纵向电导率呈二次方标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子退相干在量子输运中扮演核心角色，控制这一普遍现象对实用量子技术至关重要，但无限大尺寸拓扑绝缘体中退相干的微观机制仍不清楚。

Method: 发展了一套定量分析量子退相干如何塑造宏观拓扑绝缘体中量子自旋霍尔效应的完整理论。

Result: 退相干诱导的修正与杂质密度呈二次方关系；发现一种由量子退相干内在驱动的二阶斜散射机制，构成全新的外在自旋霍尔效应（extrinsic spin Hall effect），其强度显著高于传统的三阶斜散射机制；预言退相干诱导的自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity）与纵向电导率（longitudinal conductivity）呈二次方标度律。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了退相干在拓扑绝缘体量子输运中的关键作用，并指出宏观拓扑绝缘体为下一代自旋电子学（spintronics）应用提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Quantum decoherence-the loss of quantum coherence due to interactions with an environment-plays a central role in quantum transport, and controlling this ubiquitous yet inevitable phenomenon is essential for practical quantum technologies. Despite its importance, the microscopic mechanisms of decoherence in infinite-size topological insulators remain poorly understood. Here, we develop a comprehensive theory that quantitatively investigates how quantum decoherence shapes the quantum spin Hall effect in macroscopic topological insulators, and reveal that decoherence-induced corrections scale quadratically with impurity density. Besides, we uncover a previously unidentified mechanism of the extrinsic spin Hall effect: a second-order skew-scattering process intrinsically tied to quantum decoherence-fundamentally distinct from, yet substantially stronger than, the conventional third-order skew-scattering mechanism. Furthermore, we predict a new scaling law in which the decoherence-induced spin Hall conductivity scales quadratically with the longitudinal conductivity, providing a clear experimental signature of decoherence effects. Our results establish the essential role of decoherence in quantum transport of topological insulators and reveal that macroscopic topological insulators offer a promising platform for next-generation spintronic applications.

### [169] [Compressibility of micromagnetic solutions in tensor train format](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28008)
*Thierry Valet,Nicolas Vukadinovic*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用直接张量列（tensor-train, TT）表示来压缩微磁（micromagnetic）数据，利用三维磁体中微观磁化状态的空间稀疏性，将参数规模从传统方法的 ~L³ 和 ~(1/a)³ 分别降至 ~L¹·⁸ 和 ~(1/a)¹·²，从而在保证精度的前提下显著提升计算可扩展性，为开发超越传统模拟器局限的TT格式微磁求解器提供了理论依据和初步验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微磁模拟对近均匀网格进行离散化处理，其计算复杂度与体系线性尺寸 L 的三次方以及网格尺寸 a 的倒数的三次方成正比，无法利用三维磁体（如磁畴壁与近均匀畴区共存）中存在的显著信息稀疏性（informational sparsity），导致大体系或高分辨率模拟的计算成本急剧上升。

Method: 采用直接张量列（tensor-train, TT）表示对微磁状态数据进行压缩，以最优方式利用空间稀疏性。研究对象为软磁矩形棱柱（soft-magnetic rectangular prisms）中接近微米尺度（near-micrometer regime）的代表性磁通闭合构型（flux-closure configurations），通过评估TT压缩后的参数数量随 L 和 a 的变化规律来量化其可扩展性优势。

Result: TT压缩后的微磁数据参数数量近似按 ~L¹·⁸ 和 ~(1/a)¹·² 标度增长，远优于传统密集离散化方法的 ~L³ 和 ~(1/a)³ 标度；且该相对优势随问题规模增大和网格细化而迅速扩大。

Conclusion: 首次系统验证了TT格式在微磁学中的压缩潜力，表明该格式能够在保持受控精度的同时突破传统模拟器的可扩展性瓶颈；为未来开发基于TT格式的高效微磁求解器奠定了坚实基础，对基础研究和技术开发具有重要潜在影响。

Abstract: For three-dimensional (3D) magnetic objects with linear size $L$ exceeding a few exchange lengths, the micromagnetic state exhibits pronounced informational sparsity: low-dimensional, high-gradient regions (e.g., domain walls) coexist with near-uniformly magnetized volumetric domains. Because standard micromagnetic simulation methods discretize the magnetization on near-uniform 3D grids with linear cell size $a$, they cannot take advantage of this sparsity. The computational problem scales as $\sim L^3$ and $\sim (1/a)^3$. In this Letter, we establish that direct tensor-train (TT) representations overcome these poor scalings by exploiting the spatial sparsity optimally, while preserving accuracy in a controlled way. Focusing on representative flux-closure configurations in soft-magnetic rectangular prisms, in the near-micrometer regime, we demonstrate that the parameter count of TT-compressed micromagnetic data scales approximately as $L^{1.8}$ and $(1/a)^{1.2}$. Hence the relative advantage over dense discretizations rapidly grows with the problem size and refinement level. These first results provide a strong motivation for future developments of micromagnetic solvers in TT format which could transcend the limitations of traditional simulators, with far reaching potential impacts on fundamental research and technology development.

</details>


### [170] [Deep Strong light-matter Coupling in 3D Kane Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28042)
*Dmitriy Yavorskiy,David Hagenmuller,Noureddine Charrouj,Yurii Ivonyak,Alexander Kazakov,Yanko Todorov,Wojciech Knap,Marcin Bialek*

TL;DR: 本文在碲化汞镉体材料中利用Kane费米子的超低有效质量实现了从弱耦合到深强耦合的连续调控，在室温以上创下归一化耦合比超过1.6的记录。尽管相对论性能带结构不存在显式A²项，但实验与规范不变的微观理论一致表明，抗磁性A²项自然出现并阻止超辐射量子相变，解决了长期存在的争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深强光-物质耦合是量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）中的极端非微扰区域，其中是否存在由自发偶极有序和光子凝聚标记的超辐射量子相变（superradiant quantum phase transition）一直是一个长期且有争议的问题。先前研究提出，在具有狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermions）和Kane费米子（Kane fermions）的奇异电子体系中，因低能哈密顿量形式上缺少A²项而可能实现该相变。本研究旨在通过实验验证该理论预言，并解决相关争议。

Method: 实验采用块体碲化汞镉（mercury cadmium telluride）层与法布里-珀罗谐振器（Fabry-Perot resonator）耦合的体系，利用Kane费米子的超低有效质量实现朗道极化激元（Landau polaritons）。通过热可调载流子密度，连续调控耦合强度从弱耦合到深强耦合（deep-strong coupling）区域，并测量极化激元光谱。理论方面采用严格的规范不变微观理论（gauge-invariant microscopic theory）与实验数据进行比较。

Result: 实验实现了室温以上归一化耦合比（normalised coupling ratio）超过1.6的纪录。测量得到的极化激元光谱与规范的规范不变微观理论高度吻合。尽管相对论性Kane费米子的朗道能级（Landau level）结构是非线性的，但抗磁性A²项（diamagnetic A² term）自然出现，从而排除超辐射相变的发生。

Conclusion: 研究结果解决了围绕相对论性类物质体系的腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics）的长期争议，将深强耦合物理扩展到Kane费米子体系，并为工作于极端光-物质耦合区域的极化激元半导体器件开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Deep strong light-matter coupling represents an extreme non-perturbative regime of quantum electrodynamics, in which the interaction strength exceeds the bare frequencies of the uncoupled systems. The ground state features strong quantum correlations between photons and matter excitations, and new cavity-driven phase transitions are expected to occur. Whether a superradiant quantum phase transition, marked by spontaneous dipole ordering and photon condensation, is possible has remained a long-standing and controversial question. Such phenomena have been proposed to arise in exotic electronic systems hosting Dirac and Kane fermions, owing to the formal absence of an $A^2$ term in their low-energy Hamiltonian. Here we exploit the ultralow effective mass of Kane fermions to realise Landau polaritons in a bulk mercury cadmium telluride layer coupled to a Fabry-Perot resonator. Using thermally tunable carrier density, we continuously tune the coupling from the weak to the deep-strong regime, achieving a record normalised coupling ratio exceeding 1.6 above room temperature. The measured polariton spectra are in excellent agreement with a rigorous, gauge-invariant microscopic theory. Despite the nonlinear Landau level structure of relativistic Kane fermions, we show that a diamagnetic $A^2$ term naturally emerges and precludes a superradiant phase transition. These results resolve the long-standing controversy surrounding cavity quantum electrodynamics of relativistic-like matter systems, extend deep-strong-coupling physics to Kane fermions, and open new opportunities for polaritonic semiconductor devices operating in extreme light-matter coupling regimes.

</details>


### [171] [g-tensor Optimization in Ge/SiGe Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28081)
*Aram Shojaei,Edmondo Valvo,Maximilian Rimbach-Russ,Eliska Greplova,Ana Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种灵活的优化框架，用于设计锗基异质结构中的 g 张量（g-tensor）特性。通过数值优化量子阱（quantum well）中垂直于平面的势能形状，抑制了面内 g 张量分量，实现了无间隙单自旋量子比特（gapless single-spin qubit）编码，为大规模锗基量子计算机提供了实用设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面锗异质结构（planar germanium heterostructures）中的空穴自旋量子比特（hole-spin qubits）是构建可扩展半导体量子计算的重要平台，但量子点（quantum dot）的显著变异性导致量子比特能级不确定和自旋量化轴（spin quantization axis）方向随机，严重制约了器件性能。因此，需要一种对 g 张量的定制化控制策略来克服这些限制，实现更可靠的量子比特操作。

Method: 本文引入了一个灵活的优化框架（optimization framework）来设计 g 张量特性。作为基准测试，通过数值方法优化 SiGe-Ge-SiGe 量子阱中垂直于平面（out-of-plane）的势能形状，以抑制面内（in-plane）g 张量分量。这种势能重塑通过异质结构工程（heterostructure engineering）实现，具体方式是调整量子阱内部的硅浓度。

Result: 数值优化结果表明，通过调整量子阱中的硅浓度来重塑垂直于平面的势能形状，可以有效抑制面内 g 张量分量，从而实现了最近提出的无间隙单自旋量子比特编码方案。

Conclusion: 该研究为改善自旋响应（spin response）的可调性提供了实用的设计原则，为大规模锗基量子计算机的发展铺平了道路。此外，所提出的优化框架具有良好的可扩展性，可灵活适配其他设计目标。

Abstract: Planar germanium heterostructures hosting hole-spin qubits are among the leading platforms for scalable semiconductor-based quantum computing. Yet, device performance is hindered by significant quantum dot variability, which leads to uncertainty in qubit energy levels and random orientations of the spin quantization axis. Tailored control of the g-tensor offers a strategy to overcome these limitations and achieve more reliable qubit operations. Here, we introduce a flexible optimization framework for engineering g-tensor properties. As a benchmark, we numerically obtain the optimal reshaping of the out-of-plane potential in a SiGe-Ge-SiGe quantum well to suppress the in-plane g-tensor components and realize the recently proposed gapless single-spin qubit encoding. This reshaping is achieved through heterostructure engineering, specifically by adjusting the silicon concentration within the quantum well, though the framework remains readily adaptable to alternative design objectives. Our results provide practical design principles for improving the tunability of the spin response, paving the way towards large-scale germanium-based quantum computers.

</details>


### [172] [Giant Spin Magnetization from Quantum Geometry in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28088)
*Neelanjan Chakraborti,Sudeep Kumar Ghosh,Snehasish Nandy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于广义量子几何张量（generalized quantum geometric tensor）建立了统一框架，揭示了中心对称交变磁体（centrosymmetric altermagnets）中磁场所致线性自旋磁化的唯一量子几何机制——自旋旋转量子度量（spin-rotation quantum metric），并预测了远超传统磁体的巨大响应信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中心对称系统中能否存在线性自旋磁化的量子几何机制是一个核心问题。交变磁体（altermagnets）具有自旋分裂能带但宏观净磁化为零，因此场致响应成为探测其量子几何（quantum geometry）的直接手段，亟需统一的理论框架加以描述。

Method: 发展了基于广义量子几何张量的统一框架，该张量同时包含了布洛赫态（Bloch states）的动量平移和自旋旋转。将自旋磁化分解为平衡贡献、电场驱动贡献和磁场驱动贡献，并通过对称性分析识别各贡献的允许性。

Result: 反演对称性（inversion symmetry）禁止中心对称系统中的线性电场响应，而 $C_n T$ 对称性进一步压制了交变磁体中的平衡贡献。因此，磁场所致自旋磁化成为唯一对称性允许的线性量子几何响应，且完全源于自旋旋转量子度量。在 $\mathrm{FeSb}_2$（$d$波）和 $\mathrm{CrSb}$（$g$波）等代表材料中，预测在约 $10\,\mathrm{mT}$ 磁场下产生 $10^{-2}μ_B\,\mathrm{nm}^{-3}$ 量级的巨大线性自旋磁化，超出传统磁体数个数量级。

Conclusion: 识别了中心对称系统中自旋磁化的一种普适量子几何机制，并确立了中心对称交变磁体作为该机制实验检测和自旋电子学（spintronics）应用的理想平台。

Abstract: Altermagnets host spin-split band structures while exhibiting vanishing equilibrium spin magnetization, making field-induced responses a direct probe of their quantum geometry. A central question, in this regard, is which quantum-geometric mechanism can generate a linear spin magnetization in centrosymmetric systems. Here we develop a unified framework based on a generalized quantum geometric tensor that incorporates both momentum translations and spin rotations of Bloch states, and decompose spin magnetization into equilibrium, electric-field-driven, and magnetic-field-driven contributions. We show that inversion symmetry forbids the linear electric-field response in centrosymmetric systems, while $C_n T$ symmetry further suppresses the equilibrium contribution in altermagnets. Consequently, centrosymmetric altermagnets provide a particularly clean realization in which the magnetic-field-induced spin magnetization emerges as the only symmetry-allowed linear quantum-geometric response. We demonstrate that this contribution originates entirely from the spin-rotation quantum metric, establishing it as the sole linear quantum-geometric mechanism in such systems. Using representative centrosymmetric altermagnets, including the $d$-wave compound $\mathrm{FeSb}_2$ and the $g$-wave compound $\mathrm{CrSb}$, we show that the spin-rotation quantum metric directly controls this response. Crucially, we predict a giant linear spin magnetization of order $10^{-2}μ_B\,\mathrm{nm}^{-3}$ at magnetic fields of $\sim 10\,\mathrm{mT}$, exceeding typical experimental values for conventional magnets by several orders of magnitude. Our results identify a universal quantum geometric mechanism of spin magnetization operative in centrosymmetric systems in general, and establish centrosymmetric altermagnets as an ideal platform for its experimental detection with potential applications in spintronics.

### [173] [Observation of the Magnus Nonlinear Hall effect from Chiral Weyl Monopoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28091)
*Heda Zhang,Nikolai Peshcherenko,Ning Mao,Nianlong Zou,Jiaqiang Yan,Claudia Felser,Yang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文首次在手性外尔半金属CoSi中观测到非线性霍尔效应（NLHE），该材料中Berry曲率偶极子被对称性禁止。实验利用聚焦离子束制备的十字型器件，在零磁场下检测到稳健的二次谐波霍尔电压，并将非线性霍尔电导归因于自旋转电子波包的斜散射（skew scattering），其手性由体能带拓扑决定，类似于经典马格努斯效应。此外，NLHE信号呈现温度依赖的符号反转及随迁移率增长的线性场调制，直接反映了费米面附近拓扑外尔节点的分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非线性霍尔效应研究主要关注低对称性晶体中的Berry曲率偶极子，缺乏在高对称性手性晶格中直接探测Berry单极子（Berry monopole）的机制。

Method: 采用聚焦离子束（focused ion beam）制备的十字型器件（crossbar devices），在手性外尔半金属CoSi中测量零磁场下的二次谐波霍尔电压。

Result: 在CoSi中观测到稳健的零磁场二次谐波霍尔电压，呈现非线性霍尔效应的全部关键特征；NLHE信号随温度变化发生符号反转，并随载流子迁移率增加呈现强线性场依赖调制。

Conclusion: 实验确立了CoSi作为Berry单极子驱动的非线性输运平台的地位，提出了一种绕过传统对称性约束的斜散射途径以实现拓扑非线性霍尔响应。

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect (NLHE) connects crystalline symmetry to quantum geometry, offering a probe of band topology beyond linear transport. While most studies have focused on the Berry curvature dipole in low-symmetry crystals, mechanisms that directly probe Berry monopoles in higher-symmetry chiral lattices remain unexplored. Here, we report the observations of the NLHE in the chiral Weyl semimetal CoSi, a platform where the Berry curvature dipole is symmetry-forbidden. By employing focused ion beam-fabricated crossbar devices, we detect a robust second-harmonic Hall voltage under zero magnetic field, hosting all key signatures of the NLHE. Theoretical analysis attributes the nonlinear Hall conductivity to skew scattering of self-rotating electron wave packets, whose chirality is dictated by the underlying band topology, a process reminiscent of the classical Magnus effect. Furthermore, the NLHE signal exhibits a temperature-dependent sign reversal, and a strong, linearly field-dependent modulation that grows with carrier mobility, directly reflecting the topological Weyl nodes distribution near the Fermi level. These findings establish CoSi as a platform for Berry monopole-driven nonlinear transport, demonstrating a skew-scattering route to topological nonlinear Hall responses that bypasses conventional symmetry constraints.

### [174] [Intrinsic anomalous thermal hall effect as a signature of quantum metric in d-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28184)
*Rishi G. Gopalakrishnan,Srimayi Korrapati,Sumanta Tewari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnets）中的内禀反常热霍尔效应（intrinsic anomalous thermal Hall effect），发现该效应在无外磁场条件下由温度梯度三次方（(∇T)³）主导，其物理机制源于一种新引入的非线性热贝里联络极化率（nonlinear thermal Berry-connection polarizability），并揭示了独特的角依赖和实验可检验的温度/化学势依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索d波交变磁体中由量子几何（quantum geometry）驱动的内禀反常热霍尔效应，特别是在传统贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和量子度规（quantum metric）贡献因晶体对称性（crystalline symmetry）而消失时，寻找首个非零的非线性热输运贡献。

Method: 通过理论分析推导出非线性热贝里联络极化率这一新物理量，并基于对称性论证和量子几何框架计算热霍尔电导（anomalous thermal Hall conductance）对温度梯度阶数、晶体方向、温度和化学势的依赖性。

Result: 发现首个非零贡献出现在温度梯度的三次方阶，由非线性热贝里联络极化率主导；热霍尔电导随热梯度相对于晶轴旋转呈现独特的角分布，并表现出可由实验检验的特征温度与化学势依赖性。

Conclusion: 这些结果识别了独特的量子几何诱导热响应，并确立了交变磁体（altermagnets）作为探索内禀（即与散射时间无关）几何输运现象（geometric transport phenomena）的 promising 平台。

Abstract: We investigate the intrinsic anomalous thermal Hall effect in d-wave altermagnets, where a transverse heat current is generated by a longitudinal temperature gradient in the absence of a magnetic field, with the leading response proportional to $(\nabla T)^3$. In these systems, the intrinsic Berry curvature-driven linear and thermal quantum-metric-driven second-order anomalous thermal Hall currents vanish as a consequence of crystalline symmetry. We show that the first nonvanishing contribution arises at third order in the temperature gradient and is governed by a nonlinear thermal Berry-connection polarizability, a quantity introduced in this work. Our analysis reveals a distinctive angular dependence of the anomalous thermal Hall conductance as the applied thermal gradient is rotated with respect to the crystal axes. We also find characteristic temperature and chemical-potential dependences that can be tested experimentally. These results identify unique quantum geometry-induced thermal responses and establish altermagnets as a promising platform for exploring intrinsic (i.e., scattering-time-independent) geometric transport phenomena.

### [175] [Propulsion and far-field hydrodynamics of linked-sphere microswimmers with viscoelastic deformability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27348)
*Vimal Singh,Akash Choudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究受时间可逆驱动（reciprocal actuation）的粘弹性微型游泳者（viscoelastic microswimmers）的动力学，采用Kelvin-Voigt可变形模型分析两种（三球与四球）连接球体设计的运动学性能，发现三球设计存在最佳驱动频率、四球设计存在运动方向反转的临界频率，且远场流场主要呈现偶极（dipolar）和四极（quadrupolar）贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粘弹性（viscoelasticity）是可变形微生物运动策略的关键力学特性，也是微型机器人设计的重要基础。已有研究表明粘弹性可在时间可逆驱动下实现有效推进，但关于被动体具有粘弹性可变形性（viscoelastic deformability）的微型游泳者在受时间可逆驱动时的动力学行为尚需深入研究。

Method: 研究采用两种连接球体设计：三球设计（3-sphere design，驱动施加于一端）和四球设计（4-sphere design，驱动施加于中点）。采用Kelvin-Voigt可变形模型（Kelvin-Voigt deformability）描述被动体的粘弹性行为，分析其运动学性能与远场流体动力学信号。

Result: 三球游泳者（three-sphere swimmer）存在一个最佳驱动频率（optimal actuation frequency）；四球游泳者（four-sphere swimmer）存在一个临界频率（critical frequency），在该频率处运动方向发生反转。远场流场主要由偶极（dipolar）和四极（quadrupolar）贡献主导，其大小对驱动臂（actuator segment）的相对长度敏感。

Conclusion: 粘弹性可变形性使受时间可逆驱动的被动体也能实现有效推进，且不同设计（驱动位置）会导致截然不同的运动学行为（如频率最优与方向反转），远场流动特征受驱动器几何参数调控。

Abstract: Viscoelasticity governs the locomotion strategies of deformable microorganisms, rendering it a fundamental mechanical property of microbial motility and an integral component in the design of envisioned microbots. Recent studies have shown that it can enable effective propulsion through non-reciprocal body deformations, even under time-reversible actuation. In this work, we investigate the dynamics of model microswimmers driven by reciprocal actuation, wherein the passive body exhibits viscoelastic deformability. We consider two linked-sphere designs, distinguished by the location of actuation: applied at one end (3-sphere design) or at the midpoint of the swimmer body (4-sphere design). Adopting Kelvin-Voigt deformability, we characterize the kinematic performance of both designs: the three-sphere swimmer possesses an optimal actuation frequency, while the four-sphere swimmer exhibits a critical frequency at which the locomotion direction reverses. We examine the swimmer's far-field hydrodynamic signature and find that resulting flow field is characterized by dominant dipolar and quadrupolar contributions, whose magnitudes are sensitive to the relative length of the actuator segment.

</details>


### [176] [Topological antiqued mechanical toy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27554)
*Hirofumi Wada,Hayato Mizobata,Shuto Ueno,Taiju Yoneda*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、数值模拟和理论分析，揭示了经典玩具“雅各布天梯（Jacob's ladder）”中单向翻转波（unidirectional flipping waves）的物理机制：玩具在重力下具有双稳态（bistability），其扭结波（kink wave）属于拓扑孤子（topological soliton），但不同于Kane–Lubensky拓扑链（topological chain），玩具的柔软性（floppiness）导致了扭结与反扭结（antikink）的共存，且对称连接使其拓扑奇异（topologically singular），从而产生有趣的运动现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 雅各布天梯作为一种经典儿童玩具，其展现的单向翻转波现象长期以来缺乏物理层面上的合理解释，其设计原理的物理起源尚不明确。

Method: 结合水槽实验、数值模拟与理论分析，首先通过水槽实验排除了多米诺骨牌式（domino-like）机制；然后基于双稳态（bistability）和拓扑孤子（topological soliton）理论进行分析，并与Kane–Lubensky拓扑链进行对比；利用指数定理（index theorem）揭示了两者的本质差异；最后通过分析广义非对称玩具模型，揭示了对称连接导致的拓扑奇异性（topological singularity）。

Result: 实验排除了多米诺机制；玩具在重力下呈现双稳态，其扭结波为拓扑孤子，与Kane–Lubensky拓扑链在波动力学上具有相似性，但指数定理分析表明这种相似性仅停留在表面；玩具的柔软性允许扭结与反扭结共存，而这是拓扑链中禁止的模式；对称连接使玩具拓扑奇异，并实验观察到了扭结与反扭结波的成对湮灭（pair annihilation）。

Conclusion: 雅各布天梯的物理机制需要融合双稳态、拓扑孤子、柔软性与拓扑奇异性等多种物理概念才能完整理解，其动力学行为与Kane–Lubensky拓扑链存在本质区别。

Abstract: {\it Jacob's ladder} -- a classic children's toy -- is a simple mechanical frame comprising rigid blocks connected by strings that shows curious unidirectional flipping waves. Nonetheless, its physical origin remains elusive. By combining experiment, numeral simulation, and theory, we show that understanding the underlying design principle of this toy requires diverse physical ideas. First, we conduct a water-tank experiment that excludes the domino-like mechanism, thus defying widespread expectations. Subsequently, we analytically demonstrate that the toy is bistable under gravity, thus implying its kink wave as a class of topological solitons. The waves are surprisingly reminiscent -- both experimentally and theoretically -- to those in the Kane--Lubensky topological chain, owing to the stiffening of zero modes by the pretension under gravity. However, a close examination based on the index theorem reveals that the similarity remains superficial and that the floppiness of the toy underlies the kink and antikink coexistence -- a forbidden mode in the topological chain. By analyzing a generalized asymmetric toy, we reveal that its symmetric connection renders it topologically singular, thus resulting in amusing motions. We demonstrate these ideas by experimentally observing a dramatic pair annihilation of kink and antikink waves.

</details>


### [177] [Directional Cluster Migration Driven by Escape-Rate Asymmetry in Multi-Compartment Granular Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27611)
*Kai Kono,Hiroyuki Ebata,Shio Inagaki*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该实验研究通过垂直振动作用下的双颗粒体系，发现颗粒簇会在不同隔室间定向逐步迁移，并通过直接测量两种颗粒的流量与瞬时种群数的关系，揭示了小颗粒流量因大颗粒存在而增强、大颗粒流量因小颗粒存在而受抑（asymmetric interaction）的不对称相互机制。基于测量数据构建的最小流量模型（minimum flux model）能够复现所观察到的定向动力学行为，为振动颗粒系统中的集体输运提供了实验基础框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒体系因非弹性碰撞和摩擦而本质上是非平衡（out-of-equilibrium）系统。在机械振动驱动下，颗粒材料会表现出分聚（segregation）、团簇（clustering）和自发振荡（spontaneous oscillations）等丰富的集体行为。研究者希望通过实验揭示颗粒簇在垂直振动系统中定向逐步迁移的内在机理。

Method: 实验采用垂直振动（vertically vibrated）的双颗粒体系，包含小颗粒与大颗粒。研究者直接测量了两种颗粒的流量（flux）如何依赖于瞬时种群数（instantaneous particle populations），以量化不同颗粒种类之间的相互作用；并基于实测数据构建了一个最小流量模型。

Result: 测量结果显示存在不对称相互作用（asymmetric interaction）：大颗粒的存在会增强小颗粒的流量，而小颗粒的存在则会抑制大颗粒的流量。基于这一不对称流量关系的最小模型成功复现了实验中观察到的颗粒簇定向逐步迁移动力学。

Conclusion: 该工作为振动颗粒系统中的集体输运（collective transport）提供了一个以实验为基础的理论框架，揭示了颗粒种类间不对称流量耦合是驱动定向迁移的关键机制。

Abstract: Granular materials are inherently out-of-equilibrium systems due to energy dissipation through inelastic collisions and friction. When driven by mechanical agitation such as vibration, they exhibit rich collective behaviors including segregation, clustering, and spontaneous oscillations. Here, we report directional stepwise migration of particle clusters from one compartment to the next in a vertically vibrated granular system composed of small and large particles. To clarify the underlying mechanism, we directly measured how the flux of both particle species depends on the instantaneous particle populations. The measurements reveal an asymmetric interaction between particle species: the flux of small particles is enhanced by the presence of large particles, whereas that of large particles is suppressed by small particles. A minimal flux model incorporating these measured fluxes reproduces the observed directional dynamics and provides an experimentally grounded framework for collective transport in vibrated granular systems.

</details>


### [178] [Guided elastic waves for soft elastomer characterization: an alternative to conventional rheometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27722)
*Samuel Croquette,Pierre Chantelot,Daniel A. Kiefer,Claire Prada,Fabrice Lemoult*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于导波（guided elastic wave）的软弹性体力学表征方法，通过测量薄弹性体条带中的多模导波色散关系，结合频域粘弹性（viscoelasticity）和伸长相关声弹性（acoustoelasticity）理论框架，实现材料流变与超弹性参数的定量提取，并拓展了可测频率范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹性波传播对介质力学性质具有内在敏感性，而软弹性体（soft elastomers）的粘弹性和声弹性行为在宽频范围内缺乏统一、简便的力学表征手段。现有技术（如板-板流变测量）频带受限，无法充分覆盖材料频变响应。

Method: 采用薄弹性体条带作为波导（waveguide），支持多个面内导波模式；结合频闪测量（stroboscopic measurement）获取单色波场与的理论框架（耦合频率相关粘弹性与伸长相关声弹性），提取复值色散关系（complex-valued dispersion relations）；通过数值实现将实验色散曲线与理论定量匹配，反演流变与超弹性参数。

Result: 应用于多种商业硅酮弹性体（silicone elastomers），所得力学参数与常规板-板流变测量结果一致，且可测频率范围超越传统技术。

Conclusion: 该方法利用导波色散的多模丰富性以及波对频率和预应力的敏感性，为软弹性体力学表征提供了一条统一、宽带且实验简便的路径。

Abstract: Elastic wave propagation is intrinsically sensitive to the mechanical properties of the medium through which it travels. In soft elastomers, this makes guided elastic waves natural probes of viscoelastic and acoustoelastic behavior over a broad frequency range. In this work, we introduce a wave-based mechanical characterization method in which a thin elastomer strip acts as a waveguide supporting multiple in-plane guided modes. By combining stroboscopic measurements of monochromatic wave fields with a theoretical framework that couples frequency-dependent viscoelasticity and elongation-dependent acoustoelasticity, we extract complex-valued dispersion relations for guided modes under controlled static elongation. A dedicated numerical implementation allows these experimental dispersion curves to be quantitatively matched to theory, enabling identification of the material's rheological and hyperelastic parameters. Applied to several commercial silicone elastomers, the method yields mechanical parameters that are consistent with conventional plate-plate rheometry, while extending the accessible frequency range beyond that of conventional techniques. By exploiting the richness of guided-wave dispersion and the sensitivity of waves to both frequency and pre-stress, this approach provides a unified, broadband, and experimentally simple route to the mechanical characterization of soft elastomers.

### [179] [On Linear and Non-Linear Mechanics of Cyanobacterial Colonies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27760)

Method: 使用微吸管力传感器（micropipette force sensors）在单细胞分辨率下量化单个菌落的线性和非线性力学性质，并结合体相剪切流变学（bulk shear rheology）探测宏观力学特性。

Conclusion: 蓝藻菌落对自然混合过程引起的破碎具有高度抵抗力；力学测试可作为从物理角度更完整理解蓝藻菌落形成的有效工具。

Abstract: Toxic cyanobacterial blooms are a growing environmental concern that affects freshwater ecosystems, drinking water supplies, and public health. The cyanobacterium Microcystis is among the most important bloom forming species. It often grows in large colonies, which enhances its flotation, reduces grazing, and improves nutrient regulation. Microcystis cells are held together by a matrix of extracellular polymeric substances (EPS), making colony mechanics crucial for bloom formation. However, an analysis of the biomechanical properties of cyanobacterial colonies, and how these properties relate to environmental conditions like nutrient availability, remains largely missing. Here, we use micropipette force sensors to quantify the linear and non-linear mechanical properties of individual colonies at single-cell resolution. Bulk shear rheology complements these measurements by probing macroscopic properties. The measured tensile strength and yield stress are broadly comparable to those of bacterial biofilms and are far greater than the hydrodynamic stresses typically found in wind-mixed lakes. This implies that cyanobacterial colonies are highly resistant to fragmentation by natural mixing processes. We also show that low nutrient availability, particularly low phosphorus, produced stronger colonies, suggesting structural changes in the EPS. Overall, our results establish mechanical testing as a tool for a more complete and physically grounded understanding of cyanobacterial colony formation.

### [180] [Acoustic modulation of shear thickening transition in dense adhesive suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27876)
*Aoxuan Wang,Fabrice Toussaint,Thomas Gibaud*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过流变-超声实验与理论分析，揭示了高功率超声并非直接降低密实悬浮液的粘度，而是通过引入孔隙尺度涨落流体力学力，将不连续剪切增稠（DST）转变推向更高剪切速率，从而实现对增稠行为的连续重整化控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密实悬浮液中的不连续剪切增稠（discontinuous shear thickening, DST）会导致流动失稳，限制其在诸多系统中的加工应用。已有报道称高功率超声可降低此类材料的表观粘度，但其物理机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用流变-超声（rheo-ultrasound）联合实验装置，对粘附性玉米淀粉密实悬浮液（其剪切增稠源于嵌入非均匀密度波结构中的脆弱承力力网络）进行测量。通过分析应力概率分布的塌缩行为，并结合时间尺度分离的理论框架进行解释。

Result: 超声并未直接降低粘度，而是使剪切增稠转变向更高剪切速率移动。应力概率分布在主曲线上发生塌缩，表明体系连续演化至更类流体状态，不存在尖锐阈值。流体化机制包括边界滑移、拖曳力涨落对力网络的大规模失稳以及局域声流。

Conclusion: 超声通过在孔隙尺度引入涨落流体力学力，改变力网络的稳定性，使得维持堵塞状态（jammed states）需要更大的应力或剪切速率，从而实现对DST转变的连续重整化（renormalization）。该发现为粘附性悬浮液中的声学流体化提供了自洽的物理图像，确立了超声作为控制受限流动中不连续剪切增稠的有效工具。

Abstract: Discontinuous shear thickening (DST) in dense suspensions leads to flow instabilities that limit processing in many systems. While high-power ultrasound has been reported to reduce the apparent viscosity of such materials, the origin of this effect remains unclear. Here, we investigate dense adhesive cornstarch suspensions, where shear thickening arises from fragile, load-bearing force networks embedded in heterogeneous density-wave structures. Using a rheo-ultrasound setup, we show that ultrasound does not directly reduce viscosity but instead shifts the shear-thickening transition toward higher shear rates. This is evidenced by the collapse of stress probability distributions onto master curves, revealing a continuous evolution toward more fluid-like states without a sharp threshold. We interpret these results through a separation of time scales, in which the suspension behaves as an effectively immobile porous medium subjected to high-frequency interstitial flows. Fluidization then arises from a combination of boundary slip, bulk destabilization of force networks by drag-force fluctuations, and localized acoustic streaming. Beyond these mechanisms, we propose that ultrasound modifies the stability of force networks by introducing fluctuating hydrodynamic forces at the pore scale. As a result, larger stresses or shear rates are required to sustain jammed states, leading to a continuous renormalization of the DST transition. These findings provide a consistent physical picture of acoustic fluidization in adhesive suspensions and establish ultrasound as a powerful tool to control discontinuous shear thickening in confined flows.

*Benjamin Sorkin,Ned S. Wingreen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统通常依赖复杂的生物分子机器消耗能量来实现运动（motility），该工作试图探索一种更简化的、无需分子马达的替代推进机制。

Method: 提出一种最小化机制（minimal mechanism）：相分离蛋白被酶钝化后，由锚定在胶体表面的互补酶重新激活；该钝化-激活循环（passivation-activation cycle）诱发对称性破缺（symmetry breaking），在胶体表面附近成核并稳定一个凝聚体（condensate），从而对胶体施加排斥力以实现推进。

Conclusion: 基于生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）的推进机制可能为生物运输提供一种无需马达蛋白（motor-free）的补充路径。

Abstract: Living systems routinely consume energy to achieve motility, often using intricate biomolecular machinery. In this work, we show that active droplets can sustain indefinite self-propulsion of a spherical colloid in an otherwise homogeneous, isotropic, and autonomous environment. Our proposed minimal mechanism consists of phase-separating proteins, enzymes passivating them, and complementary enzymes anchored to the colloid surface that reactivate the proteins. This passivation-activation cycle gives rise to a symmetry breaking - nucleation and stabilization of a condensate near the colloid surface, which in turn exerts a repulsive force on the colloid. We numerically demonstrate that this mechanism can propel micron-sized colloids at speeds of up to a hundred microns per second. This propulsion mode is strongly resistant to Brownian fluctuations and external forces, suggesting that propulsion mechanisms based on biomolecular condensates may offer a complementary, motor-free route to biological transport.

### [182] [Mapping the Phase Diagram of the Vicsek Model with Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28167)
*Grace T. Bai,Brandon B. Le*

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习方法对Vicsek群集模型在三维参数空间中的相结构进行分类与插值，通过K-Means聚类生成有序、无序和共存相标签，训练神经网络分类器达到0.92的准确率，成功解析了狭窄的共存区域并推断出全局相图。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对Vicsek模型在三维参数空间(η, ρ, v₀)进行模拟采样，利用长时间动力学观测量（long-time dynamical observables）表征每个参数点；采用K-Means聚类将各点分配至无序相（disorder）、有序相（order）或共存相（coexistence）；以聚类标签为监督信号训练神经网络分类器，学习参数到相的映射关系。

Result: 神经网络分类器达到0.92的分类准确率；生成的相图清晰地分辨出有序相与无序相之间狭窄的共存区域，并将推断的相边界扩展至原始模拟采样点之外。

Conclusion: 该机器学习框架为集体运动模型提供了一种从稀疏模拟数据系统性地推导全局相图的方法，具有通用性和可推广性。

Abstract: In this study, we use machine learning to classify and interpolate the phase structure of the Vicsek flocking model across the three-dimensional parameter space $(η,ρ,v_0)$. We construct a dataset of simulated parameter points and characterize each point using long-time dynamical observables. These observables are then used as inputs to a K-Means clustering procedure, which assigns each point to a disorder, order, or coexistence phase. Using these clustered labels, we train a neural-network classifier to learn the mapping from model parameters to phase behavior, achieving a classification accuracy of 0.92. The resulting phase map resolves a narrow coexistence region separating the ordered and disordered phases and extends the inferred phase boundaries beyond the originally sampled simulation points. More broadly, this approach provides a systematic way to convert sparse simulation data into a global phase diagram for collective-motion models.

### [184] [Anomalous tunneling as a low-energy theorem for Nambu-Goldstone modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27489)
*Keisuke Fujii,Daichi Kagamihara,Masaru Hongo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本论文基于低能有效场论（low-energy effective field theory, EFT）证明，Nambu-Goldstone (NG) 模的反常隧穿（anomalous tunneling）是一项由对称性和标度性（scaling）决定的普适低能定理：在对称性保持的局域势下，长波极限中透射系数趋于1；而对称性破缺扰动则会抑制透射，导致反常隧穿消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反常隧穿现象（势垒透射系数在入射能量趋零时趋于1）已在自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking, SSB）系统（如超流体）中被观测到，但其产生的普适条件尚不清楚。本文旨在建立该现象的普适理论基础。

Method: 采用低能有效场论（EFT）框架，将NG模在外部势中的散射问题表述为空间依赖的EFT系数形式；通过对称性与标度性分析，区分对称性保持与对称性破缺两类局域势对隧穿行为的影响。

Result: 对称性保持的局域势在长波极限下是无关（irrelevant）的，导致完美透射（perfect transmission），即反常隧穿；而对称性破缺扰动是相关（relevant）的，会抑制透射，使反常隧穿消失。该普适行为分别以超流体声子（phonons）和磁振子（magnons）为例进行了展示。

Conclusion: 反常隧穿是Nambu-Goldstone模的一个普适低能定理，其成立与否完全由外部势是否保持对称性决定。该结果为理解SSB系统中低能输运行为提供了统一的理论视角。

Abstract: Anomalous tunneling refers to the phenomenon in which the transmission coefficient through a potential barrier approaches unity as the energy of an incident particle or quasiparticle tends to zero. This counterintuitive effect has been reported in systems exhibiting spontaneous symmetry breaking (SSB), such as superfluids, yet the general conditions for its occurrence remain unclear. In this Letter, we establish that anomalous tunneling of Nambu-Goldstone (NG) modes is a universal low-energy theorem dictated solely by symmetry and scaling, using a low-energy effective field theory (EFT) framework. We formulate the scattering of NG modes by external potentials in terms of spatially dependent EFT coefficients and demonstrate that symmetry-preserving localized potentials are irrelevant in the long-wavelength limit, leading to perfect transmission. In contrast, symmetry-breaking perturbations are relevant and suppress transmission, resulting in the absence of anomalous tunneling. We illustrate this universal behavior with explicit examples of superfluid phonons and magnons.

</details>


### [185] [Quantum integrable matrix models of spinor Bose gases in one spatial dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27885)
*Hannes Köper,Thomas Gasenzer*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明一维具有排斥密度-密度相互作用和反铁磁自旋-自旋耦合的简并自旋子（spinor）玻色气体可由非线性薛定谔模型的量子可积矩阵推广描述，并利用代数Bethe-ansatz构建了任意大小矩阵场算符的本征态，推导了相应的Bethe方程。通过分析2×2模型（对应自旋-1玻色气体），导出了平衡热力学积分方程，计算了基态相图，并发现配对束缚态会修改一维相互作用玻色子的泡利不相容原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理任意自旋多重态（spin multiplets）及其自旋-自旋相互作用方面存在局限，本文旨在将先前的技术推广到更一般的矩阵场算符情形，以统一描述一维简并自旋子玻色气体中的量子可积结构。

Method: 采用代数Bethe-ansatz技术构造任意尺寸矩阵场算符的本征态，并推导相应的Bethe方程（Bethe equations）。针对2×2矩阵模型（即自旋-1玻色气体），进一步推导描述平衡热力学性质的积分方程组，并通过数值与解析相结合的方法计算基态相图（ground state phase diagram）。

Result: 建立了由m×n矩阵玻色场算符描述的一维量子可积模型，并获得了任意自旋多重态下的本征态与守恒量谱。对于自旋-1玻色气体，在化学势与外磁场构成的参数平面上得到了基态相图。发现了配对束缚态（paired bound states）对泡利不相容原理的修正：当Lieb参数γ>4/3时，任意两个准粒子快度（quasiparticle rapidities）均不能重合。

Conclusion: 本文提出的矩阵推广的量子可积框架为一维简并自旋子玻色气体的严格求解提供了统一途径，揭示了配对束缚态对一维玻色子统计性质的重要影响，为理解低维量子多体系统中的自旋-电荷关联奠定了基础。

Abstract: Degenerate spinor Bose gases with repulsive density-density interaction and anti-ferromagnetic spin-spin coupling in one spatial dimension are shown to be described by a quantum integrable matrix extension of the nonlinear Schrödinger model, whose fundamental fields are described by an $m\,\times\,n$ matrix of bosonic field operators. The eigenstates of this model are constructed for arbitrarily sized matrix field operators by means of algebraic Bethe-ansatz techniques, and the corresponding Bethe equations governing the spectra of conserved quantities are derived. The approach thus generalizes previously chosen techniques to account for arbitrary spin multiplets and their spin-spin interaction. Focusing on the specific case of the $2\times2$ model, which is shown to correspond to a spin-$1$ Bose gas, a set of integral equations is derived, which describe its equilibrium thermodynamic properties. From these, the ground state phase diagram is computed both, numerically and analytically in the parameter plane spanned by the chemical potential and an external magnetic field. Furthermore, the existence of paired bound states is shown to modify the Pauli exclusion principle for interacting bosons in one dimension. In particular, it is found that no two quasiparticle rapidities can coincide, provided that the Lieb parameter satisfies $γ>4/3$.

</details>


### [186] [Bosonic Josephson junction dynamics: interplay between quantum and thermal fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27809)
*Andrea Bardin,Francesco Lorenzi,Luca Salasnich*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在平均场（mean-field）描述之外，考虑热涨落和量子涨落对玻色约瑟夫森结（Bosonic Josephson junction）超流动力学的影响，推导了修正的运动方程，并系统分析了两种涨落在不同动力学量上的相反作用及其相对重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的平均场理论未能充分描述热涨落与量子涨落对约瑟夫森结超流动力学的贡献，需要超越平均场框架来更准确地预测动力学行为。

Method: 采用考虑均匀气体中涨落的 formalism，在非凝聚组分输运可忽略的假设下，结合双阱近似（two-site approximation）推导出修正的运动方程，并以半解析方式预测两种涨落对动力学量的影响。

Result: 热涨落降低约瑟夫森频率（Josephson frequency），并增大宏观量子自俘获（macroscopic quantum self-trapping）和自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）的临界强度；量子涨落则表现出相反的作用。通过计算近期玻色约瑟夫森结实验的相关参数，发现可实验实现的区域主要由量子涨落主导。

Conclusion: 量子涨落与热涨落在所有动力学量上作用相反，且在实际实验条件下量子涨落占据主导地位。

Abstract: We investigate the superfluid dynamics of a Josephson junction beyond the mean-field description, incorporating the role of thermal fluctuations as well as quantum fluctuations. Using a formalism that accounts for the fluctuations in a homogeneous gas, and under the assumption that the transport of the non-condensed component is negligible, we derive a corrected equation of motion within the two-site approximation. The resulting corrections for the typical dynamical quantities, like the Josephson frequency, the strength of macroscopic quantum self-trapping, and the threshold for spontaneous symmetry breaking, allow us to predict the effects of both types of fluctuations and assess their relative importance in different regimes in a semianalytical fashion. For all the dynamical quantities, the quantum fluctuations are shown to play an opposite role with respect to the thermal fluctuations. Josephson frequency is decreased by thermal fluctuations and both the critical strenghts of macroscopic quantum self trapping and spontaneous symmetry breaking are increased. We assess the experimentally accessible regimes by calculating the relevant parameters of recent experimental realizations of Bosonic Josephson junction and show that the expected regime is dominated by quantum fluctuations.

</details>


### [187] [Observation of Vinen turbulence during far-from-equilibrium Bose-Einstein condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28191)
*Sebastian J. Morris,Martin Gazo,Simon M. Fischer,Haoyu Zhang,Christopher J. Ho,Nigel R. Cooper,Christoph Eigen,Zoran Hadzibabic*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过实验观测了均匀三维玻色气体中的量子湍流（quantum turbulence）衰变过程，利用物质波放大技术（matter-wave techniques）测量涡旋线长度密度（vortex line-length density）$\mathcal{L}$，发现其衰变行为与Vinen“超量子”湍流（ultraquantum turbulence）的理论预言一致。弱相互作用气体的宏观动力学与不可压缩流体相符，且$\mathcal{L}$的衰变不依赖于原子间相互作用强度，与强相互作用的超流氦类似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远非平衡量子流体的弛豫过程与长程序（long-range order）的出现密切相关，理论上该过程与涡旋线构成的湍流各向同性缠结（turbulent isotropic tangle of vortex lines）的衰变有关。本文旨在通过实验观测并研究这种衰变现象，以检验相关理论预言。

Method: 研究采用均匀三维原子玻色气体（homogeneous 3D atomic Bose gas）作为实验体系。通过物质波技术放大气体密度分布，并对放大后云团的薄层进行成像，从而观测随机取向的涡旋线印记，并测量涡旋线长度密度$\mathcal{L}$。

Result: 观测到的$\mathcal{L}$衰变行为与Vinen“超量子”湍流预言一致。尽管弱相互作用气体具有高度可压缩性（highly compressible），其大尺度动力学行为与不可压缩流体（incompressible hydrodynamic fluid）一致，且$\mathcal{L}$的衰变不依赖于原子间相互作用强度，与强相互作用的超流氦（superfluid helium）中的行为相似。

Conclusion: 弱相互作用的均匀三维玻色气体中的量子湍流衰变，在宏观尺度上展现出与不可压缩流体及强相互作用超流体类似的行为，表明该体系的非平衡弛豫过程具有普适性特征。

Abstract: Relaxation of far-from-equilibrium quantum fluids, intimately related to the emergence of long-range order, is theoretically associated with the decay of a turbulent isotropic tangle of vortex lines. We observe and study such decaying quantum turbulence in a homogeneous 3D atomic Bose gas. Using matter-wave techniques to magnify the gas density distribution, and then imaging a thin slice of the magnified cloud, we observe imprints of randomly oriented vortex lines and measure the vortex line-length density $\mathcal{L}$. The observed decay of $\mathcal{L}$ agrees with the prediction for Vinen `ultraquantum' turbulence. Although our weakly interacting gases are highly compressible, their large-scale dynamics are consistent with the behavior of an incompressible hydrodynamic fluid, with the decay of $\mathcal{L}$ not depending on the strength of the interatomic interactions and being similar to that in the strongly interacting superfluid helium.

</details>

### [188] [Stepping up enhanced rate calculations with EATR-flooding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27136)
*Nicodemo Mazzaferro,Willmor J Pena Ccoa,Pilar Cossio,Glen M. Hocky*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出EATR-flooding方法，通过跨多组模拟逐步提升偏置势强度，替代原有对时间依赖偏置的需求，从而在更广泛的准静态偏置方案中准确计算缓慢生物分子过程的速率常数，并具备过偏置内检与单一γ参数预测等优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖时间偏置的速率常数方法（如EATR）对于准静态偏置方案（如“flooding”或OPES）适用性有限，需要一种不依赖时间变化偏置但仍能准确估计速率常数的通用方法。

Method: 提出EATR-flooding方法，通过跨多组模拟逐步提升偏置势（biasing potential）的强度，替代原有对时间依赖偏置（time-dependent bias）的需求，并利用一个学习得到的集体变量质量因子γ修正偏置效率。

Result: 在粗粒化蛋白质系统上验证了EATR-flooding与标准EATR相比精度相当且效率无显著损失，在全原子腔体-配体模型上也展示了良好性能；该方法具备过偏置（over-biasing）内部检查功能，且对于给定集体变量仅需预测单一γ参数。

Conclusion: EATR-flooding不仅适用于OPES模拟，还可推广到更一般的基于集体变量偏置的增强采样（CV biasing enhanced sampling）方法，具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: Several recent methods have shown that it is possible to compute rate constants of very slow biomolecular processes using simulations where a time-dependent bias is added along one or several collective variables (CVs). We previously reported the exponential average time-dependent rate (EATR) method, which can improve upon these approaches by accounting for how efficiently the external biasing potential modifies the observed rate using a learned CV-quality factor $γ$. This results in more accurate rate estimates using the same data when biasing a suboptimal coordinate. However, as formulated EATR depended on the biasing potential varying over time to properly determine the biasing efficiency, which limits the method's applicability to quasi-static biasing schemes such as ``flooding'' or on-the-fly probability enhanced sampling (OPES). Here, we present the EATR-flooding approach, which generalizes our method by replacing the need for a time dependent bias by instead varying (stepping up) the strength of the biasing potential across multiple sets of simulations. We implement this approach as an open-source Python library, and demonstrate that this approach is accurate without substantial loss of efficiency compared to standard EATR for a coarse-grained protein system, and also show good performance on a fully atomistic cavity-ligand model. Two additional appealing features of EATR-flooding are an internal check for over-biasing and the fact that only a single $γ$ parameter is predicted for a given choice of CVs, as compared to our earlier results where $γ$ empirically depended on biasing rate. Finally, we believe EATR-flooding applies not only to OPES simulations but more generally to CV biasing enhanced sampling approaches, making it broadly useful.

</details>

### [189] [Phase-Transition-Driven Hyperbolic Optical Response and Directional Polaritons in Epitaxial VO2 Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27005)
*Maria Chiara Paolozzi,Annalisa D Arco,Ilaria Martinelli,Lorenzo Mosesso,Jacopo Sera,Alessandro D Elia,Augusto Marcelli,Yingxue Chen,Chongwen Zou,Maria Cristina Larciprete,Marco Centini,Stefano Lupi,Salvatore Macis*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究了二氧化钒（VO2）在金属金红石相中因晶体各向异性诱导的双曲光学行为，利用宽波段偏振光谱测量提取了光学电导率和介电函数，定量评估了其作为热可切换双曲光学介质的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二氧化钒在约67°C发生可逆的金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition, MIT），伴随显著的电子、结构和光学变化，使其成为动态可调光子与光电器件的理想平台。本文旨在探究VO2在金红石金属相中由本征晶体各向异性如何诱导双曲光学行为。

Method: 制备了两块不同厚度的外延VO2薄膜，生长在(110)取向的MgF2衬底上。采用覆盖红外到紫外光谱范围的宽波段偏振光谱测量，分别独立研究单斜相和金红石相的光学响应，从中提取光学电导率和介电函数。

Result: 在金红石金属相中观察到显著的各向异性，沿金红石c轴方向自由载流子响应增强。在近红外窄光谱窗口内，两个主轴方向的介电张量实部符号相反，表明出现了II型双曲色散（hyperbolic type-II dispersion）。通过品质因子（quality factor）和介电各向异性度对双曲响应进行了定量评估。

Conclusion: 本研究扩展了对相变材料中各向异性驱动光学现象的理解，表明VO2薄膜可作为热可切换双曲光学介质，为可调谐和可重构光子应用提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Optical anisotropy in crystalline solids enables direction-dependent light-matter interactions and underpins a variety of advanced photonic functionalities. In this context, Vanadium dioxide (VO2) represents a prototypical material that undergoes a reversible MIT near 67°C, accompanied by pronounced electronic, structural, and optical modifications. The MIT not only dramatically modifies the VO2 electrical conductivity but also reshapes its anisotropic optical response, making VO2 an exceptional platform for dynamically tunable photonic and optoelectronic devices. In this work, we investigate how the intrinsic crystalline anisotropy of VO2 induces a hyperbolic optical behavior in the metallic rutile phase. We study two epitaxial VO2 thin films of different thicknesses grown on (110) oriented MgF2 substrates. Broadband polarized spectroscopic measurements, spanning the infrared to UV spectral range, are employed to independently investigate the optical response in both the monoclinic and rutile phases. From these measurements, we extract the optical conductivity and the dielectric function, revealing a pronounced anisotropy in the rutile metallic phase, with an enhanced free-carrier response along the rutile c axis. Our data show that, within a narrow near-infrared spectral window, the real parts of the dielectric tensor components along the two principal axes acquire opposite signs, indicating the emergence of a hyperbolic type-II dispersion. The hyperbolic response is quantitatively evaluated through the quality factor and the degree of dielectric anisotropy, enabling a systematic assessment of VO2 as a thermally switchable, hyperbolic optical medium. These findings expand the understanding of anisotropy-driven optical phenomena in phase-change materials and highlight VO2 thin films as a promising platform for tunable and reconfigurable photonic applications.

</details>


### [190] [Second harmonic generation and third harmonic generation in topological insulator-based van der Waals metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27864)
*Alessandra Di Gaspare,Sara Ghayeb,Craig Knox,Edmund H. Linfield,Joshua Freeman,Miriam S. Vitiello*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用嵌入有 Bi2Se3 或 (InxBi(1-x))2Se3/Bi2Se3 范德华异质结构的单/双开口环谐振器阵列，在拓扑绝缘体中实现了6.4 THz（偶次）至9.7 THz（奇次）的高次谐波产生（HHG），该现象来自体态的奇次谐波（中心对称性）与拓扑表面态的奇偶谐波混合（对称性破缺）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator, TI）被预测可支持体态和拓扑表面的非常规高次谐波产生（HHG），但两者通常难以区分，且至今缺乏实验验证。

Method: 利用单/双开口环谐振器（split ring resonator）阵列提供强光场放大，并嵌入 Bi2Se3 或 (InxBi(1-x))2Se3/Bi2Se3 范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures），在太赫兹（THz）频率下驱动 HHG 实验。

Result: 成功在6.4 THz（偶次）至9.7 THz（奇次）频率范围内实现了上转换，其中体态中心对称性（centro-symmetry）仅贡献奇次谐波，而拓扑表面态的对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）同时贡献奇次和偶次谐波。

Conclusion: 实验证明了拓扑绝缘体可同时产生奇偶次高次谐波，其中偶次谐波来源于拓扑表面态的对称性破缺，为区分体态与表面态贡献提供了依据，并拓展了太赫兹频段的上转换技术。

Abstract: High-order harmonic generation (HHG) in solids - the frequency up-conversion of an optical signal - is governed by symmetries. At terahertz (THz) frequencies, HHG is a key technology to access high frequency spectral windows that are usually difficult to cover using conventional solid state laser technologies. This effect has been recently exploited in graphene where HHG has been demonstrated, albeit only at odd multiples of the driving frequency owing to its inherent centro-symmetry. In topological insulators (TIs), the combination of spin-orbit interaction and time-reversal symmetry create an insulating bulk state with an inverted band order, inseparably connected with conducting surface states. TIs have been predicted to support unconventional high harmonic generation from the bulk and topological surface, which are usually difficult to be distinguished. However, no experimental results have been provided, so far. Here, we exploit the strong optical field amplification provided by an array of single or double split ring resonators, with embedded Bi2Se3 or (InxBi(1-x))2Se3/ Bi2Se3 van der Waals heterostructures, to achieve up-conversion in the 6.4 (even) - 9.7 (odd) THz frequency range. This results from bulk centro-symmetry (odd states) and symmetry breaking in the topological surface states (odd and even).

</details>
